## 0. лӘ©м ҒВ·authorityВ·мқҙлІҲ лӢЁкі„ мӨ‘лӢЁм„ 

мқҙ л¬ём„ңлҠ” кё°мЎҙ л№„көҗ л¬ём„ңлҘј лӢӨмӢң мҡ”м•Ҫн•ҳлҠ” л¬ём„ңк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. нҳ„мһ¬ `main`, лі„лҸ„ candidate branch,
мқҪкё° м „мҡ© runtime/schema кҙҖм°°, м ҖмһҘ owner кі„м•Ҫмқ„ н•ң кё°мӨҖм„ мңјлЎң л¬¶кі , лӢӨмқҢ к°ңл°ңмһҗк°Җ мҠ№мқёлҗң phaseлҘј
exact bounded child packetмңјлЎң лӮҙлҰҙ мҲҳ мһҲкІҢ л§Ңл“ңлҠ” **кө¬м¶• л§ҲмҠӨн„°н”Ңлһң**мқҙлӢӨ. мқҙ л¬ём„ңмқҳ phase card
мһҗмІҙлҠ” file-write к¶Ңн•ңмқҙ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ.

AuthorityлҠ” лӢӨмқҢ мҲңм„ңлЎң м Ғмҡ©н•ңлӢӨ.

1. м ҖмһҘмҶҢ лЈЁнҠё `AGENTS.md`
2. `AGENT_EXECUTION_CONTRACT_V0.md`
3. `DEVELOPMENT_ROADMAP_V0.md`
4. ownerк°Җ мқҙлІҲ мӢӨн–үмқ„ мң„н•ҙ м§Җм •н•ң
   `HIGH_PERFORMANCE_PC_TASK_ENGINE_BUILD_MASTER_PLAN_PROMPT_V0.md`
5. `TASK_ENGINE_CONTEXT_FOUNDATION_CROSS_VALIDATION_V0.md`мқҳ CV-01~CV-09мҷҖ
   owner-fixed P0~P10 м„ н–ү л¶ҲліҖмӢқ: мһҗлҸҷ м •лӢөмқҙ м•„лӢҲлқј public evidenceлЎң лҸ…лҰҪ нҢҗм •н•  кІҖмҰқ packet
6. кё°мЎҙ lifecycleВ·redesignВ·ENGINE-12/13В·нҶөн•© кІҖмҰқ л¬ём„ң: ліҖкІҪ лҢҖмғҒмқҙ м•„лӢҲлқј л№„көҗ oracle

2026-07-18 мһҘл№„ м—ӯн•  ліҙм •мқҖ нҳ„мһ¬ target device assignmentл§Ң лҢҖмІҙн•ңлӢӨ.
`task_engine_redesign/**`мҷҖ нҶөн•© кІҖмҰқ л¬ём„ңмқҳ кіјкұ° Mac-primary л¬ёкө¬лҠ” byte-stable л№„көҗ oracleлЎң
к·ёлҢҖлЎң ліҙмЎҙн•ҳл©°, нҳ„мһ¬ runtime м§ҖмӢңлӮҳ HPP cutover мҰқкұ°лЎң мӮ¬мҡ©н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

мҙҲкё° кі„нҡҚ ліҙм • лӢЁкі„мқҳ н—Ҳмҡ© лІ”мң„лҠ” мқҙ л¬ём„ңмҷҖ `CHANGELOG.md`мқҳ мһ‘м„ұВ·кІҖмҰқВ·кіөк°ң Git publishлҝҗмқҙм—ҲлӢӨ.
к·ё м ңн•ңмқҖ мң„ н‘ңмқҳ owner task envelopeк°Җ лі„лҸ„ мҠ№мқён•ң 2026-07-19 bounded кө¬нҳ„ sliceлЎң лҢҖмІҙлҗҳм—ҲлӢӨ.
мқҙлІҲ sliceлҠ” public мҪ”л“ңВ·н…ҢмҠӨнҠё, private metadata receipt, мӢӨм ң мӣҗмІң 5кұҙмқҳ кІ©лҰ¬ custody,
standalone ERP copy, CSV/XLSX, temporary localhost MCP, held knowledge/RAG previewк№Ңм§Җл§Ң н—Ҳмҡ©н–ҲлӢӨ.

лӢӨмқҢ н–үмң„лҠ” bounded pilotмқҙ лҒқлӮң л’Өм—җлҸ„ лі„лҸ„ production activation мҠ№мқё м „к№Ңм§Җ мӨ‘лӢЁн•ңлӢӨ.

- мҡҙмҳҒ ERP DB schema/data migration, backfill, accepted/current pointer ліҖкІҪ
- кё°мЎҙ TaskDriver лҳҗлҠ” mail/voice/file writer мӨ‘м§ҖВ·көҗмІҙ, schedulerВ·alertВ·network service нҷңм„ұнҷ”
- мҡҙмҳҒ clone к°ұмӢ , HPP sole-writer cutover, Mac mini failover/failback мҠ№кІ©
- workspace/OneDrive/junction renameВ·мқҙлҸҷВ·мӮӯм ңВ·repair
- private мӣҗл¬ёВ·м—…л¬ҙ payloadмқҳ public ліөмӮ¬, Drive/NotebookLM publication, live RAG ingestion
- LAN listener, firewall, team credentialВ·mTLS л°ңкёү лҳҗлҠ” production download к¶Ңн•ң нҷңм„ұнҷ”

### ASSUMPTIONS

- ownerк°Җ л§җн•ң вҖңлІ”мң„к°Җ л„“м–ҙмЎҢлӢӨвҖқлҠ” core TaskDriverл§Ңмқҙ м•„лӢҲлқј м ҖмһҘ кІҪкі„, м§ҖмӢқ кі„мёө, PC м—ӯн• ,
  AX Workspace, AgentRun, Engineering IQк№Ңм§Җ **кі„нҡҚм—җ нҸ¬н•Ё**н•ҳлқјлҠ” лң»мңјлЎң н•ҙм„қн•ңлӢӨ.
- AX WorkspaceВ·AgentRunВ·Engineering IQВ·MLмқҖ core TaskDriverмқҳ м„ н–үмЎ°кұҙмқҙ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. к°Ғк°Ғ нӣ„мҶҚ phaseмҷҖ
  лі„лҸ„ owner gateлҘј к°–лҠ”лӢӨ.
- кҙҖм°°н•ҳм§Җ лӘ»н•ң мӮ¬мӢӨмқҖ м¶”м •н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. `UNKNOWN`мқҖ л°ҳл“ңмӢң `DEFER` лҳҗлҠ” gateлЎң м—°кІ°н•ңлӢӨ.
- мқҙ ліҙм •мқҖ public `main`мқҳ мҪ”л“ңВ·кі„м•Ҫл§Ң лӢӨмӢң лҢҖмЎ°н–ҲлӢӨ. м•„лһҳмқҳ кіјкұ° runtime/DB aggregateмҷҖ
  host/profile кҙҖм°°мқҖ `HISTORICAL_REPORTED`мқҙл©° мқҙлІҲ ліҙм •м—җм„ң fresh мһ¬кҙҖм°°н•ң CURRENTк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ.
- `ui-workspace`лҠ” canon/orchestration rootк°Җ м•„лӢҲлқј root contractлҘј мҶҢл№„н•ҳлҠ” **derived UI consumer**лӢӨ.
- нҶөн•© мӢңк°„м¶•В·contextВ·мғқлӘ…мҲҳлҠ” н•ҳлӮҳмқҳ кұ°лҢҖ мӣҗмһҘмқҙ м•„лӢҲлқј source-local append-only мқҙл Ҙл“Өмқ„
  project-qualified exact typed refлЎң н•Ёк»ҳ мқҪлҠ” rebuildable projectionмқҙлӢӨ.
- ingressмқҳ м•Ҳм „ кё°ліёк°’мқҖ pointer/hash/referenceлӢӨ. лӢӨл§Ң MCP uploadмІҳлҹј мӨ‘м•ҷ м„ңл№„мҠӨк°Җ bytesлҘј м§Ғм ‘
  мҲҳл №н•ң кІҪмҡ° к·ё service inboxк°Җ source custodyлҘј к°Җм§Җл©°, project мҠ№кІ©В·copy/move/deriveлҠ” лі„лҸ„
  promoter authorityмҷҖ receipt м—ҶмқҙлҠ” мқјм–ҙлӮҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
- personal WorkSessionмқҳ кі„нҡҚ кё°ліё cardinalityлҠ” `{task assignment epoch, account}`лӢ№ active primary
  н•ҳлӮҳлӢӨ. checkpointлҠ” м—¬лҹ¬ к°ңмқј мҲҳ мһҲм§Җл§Ң closeoutмқҖ мҷ„лЈҢ м ңм•Ҳмқј лҝҗ ERP кіөмӢқ мҷ„лЈҢк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ.
  exact local outbox pathВ·м•”нҳёнҷ”В·ліҙмЎҙВ·missing SLAлҠ” `VERIFY_HP`лӢӨ.
- ERP UI/MCPлҘј accepted derived dataмқҳ мЈј мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ мЎ°нҡҢл©ҙмңјлЎң м„Өкі„н•ңлӢӨ. CSV/ICS/XLSXлҠ” к°җмӮ¬В·мҳӨн”„лқјмқё
  snapshotмқҙл©°, knowledge queryлҠ” `project|common` scopeлҘј лӘ…мӢңн•ҳкі  implicit fallbackмқ„ н—Ҳмҡ©н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
- нҳ„мһ¬ Hiworks POP3 кі„м • мҲҳм§‘мқҖ л°ӣмқҖнҺём§Җн•Ёл§Ңмқ„ ліҙмһҘн•ҳл©° нҢҖмӣҗлі„ ліҙлӮёнҺём§Җн•Ё м „мІҙлҘј ліҙмһҘн•ңлӢӨкі 
  к°Җм •н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. owner Outlook reconcileмқҳ local Sent Items, Soulforge SMTP outbound log, н–Ҙнӣ„
  owner-approved team sent sourceлҠ” м„ңлЎң лӢӨлҘё кҙҖмёЎмӣҗмқҙл©° exact message identityк°Җ м—Ҷмңјл©ҙ мһҗлҸҷ лі‘н•©н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
- owner-approved Slack project channelмқҳ stable `workspace_id+channel_id` bindingмқҖ н•ҙлӢ№ мұ„л„җ л©”мӢңм§Җмқҳ
  authoritative default project scopeлӢӨ. мұ„л„җлӘ…мқҖ н‘ңмӢңк°’мқј лҝҗ identityк°Җ м•„лӢҲл©°, DMВ·мқјл°ҳВ·кіөмҡ©В·лҜёл§Өн•‘
  мұ„л„җмқҖ projectлЎң м¶”м •н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. Slack л©”мӢңм§Җм—җм„ң л°ңкІ¬н•ң м—…л¬ҙлҠ” н•ӯмғҒ candidateмқҙкі  кіөмӢқ мҷ„лЈҢк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ.
- HPPВ·нҡҢмӮ¬ м—…л¬ҙ PCВ·MacBook AirВ·Mac miniмқҳ лҸҷмқјн•ң logical `_workspaces/<project>` topologyмҷҖ кё°мЎҙ
  OneDrive junctionмқҖ owner-confirmed baselineмңјлЎң **лҸҷкІ°**н•ңлӢӨ. мқҙ кі„нҡҚмқҖ rename, rematerialize,
  bootstrap, repair лҳҗлҠ” topology deltaлҘј л§Ңл“Өм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. Exact junction targetкіј sync/runtime healthлҠ”
  private `VERIFY_HP`мқҙл©° public л¬ём„ңм—җм„ң м¶”м •н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
- `_workspaces/<project>`лҠ” Soulforgeмқҳ мӢӨм ң logical project worksite/bodyмқҙл©° actual project
  payloadВ·artifact ownerлӢӨ. кё°мЎҙ OneDrive junctionмқҖ к·ё bodyмқҳ physical materialization/shared-sync
  mechanismмқҙлӢӨ. м ңмҷё лІ”мң„лҠ” active DB/WAL/SHM, accepted central ingress RAW/quarantine, central
  queue/outbox/checkpointмҷҖ active runtime truthлЎң мўҒнһҢлӢӨ.
- HPPлҠ” private physical central RAW/ERP/runtime custody planeмқ„ мҶҢмң н•ңлӢӨ. Public кі„м•ҪмқҖ logical storage
  classмҷҖ authorityл§Ң мқҙлҰ„ л¶ҷмқҙл©° exact drive path, IP/domain, CA/certificate rosterмҷҖ live bindingмқҖ
  private `VERIFY_HP`лЎң лӮЁкёҙлӢӨ. лӢӨлҘё PCлҠ” HPP disk/UNC/SMB/SQLite/central queueлҘј м§Ғм ‘ м—ҙкұ°лӮҳ м“°м§Җ м•Ҡкі 
  approved MCP/APIлЎң submit/queryн•ңлӢӨ.

## 1. мЈјмқёмқҙ лЁјм Җ мқҪлҠ” мү¬мҡҙ м „мІҙ кө¬м¶• к·ёлҰј

нҳ„мһ¬ ERPм—җлҠ” н•  мқј н–үкіј м—¬лҹ¬ мһ…л ҘВ·мЎ°нҡҢ кё°лҠҘмқҙ мһҲлӢӨ. к·ёлҹ¬лӮҳ вҖңмҷң мқҙ н•  мқјмқҙ мғқкІјлҠ”м§ҖвҖқ, вҖңлҲ„к°Җ
м Ғмҡ©мқ„ н—Ҳмҡ©н–ҲлҠ”м§ҖвҖқ, вҖңк°ҷмқҖ мҡ”мІӯмқ„ лӢӨмӢң л°ӣм•„лҸ„ к°ҷмқҖ кІ°кіјмқём§ҖвҖқ, вҖңкіјкұ° мӢңм җм—җ л¬ҙм—Үмқҙ мң нҡЁн–Ҳкі 
л¬ҙм—Үмқ„ м•Ңкі  мһҲм—ҲлҠ”м§ҖвҖқлҘј source-local append-only мқҙл Ҙкіј exact refлЎң мһ¬мғқн•ҳлҠ” мӨ‘мӢ¬ кі„м•ҪмқҖ м•„м§Ғ
мҷ„м„ұлҗҳм§Җ м•Ҡм•ҳлӢӨ.

лӘ©н‘ңлҠ” мһ…л Ҙмқ„ кі§л°”лЎң н•  мқјлЎң м“°м§Җ м•Ҡкі , лЁјм Җ м•Ҳм „н•ң м ңм•ҲмңјлЎң л§Ңл“  л’Ө к¶Ңн•ңкіј мӨ‘ліөмқ„ кІҖмӮ¬н•ҳкі ,
мҳӨм§Ғ н•ҳлӮҳмқҳ ERP writerл§Ң м Ғмҡ©н•ҳкІҢ н•ҳлҠ” кІғмқҙлӢӨ. мҷ„лЈҢ л’Өм—җлҠ” кІҖмҰқкіј нӣ„мҶҚ нӣ„ліҙк°Җ мғқкё°м§Җл§Ң,
RAGВ·WikiВ·мғқлӘ…лӮҳл¬ҙ к°ҷмқҖ мЎ°нҡҢл©ҙмқҖ мӣҗліё н•  мқјмқ„ м§Ғм ‘ кі м№ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

```mermaid
flowchart LR
  P0["P0 C00A кіөк°ң preflight вҶ’ C00Q н•©м„ұ лҸ„кө¬ вҶ’ C00B мҠ№мқё мЎ°нҡҢ"] --> P1["P1 мһ…л Ҙлі„ append-only history + coverage"]
  P1 --> P2["P2 stable IDВ·typed refВ·м—¬лҹ¬ clock"]
  P2 --> P3["P3 immutable source/file revision lineage"]
  P3 --> P4["P4 exact revision-bound RAGВ·Wiki"]
  P3 --> H7["H07 Slack message/revision Shadow"]
  P4 --> P5["P5 validated context + context_acceptance_gate"]
  H7 --> P5
  P5 --> P6["P6 candidate-only task discovery"]
  P6 --> P7["P7 TaskDriver нҢҗлӢЁВ·authorityВ·idempotency"]
  P7 --> P8["P8 sole ERP writer + mail outbox"]
  P8 --> P9["P9 one-project pilotВ·feedbackВ·read-only life trees"]
  P9 --> P10["P10 separately approved activationВ·failoverВ·AX/AgentRun/ML"]
```

P0 лӮҙл¶Җм—җм„ңлҸ„ `C00AвҶ’C00QвҶ’C00B`лҘј кұҙл„Ҳлӣ°м§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. C00Aмқҳ retained `BLOCKED` receiptлҠ” P1мқ„
м—ҙм§Җ м•Ҡмңјл©°, C00Qмқҳ retained formal receiptлҸ„ public/synthetic лҸ„кө¬ кё°л°ҳл§Ң мҰқлӘ…н•ңлӢӨ. C00BлҠ” лӢӨмӢң лі„лҸ„ мҠ№мқёлҗң
query-only live metadataл§Ң мқҪлҠ”лӢӨ. Hard gateлҠ” м„ё к°Җм§ҖлӢӨ. P5мқҳ deterministic acceptance receipt м „м—җлҠ” P6лҘј мӢңмһ‘н•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡкі ,
P6 acceptance м „м—җлҠ” P7мқ„, P7 acceptance м „м—җлҠ” P8 schema/writerлҘј мӢңмһ‘н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. P9 pilot
мҠ№мқёмқҖ P10 activation мҠ№мқёмқҙ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ.

м„ё нӣ„мҶҚ ліҙм •мқҖ мқҙ critical pathлҘј лӢӨмӢң л§Ңл“Өм§Җ м•Ҡкі  мҳҶм—җм„ң к°ҷмқҖ phase receiptлҘј мҶҢл№„н•ңлӢӨ.

```mermaid
flowchart LR
  SRC["мӣҗмІңВ·нҢҖмӣҗ PC"] --> ING["pointer/upload receipt\nquarantineВ·promotion gate"] --> HIST["accepted history/context"]
  TASK["ERP assigned task"] --> WS["start/bind вҶ’ checkpoints вҶ’ closeout"] --> PROP["completion proposal"] --> DONE["лі„лҸ„ к¶Ңн•ңмқҳ ERP кіөмӢқ мҷ„лЈҢ"]
  HIST --> Q["ERP UI/MCP primary query\nexplicit project|common scope"]
  Q --> KC["knowledge candidate only"]
  ING -. "projectorмҷҖ лі„лҸ„ authority" .-> HIST
  WS -. "task current write 0" .-> TASK
```

н•ңлҲҲм—җ ліҙлҠ” нҢҗм •мқҖ лӢӨмқҢкіј к°ҷлӢӨ.

| кө¬л¶„ | мү¬мҡҙ лң» | нҳ„мһ¬ нҢҗм • |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `CURRENT` | м§ҖкёҲ мҪ”л“ңВ·schemaВ·кІҖмҰқм—җм„ң мӢӨм ңлЎң нҷ•мқён•ң кІғ | мһ…л Ҙлі„ кё°лҠҘ, ERP current row, нҢҢмқј нҷңлҸҷ, B9/ENGINE-12 мқҪкё° нҲ¬мҳҒмқҖ л¶Җл¶„ кө¬нҳ„ |
| `TARGET` | owner мҠ№мқё л’Ө л§Ңл“Өм–ҙм•ј н•  мөңмў… кө¬мЎ° | TaskIntent/TaskDriver/receipt, лӢЁмқј writer, typed relation/revision/time ledger, м•Ҳм „н•ң closed loop |
| `VERIFY_HP` | кі м„ұлҠҘ PC лҳҗлҠ” мҠ№мқёлҗң pilotм—җм„ң лӢӨмӢң мҰқлӘ…н•  кІғ | live writer, мӢӨм ң consumer, replay, backup/restore, one-project migration, PC binding |

## 2. exact Git/runtime кё°мӨҖм„ кіј мҰқкұ° к°•лҸ„

### 2.1 Gitкіј candidate branch

| н•ӯлӘ© | кҙҖм°° кІ°кіј | к°•лҸ„ |
| --- | --- | --- |
| public `main` | кі„нҡҚ ліҙм • мөңмҙҲ кҙҖм°° мӢң `9df7e57765d818be65f6250da8435826d0a2eea2`; лӢ№мӢң `origin/main`кіј лҸҷмқј | `HISTORICAL_REPORTED` |
| candidate branch | мөңмҙҲ кҙҖм°° мӢң `codex/task-engine-rag-v1@927b3fb045ebf749077951417463c47f12a549bd`; merge-base `15e988b4cdbd5db7a34eb580f754db7c3aa508cc`; `main...candidate=25/2` | `HISTORICAL_REPORTED` |
| candidate delta | кіјкұ° нҢҢмқј/line нҶөкі„лҠ” мғҲ mainм—җм„ң мһ¬кі„мӮ°н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ; bounded file-by-file reimplementation мӣҗм№ҷл§Ң мң м§Җ | `UNKNOWN/VERIFY_HP` |
| immutable oracle | `main`м—җм„ң lifecycle, ENGINE-13, `task_engine_redesign/**` кё°мӨҖ blob diff `0` | `OBSERVED` |
| candidate oracle drift | candidateк°Җ ENGINE-13кіј redesign л¬ём„ңлҘј мҲҳм •н•Ё | `OBSERVED`; нҶөн•© л•Ң н•ҙлӢ№ л¬ём„ң ліҖкІҪмқҖ м ңкұ° лҢҖмғҒ |
| worktree м•Ҳм •м„ұ | кі„нҡҚ ліҙм • мӢңмһ‘ мӢң targetмқҖ owner-designated untracked file, `index.lock` м—ҶмқҢ | `OBSERVED`; кө¬нҳ„ м§Ғм „ clean/overlap мһ¬нҷ•мқё н•„мҡ” |

мң„ SHAВ·merge-baseВ·divergence мҲҳм№ҳлҠ” лӘ…мӢңлҗң кі„нҡҚ кҙҖм°° мӢңм җмқҳ snapshotмқҙл©° нҳ„мһ¬ Git мғҒнғңлҘј лң»н•ҳм§Җ
м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. C00A/C00Q/C00BлҠ” к°Ғ owner мҠ№мқё мӢңм җмқҳ exact HEAD/originмқ„ лі„лҸ„лЎң лӢӨмӢң pinн•ҳкі  л¶Ҳмқјм№ҳн•ҳл©ҙ мӨ‘лӢЁн•ңлӢӨ.

Candidate branchлҠ” нҶөм§ёлЎң merge/cherry-pickн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. мөңмӢ  `main`м—җм„ң нҢҢмқјлі„лЎң лӢӨмӢң кІҖнҶ н•ҳкі ,
л¶ҲліҖ oracle ліҖкІҪмқҖ лІ„лҰ° л’Ө bounded sliceлЎң мһ¬кө¬нҳ„н•ңлӢӨ.

### 2.2 кіјкұ° runtimeВ·DB read-only кҙҖм°° вҖ” мқҙлІҲ ліҙм •м—җм„ң fresh мһ¬кҙҖм°°н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ

| н•ӯлӘ© | кҙҖм°° кІ°кіј | м ңн•ң |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ERP health | кіјкұ° loopback health HTTP `200`, schema label `dev_erp.v1` | `HISTORICAL_REPORTED`; live completeness `UNKNOWN/VERIFY_HP` |
| runtime revision | кіјкұ° runtime checkoutмқҖ лӢ№мӢң public кё°мӨҖм„ ліҙлӢӨ мҳӨлһҳлҗң revision | `HISTORICAL_REPORTED`; нҳ„мһ¬ `main`кіј live лҸҷмһ‘мқ„ лҸҷмқјмӢң кёҲм§Җ |
| DB guard | кіјкұ° Node SQLite `readOnly:true` + `PRAGMA query_only=ON` кҙҖм°° | `HISTORICAL_REPORTED`; fresh query-only receipt н•„мҡ” |
| н•өмӢ¬ table | кіјкұ° `core_item`, `event_log`, `completion_log` кҙҖм°°кіј TaskDriver кі„м—ҙ table л¶Җмһ¬ ліҙкі  | `HISTORICAL_REPORTED`; accepted C00Q tool л’Ө P0/C00Bм—җм„ң мһ¬нҷ•мқё |
| aggregate | кіјкұ° aggregate мҲҳм№ҳлҠ” stale snapshotмқҙлҜҖлЎң CURRENT к·јкұ°м—җм„ң м ңмҷё | `HISTORICAL_REPORTED`; public л¬ём„ңм—җм„ң live count мһ¬мЈјмһҘ кёҲм§Җ |
| мғҒнғң aggregate | кіјкұ° мғҒнғң countлҠ” stale snapshotмқҙлҜҖлЎң CURRENT к·јкұ°м—җм„ң м ңмҷё | `HISTORICAL_REPORTED`; P0/C00B next proof |
| zero-mutation guard | кіјкұ° sizeВ·mtime л¶ҲліҖ ліҙкі , full hash лҜёнҷ•мқё | `HISTORICAL_REPORTED`; fresh equivalent zero-mutation evidence н•„мҡ” |

### 2.3 кіјкұ° PC м—ӯн• В·лЎңм»¬ мӨҖл№„ мғҒнғң вҖ” live bindingмқҖ м¶”лЎ н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ

| н•ӯлӘ© | кҙҖм°° кІ°кіј | нҢҗм • |
| --- | --- | --- |
| кіјкұ° logical role/profile | `tool_pc`, `owner-with-state`лЎң ліҙкі лҗЁ | `HISTORICAL_REPORTED`; нҳ„мһ¬ live bindingмңјлЎң мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ© кёҲм§Җ |
| operational primary | 2026-07-18 ownerк°Җ HPPлҘј central ingress/custodyВ·voice processingВ·Task Engine/AX м •мғҒ TARGETмңјлЎң м§Җм • | `source_supported` target only; exact live binding/cutoverлҠ” `UNKNOWN/VERIFY_HP`, мҡҙмҳҒ нҷңм„ұнҷ” `DEFER` |
| Mac voice role | HPP unavailable/cutover м „ existing collectorмқҳ temporary failover, мқҙнӣ„ source-local HOLD/outboxВ·fallback/mirror | `source_supported`; лҸҷмӢң shared writer, HPP central custody, mail/project-history к¶Ңн•ңмңјлЎң нҷ•мһҘ кёҲм§Җ |
| readiness/skill/junction/companion | кіјкұ° мӢӨн–ү кІ°кіјл§Ң мЎҙмһ¬ | `HISTORICAL_REPORTED`; мқҙлІҲ ліҙм •мқҳ CURRENT к·јкұ° м•„лӢҳ |
| established `_workspaces/<project>` topology | owner-confirmed identical actual logical project worksite/bodyмҷҖ OneDrive junction materialization baseline | `source_supported` logical-owner baseline only; exact targetsВ·sync healthВ·HPP TARGET physical bindingмқҖ private `VERIFY_HP`, topology ліҖкІҪ `0` |

### 2.4 мҰқкұ° л“ұкёү

- `OBSERVED`: лӘ…мӢңлҗң кҙҖм°° мӢңм җ/refм—җм„ң exact ref, мҪ”л“ң symbol, read-only schema/aggregate, validator
  кІ°кіјлЎң нҷ•мқё. к°ҷмқҖ refм—җм„ң лӢӨмӢң нҷ•мқён•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҖ к°’мқҖ нҳ„мһ¬к°’мңјлЎң нҷ•мһҘн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
- `HISTORICAL_REPORTED`: мқҙм „ plan мһ‘м„ұ л•Ңмқҳ кҙҖм°°лЎң кё°лЎқлҗҗмңјлӮҳ мқҙлІҲ ліҙм •м—җм„ң fresh мһ¬кҙҖм°°н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ.
- `source_supported`: public owner/source кі„м•Ҫмқҙ bounded claimмқ„ м§Ғм ‘ л’·л°ӣм№Ён•Ё. live binding, runtime
  кө¬нҳ„ лҳҗлҠ” activation мҰқкұ°лЎң нҷ•мһҘн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
- `REPORTED`: кё°мЎҙ л¬ём„ңлӮҳ candidate branchк°Җ мЈјмһҘн•ҳм§Җл§Ң мқҙлІҲ кё°мӨҖм„ м—җм„ң мһ¬мӢӨн–үн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ.
- `UNKNOWN`: м•Ҳм „н•ң мқҪкё° м „мҡ© мҰқлӘ…мқҙ м—Ҷкұ°лӮҳ runtime revisionмқҙ лӢ¬лқј лӢЁм •н•  мҲҳ м—ҶмқҢ.
- `TARGET`: owner мҠ№мқё л’Ө кө¬нҳ„н•  кі„м•Ҫ.
- `VERIFY_HP`: кі м„ұлҠҘ PCмқҳ clean worktree, synthetic fixture лҳҗлҠ” лі„лҸ„ мҠ№мқёлҗң pilotм—җм„ң мҰқлӘ….

### 2.5 мқҙм „ plan мЎ°мӮ¬ лӘ…л №кіј мқҙлІҲ ліҙм • мҰқкұ°мқҳ л¶„лҰ¬

м•„лһҳ н‘ңлҠ” **мқҙм „ plan мһ‘м„ұ лӢ№мӢң кё°лЎқмқ„ ліҙмЎҙн•ң historical log**лӢӨ. мқҙлІҲ correction мӢӨн–ү кё°лЎқмңјлЎң
мһ¬мЈјмһҘн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. кІҪлЎңВ·hostnameВ·м—…л¬ҙ payloadлҘј кіөк°ңн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҸ„лЎқ runtime/private мң„м№ҳлҠ” logical labelлЎңл§Ң м ҒлҠ”лӢӨ.
мқҙ м Ҳкіј В§6.5мқҳ `node tools/...` лӘ…л № л°Ҹ `docs/contracts/...` schema кІҪлЎңлҠ”
`ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp`лҘј cwdлЎң мӮјмқҖ app-relative н‘ңкё°лӢӨ. Repo rootм—җм„ң мӢӨн–үн•ҳкұ°лӮҳ м°ҫмқ„ л•ҢлҠ”
к°Ғк°Ғ `node ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/tools/...`,
`ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/docs/contracts/...`лЎң н•ҙм„қн•ңлӢӨ.

| лӘ…л №/кІҖмӮ¬ | exit | кІ°кіј мҡ”м•Ҫ |
| --- | ---: | --- |
| `git fetch --prune origin` + `git rev-list --left-right --count HEAD...origin/main` | 0 | public main `0/0` |
| `git status --porcelain=v2 --branch` | 0 | public main clean; runtime checkoutлҸ„ лі„лҸ„ clean |
| `git merge-base`, `git rev-list main...candidate`, `git cherry` | 0 | лӢ№мӢң drift мҲҳм№ҳлҠ” нҳ„мһ¬ к¶Ңмң„к°Җ м•„лӢҳ; мӣҗліё correction кҙҖм°° кё°мӨҖмқҖ В§2.1мқҳ `25/2`, candidate кі мң  commit 2к°ң |
| immutable paths `git diff --exit-code <oracle>...HEAD -- <paths>` | 0 | лӢ№мӢң main oracle ліҖнҷ” м—ҶмқҢ |
| `npm.cmd run skills:sync -- --all` | 0 | tracked skills materialized |
| `npm.cmd run guild-hall:doctor -- --profile owner-with-state --device-capabilities --json` | 0 | advisory capability probe |
| `npm.cmd run guild-hall:doctor -- --profile owner-with-state` | 1 | 48/51; hardening skill/Stop hooks 3к°ң gap |
| `npm.cmd run guild-hall:workspace-junction:audit` | 1 | single-root, extra alias 5к°ң; repair м•Ҳ н•Ё |
| companion repos `git fetch` + `git pull --ff-only` | 0 | clean behind-onlyлҘј к°Ғк°Ғ fast-forward, мөңмў… `0/0` |
| `node tools/runtime_ops.mjs health --json` | 0 | HTTP 200, schema label нҷ•мқё |
| `node --input-type=module <SQLite readOnly/query_only probe>` | 0 | query_only 1, integrity ok, FK violation 0, aggregateл§Ң мЎ°нҡҢ |
| live DB/WAL `Get-FileHash` | nonzero | file lock; hash мҰқкұ°лЎң мӮ¬мҡ©н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ |
| `npm.cmd run validate:file-activity` | 0 | synthetic 36/36 |
| `npm.cmd run validate:rag` | 0 | common RAG v0 28/28 |
| context/life-tree focused `node --test` | 1 | 15/17 pass, endpoint 2кұҙ `server not ready` |
| `node tools/runtime_release_audit.mjs --core-only-release --require-live --json` | 1 | release blockers 6мў…; activation л¶Ҳк°Җ |
| plan file `git add -N` нӣ„ scoped `git diff --check -- <plan>` | 0 | untracked мӢ к·ң л¬ём„ң лӮҙмҡ©к№Ңм§Җ нҸ¬н•Ён•ҙ whitespace error м—ҶмқҢ |

### 2.6 CV-01~CV-09 correction matrix

м•„лһҳ `CONFIRMED`лҠ” public `main@9df7e577...`мқҳ кі„м•ҪВ·мҪ”л“ң лҳҗлҠ” мқҙлІҲ read-only лӘ…л №мқҙ н•ҙлӢ№ нҢҗм •мқ„
м§Ғм ‘ л’·л°ӣм№Ён•ңлӢӨлҠ” лң»мқҙлӢӨ. `UNKNOWN_BLOCKED`лҠ” кі„м•Ҫ мқҳлҸ„лҠ” нҷ•мқён–Ҳм§Җл§Ң current writer/default-rootмқҳ
мҷ„м „н•ң inventoryк°Җ м—Ҷм–ҙ н•©кІ©мқ„ мЈјмһҘн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨлҠ” лң»мқҙлӢӨ. Live completenessлӮҳ кө¬нҳ„ мҷ„лЈҢлҘј лң»н•ҳм§Җ
м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. нҠ№нһҲ CV-06кіј CV-07мқҖ **gapмқҳ мЎҙмһ¬к°Җ CONFIRMED**лҗң кІғмқҙл©° gapмқҙ кө¬нҳ„мңјлЎң лӢ«нҳ”лӢӨлҠ” лң»мқҙ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ.

| ID | verdict | exact public evidence | corrected plan consequence | next proof |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| CV-01 | `CONFIRMED` | root `AGENTS.md`мқҳ public-tracking кёҲм§Җ; мқҙлІҲ `git ls-files -- '_workspaces/**'` кІ°кіјлҠ” boundary л¬ём„ң `_workspaces/README.md` 1к°ңлҝҗмқҙкі  changed-scope path validator violation `0` | public planВ·fixtureм—җлҠ” payload/body/chunkлҘј л‘җм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ | к°Ғ кө¬нҳ„ sliceмқҳ ліҖкІҪ scopeм—җм„ң tracked payload/body/chunk sentinel `0` мһ¬нҷ•мқё |
| CV-02 | `UNKNOWN_BLOCKED` | `task_engine_redesign/02_OWNER_BOUNDARIES_AND_STORAGE.md` LOCKED н‘ңлҠ” project payload=`_workspaces/<project>/...`, common payload=`_workspaces/knowledge/**`, metadata=`_workmeta/**`лҘј кі м •н•ҳм§Җл§Ң current writer/default-root м „мІҙ inventoryлҠ” мқҙлІҲ public-only correctionм—җм„ң мӢӨн–үн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ | project/common/system ownerлҘј н•©м№ҳкұ°лӮҳ fallbackн•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡкі  P0/C00B н•©кІ©мқ„ м°ЁлӢЁ | accepted C00Q tool л’Ө P0/C00B asset-kindлі„ current writer/default-root/consumer inventory |
| CV-03 | `CONFIRMED` | `PROJECT_CONTEXT_GRAPH_MODEL_V0.md`мқҳ `project_context/**`В·`reports/context_graph/**`; `PROJECT_FILE_ACTIVITY_REVISION_V0.md`мқҳ `reports/file_activity/{observations,events,checkpoints,projections}/**` | В§7 owner treeм—җ л‘җ ownerлҘј лӘ…мӢңн•ҳкі  proposed history viewsмҷҖ кө¬л¶„ | P0/C00B physical owner/path inventory |
| CV-04 | `CONFIRMED` | context `sources.csv`лҠ” `source_id/content_hash/occurred_at/ingested_at`, `edges.csv`лҠ” node IDsл§Ң ліҙмң ; `TEMPORAL_KNOWLEDGE_ONTOLOGY_V0.md` В§5~6мқҖ `source_revision_id`, `content_id`, typed ref, `valid_at/known_at`мқ„ мҡ”кө¬ | P2/P3м—җм„ң lossless schema/crosswalk receipt м „ P4/P5 кёҲм§Җ | HP-HISTORY exact-ref/orphan/cutoff tests |
| CV-05 | `CONFIRMED` | мқҙм „ WBSк°Җ C01 TaskDriver-firstмҳҖкі  cross-validation packetмқҖ P0вҶ’P10мқ„ owner-fixedлЎң кі м • | В§1В·В§12В·В§15лҘј P0вҶ’P10мңјлЎң көҗм •; P5вҶ’P6вҶ’P7вҶ’P8 hard gate | к°Ғ phase acceptance receiptмҷҖ dependency lint |
| CV-06 | `CONFIRMED` | `src/erp_mcp_service.mjs`мқҳ `erp_mcp_work_session` tableкіј idempotent `publishWorkSession()`В·replay testлҠ” мЎҙмһ¬; dev-ERP л°– whole-conversation/OS capture ownerлҠ” public contractм—җ м—ҶмқҢ | structured WorkSession receiptлҠ” CURRENTлЎң мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ©н•ҳкі  whole conversation/OS surveillanceлҠ” кё°ліё `OFF/DEFER`; AgentRunмқҖ P1 м„ н–үмЎ°кұҙ м•„лӢҳ | H03 coverage + direct-writer audit; D19 capture boundary кІ°м • |
| CV-07 | `CONFIRMED` | dev-ERP `Store.applyTemplate`/anchor mutationмқҖ мһҲмңјлӮҳ `TEMPORAL_KNOWLEDGE_ONTOLOGY_V0.md` В§5.7мқҙ мҡ”кө¬н•ҳлҠ” external schedule occurrenceвҶ’exact record revisionмқҳ standalone owner/path/writerлҠ” лҜём • | schedule historyлҠ” P1 gap; D20 кІ°м •кіј exact revision/event writer м „ P5 acceptance кёҲм§Җ | H03/SE fixtureм—җм„ң current+append-only event, stale revision, replay кІҖмҰқ |
| CV-08 | `CONFIRMED` | `task_engine_redesign/03_INPUT_AND_TEMPORAL_MODEL.md` В§source-local firstмҷҖ мӣ”лі„ partition к·ңм№ҷ | вҖңк°ҷмқҖ/н•ҳлӮҳмқҳ мӣҗмһҘвҖқмқ„ source-local ledgers + exact-ref projectionмңјлЎң көҗм • | H06 five-lane replay/export parity |
| CV-09 | `CONFIRMED` | root `AGENTS.md` м •ліё кө¬мЎ°лҠ” `.registry/.unit/.workflow/.party/.mission/guild_hall/_workspaces`; `ui-workspace`лҠ” derived UI consumer | В§0В·В§5В·В§7м—җм„ң canon ownerмҷҖ derived UIлҘј л¶„лҰ¬ | path/owner lintмҷҖ UI write-authority test |

2026-07-15 owner кё°ліём•Ҳмқҳ `CV-F10 ingress`, `CV-F11 personal session`, `CV-F12 query/knowledge`лҠ”
CV-01~CV-09лҘј мһ¬лІҲнҳёнҷ”н•ҳкұ°лӮҳ P0~P10мқ„ л°”кҫём§Җ м•ҠлҠ” нӣ„мҶҚ findingмқҙлӢӨ. к°Ғк°Ғ В§3.5В·D27В·HP-INGRESS,
В§6.2A/В§10В·D28В·HP-SESSION, В§6.5A/В§9.3В·D29В·HP-QUERYлЎң лӢ«лҠ”лӢӨ. мқҙ plan mappingмқҖ кө¬нҳ„ лҳҗлҠ”
live acceptance мҰқкұ°к°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ.

## 3. кі м„ұлҠҘ PC `CURRENT / TARGET / VERIFY_HP` read-only inventory

### 3.1 мһ…л Ҙкіј нҳ„мһ¬ ERP

| мҳҒм—ӯ | `CURRENT` | `TARGET` | `VERIFY_HP` |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| л©”мқј | JS `project_mail_history_writer.mjs`, Python `ProjectMailHistoryWriter`, Outlook `outlook_mail_reconcile.mjs`к°Җ project historyлҘј м“ҙлӢӨ. Outlook reconcileмқҖ local кё°ліё ліҙлӮёнҺём§Җн•Ёкіј л°ӣмқҖнҺём§Җн•Ё metadataлҘј мқҪм§Җл§Ң current PowerShell rowлҠ” sent itemмқҳ exact Internet Message-IDВ·мҲҳмӢ мһҗ мЈјмҶҢ snapshotмқ„ ліҙмһҘн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. нҢҖ account collectorлҠ” Hiworks POP3 кё°л°ҳ л°ӣмқҖнҺём§Җн•Ё мӨ‘мӢ¬мқҙкі , Soulforge SMTP outbound logлҠ” к·ё senderлҘј кұ°м№ң л°ңмҶЎл§Ң м•ҲлӢӨ. assignment/eventмҷҖ CSV/XLSX publishлҸ„ н•ҳлӮҳмқҳ atomic generationмқҙ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. | project-independent `mail_occurrence_id` н•ҳлӮҳм—җ source/account/folderлі„ `mailbox_observation`мқ„ м—¬лҹ¬ к°ң м—°кІ°н•ҳкі  sender/to/cc/bcc roleмқ„ лі„лҸ„ relationмңјлЎң ліҙмЎҙн•ңлӢӨ. | мқҢм„ұ | мҠ№мқёлҗң routeмқҳ consumer мЎҙмһ¬; raw audio/transcriptлҘј м§Ғм ‘ мқҪм§Җ м•ҠлҠ” кІҪкі„ | мҠ№мқёлҗң transcript revisionм—җм„ң нӣ„ліҙ мғқм„ұ, мӮ¬лһҢ matcher/authority л¶„лҰ¬ | мӢӨм ң route coverage, лҲ„лқҪВ·мӨ‘ліөВ·revision exact join |
| SE мқјм • | template spawn, anchor date мқҙлҸҷ, 1-hop due мһ¬кі„мӮ°мқҖ мһҲмңјлӮҳ external master scheduleмқҳ append-only revision/event ownerВ·pathВ·writerлҠ” лҜём • | external schedule current rowмҷҖ immutable revision/eventлҘј л¶„лҰ¬н•ң л’Ө exact revisionвҶ’context м—°кІ° | D20 owner/path/writer, stale revision, replay parity |

| мӮ¬лһҢ/Codex | `erp_mcp_work_session`мқҖ `(account_id,idempotency_key)` replay/conflictлҘј к°Җм§„ **м„ңлЎң лҸ…лҰҪлҗң bounded structured result record**лӢӨ. start/bind, assignment epoch, ordered checkpoint, closeout, durable client outbox/ackлҠ” м—ҶлӢӨ | кё°мЎҙ one-shot recordлҠ” compatibility мһ…л ҘмңјлЎң ліҙмЎҙн•ҳкі , лі„лҸ„ personal WorkSession start/bindвҶ’checkpointвҶ’closeoutвҶ’completion proposal lifecycleмқ„ feature-OFFлЎң м„Өкі„; whole conversation/OS surveillanceлҠ” `OFF/DEFER` | stable opaque thread ref к°ҖлҠҘм„ұ, node binding, local outbox path/м•”нҳёнҷ”/ліҙмЎҙ, missing SLA, one-active-primary cardinality |
| payload ingress | mail/voice/file source owner, chat attachment inboxмҷҖ MCP artifact inboxк°Җ к°Ғк°Ғ мЎҙмһ¬н•ңлӢӨ. м—…лЎңл“ңлҠ” service-owned byte copyлҘј л§Ңл“Өм§Җл§Ң кіөнҶө promotion receiptВ·promoter authorityлҠ” м—ҶлӢӨ | pointer/hash/reference кё°ліё; мӨ‘м•ҷ service custody лҳҗлҠ” explicit мҠ№мқё л•Ңл§Ң copy/move/derive. source writerВ·promoterВ·history projectorВ·TaskEngine coordinatorлҘј л¶„лҰ¬ | mail raw/attachment custody кІҪкі„, quarantine/scan/ACL/retention/backup owner, per-source promotion destination |
| ERP current row | `core_item`, `createItem()`, `setItemStatus()`, `itm_*` allocator | event replayмқҳ materialized current projection; кё°мЎҙ ID мң м§Җ | actual sole writer, transaction/event parity, duplicate reservation |
| ERP event/history | generic `event_log`; completion лі„лҸ„, status mutationкіј event appendк°Җ л¶„лҰ¬ | typed append-only `task_event`; compatibility mirrorлҠ” н•ңмӢң мң м§Җ | reopen/re-done/reanchor adversarial replay |
| мҷ„лЈҢ | `completion_log`; нҳ„мһ¬ reopenмқҖ л§Ҳм§Җл§ү мҷ„лЈҢ н–үмқ„ `DELETE` | completion/reversalмқҖ append-only; artifact/decision/verification/outcome exact ref | legacy row crosswalkмҷҖ free-text-only count |
| м—…л¬ҙ мғҒнғң | `unclassified/open/doing/waiting/blocked/done/archived` | мқј мғҒнғңмҷҖ Driver нҢҗлӢЁ мғҒнғңлҘј л‘җ м¶•мңјлЎң л¶„лҰ¬ | archived/cancelled/merged crosswalk owner кІ°м • |

### 3.2 IDВ·мӢңк°„м¶•В·м§ҖмӢқВ·мЎ°нҡҢл©ҙ

| мҳҒм—ӯ | `CURRENT` | `TARGET` | `VERIFY_HP` |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| typed ID/ref | л¬ём„ң кі„м•Ҫкіј мқјл¶Җ adapterлҠ” мһҲмңјлӮҳ ID namespaceк°Җ л¶„мӮ° | `{entity_type, owner_surface, entity_id}`мҷҖ project-qualified exact ref к°•м ң | bare/fuzzy join, collision, orphan, alias count |
| source/file revision | file activity revisionмқҖ к°•н•Ё; кіөнҶө SourceRevision мҡҙмҳҒ мӣҗмһҘмқҖ м—ҶмқҢ | logical sourceвҶ’immutable revisionвҶ’node observation lineage | sourceлі„ revision лҲ„лқҪВ·мӨ‘ліөкіј HWPвҶ’HWPX receipt |
| мӢңк°„м¶• | occurrence кҙҖл Ё fieldк°Җ мқјл¶Җ мЎҙмһ¬ | `valid_at`мҷҖ `known_at`мқ„ л¶„лҰ¬н•ң point-in-time replay | null/regression/orderingкіј л‘җ лІҲ replay digest |
| relation ledger | ontology м–ҙнңҳВ·relation matrix кі„м•ҪмқҖ мЎҙмһ¬ | append/supersede RelationEventмҷҖ exact endpoint | multi-parent, stale alias, fuzzy-confirmed `0` |
| project context | gate/skeleton/work/history branchмҷҖ B9a~c мқҪкё° лӘЁлҚё | owner relation ledgerм—җм„ң B9d knowledge backlinkк№Ңм§Җ нҲ¬мҳҒ | gateвҶ’branchвҶ’eventвҶ’taskвҶ’fruit coverage |
| RAG | кіөмҡ© `_workspaces/knowledge/rag` кё°ліё кІҪлЎңк°Җ м—¬лҹ¬ consumerм—җ кі м • | project/common/system resolver, exact source revision, consumer м „нҷҳ | лӘЁл“  asset/consumer inventory, foreign-project/orphan/collision `0` |
| Wiki | м ңн•ңлҗң Markdown readerмҷҖ metadata shell | immutable WikiRevision writer, claim/source relation, project ACL | writer owner, cross-project isolation, body м ҖмһҘ кІҪкі„ |
| ERP UI/MCP query | personal MCPлҠ” agenda/task/mail/artifactмҷҖ one-shot WorkSession л“ұ 8к°ң лҸ„кө¬лҘј м ңкіөн•ҳм§Җл§Ң project-history/RAG/Wiki accepted-generation queryлҠ” м—ҶлӢӨ. мқёмҰқ кіјм •мқҳ token `last_used_at` audit touchлҠ” л°ңмғқн•  мҲҳ мһҲлӢӨ | accepted project-history/context/knowledgeмқҳ primary user query surface. `scope=project|common` н•„мҲҳ, implicit fallback м—ҶмқҢ, exact generation/revision/locator/claim ceiling л°ҳнҷҳ | explicit ACLкіј existence-leak м •мұ…, APIвҶ”CSV/XLSX parity, generation pinning/cursor, feature binding/team pilot |
| ENGINE-12 | мқёмҰқ GET, project м ‘к·ј кІҖмӮ¬, mail/ERP/SE/voice/Codex/file adapterмҷҖ мқјмқј л ҢмҰҲ | TaskDriver/task_event/typed ref/bitemporal adapter | `HISTORICAL_REPORTED`: лӢ№мӢң 17 test мӨ‘ 15 pass; `server not ready` 2кұҙ мӣҗмқё мһ¬нҳ„ |
| B9 | мһҘкё° мғқлӘ…лӮҳл¬ҙ B9a~c кө¬нҳ„, B9d лҜёмҷ„лЈҢ | м§ҖмӢқ backlinkмҷҖ exact completion/outcome fruit | projectionмқҙ owner rowлҘј м“°м§Җ м•ҠлҠ”м§Җ м „нӣ„ digest |
| AX Workspace | мҷ„м„ұлҗң AX м •ліё/UIлҠ” м—Ҷкі  ERP MCPм—җлҠ” idempotent one-shot structured result persistence/APIл§Ң л¶Җл¶„ кө¬нҳ„ | one-shot facadeлҠ” ліҙмЎҙн•ҳкі  лі„лҸ„ assignment-bound personal lifecycleВ·accepted query clientлҘј AX-G1 мқҙнӣ„ feature-OFFлЎң кө¬м¶• | P9 core л’Ө D28/D29мҷҖ лі„лҸ„ owner gate; thread/node/outbox capabilityВ·whole-conversation capture м—ҶмқҢ |

| Engineering IQ/ML | canonical traceмҷҖ verified label pool м—ҶмқҢ | trace лЁјм Җ, м¶©л¶„н•ң кІҖмҰқ label л’Ө ranking/ML нӣ„ліҙ | label н’Ҳм§ҲВ·мҲҳлҹүВ·нҺён–Ҙ кё°мӨҖ owner кІ°м • |

### 3.3 м§ҖкёҲк№Ңм§Җ н•ң кІғкіј лӮЁмқҖ кІғ

мқҙлҜё н•ң кІғ:

- mail/voice/SE/file/Codex кҙҖл Ё мһ…л Ҙкіј ERP read/write кё°лҠҘмқ„ к°Ғк°Ғ л¶Җл¶„ кө¬нҳ„
- ERP current row, generic event, completion log, task ledger/autosyncлҘј мҡҙмҳҒ
- file activity synthetic кІҖмҰқ, B9 мһҘкё° view, ENGINE-12 мқјмқј viewмҷҖ UIлҘј кө¬м¶•
- кіөмҡ© RAG v0мҷҖ knowledge projectionмқ„ кө¬м¶•
- candidate branchм—җм„ң TaskDriver/temporal ID/project RAGмқҳ мҙҲкё° кө¬нҳ„ к°ҖлҠҘм„ұмқ„ мӢңн—ҳ

лӮЁмқҖ н•өмӢ¬:

- лӘЁл“  мһ…л Ҙмқ„ candidate-onlyлЎң лӘЁмңјлҠ” TaskIntentмҷҖ TaskDriver нҢҗлӢЁ мӣҗмһҘ
- лӢЁмқј ERP writer, task ID reservation, atomic event/current/receipt transaction
- мӮӯм ң м—ҶлҠ” completion/reopen, л‘җ мғҒнғңм¶•, deterministic replay
- кіөнҶө SourceRevision/RelationEventмҷҖ `valid_at/known_at`
- project/common/system RAGВ·WikiВ·ontology owner м „нҷҳ
- B9/ENGINE-12лҘј source-local historiesмқҳ exact-ref read-only projectionмңјлЎң м—°кІ°
- immutable multi-PC packet, sole reconciler, лі„лҸ„ ERP writer, backup/restore/failover
- core pilot л’Ө AX Workspace/AgentRun/Engineering IQ/MLмқ„ лі„лҸ„ phaseлЎң м§„н–ү

### 3.4 P1 five-lane history foundation

Task discoveryліҙлӢӨ лЁјм Җ лӢӨмқҢ лӢӨм„Ҝ laneмқҳ append-only historyмҷҖ coverageлҘј лӢ«лҠ”лӢӨ. кё°мҲ  source
ownerлҠ” к·ёлҢҖлЎң мң м§Җн•ҳл©°, мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗмҡ© CSV/XLSXлҠ” source truthк°Җ м•„лӢҢ `TARGET proposed derived view`лӢӨ.

| lane | `CURRENT` (public evidence) | `TARGET` | `VERIFY_HP` |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| mail | gateway мӣ”лі„ collector event/dedupe stateмҷҖ нҳ„мһ¬ `soulforge.project_mail_history.private.v1` CSV/XLSX/ICS projection; JS/Python/Outlook м„ё writer, Outlook CSV-only, `scan_mail_ledger.mjs` consumer | project-independent occurrence + append-only classification/reclassification event + atomic outbox; existing CSV/ICS/XLSX кІҪлЎңлҠ” к°ҷмқҖ generationмқҳ rebuildable projection | caller zero/allowlist, DBвҶ”CSVвҶ”XLSX parity, lock/lease/epoch, partial Mac gap, failover/failback |
| voice | `_workspaces/system/voice_capture/**` payload/source ownerмҷҖ `_workmeta/<project>/reports/voice_source_events/**` metadata event owner; нҳ„мһ¬ л§ҘлҜёлӢҲ temporary failover, TARGET HPP voice processing primary | кё°мЎҙ technical eventлҘј common envelopeлЎң exportн•ҳкі  **proposed** `reports/мқҢм„ұ_мқҙл Ҙ` мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗ view мғқм„ұ; raw audio/transcriptлҠ” source ownerм—җ мң м§Җ | exact writer lease/epochмҷҖ cutover/failback receipt, session/bundle/revision coverage, consumer ack, partial/failed capture gap, supersession replay |
| structured PC work | dev-ERPмқҳ unordered one-shot `erp_mcp_work_session` result record + metadata-only daily ledger; start/bind/ordered closeoutВ·durable client ackлҠ” м—Ҷкі  м „мІҙ лҢҖнҷ”/OS к°җмӢңлҠ” кө¬нҳ„В·мҠ№мқёлҗҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ | мҠ№мқёлҗң bounded recordл§Ң H03 occurrenceлЎң м—°кІ°н•ҳкі , personal lifecycleмқҖ P9 мқҙнӣ„ AX side-cardлЎң л¶„лҰ¬н•ңлӢӨ. daily ledger/context/execution receiptлҠ” мӣҗ sourceлӮҳ H05 runмқ„ к°ҖлҰ¬нӮӨлҠ” relationВ·projectionВ·coverage refлЎңл§Ң мӮ¬мҡ©н•ҙ **proposed** `reports/PC_м—…л¬ҙ_мқҙл Ҙ` view мғқм„ұ | H03 direct writer `0`; AXм—җм„ң capture scope/consent, node/thread binding, outbox/ack, missing-closeout; whole conversation/OS surveillance `OFF/DEFER` |
| file | `guild_hall/file_activity/**`мҷҖ `_workmeta/<project>/reports/file_activity/{observations,events,checkpoints,projections}/**`; complete/partial/failed scanкіј exact file revision | кё°мЎҙ observation/event/revision ownerлҘј ліҙмЎҙн•ҳкі  **proposed** `reports/нҢҢмқј_мқҙл Ҙ` viewл§Ң нҢҢмғқ | authenticated producer, complete-scan coverage, conflict/revision replay, live reconciler binding |
| run/log | `_workmeta/<project>/runs/<run_id>/**` мӢӨн–ү metadataВ·нҢҗлӢЁВ·кІҖмҰқ logмҷҖ five-field/daily-ledger refs; raw artifactлҠ” worksite owner | run/validator/receipt typed refsлҘј envelopeлЎң м—°кІ°н•ҳкі  **proposed** `reports/мӢӨн–ү_мқҙл Ҙ` view мғқм„ұ | run completeness, validator receipt/ref integrity, raw exclusion; `AgentRun`мқҖ P1 prerequisiteк°Җ м•„лӢҳ |

#### 3.4.1 Common history envelope (`TARGET`, H00)

лӘЁл“  lane adapterлҠ” мһҗкё° source-local recordлҘј ліөмӮ¬н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. Event envelopeмҷҖ coverage receiptлҠ”
м„ңлЎң лҸ…лҰҪлҗң recordмқҙл©°, zero-event windowлҘј н‘ңнҳ„н•ҳл Өкі  к°Җм§ң eventлҘј л§Ңл“Өм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

```yaml
schema_version: soulforge.project_history_envelope.v1
occurrence_id: <stable-project-independent-id>
lane: mail|voice|structured_pc_work|file|run_log
source_owner_ref: <typed-owner-ref>
native_occurrence_ref: <typed-native-ref>
event_ref: <exact-append-only-event-ref>
source_revision_ref: <exact-revision-ref-or-null>
content_ref: <content-id-or-null>
project_ref: <classification-target-or-null>
event_at: <strict-utc-or-declared-unknown>
valid_at: <strict-utc-or-declared-unknown>
observed_at: <strict-utc-or-null>
known_at: <strict-utc>
recorded_at: <strict-utc>
classification_before: <typed-state-or-null>
classification_after: <typed-state-or-null>
supersedes_event_ref: <exact-ref-or-null>
metadata_digest: sha256:<64hex>
raw_payload_copied: false
```

```yaml
schema_version: soulforge.project_history_coverage_receipt.v1
lane: mail|voice|structured_pc_work|file|run_log
source_owner_ref: <typed-owner-ref>
project_ref: <classification-target-or-null>
window_start: <strict-utc>
window_end: <strict-utc>
state: complete_with_events|complete_no_events|partial|failed|not_collected|not_applicable
event_count: <integer-or-null>
gap_codes: []
applicability_ref: <approved-rule-ref-or-null>
ordered_event_digest: sha256:<64hex>
metadata_digest: sha256:<64hex>
raw_payload_copied: false
```

`complete_with_events`лҠ” мӢӨм ң мҲҳм§‘кіј `event_count >= 1`, `complete_no_events`лҠ” мӢӨм ң мҲҳм§‘кіј
`event_count: 0`мқ„ лң»н•ңлӢӨ. `partial`мқҖ м •нҷ•н•ң `event_count >= 0`кіј non-empty gapмқ„ н•Ёк»ҳ к°Җм§„лӢӨ.
`failed`мҷҖ `not_collected`лҠ” `event_count: null`кіј non-empty gapмқ„ к°Җм§Җл©° мӮ¬кұҙ м—ҶмқҢмңјлЎң н•ҙм„қн•ҳм§Җ
м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. `not_applicable`мқҖ `event_count: null`, empty gap, owner-approved `rule_revision` applicability
refк°Җ лӘЁл‘җ мһҲмқ„ л•Ңл§Ң н—Ҳмҡ©н•ңлӢӨ. мқҙ мғҒнғңл“Өмқ„ к°ҷмқҖ 0мңјлЎң н‘ңнҳ„н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. JoinмқҖ occurrence/event/revision/
contentмқҳ project-qualified typed refл§Ң н—Ҳмҡ©н•ҳкі  м ңлӘ©, мӢңк°„ к·јм ‘, filename, LLM similarity к°ҷмқҖ fuzzy
joinмқҖ review candidateк№Ңм§Җл§Ң н—Ҳмҡ©н•ңлӢӨ.

#### 3.4.2 Proposed user-facing derived views (`TARGET`, source truth м•„лӢҳ)

| lane | metadata CSV | human XLSX | technical source owner preserved |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| mail | кё°мЎҙ `_workmeta/<project>/reports/л©”мқј_мқҙл Ҙ/л©”мқј_мқҙл Ҙ.csv` | кё°мЎҙ `_workspaces/<project>/reports/л©”мқј_мқҙл Ҙ/л©”мқј_мқҙл Ҙ.xlsx` | gateway/source event + P8 mail assignment event/outbox |
| voice | **proposed** `_workmeta/<project>/reports/мқҢм„ұ_мқҙл Ҙ/мқҢм„ұ_мқҙл Ҙ.csv` | **proposed** `_workspaces/<project>/reports/мқҢм„ұ_мқҙл Ҙ/мқҢм„ұ_мқҙл Ҙ.xlsx` | `reports/voice_source_events/**` |
| structured PC work | **proposed** `_workmeta/<project>/reports/PC_м—…л¬ҙ_мқҙл Ҙ/PC_м—…л¬ҙ_мқҙл Ҙ.csv` | **proposed** `_workspaces/<project>/reports/PC_м—…л¬ҙ_мқҙл Ҙ/PC_м—…л¬ҙ_мқҙл Ҙ.xlsx` | ERP MCP WorkSession + approved structured instruction; daily ledger/contextлҠ” derived projection |
| file | **proposed** `_workmeta/<project>/reports/нҢҢмқј_мқҙл Ҙ/нҢҢмқј_мқҙл Ҙ.csv` | **proposed** `_workspaces/<project>/reports/нҢҢмқј_мқҙл Ҙ/нҢҢмқј_мқҙл Ҙ.xlsx` | `reports/file_activity/**` |
| run/log | **proposed** `_workmeta/<project>/reports/мӢӨн–ү_мқҙл Ҙ/мӢӨн–ү_мқҙл Ҙ.csv` | **proposed** `_workspaces/<project>/reports/мӢӨн–ү_мқҙл Ҙ/мӢӨн–ү_мқҙл Ҙ.xlsx` | `_workmeta/<project>/runs/<run_id>/**` |

CSVмҷҖ XLSXлҠ” к°ҷмқҖ accepted event cutoff, `projection_generation_id`, active `projector_epoch`, row count,
ordered row digestлҘј к°Җм ём•ј н•ңлӢӨ. Mail viewлҠ” м—¬кё°м—җ нҸ¬н•Ё eventлі„ `classification_epoch`лҘј м •л ¬н•ҙ л§Ңл“ 
`source_epoch_digest`мҷҖ `max_classification_epoch`лҸ„ к°ҷм•„м•ј н•ңлӢӨ. л¶„лҘҳмҷҖ нҲ¬мҳҒ epochлҠ” м„ңлЎң лӢӨлҘё roleмқҳ
fenceмқҙлҜҖлЎң к°ҷмқҖ мҲ«мһҗлқјкі  к°Җм •н•ҳкұ°лӮҳ н•ҳлӮҳмқҳ `fencing_epoch`лЎң н•©м№ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. мӣҗл¬ё mail/voice/file/run payloadлҠ” source/worksite ownerм—җ лӮЁкі ,
projection writerк°Җ body, transcript, attachment, file byte, raw logлҘј мқҪкұ°лӮҳ л‘җ лІҲм§ё truthлҘј л§Ңл“Өм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
кё°мЎҙ v1 mail viewмқҳ subject/counterpart к°ҷмқҖ display metadataлҠ” H06 technical sourceлЎң мӮ¬мҡ©н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
D22/D24к°Җ owner-approved redacted projection-field allowlistлҘј м •н•ҳкё° м „м—җлҠ” v2/export acceptanceлҘј
мЈјмһҘн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
м •мғҒ мҡҙмҳҒм—җм„ң мқҙ лӢӨм„Ҝ мў…лҘҳмқҳ CSV/XLSXлҘј м“°лҠ” мЈјмІҙлҠ” HPP `project_history_projector` н•ҳлӮҳлӢӨ. MailмқҖ
DB assignment event/outboxвҶ”CSV/ICS/XLSXк№Ңм§Җ parityлҘј мҡ”кө¬н•ҳкі , лӮҳлЁём§Җ laneмқҖ canonical technical
event/ref+accepted cutoffвҶ”CSV/XLSX parityлҘј мҡ”кө¬н•ңлӢӨ. Mac miniмҷҖ лӢӨлҘё PCлҠ” к°җмӢңВ·gap/alert candidateл§Ң
л§Ңл“Өл©°, лі„лҸ„ мҠ№мқёлҗң emergency leaseк°Җ м—Ҷмңјл©ҙ мқҙ нҢҢмқјмқ„ м“°м§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

мқҙ нҢҢмқјл“ӨмқҖ accepted generationмқҳ **к°җмӮ¬В·мӮ¬лһҢ м—ҙлһҢВ·мҳӨн”„лқјмқё snapshot**мқҙм§Җ live event bus, кё°ліё
query source лҳҗлҠ” reverse-import sourceк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. к°ҷмқҖ generation manifestлҠ” API result digestлҸ„
нҸ¬н•Ён•ҳл©° API/CSV/XLSX parityлҘј нҶөкіјн•ң л’Өм—җл§Ң accepted current pointerлҘј м „м§„мӢңнӮЁлӢӨ. нҢҖмӣҗмқҖ кё°ліём ҒмңјлЎң
ERP UI/MCPм—җм„ң к°ҷмқҖ accepted generationмқ„ мЎ°нҡҢн•ҳкі , GitмқҖ private metadata history/к°җмӮ¬ м „лӢ¬м—җл§Ң м“ҙлӢӨ.

#### 3.4.3 H01~H05 public-safe readiness мһ¬кІҖнҶ мҷҖ P1 ліҙм • (2026-07-15)

мқҙ н‘ңлҠ” live/private completenessлҘј мЎ°мӮ¬н•ң кІ°кіјк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. public кі„м•ҪВ·мҪ”л“ңмҷҖ н•©м„ұ fixtureл§Ң лӢӨмӢң
лҢҖмЎ°н•ң `CURRENT`мқҙл©°, H00 owner ratificationмқҙлӮҳ к°Ғ technical owner acceptanceлҘј лҢҖмӢ н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

| slice | лӢӨмӢң нҷ•мқён•ң `CURRENT` | P1 н•„мҲҳ ліҙм • / мӨ‘лӢЁм„  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| H00 | `PROJECT_HISTORY_ENVELOPE_V0.md`мҷҖ pure helperлҠ” event envelopeмҷҖ coverage receiptлҘј л¶„лҰ¬н•ң `canon_candidate`мқҙкі  В§3.4.1мқҖ к·ё лҸ…лҰҪ pairлҘј мһ¬нҳ„н•ңлӢӨ. м•„м§Ғ owner-ratified canonмқҖ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. | ownerк°Җ exact independent pairлҘј ratifyн•ҳкё° м „ H01~H05 adapterлҘј кө¬нҳ„н•ҳкұ°лӮҳ кё°мЎҙ sourceм—җ мҶҢкёү м Ғмҡ©н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. |
| H01 mail | JS `upsertProjectMailHistory()`лҠ” assignment/CLIм—җм„ң, Python `ProjectMailHistoryWriter`лҠ” mail-candidate queueм—җм„ң нҳём¶ңлҗҳкі  Outlook `applySentDeltas()`лҠ” CSVл§Ң м§Ғм ‘ к°ұмӢ н•ңлӢӨ. `scan_mail_ledger.mjs`лҠ” CSV consumerмқҙл©°, м„ё writerмқҳ classification eventВ·DBмҷҖ CSV/XLSXлҠ” н•ң atomic generation/outboxк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. | H01мқҖ `H01A` project-independent occurrenceВ·append-only classification contract/shadowмҷҖ `H01B` coverage acceptanceлЎң лӮҳлҲҲлӢӨ. H01AлҠ” H00кіј D26 exact mail owner/ID grammarк°Җ, H01BлҠ” D25 mail coverage policyк°Җ м„ н–үн•ңлӢӨ. D21мқҖ P8 syntheticвҶ’P9 durable owner/pilotвҶ’P10 live, D23 source factsлҠ” D25 inputВ·emergency fallbackмқҖ P10мқҙлӢӨ. D22 display projectionмқҖ H06/P8, DB/outboxлҠ” P8, bounded cutoverлҠ” P9, RTO/RPOВ·approverлҠ” P10 gateлӢӨ. кё°мЎҙ writer ліҖкІҪ, file/DB м—°кІ°, live caller `0`, parityВ·failover мҷ„лЈҢ мЈјмһҘмқҖ кёҲм§Җн•ңлӢӨ. |
| H02 voice | Mac temporary-failover collectorмқҳ recording/session/library, accepted route, producer receiptмҷҖ consumer ackлҠ” кө¬нҳ„лҸј мһҲлӢӨ. TARGET HPP voice primary cutoverлҠ” лҜёмӢӨн–үмқҙл©° cited public voice surfaceм—җм„ңлҠ” common envelope, route/retranscription supersession, D25 gap mappingмқ„ м°ҫм§Җ лӘ»н–ҲлӢӨ. | `recording_id`лҘј native occurrence нӣ„ліҙлЎң л‘җкі  sessionкіј meeting bundleмқҖ relation/grouping refлЎң л¶„лҰ¬н•ңлӢӨ. HPP cutover м „ exact writer lease/epochмҷҖ queue catch-upмқ„ мҰқлӘ…н•ҳкі , route/coverage ambiguityк°Җ лӮЁмңјл©ҙ adapterлҘј мӢңмһ‘н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. |
| H03 structured PC work | ERP MCP WorkSessionмқҳ bounded/idempotent publish, metadata-only daily ledger, dev-ERP `codex_instruction` metadata projectionмқҙ мһҲлӢӨ. лі„лҸ„ task-chat payload ownerмҷҖ completion-hookмқҳ full-message summarization кІҪлЎңлҸ„ мЎҙмһ¬н•ңлӢӨ. | H03A structured adapterмҷҖ H03B external schedule contractлҘј лӮҙл¶Җ лӢЁкі„лЎң л¶„лҰ¬н•ңлӢӨ. daily ledgerмҷҖ context life treeлҠ” source truthк°Җ м•„лӢҢ нҢҢмғқ projectionмқҙлҜҖлЎң native occurrence/event countм—җ л„Јм§Җ м•Ҡкі  source eventлҘј к°ҖлҰ¬нӮӨлҠ” projection/coverage refлЎңл§Ң м“ҙлӢӨ. whole task-chat payloadмҷҖ task-chat completion-hook/full-message summaryлҸ„ coverageк°Җ м•„лӢҲл©° adapter мһ…л Ҙм—җм„ң кұ°л¶Җн•ңлӢӨ. bounded WorkSessionмқҳ мҠ№мқёлҗң `summary` н•„л“ңлҠ” мқҙ кёҲм§ҖмҷҖ кө¬л¶„н•ңлӢӨ. H03 мөңмў… receiptлҠ” D20 exact schedule owner/path/writerмҷҖ л‘җ лӢЁкі„ acceptanceк°Җ лӘЁл‘җ мһҲм–ҙм•ј н•ңлӢӨ. |
| H03 external SE schedule | ERP лӮҙл¶Җ template spawn, anchor move, 1-hop due мһ¬кі„мӮ°кіј generic eventлҠ” мһҲмңјлӮҳ external master schedule current/revision/eventмқҳ standalone ownerк°Җ м—ҶлӢӨ. | D20мқҳ exact owner identity, current path, immutable event/revision path, sole writerк°Җ кІ°м •лҗ  л•Ңк№Ңм§Җ H03BмҷҖ schedule-derived task discoveryлҘј HOLDн•ңлӢӨ. ERP лӮҙл¶Җ template eventлҘј external master revisionмңјлЎң к°ҖмһҘн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. |
| H04 file | five-ID, exact content/revision, observation/event/checkpoint, sole reconciler candidateмҷҖ bounded life-tree projectionмқҙ кө¬нҳ„лҸј мһҲлӢӨ. projectionмқҖ live collector/ERP correlation л¶Җмһ¬лҘј нҸ¬н•Ён•ҙ мқҳлҸ„м ҒмңјлЎң `partial`мқҙлӢӨ. | adapterлҠ” caller-supplied immutable event/checkpoint refмҷҖ bounded replaceable projection/coverage refл§Ң л°ӣкі  filesystemмқ„ scanн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. bounded projectionмқ„ complete ledgerлЎң мҠ№кІ©н•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡкі  truncation/live gapsлҘј D25 receiptм—җ ліҙмЎҙн•ңлӢӨ. |
| H05 run/log | `_workmeta/<project>/runs/**`лҠ” мң„м№ҳ ownerм§Җл§Ң лӘЁл“  runм—җ кіөнҶөмқё manifest schemaк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. `soulforge.workflow_receipt.v1`мқҖ нҳ„мһ¬ `workflow_id: report_authoring_v0` м „мҡ©мқҙлӢӨ. five-fieldмқҳ current `id`лҠ” мқјл¶Җ н•„л“ңл§Ң hashн•ҳкі  same-ID full-record conflictлҘј кІҖмҰқн•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡмңјл©° м „мҡ© raw/secret boundary validatorлҸ„ м—ҶлӢӨ. | мҠ№мқёлҗң exact schema+explicit ref allowlistл§Ң мһ…л ҘмңјлЎң л°ӣкі  run directory recursion, raw/stage log, transcript, arbitrary manifestлҘј кұ°л¶Җн•ңлӢӨ. мөңмҙҲ eligible нӣ„ліҙлҠ” exact schema validationкіј `job_id` uniqueness/immutabilityлҘј мҰқлӘ…н•ң report-authoring receiptлҝҗмқҙлӢӨ. five-fieldлҠ” full-record digest, collision conflict, boundary validator м „м—җлҠ” native occurrence allowlistм—җм„ң м ңмҷён•ңлӢӨ. daily ledger/contextлҠ” м–ҙлҠҗ laneм—җм„ңлҸ„ native occurrenceк°Җ м•„лӢҲл©° H01~H05 мӣҗ sourceлҘј к°ҖлҰ¬нӮӨлҠ” derived relation refлЎңл§Ң м“ҙлӢӨ. |
| H06 | accepted H01~H05 lane receiptк°Җ м•„м§Ғ м—Ҷкі  D22/D24~D26лҸ„ лҜёнҷ•м •мқҙлӢӨ. | м§ҖкёҲмқҖ readiness/fixture м„Өкі„к№Ңм§Җл§Ң н—Ҳмҡ©н•ңлӢӨ. H00 ratification, H01~H05 acceptance, D22/D24 view+redacted field target, D25 coverage vocabulary, D26 source-to-lane allowlist л’Өм—җл§Ң replay/export acceptanceлҘј мӢңмһ‘н•ңлӢӨ. |

2026-07-19 кө¬нҳ„мқҖ мқҙ мӨ‘лӢЁм„ мқ„ мҪ”л“ңлЎң кі м •н–ҲлӢӨ. `project_history_readiness.mjs`лҠ”
public gate map, candidate-only lane profile, synthetic one-project ShadowмҷҖ H06 coverage/replayл§Ң
кІҖмҰқн•ҳл©° live adapterлҘј м ңкіөн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. н•ҙлӢ№ suite PASSлҠ” C00B/P0/H00/H01~H06/P1 acceptance,
actual project promotion, production export лҳҗлҠ” writer к¶Ңн•ңмқ„ л§Ңл“Өм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

H03мқҳ лӮҙл¶Җ мҲңм„ңлҠ” `H03A structured PC work synthetic adapter вҶ’ H03B external schedule
current/revision/event contract+fixture вҶ’ H03 combined acceptance`лӢӨ. H03AлҠ” H00 ratification, D19
boundary, м Ғмҡ© к°ҖлҠҘн•ң D26 WorkSession mapping ratification л’Өм—җл§Ң м§„н–үн•ңлӢӨ. H03BлҠ” D20кіј м Ғмҡ© к°ҖлҠҘн•ң
D26 schedule mapping л’Өм—җл§Ң м§„н–үн•ңлӢӨ. л‘җ лӢЁкі„к°Җ лӘЁл‘җ acceptedмқҙкі  D25 coverage policyк°Җ м Ғмҡ©лҸјм•ј
H03 combined acceptanceлҘј мЈјмһҘн•  мҲҳ мһҲлӢӨ. H05мқҳ мөңмҙҲ allowlist нӣ„ліҙлҠ” report-authoring м „мҡ©
`soulforge.workflow_receipt.v1`лҝҗмқҙл©° exact schema validationкіј `job_id` uniqueness/immutabilityлҘј лЁјм Җ
мҰқлӘ…н•ңлӢӨ. five-fieldлҠ” full-record digestВ·same-ID conflictВ·raw/secret boundary validator кі„м•Ҫмқ„ лі„лҸ„
мҠ№мқёл°ӣкё° м „ relation refлЎңл§Ң ліҙмЎҙн•ңлӢӨ. schemaк°Җ м—ҶлҠ” `runs/**` нҢҢмқјмқҖ мқҙлҰ„мқҙлӮҳ мң„м№ҳл§ҢмңјлЎң мҲҳмҡ©н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

H01мқҳ лӮҙл¶Җ мҲңм„ңлҠ” `H01A exact legacy caller graph evidence + mail occurrence/classification contract shadow вҶ’
H01B D25 policy-bound coverage receipt`лӢӨ. Caller graphлҠ” H01 packetмқҳ read-only мһ…л Ҙмқј лҝҗ `MAIL-01`
cutover acceptanceк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. H01AлҠ” `MAIL-03` мӨ‘ project-independent occurrenceмҷҖ append-only
reclassification мқҳлҜё, `MAIL-12` shadow raw/private л°°м ңл§Ң кІҖмҰқн•ңлӢӨ. DB current/FK, outbox, lock,
classification/projector epoch, display projectionкіј same-generation file parityлҠ” P8 мҶҢмң лӢӨ. `MAIL-11`мқҳ
six-state/count-null мқҳлҜёлҠ” H00мқ„ мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ©н•ҳкі , mail expected source setВ·windowВ·freshnessВ·gap/applicabilityлҠ”
D25к°Җ кіөкёүн•ңлӢӨ. D21~D23/D22 л¶Җмһ¬лҘј мқҙмң лЎң H01 pure contract/shadowлҘј P8 л’ӨлЎң лҜёлЈЁм§Җ м•Ҡмңјл©°, л°ҳлҢҖлЎң
H01мқ„ нҶөкіјн–ҲлӢӨлҠ” мқҙмң лЎң HPP/Mac м—ӯн• В·leaseВ·failover к¶Ңн•ңмқ„ л§Ңл“Өм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

#### 3.4.4 D26 five-lane typed native occurrence нӣ„ліҙ map (`TARGET`, owner ratification pending)

кіөнҶө envelopeлҠ” source-local immutable occurrenceлҘј ліөмӮ¬н•ҳлҠ” л‘җ лІҲм§ё мӣҗмһҘмқҙ м•„лӢҲлқј exact
`{entity_type, owner_surface, entity_id}` typed refлЎң к°ҖлҰ¬нӮӨлҠ” adapter м¶ңл ҘмқҙлӢӨ. к°ҷмқҖ physical source
recordлҘј л‘ҳ мқҙмғҒмқҳ laneм—җм„ң native occurrenceлЎң мӨ‘ліө мӮ°мһ…н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. м•„лһҳ к°’мқҖ public кі„м•Ҫм—җм„ң лҸ„м¶ңн•ң
нӣ„ліҙмқҙл©° `TBD`к°Җ н•ҳлӮҳлқјлҸ„ лӮЁкұ°лӮҳ D26 owner ratificationВ·H01~H05 binding/existence кІҖмҰқмқҙ м—Ҷмңјл©ҙ exact
allowlist, canon, live mappingмқҙ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ.

| lane/source subtype | `entity_type` нӣ„ліҙ | `owner_surface` нӣ„ліҙ/мғҒнғң | `entity_id` source нӣ„ліҙ | event/revision кҙҖкі„мҷҖ мӨ‘лӢЁм„  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| mail | `mail_occurrence` | `TBD` вҖ” H01/D26 exact mail occurrence owner | H01 ownerк°Җ provider message occurrenceм—җ project-independentн•ҳкІҢ кІ°н•©н•ң opaque `mail_occurrence_id` | л¶„лҘҳВ·мһ¬л¶„лҘҳ append eventмҷҖ мҠ№мқёлҗң exact message/body revision; projectк°Җ л“Өм–ҙк°„ legacy `мқҙл ҘнӮӨ`, thread ref, current assignmentлҠ” identity кёҲм§Җ |
| voice | `voice_recording` | `voice_capture` candidate | `recording_id` | captureВ·transcriptionВ·retranscriptionВ·route eventмҷҖ audio/transcript exact revision mappingмқҖ H02 `TARGET/TBD`; `session_id`мҷҖ `meeting_bundle_id`лҠ” grouping/ref |
| structured PC work / WorkSession | `erp_mcp_work_session` | `dev_erp` candidate | `erp_mcp_work_session.id` | bounded WorkSession recordл§Ң; idempotency conflictмҷҖ existenceлҘј H03Aк°Җ кІҖмҰқ |
| structured PC work / instruction | `instruction_packet` | `TBD` вҖ” D19 approved packet owner | owner-approved exact instruction packet ID | whole task-chatкіј task-chat completion-hook/full-message summaryлҠ” м ңмҷё; WorkSession `summary`лҠ” лі„лҸ„ н—Ҳмҡ© н•„л“ң |
| structured PC work / external schedule | `schedule_row` | `TBD` вҖ” D20 exact owner | D20мқҙ м •н•ң stable schedule-row ID | exact version/snapshot eventмҷҖ current rowлҘј л¶„лҰ¬; D20 м „ H03B HOLD |
| file | `TBD` вҖ” H04к°Җ `file_observation`, `file_reconciliation_event`, `erp_upload_event` subtypeлі„ кІ°м • | `file_activity` лҳҗлҠ” `dev_erp` candidate, subtypeлі„ owner нҷ•м • н•„мҡ” | `observation_id`, reconciliation `event_id`, `erp_upload_event_id` мӨ‘ owner-approved exact event occurrence | `logical_file_id`лҠ” file lineage/grouping ref, `revision_id`/`content_id`лҠ” exact revision refлӢӨ. upload receiptлҠ” file-lane occurrence нӣ„ліҙмқј лҝҗ project promotionВ·`ArtifactRevision` acceptanceВ·knowledge acceptanceк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. pathВ·filenameВ·mtimeВ·hash лӢЁлҸ… identity кёҲм§Җ |
| run/log / report authoring | `workflow_job` | `report_authoring_v0` candidate | exact-schema receiptмқҳ `job_id` | нҳ„мһ¬ `workflow_id: report_authoring_v0`м—җл§Ң м Ғмҡ©; `job_id` uniqueness/immutabilityмҷҖ validator refлҘј H05к°Җ кІҖмҰқ |
| run/log / five-field | `TBD` | `five_field_session_capture_v0` candidate | **current capture `id`лҠ” ineligible** | full-record digest, same-ID conflict, raw/secret boundary validatorлҘј ownerк°Җ мҠ№мқён•ҳкё° м „ native occurrence мӮ°мһ… кёҲм§Җ; `session_ref`лҠ” grouping ref |

derived daily-ledger/context rowк°Җ H01~H05 source eventлӮҳ runмқ„ мҡ”м•Ҫн•ҳл©ҙ мӣҗ source occurrenceлҘј relationмңјлЎң
к°ҖлҰ¬нӮ¬ лҝҗ мғҲ project-history native occurrence, event лҳҗлҠ” coverage countлҘј л§Ңл“Өм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. source refк°Җ
м—Ҷкұ°лӮҳ к°ҷмқҖ physical recordк°Җ л‘җ lane нӣ„ліҙлЎң л“Өм–ҙмҳӨл©ҙ adapterлҠ” м¶”м •н•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡкі  мӨ‘лӢЁн•ҳл©° кі„нҡҚ мғҒнғңлҘј
`UNKNOWN/VERIFY_HP`лЎң мң м§Җн•ңлӢӨ. D25 ratification м „м—җлҠ” мқҙ мғҒнғңлҘј н‘ңнҳ„н•  мғҲ gap codeлҘј л°ңлӘ…н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

#### 3.4.5 л°ӣмқҖл©”мқјВ·ліҙлӮёл©”мқј нҶөн•©кіј Slack project context (`TARGET`, H01C/H07)

мқҙ addendumмқҖ кё°мЎҙ H00~H06 five-lane bounded pilotмқ„ л¬ҙнҡЁнҷ”н•ҳкұ°лӮҳ м—¬м„Ҝ лІҲм§ё laneмңјлЎң мҶҢкёү мһ¬н•ҙм„қн•ҳм§Җ
м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. Mail нҷ•мһҘмқҖ H01 лӮҙл¶Җ `H01C`, SlackмқҖ лі„лҸ„ communication-history extension `H07AвҶ’H07B`лЎң
м¶”к°Җн•ңлӢӨ. H06мқҖ кё°мЎҙ five-lane P1 core exitмқҙкі , ownerк°Җ Slackмқ„ нҢҖ project sourceлЎң м Ғмҡ©н•ң нҳ„мһ¬ мҡҙмҳҒ
лІ”мң„м—җм„ңлҠ” H07B receiptк°Җ м—Ҷмңјл©ҙ P5 `context_acceptance_gate`к°Җ Slack coverageлҘј completeлЎң к°„мЈјн•  мҲҳ м—ҶлӢӨ.

##### Mail: н•ң нҶөкіј м—¬лҹ¬ mailbox кҙҖмёЎмқ„ л¶„лҰ¬н•ңлӢӨ

```text
logical mail occurrence 1к°ң
в”ңв”Җ owner Sent Items observation      role=sender
в”ңв”Җ member A Inbox observation        role=to
в”ңв”Җ member B Inbox observation        role=cc
в””в”Җ outbound transport observation    role=sender_transport (мһҲмқ„ л•Ңл§Ң)
```

| лҢҖмғҒ | `CURRENT` | `TARGET` | м•Ҳм „ мӨ‘лӢЁм„  |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| owner ліҙлӮёл©”мқј | `outlook_mail_reconcile.mjs`к°Җ local Outlook кё°ліё ліҙлӮёнҺём§Җн•Ё metadataлҘј мқҪлҠ”лӢӨ. current rowлҠ” EntryID/ConversationID fingerprint, мӢңк°Ғ, м ңлӘ©, recipient count мӨ‘мӢ¬мқҙл©° exact Internet Message-IDмҷҖ recipient address snapshotмқҖ ліҙмһҘн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. | owner-approved Outlook sourceм—җм„ң opaque exact message occurrence refмҷҖ sender/to/cc/bcc role snapshotмқ„ м·Ёл“қн•ҳкі  H01C observationмңјлЎң м—°кІ° | Outlook local EntryIDлӮҳ м ңлӘ©+мӢңк°Ғл§ҢмңјлЎң лӢӨлҘё mailbox copyлҘј confirmed mergeн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ |
| нҢҖмӣҗ л°ӣмқҖл©”мқј | нҳ„мһ¬ Hiworks POP3 collectorк°Җ accountлі„ л°ӣмқҖнҺём§Җн•Ёмқ„ мҲҳм§‘н•ңлӢӨ. | accountлі„ source observationмқ„ мң м§Җн•ҳлҗҳ к°ҷмқҖ exact message occurrenceл©ҙ project/task нӣ„ліҙлҠ” н•ң лІҲл§Ң мғқм„ұ | н•ң accountмқҳ 0кұҙмқ„ м „мІҙ mail 0кұҙмңјлЎң н•ҙм„қн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ |
| нҢҖмӣҗ ліҙлӮёл©”мқј | current POP3лҠ” sent folder sourceк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. нҢҖмӣҗмқҙ Hiworks web/к°Ғмһҗ clientм—җм„ң м§Ғм ‘ ліҙлӮё м „мІҙ лӮҙм—ӯмқҳ HPP sourceлҠ” `UNKNOWN`мқҙлӢӨ. | D33м—җм„ң Hiworks archive/export/API capability, мҠ№мқёлҗң outbound journal, лҳҗлҠ” к°Ғ clientмқҳ bounded sent adapter мӨ‘ н•ҳлӮҳлҘј exact sourceлЎң м„ нғқ | sourceлҘј м •н•ҳкё° м „ вҖңнҢҖ м „мІҙ sent coverage completeвҖқ мЈјмһҘ кёҲм§Җ; л№„л°ҖлІҲнҳёВ·tokenВ·ліёл¬ёмқ„ plan/ledgerм—җ кё°лЎқн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ |
| Soulforge л°ңмҶЎ | SMTP outbound snapshot/logлҠ” Soulforge senderлҘј кұ°м№ң mailл§Ң кҙҖмёЎн•ңлӢӨ. | к°ҷмқҖ exact message occurrenceмқҳ transport observationмңјлЎң м—°кІ° | лӘЁл“  мӮ¬лһҢмқҳ ліҙлӮёнҺём§Җн•Ё лҢҖмІҙл¬јлЎң кіјлҢҖ мЈјмһҘн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ |

H01Cмқҳ logical identity мҡ°м„ мҲңмң„лҠ” source/providerк°Җ ліҙмҰқн•ң RFC Internet Message-ID лҳҗлҠ” equivalent native
occurrence refлӢӨ. лҸҷмқј occurrenceм—җ м—¬лҹ¬ account/folder observationмқ„ appendн•ңлӢӨ. `In-Reply-To`мҷҖ
`References`лҠ” **thread relation**мқҙм§Җ к°ҷмқҖ message identityк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. subject/time/size/recipient-count,
ConversationIDлӮҳ LLM similarityлҠ” reconciliation candidateл§Ң л§Ңл“Ө мҲҳ мһҲкі  мһҗлҸҷ confirmed mergeлҠ” кёҲм§Җн•ңлӢӨ.
лі„лҸ„лЎң ліҙлӮё л‘җ нҶөмқҖ ліёл¬ёмқҙ к°ҷм•„лҸ„ exact occurrence refк°Җ лӢӨлҘҙл©ҙ м„ңлЎң лӢӨлҘё mailмқҙлӢӨ.

мҲҳмӢ мһҗ мқҳлҜёлҠ” account-relative relationмңјлЎң ліҙмЎҙн•ңлӢӨ.

- `sender`: л°ңмӢ  мЈјмІҙ. ownerк°Җ нҢҖмӣҗм—җкІҢ ліҙлӮё м—…л¬ҙм§ҖмӢңлҠ” мқҙ occurrenceм—җм„ң н•ң лІҲл§Ң нӣ„ліҙнҷ”н•ңлӢӨ.
- `to`: м§Ғм ‘ мҲҳмӢ мһҗ нӣ„ліҙм§Җл§Ң м—¬лҹ¬ ToлҘј мһҗлҸҷмңјлЎң м—¬лҹ¬ кіөмӢқ н• мқјлЎң л§Ңл“Өм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
- `cc`: кіөмң В·мқём§Җ evidenceмқҙл©° кё°ліё лӢҙлӢ№мһҗ/мҷ„лЈҢ мұ…мһ„мһҗлЎң мҠ№кІ©н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
- `bcc`: sender copyлӮҳ мҠ№мқёлҗң transport sourceк°Җ мҰқлӘ…н•  л•Ңл§Ң кё°лЎқн•ңлӢӨ. мҲҳмӢ  copyм—җм„ң м¶”м •н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
- reply/forwardлҠ” мғҲ occurrenceлӢӨ. parent/thread relationмңјлЎң м—°кІ°н•ҳл©° reply мһҗмІҙлҘј мҷ„лЈҢлЎң к°„мЈјн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

##### Slack: channel bindingмқҙ projectлҘј кІ°м •н•ҳкі  лӮҙмҡ©мқҖ task candidateл§Ң л§Ңл“ лӢӨ

Slack source truthлҠ” HPP private cross-project stateмқҳ logical `collaboration/slack` ownerм—җ лӮЁкі , raw message
bodyлӮҳ attachment byteлҘј public Git лҳҗлҠ” `_workmeta`м—җ ліөмӮ¬н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. proposed project viewлҠ”
`_workmeta/<project_code>/reports/нҳ‘м—…_мқҙл Ҙ/нҳ‘м—…_мқҙл Ҙ.csv`мҷҖ
`_workspaces/<project_code>/reports/нҳ‘м—…_мқҙл Ҙ/нҳ‘м—…_мқҙл Ҙ.xlsx`мқҙл©° D34мқҳ field/path ratification м „м—җлҠ”
нҸҙлҚ”лҘј л§Ңл“Өкұ°лӮҳ exportн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

| Slack object | stable identity / relation | projectВ·task мқҳлҜё |
| --- | --- | --- |
| workspace/channel | `workspace_id+channel_id`; channel nameмқҖ revision/display metadata | owner-approved effective-dated bindingмқҙ мһҲмңјл©ҙ channelмқҳ authoritative default project scope. renameмқҖ projectлҘј л°”кҫём§Җ м•ҠмқҢ |
| message | `(workspace_id,channel_id,message_ts)` logical message ref; Events API outer `event_id`лҠ” delivery dedupe ref | channel projectлҘј мғҒмҶҚн•ҳм§Җл§Ң request/commitment/decisionмқҖ candidate-only |
| thread | root `thread_ts`; repliesлҠ” к°Ғмһҗ message occurrence | root/reply лӘЁл‘җ channel project. replyВ·reactionмқҖ кіөмӢқ мҷ„лЈҢк°Җ м•„лӢҳ |
| edit/delete | original message refм—җ append-only revision/supersession/tombstone event | current viewлҠ” rebuild к°ҖлҠҘн•ҙм•ј н•ҳкі  кіјкұ° evidenceлҘј overwrite/deleteн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ |
| author | Slack `user_id`вҶ’ERP account private mapping | mapping м—Ҷмңјл©ҙ unknown actor; мқҙлҰ„В·н‘ңмӢңлӘ…мңјлЎң мһҗлҸҷ кІ°н•© кёҲм§Җ |
| file/link | Slack file/message pointerвҶ’D27 artifact/source revision candidate | мһҗлҸҷ лӢӨмҡҙлЎңл“ңВ·project promotionВ·RAG/Wiki мҠ№кІ© кёҲм§Җ |

H07AлҠ” Slack App identity, channel allowlist/binding, minimal OAuth scope, Socket Mode лҳҗлҠ” approved HTTPS Events
delivery, event retry/dedupe, Web API bounded backfill/reconciliation, cursorмҷҖ coverage contractл§Ң syntheticмңјлЎң
кі м •н•ңлӢӨ. H07BлҠ” P3 immutable revision contract л’Ө exact message/edit/delete revisionкіј project-context adapterлҘј
ShadowлЎң кІҖмҰқн•ңлӢӨ. BotмқҖ approved project channelм—җ лӘ…мӢңм ҒмңјлЎң м°ём—¬н•ҙм•ј н•ҳл©° DMВ·general/commonВ·unmapped
channel, Slack Connect мҷёл¶Җ workspace, archived channelмқҖ D34 rule м—ҶмқҙлҠ” `unclassified/HOLD`лӢӨ. HPP мқҙмҷё
normal collector, automatic channel join, message posting, reaction, delete, task/knowledge writerлҠ” кё°ліё `OFF`лӢӨ.

### 3.5 Payload ingress custodyмҷҖ promotion (`TARGET`, л¬јлҰ¬ bindingмқҖ `VERIFY_HP`)

P1 history adapterлҠ” metadata refлҘј л°ӣлҠ” кІҪкі„мқҙкі  payload promoterк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. нҳ„мһ¬ sourceлі„ ingressк°Җ
л¶„лҰ¬лҸј мһҲмңјлҜҖлЎң м•„лһҳ н‘ңмқҳ лҜём • ownerлҘј кіөнҶө inbox н•ҳлӮҳлЎң м¶”м •н•ҳкұ°лӮҳ мӢӨм ң нҸҙлҚ”лҘј л§Ңл“Өм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

| source kind | `CURRENT` custody/staging | quarantineВ·security нҳ„мһ¬ к°•лҸ„ | `TARGET` promotion кІҪкі„ | лӮЁмқҖ `VERIFY_HP` |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| mail raw/attachment | gateway mailbox stateк°Җ raw/event/attachmentлҘј materializeн•ҳлҠ” кі„м•Ҫкіј rootмқҳ approved worksite payload мӣҗм№ҷ мӮ¬мқҙм—җ tensionмқҙ мһҲлӢӨ | extension/policy filterВ·hashВ·large-file referenceлҠ” мһҲмңјлӮҳ malware scan enforcement мҰқкұ°лҠ” м—ҶмқҢ | classificationкіј `mail-candidate:promote`лҠ” attachment bytes delta `0`; лі„лҸ„ promoterл§Ң approved storage bindingмңјлЎң мҠ№кІ© | raw/attachment physical owner, ACL, retention/legal hold, scan, backup/restore |
| ERP chat attachment | service-owned `codex-task-attachments` inbox copy | opaque item bindingВ·path isolation; production security policyлҠ” лі„лҸ„ | upload receiptмҷҖ project/artifact promotionмқ„ л¶„лҰ¬ | quarantine/retention/scanкіј official destination |
| personal MCP artifact | service-owned `mcp-artifacts` inbox copy; size/hash/extension/one-time URL кІҖмҰқ | production blockerм—җ malware scanВ·backup/restoreВ·retentionмқҙ лӮЁмқҢ | central custody receipt л’Ө explicit human-approved project promotion | scan engine/policy, ACL, retention, rollback |
| HPP evidence ingress MCP source foundation (2026-07-17 нӣ„мҶҚ кө¬нҳ„) | ERPмҷҖ л¶„лҰ¬лҗң feature-OFF serviceк°Җ authenticated chunk/file, bounded PC work/run receiptлҘј кё°мЎҙ HPP local outbox 3к°ң laneм—җл§Ң м „лӢ¬; н•©м„ұ 3-user/process E2EмҷҖ мӢӨм ң TLS socketмқ„ м“ҙ н•©м„ұ RFC1918 mTLS E2E PASS | bearer hashВ·account/device/agentВ·exact project/capability ACL, hash/size/resume/dedupe/revoke, loopback backend, strict RFC1918 exact bindВ·TLS 1.3В·client certificate registryВ·server pinВ·Host/identity кІ°н•©В·request/space quota кө¬нҳ„. malware scanВ·backup/retention мҡҙмҳҒм№ҳлҠ” лҜёкө¬нҳ„ | HPP custody ackк№Ңм§Җл§Ң мҶҢмң н•ҳл©° project promoter/accepted history/Task completionмқҖ н•ӯмғҒ false | мӢӨм ң HPP LAN listener/firewall/cert/tokenкіј л¬јлҰ¬ PCлҠ” лӘЁл‘җ OFF. D27 exact owner/binding, scan/backup/retention, one-seat physical canaryк°Җ лӮЁмңјл©° P0~P10В·A8-CANARY мһҗлҸҷ unlock м—ҶмқҢ |
| voice/audio/transcript | voice source ownerк°Җ rawмҷҖ revisionмқ„ ліҙмң н•ҳкі  projectм—җлҠ” pointer/eventлҘј route | provider summaryлҠ” untrusted quarantine; consent/retentionмқҖ лі„лҸ„ owner gate | source revision/pointerл§Ң history/contextлЎң м „лӢ¬; raw copyлҠ” лі„лҸ„ мҠ№мқё | speaker ACL, consent, retention, exact promotion н•„мҡ”м„ұ |
| external SE schedule | current/revision/event ownerВ·pathВ·writerк°Җ лҜём • | `UNKNOWN` | D20 exact ownerмқҳ typed revisionл§Ң ingest | source custodyмҷҖ writer кІ°м • м „ м „мІҙ HOLD |
| project file/activity | bytesлҠ” project worksite, observation/revisionмқҖ file-activity owner | hash/stat кҙҖмёЎмқҖ malware scanмқҙ м•„лӢҳ | observation/upload receiptмҷҖ storage binding/ArtifactRevision acceptanceлҘј л¶„лҰ¬ | upload subtype, promoter, scan/retention/backup |
| run/log | exact workflow receiptмҷҖ `_workmeta` metadataл§Ң eligible; raw/stage logмҷҖ `runs/**` recursion кёҲм§Җ | schema/raw sentinelл§Ң; generic security scan м•„лӢҳ | approved receipt/refл§Ң ingest, payloadлҠ” worksite ownerм—җ мң м§Җ | sourceлі„ schema allowlistмҷҖ retention |

Ingress operationмқҳ м•Ҳм „ к·ңм№ҷмқҖ лӢӨмқҢкіј к°ҷлӢӨ.

1. `reference`к°Җ кё°ліёмқҙл Өл©ҙ мӣҗ sourceмқҳ durability, мһ¬мЎ°нҡҢ к°ҖлҠҘм„ұ, exact revision/hash/size, ACL нҳёнҷҳ,
   retentionмқ„ лӘЁл‘җ мҰқлӘ…н•ҙм•ј н•ңлӢӨ. мҰқлӘ…лҗҳм§Җ м•Ҡмңјл©ҙ мһҗлҸҷ copy лҢҖмӢ  `HOLD`лӢӨ.
2. MCP/chat uploadмІҳлҹј мӨ‘м•ҷ serviceк°Җ bytesлҘј м§Ғм ‘ мҲҳл №н•ҳл©ҙ service inboxк°Җ мғҲ **storage binding**мқҳ
   custodyлҘј к°–лҠ”лӢӨ. к°ҷмқҖ bytesлқјкі  мғҲ content truthк°Җ мғқкё°лҠ” кІғмқҖ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ.
3. `copy|move|derive`лҠ” owner-approved operationкіј idempotent promotion receiptк°Җ мһҲм–ҙм•ј н•ңлӢӨ. `derive`лҠ”
   мғҲ immutable derived revisionмқ„ л§Ңл“Өкі  мӣҗ revisionмқ„ к°ҖлҰ¬нӮЁлӢӨ. `move|delete` кё°ліёк°’мқҖ кёҲм§ҖлӢӨ.
4. promoterлҠ” source writer, mail classification coordinator, project-history projector,
   TaskEngine coordinatorмҷҖ лӢӨлҘё logical authorityлӢӨ. role мқҙлҰ„В·physical ownerВ·staging/quarantine/promoted
   pathлҠ” D27 м „ `VERIFY_HP`мқҙл©° мқҙ кі„нҡҚм—җм„ң мғқм„ұн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
5. HPP `transfer_service`л§Ң quarantine/inbox binaryлҘј м“°кі  HPP `promoter`л§Ң accepted project storage
   bindingмқ„ м“ҙлӢӨ. Client requestлҠ” server/local/UNC/SMB destination pathлҘј л°ӣм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
6. MCPлҠ” control planeмқҙкі  XLSX/PPT/HWPX/PDF/ZIP/audio л“ұ bytesлҠ” authenticated HTTPS data planeмңјлЎң
   м „мҶЎн•ңлӢӨ. нҳ„мһ¬ HPP targetмқҖ strict private office LANл§Ң н—Ҳмҡ©н•ҳкі  backendлҠ” loopback+mTLS reverse
   proxy л’Өм—җ л‘”лӢӨ. VPN/Tailscale/remote access, public Internet ingress, port forwarding/Funnel,
   direct SMBлҠ” `OFF/DEFER`мқҙл©° лі„лҸ„ future owner approvalВ·threat modelВ·trust/CA/ACLВ·acceptance gateк°Җ н•„мҡ”н•ҳлӢӨ.
7. Upload/download ticketмқҖ `user_id+device_id+agent_id+opaque thread_ref+task_id+project_id+artifact_id+revision_id+action+method+audience+hash+size+expiry`лҘј
   кІ°л°•н•ңлӢӨ. URLл§ҢмңјлЎң bearer authorityк°Җ лҗҳм§Җ
   м•Ҡмңјл©° finalizeлҠ” idempotent, revoke-raceлҠ” fail closedлӢӨ.

## 4. лӘЁл“  surfaceмқҳ `REUSE / MODIFY / BUILD / DEFER / REMOVE` мҙқлӘ©лЎқ

л¶„лҘҳлҠ” н•ң surfaceлӢ№ мЈјлҗң мһ‘м—… н•ҳлӮҳл§Ң н‘ңмӢңн•ңлӢӨ. `UNKNOWN`мқҖ кө¬нҳ„ м¶”м •мңјлЎң л©”мҡ°м§Җ м•Ҡкі 
`DEFER` лҳҗлҠ” owner gateлЎң ліҙлӮёлӢӨ. кё°мЎҙ reader/кІҪлЎңлҠ” consumer `0`мқ„ мҰқлӘ…н•ҳкё° м „ мӮӯм ңн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

к°Ғ surface recordлҠ” м•„лһҳ м„ё н‘ңлҘј `ID`лЎң joinн•ҙ мқҪлҠ”лӢӨ. лЁјм Җ `domain` н•„л“ңлҘј кі м •н•ңлӢӨ.

| ID | domain | ID | domain | ID | domain |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| S01 | canon/storage | S09 | TaskDriver core | S17 | AX Workspace |
| S02 | mail intake | S10 | identity/time/relation | S18 | AgentRun |
| S03 | voice intake | S11 | project context | S19 | Engineering IQ |
| S04 | SE schedule | S12 | RAG storage | S20 | ML/ranking |
| S05 | file activity | S13 | Wiki/ontology/knowledge | S21 | operations |
| S06 | person/Codex intake | S14 | life-tree projection | S22 | branch integration |
| S07 | ERP task current | S15 | compatibility ledger | S23 | legacy retirement |
| S08 | task event/completion | S16 | multi-PC runtime | S24 | immutable oracle patch |
| S25 | Slack project communication |  |  |  |  |

| S21 | actual alert/network/scheduler primaryмҷҖ recovery | zero-blocker audit + explicit G01 gate |
| S22 | candidate codeк°Җ latest mainм—җ к·ёлҢҖлЎң м Ғмҡ© к°ҖлҠҘн•ңм§Җ | C01A/C01B/C02/C03/C04A/C04B/C05/C06A/C06B file-by-file patch/test; wholesale merge м—ҶмқҢ |
| S23 | consumer `0`кіј verified rollback | complete consumer scan + old reader restore drill |
| S24 | м—ҶмқҢ; candidate-only driftк°Җ exact diffлЎң кҙҖм°°лҗЁ | integration patchм—җм„ң н•ҙлӢ№ hunks 0мқём§Җ immutable blob check |
| S25 | exact Slack app/workspace/channel authority, project binding, cursor/retention, edit/delete and attachment owner | D34+H07A public synthetic л’Ө P3-bound H07B; live one-channel canaryлҠ” separate private Level 3 |

`REMOVE`лҠ” S24мІҳлҹј **candidate integrationм—җм„ң лІ„лҰҙ ліҖкІҪ**м—җл§Ң м Ғмҡ©н•ңлӢӨ. нҳ„мһ¬ мҡҙмҳҒ reader, legacy
path, source originalмқҖ consumer `0`кіј rollback drillмқ„ мҰқлӘ…н•ҳкё° м „м—җлҠ” м ңкұ°н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

## 5. мөңмў… TARGET architectureмҷҖ owner/write кІҪкі„

### лҸ„мӢқ 1 вҖ” TARGET м „мІҙ architectureмҷҖ м“°кё° кІҪкі„

```mermaid
flowchart TB
  subgraph SO["source-local owners вҖ” payload/current/revision authority"]
    M["mail"]
    V["voice/transcript"]
    S["external SE schedule"]
    F["file activity"]
    W["structured PC work + run/log"]
  end
  ING["Ingress receipt + optional promotion<br/>pointer by default; promoter separate"]
  H["P1 append-only lane histories<br/>common envelope + coverage/gap"]
  ID["P2 typed IDs/refs/clocks"]
  REV["P3 immutable revision/relation lineage"]
  RW["P4 exact revision-bound RAG/Wiki"]
  CTX["P5 deterministic context assembly<br/>context_acceptance_gate"]
  DISC["P6 candidate-only task discovery<br/>ERP write 0"]
  TD["P7 TaskDriver<br/>why/why-now + authority + idempotency"]
  TC["P8 sole TaskEngineTransactionCoordinator<br/>task tables: reservation/event/current/receipt"]
  MO["P8 mail assignment event + outbox<br/>HPP classification coordinator"]
  PH["HPP five-lane project-history projector<br/>sole normal CSV/ICS/XLSX writer"]
  CL["enrolled work PCs / Macs<br/>MCP control only; direct storage 0"]
  HX["HPP private custody<br/>mTLS proxy + transfer service<br/>RAW/ERP/runtime logical classes"]
  OD["OneDrive junction materialization<br/>actual _workspaces project files"]
  PILOT["P9 one-project pilot + feedback"]
  READ["P9 read-only B9/ENGINE-12/context views"]
  QRY["ERP UI/MCP primary query<br/>accepted generation + explicit scope"]
  UI["ui-workspace<br/>derived UI consumer"]
  ACT["P10 separate activation/failover/AX/AgentRun/ML gates"]

  SO --> ING --> H --> ID --> REV --> RW --> CTX
  CL -->|"MCP control + authenticated HTTPS binary"| HX --> ING
  CL --> OD
  OD -. "active DB/central RAW/queue/outbox/runtime 0" .-> HX
  CTX -->|"accepted receipt only"| DISC --> TD --> TC --> PILOT
  M --> MO --> H
  H --> PH
  MO --> PH
  PILOT --> READ --> QRY --> UI
  PILOT --> ACT
  RW --> READ
  RW --> QRY
  ING -. "payload promotion only with separate authority" .-> REV
  UI -. "owner rows write 0" .-> SO
```

### 5.1 н•ң мӨ„ owner к·ңм№ҷ

- мӣҗмІң лӮҙмҡ©мқҖ мӣҗмІң ownerк°Җ к°Җм§„лӢӨ. SoulforgeлҠ” мҠ№мқёлҗң revision/pointerл§Ң м—°кІ°н•ңлӢӨ.
- P1~P5к°Җ acceptedлҗҳкё° м „м—җлҠ” task candidate/Driver/ERP schema workлҘј мӢңмһ‘н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
- TaskDriver ledgerлҠ” мҷң/лҲ„к°Җ/м–ём ң м Ғмҡ©мқ„ н—Ҳмҡ©н–ҲлҠ”м§ҖлҘј к°Җм§„лӢӨ. кіөмӢқ м—…л¬ҙ мғҒнғңлҠ” к°–м§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
- `TaskEngineTransactionCoordinator` н•ҳлӮҳл§Ң TaskEngineмқҳ Driver/task/current/receipt н…Ңмқҙлё”м—җ м“ҙлӢӨ.
  candidate/decision/apply лӘ…л №мқҖ м„ңлЎң лӢӨлҘё logical authority attestationмқ„ мҡ”кө¬н•ҳм§Җл§Ң мқҙ task-table
  writer/processлҠ” лҠҳ н•ҳлӮҳлӢӨ.
- CoordinatorлҠ” apply л•Ң task ID мҳҲм•Ҫ, Driver apply event, task event, current row, receiptлҘј н•ң
  transactionмңјлЎң м“ҙлӢӨ. лі„лҸ„ л¬јлҰ¬ writerлҘј мӣҗн•ҳл©ҙ outbox protocolмқ„ мғҲлЎң м„Өкі„н•ҙм•ј н•ҳлҜҖлЎң V0м—җлҠ”
  мұ„нғқн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
- Mail л¶„лҘҳлҠ” HPP `mail_classification_coordinator` н•ҳлӮҳл§Ң mail identity/current/event/outbox н…Ңмқҙлё”м—җ
  м“ҙлӢӨ. л‘җ coordinatorк°Җ к°ҷмқҖ dev-ERP SQLiteлҘј м“°лҚ”лқјлҸ„ м„ңлЎңмқҳ table write к¶Ңн•ңмқҖ м—Ҷкі , file
  projectorлҠ” DB task/mail currentлҘј л°”кҫём§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
- file reconcilerмҷҖ TaskEngine coordinatorлҠ” лі„лҸ„ logical identity/authorityлӢӨ. к°ҷмқҖ л¬јлҰ¬ PCм—җ мһҲм–ҙлҸ„ н•©м№ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
- н”„лЎңм қнҠёлі„ 5к°ң мӮ¬лһҢмҡ© мқҙл Ҙ CSV/XLSXлҠ” HPPмқҳ `project_history_projector`л§Ң м •мғҒ мҡҙмҳҒм—җм„ң м“ҙлӢӨ.
  мқҢм„ұВ·нҢҢмқјВ·run л“ұ кё°мҲ  мӣҗмһҘмқҖ кё°мЎҙ source ownerк°Җ кі„мҶҚ м“°л©°, projectorлҠ” accepted event/refлҘј мқҪм–ҙ
  derived viewл§Ң мһ¬мғқм„ұн•ңлӢӨ. Macмқ„ нҸ¬н•Ён•ң лӢӨлҘё PCмқҳ normal project-history write allowlistлҠ” л№„м–ҙ мһҲлӢӨ.
- B9, ENGINE-12, RAG/Wiki graph, dashboardлҠ” projectionмқҙлӢӨ. мЎ°нҡҢ мҡ”мІӯмңјлЎң owner rowлҘј л°”кҫём§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
- feedbackмқҖ sourceлі„ handoff нӣ„ліҙмҷҖ knowledge нӣ„ліҙлЎң л¶„лҰ¬н•ҳл©°, мһҗлҸҷмңјлЎң source truthк°Җ лҗҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
- `ingress_promoter` нӣ„ліҙлҠ” source custody/storage binding/promotion receiptл§Ң мҶҢмң н•ңлӢӨ. source writer,
  mail classification coordinator, history projector, TaskEngine coordinator к¶Ңн•ңмқ„ л№ҢлҰ¬м§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
- `personal_work_session_coordinator` нӣ„ліҙлҠ” assignment binding/session event/ingest receipt/completion
  proposal linkл§Ң м“ҙлӢӨ. closeoutВ·proposalлЎң task current/event, project history, Wiki/RAGлҘј м§Ғм ‘ м“°м§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
- ERP UI/MCP query adapterлҠ” accepted generationмқ„ мқҪлҠ” primary user surfaceмқј лҝҗ ownerк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ.
  лӘЁл“  knowledge queryлҠ” explicit `project|common` scopeлҘј мҡ”кө¬н•ҳкі  м„ңлЎң fallbackн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
- HPP `transfer_service`лҠ” quarantine/inbox binaryмқҳ мң мқј writerмқҙкі  HPP `promoter`лҠ” project storage
  bindingмқҳ мң мқј writerлӢӨ. ClientВ·OneDrive syncВ·history projectorлҠ” мқҙ л‘җ к¶Ңн•ңмқ„ к°–м§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
- лӢӨлҘё PCмқҳ direct HPP drive/UNC/SMB/SQLite/WAL/SHM/queue м ‘к·ј allowlistлҠ” л№„м–ҙ мһҲлӢӨ. HPP outage л•ҢлҠ”
  durable local outbox/HOLD лҳҗлҠ” last-accepted read-onlyл§Ң н—Ҳмҡ©н•ҳл©° remote mountлӮҳ split writerлЎң
  мҡ°нҡҢн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
- AI delegationмқҖ human grant, trusted device, agent policy, task/object/actionмқҳ көҗм§‘н•©мқҙл©° к°ҖмһҘ мқҙлҘё
  parent expiryлҘј м Ғмҡ©н•ҳкі  parent revokeк°Җ child grantВ·ticketм—җ cascadeн•ңлӢӨ.

### 5.2 л¬јлҰ¬ owner м„ нғқ

TaskIntent/TaskDriver/ApplicationReceiptмқҳ к¶ҢмһҘ л¬јлҰ¬ ownerлҠ” **нҳ„мһ¬ dev-ERP SQLite DB м•Ҳмқҳ мғҲ
append-only table**мқҙлӢӨ. мқҙмң лҠ” task ID мҳҲм•ҪВ·кіөмӢқ task eventВ·`core_item` к°ұмӢ В·receiptлҘј н•ҳлӮҳмқҳ
SQLite transactionмңјлЎң л¬¶мқ„ мҲҳ мһҲкё° л•Ңл¬ёмқҙлӢӨ. лі„лҸ„ JSON нҸҙлҚ”лӮҳ л‘җ лІҲм§ё DBлҘј л§Ңл“Өл©ҙ task truthмҷҖ
ліөкө¬ кІҪкі„к°Җ л‘ҳлЎң к°Ҳлқјм§„лӢӨ.

мқҙ м„ нғқмқҖ owner кІ°м • D01мқҙ н•„мҡ”н•ҳлӢӨ. мҠ№мқё м „м—җлҠ” schemaлҘј м„Өм№ҳн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. project мӣҗл¬ё,
RAG body, Wiki bodyлҠ” dev-ERP DBм—җ л„Јм§Җ м•Ҡкі  к°Ғк°Ғмқҳ мҠ№мқёлҗң payload ownerм—җ л‘”лӢӨ.
мқҙ logical DB м„ нғқмқҖ HPPмқҳ exact physical drive/pathлҘј кіөк°ңн•ҳкұ°лӮҳ OneDrive project workspaceлҘј active
DB planeмңјлЎң л§Ңл“ лӢӨлҠ” лң»мқҙ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. HPP private bindingкіј backup ownerлҠ” `VERIFY_HP`лӢӨ.

### 5.3 optional agent-client owner matrix

мҷёл¶Җ agent лҸ„кө¬лҠ” AXВ·TaskEngineкіј к°ҷмқҖ м •ліё кі„мёөмқҙ м•„лӢҲлқј Soulforge MCP л’Өмқҳ м„ нғқм Ғ client adapterлӢӨ.
ERP/TaskEngineмқҙ мҶҢмң н•ҳлҠ” м§„мӢӨмқҖ **кіөмӢқ task identity, assignment epoch, м—…л¬ҙ мғҒнғң, apply receipt,
official completion**мңјлЎң н•ңм •н•ңлӢӨ. Source fact, payload/ArtifactRevision, accepted history/context,
Wiki/RAG knowledgeмҷҖ mission/workflow/partyлҠ” кё°мЎҙ ownerлҘј мң м§Җн•ҳл©° MCP мһҗмІҙлҸ„ мқҙ м§„мӢӨмқ„ мҶҢмң н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

| logical client role | нӣ„ліҙ кө¬нҳ„ | н—Ҳмҡ© мұ…мһ„ | client-localлЎңл§Ң лӮЁкёё мғҒнғң | кёҲм§Җ |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `TeamAgentGatewayAdapter` | Hermesнҳ• persistent agent shell | мӮ¬лһҢ/Slack л“ұ channel session, Soulforge MCPмқҳ мөңмҶҢ allowlist query, м•ҢлҰјВ·handoffВ·candidate м ңм¶ң | transcript, preference memory, local goal/Kanban/delegation мғҒнғң | ERP task/current/done, accepted knowledge, `.mission/.workflow/.party` mutation |
| `EngineeringWorkbenchAdapter` | Orcaнҳ• multi-agent engineering workbench | н•ң approved WorkSession м•Ҳм—җм„ң bounded subtask л¶„л°°, кІ©лҰ¬ worktree, diffВ·artifactВ·validator candidate мҲҳм§‘ | native task/dispatch/decision gate/worker-finished/branch/PR мғҒнғң | official completion, direct main/push/PR, live ERP/DB/RAG write, лӢӨлҘё agent shell мӢӨн–ү |
| direct worker client | Codex/мҠ№мқёлҗң MCP client | мһ‘мқҖ м—…л¬ҙмқҳ м§Ғм ‘ queryвҶ’workвҶ’checkpoint/proposal | local thread/tool state | TaskEngine coordinator мӮ¬м№ӯ, raw transcript мһҗлҸҷ мҲҳм§‘ |

л‘җ adapterлҠ” sibling MCP clientлӢӨ. Hermesнҳ• gatewayк°Җ Orcaнҳ• workbenchлҘј мӢӨн–үн•ҳкұ°лӮҳ к·ё л°ҳлҢҖк°Җ лҗҳлҠ”
parent/child orchestration chainмқҖ кёҲм§Җн•ңлӢӨ. к°ҷмқҖ `{assignment epoch,account}` WorkSessionм—җлҠ” write-capable
surface coordinator н•ҳлӮҳл§Ң мЎҙмһ¬н•ҳл©° child agentлҠ” MCP checkpointВ·completion proposalмқ„ м§Ғм ‘ м“°м§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
SurfaceлҘј л°”кҫёл Өл©ҙ old delegationмқ„ revokeн•ҳкі  terminal handoffмҷҖ superseding bindingмқ„ лЁјм Җ кё°лЎқн•ңлӢӨ.

Text/codeлҠ” isolated worktree candidateлЎң лі‘л ¬нҷ”н•  мҲҳ мһҲлӢӨ. Allegro/OrCAD, HWPX, Excel, PowerPoint,
CAD л“ұ mergeк°Җ м•Ҳм „н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҖ binary engineering artifactлҠ” м—¬лҹ¬ agentк°Җ read/reviewн•  мҲҳ мһҲм–ҙлҸ„ мӢӨм ң
artifact revision writerлҠ” н•ҳлӮҳлҝҗмқҙлӢӨ. Drag/drop/chat attachmentлҠ” project acceptanceк°Җ м•„лӢҲл©° В§3.5мқҳ
authenticated HTTPS custodyвҶ’promotionвҶ’exact ArtifactRevision кІҪкі„лҘј к·ёлҢҖлЎң л”°лҘёлӢӨ.

## 6. codeВ·DBВ·APIВ·IDВ·event мғҒм„ё м„Өкі„

### 6.1 мҪ”л“ң deltaмҷҖ caller/consumer

| нҢҢмқј/module | symbol лҳҗлҠ” мұ…мһ„ | caller | consumer | кі„нҡҚ |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `guild_hall/shared/temporal_identity.mjs` | `validateTypedRef`, canonical serialization, Source/Revision/RAG ID builder, collision guard | source/RAG/task adapters | ledger validators | candidate кө¬нҳ„мқ„ C01A/P2м—җм„ң мһ¬кІҖнҶ н•ҙ `BUILD`; кё°мЎҙ owner IDлҠ” `preserveOwnerIssuedIdentity`лЎң мң м§Җ |
| `guild_hall/shared/temporal_relation.mjs`, proposed `temporal_owner_adapter.mjs` | relation validatorмҷҖ кё°мЎҙ source-revision/knowledge-binding owner adapter; generic ledger writer кёҲм§Җ | C06A/C09L | B9/RAG/ERP typed refs | C06A synthetic validator/adapter, C09LмқҖ м •ліё кІҪлЎңмқҳ approved private materializationл§Ң |
| `ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/src/task_driver.mjs` | `build/validateTaskIntent`, `build/validateTaskDriver`, policy/revocation, event, replay, follow-up candidate | intake adapters, API | persistence, tests, projections | candidateмқҳ pure coreлҘј мөңмӢ  mainм—җ bounded мһ¬кө¬нҳ„ |
| `ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/src/task_driver_persistence.mjs` | install, immutable insert, replay, `applyTaskDriverDecisionSet` | serverмқҳ мң мқј apply route | dev-ERP DB | C02м—җм„ң synthetic DB м „мҡ©мңјлЎң лЁјм Җ кө¬м¶•; allocator/reservationкіј typed task eventлҘј ліҙк°• |
| `ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/src/task_engine_runtime_binding.mjs`, `tools/task_engine_runtime_binding.mjs` | local binding fail-closed loaderмҷҖ compare-and-swap atomic writer | server/coordinator/runtime audit | local operator | C08F/P8м—җм„ң public schemaВ·synthetic/feature-OFF foundation кө¬м¶•; C09D/C10/G00/G01мқҖ к°ҷмқҖ loader/writerл§Ң мӮ¬мҡ© |
| `ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/src/store.mjs` | `createItem`, `setItemStatus`, `appendEvent`, completion/reopen | server, schedule, intake, autosync | ERP UI, ledger | C03м—җм„ң лӮҙл¶Җ projection adapterлЎң м ңн•ң; reopen `DELETE`лҘј reversal appendлЎң көҗмІҙ |
| `ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/server.mjs` | auth, task routes, life-tree routes | HTTP client/ERP UI | store/Driver service | C03м—җм„ң Driver APIмҷҖ projection GETмқ„ л¶„лҰ¬; м§Ғм ‘ mutation routeлҠ” compatibility adapterлЎң кі„мёЎ |
| `ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/tools/auto_intake_cycle.mjs` | мһҗлҸҷ intake orchestration | bounded CLI/scheduler | mail task flow | C04A/P6м—җм„ң candidate-only нҳём¶ң; auto-open м ңкұ°к°Җ м•„лӢҲлқј policy-gated compatibilityлЎң м „нҷҳ |
| `ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/tools/mail_to_task_ledger.mjs` | mail candidate ledger | mail intake | task flow | C04A/P6м—җм„ң typed source revisionкіј Driver receipt м—°кІ° |
| `ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/tools/voice_to_task_candidates.mjs` | voice accepted-route candidate | voice delivery receipt | task flow | C04A/P6м—җм„ң TaskIntent adapter м¶”к°Җ; raw audio/transcript л№„мЎ°нҡҢ мң м§Җ |
| `guild_hall/file_activity/file_activity.mjs` | file five-ID/revision/reconciler | node packet | file ledger | кё°мЎҙ core `REUSE`; C04A/C04B/C07Bм—җм„ң source/task relationВ·immutable transportл§Ң м¶”к°Җ |
| `guild_hall/rag/project_rag_paths.mjs` | owner-aware resolver/containment/collision | all RAG writers/readers | project/common RAG | C05м—җм„ң candidate кө¬нҳ„мқ„ мһ¬кІҖнҶ н•ҙ кө¬м¶• |
| `guild_hall/rag/source_text_index.mjs` л“ұ кё°мЎҙ RAG consumer | нҳ„мһ¬ common кё°ліё кІҪлЎң | RAG CLI/automation/UI | index/work card/answer | C05м—җм„ң resolverлҘј мЈјмһ…; legacy defaultлҠ” compatibility readл§Ң мң м§Җ |
| `ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/src/context_graph.mjs` | B9 projection | DB/relation adapters | B9 UI | C07B/P9м—җм„ң task event/relation adapter м¶”к°Җ; write API кёҲм§Җ |
| `ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/src/context_life_tree.mjs` | ENGINE-12 мқјмқј projection | mail/ERP/SE/voice/Codex/file adapters | life-tree UI/API | C07A/P5м—җм„ң cutoff acceptanceлҘј кі м •н•ҳкі  C07B/P9м—җм„ң Driver/task event adapter м¶”к°Җ |
| `ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/src/file_activity_life_tree_projection.mjs` | fileвҶ’life-tree strict projection | file ledger | ENGINE-12 | exact ID logic `REUSE`, typed relationл§Ң `MODIFY` |
| `ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/src/autosync.mjs`, `tools/task_ledger.mjs` | мҷёл¶Җ мһҘл¶Җ нҳёнҷҳ | store hook/CLI | legacy ledger reader | C03м—җм„ң one-way projectionмңјлЎң м ңн•ңн•ҳкі  conflict report м¶”к°Җ |
| `ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/src/erp_mcp_service.mjs`, `ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp-mcp/src/tools.mjs` | CURRENT one-shot WorkSession, account-scoped query/upload; TARGET personal lifecycle/query facade | personal MCP | dev-ERP service | current 8 toolsлҠ” `REUSE`; AX01/Q8м—җм„ң start/bind/checkpoint/closeout/proposal receiptмҷҖ accepted queryлҘј feature-OFF `MODIFY`. current recordлҘј lifecycle eventлЎң мҶҢкёү мһ¬н•ҙм„қ кёҲм§Җ |
| `ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp-mcp/ingress_server.mjs`, `src/ingress_*`, `schema/ingress_*` | feature-OFF HPP evidence ingress source foundation; file/structured-PC-work/run receiptл§Ң existing local outboxлЎң м „лӢ¬ | enrolled client нӣ„ліҙ | HPP ingress receiver нӣ„ліҙ; ERP/promoter/history/TaskEngine owner м•„лӢҳ | public synthetic + multi-process loopback E2EлҠ” `BUILD`; private binding кё°ліё OFF. D27~D29 acceptance, malware scan/quota/TLS/mTLS, one-seat A8-CANARYмҷҖ team rolloutмқҖ кі„мҶҚ `VERIFY_HP/HOLD` |
| proposed `guild_hall/ingress/*` contract/helper (exact path D27) | storage binding, promotion decision/receipt validator; payload transportмҷҖ projector кёҲм§Җ | source-specific approved adapter | project/artifact/knowledge owner нӣ„ліҙ | P2/P3 pure lineage нӣ„ P8 feature-OFF contractл§Ң `BUILD`; exact pathВ·roleмқҖ owner packet м „ мғқм„ұ кёҲм§Җ |
| proposed dev-ERP accepted-generation query adapter (exact path D29) | project history/context/knowledge resultмқҳ scopeВ·ACLВ·generationВ·revisionВ·claim ceiling | ERP UI/personal MCP | read models | Q4 schema л’Ө Q8 feature-OFF `BUILD`; implicit fallbackВ·snapshot reverse importВ·read-side owner mutation кёҲм§Җ |
| `ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/tools/task_engine_inventory.mjs` | five-lane query-only inventoryмҷҖ deterministic manifest | C00B/C09 operator | P0 receipt/review/pilot | public/synthetic formal C00Q receiptлҠ” retained evidenceлӢӨ. н•ҙлӢ№ execution approvalмқҖ л§ҢлЈҢлҗҗкі  live/private bindingкіј C00B strict PASSлҠ” `HOLD` |
| `ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/tools/a8_synth_secure_access.mjs` | 60-ID public/pathless/feature-OFF secure-access verifierмҷҖ deterministic receipt | A8-SYNTH review | D27~D29 security contract review | source foundationкіј strict schema/focused adversarial testлҠ” мЎҙмһ¬н•ңлӢӨ. public synthetic fixtureмқҳ PASSлҠ” owner acceptanceВ·`VERIFY_HP`В·A8-CANARYВ·P0~P10В·team/productionмқ„ unlockн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ |
| `ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/tools/task_engine_migration_dry_run.mjs`, `task_engine_schema_migration.mjs` | deterministic migration manifest, gated schema apply | C09/C09R/C10 operator | review/restore/pilot | C09Aм—җм„ң synthetic-onlyлЎң кө¬м¶•; м„ё prerequisite м—ҶлҠ” live applyлҠ” fail-closed |

лҚ” лӢЁмҲңн•ң лҢҖм•Ҳмқё вҖңк°Ғ intakeк°Җ `createItem()`мқ„ кі„мҶҚ нҳём¶ңн•ҳлҗҳ eventл§Ң лҚ” лӮЁкё°лҠ” л°©мӢқвҖқмқҖ мұ„нғқн•ҳм§Җ
м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. authorityВ·idempotencyВ·reservationВ·replayлҘј callerл§ҲлӢӨ мӨ‘ліө кө¬нҳ„н•ҳкІҢ лҗҳкі , direct writerк°Җ
м—¬лҹ¬ к°ң лӮЁкё° л•Ңл¬ёмқҙлӢӨ. л°ҳлҢҖлЎң мІҳмқҢл¶Җн„° AX WorkspaceмҷҖ AgentRunк№Ңм§Җ н•ң serviceлЎң н•©м№ҳлҠ” кІғлҸ„
мұ„нғқн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. core safetyлҘј л¶Ҳн•„мҡ”н•ҳкІҢ лҠҰм¶ҳлӢӨ.

### 6.2 DB лӘ©н‘ң schema

мғҲ tableмқҖ кё°мЎҙ `meta.schema_version` мІҙкі„мҷҖ лі„лҸ„ key
`task_driver_persistence_schema_version=soulforge.task_driver_persistence.v1`лЎң м¶”м Ғн•ңлӢӨ. C02м—җм„ңлҠ”
temporary synthetic DBм—җл§Ң м„Өм№ҳн•ңлӢӨ. Live м„Өм№ҳлҠ” accepted C00Q inventory guard, C09A migration лҸ„кө¬ кІҖмҰқ, C09 inventory, C09R valid
restore receiptлҘј лӘЁл‘җ нҶөкіјн•ң л’Ө C10м—җм„ң лі„лҸ„лЎң мҠ№мқён•ҙм•ј н•ңлӢӨ.

м•„лһҳ `valid_at`/`known_at` columnмқҖ owner-ratified clock crosswalk м „к№Ңм§Җ provisional normalized
query-cutoff fieldлӢӨ. Persisted source eventмқҳ owner-native мӮ¬мӢӨ мӢңкі„
(`occurred_at`/`effective_from|to`/`project_applied_at`)мҷҖ мқём§Җ мӢңкі„
(`recorded_at`/`ingested_at`)лҘј payloadмқҳ exact ref/fieldм—җм„ң ліҙмЎҙн•ҳкі , cutoffлЎң losslessн•ҳкІҢ
мҷ•ліөлҗЁмқ„ P2 fixtureк°Җ мҰқлӘ…н•ҙм•ј н•ңлӢӨ. Source-native clockмқ„ cutoffлЎң лҚ®м–ҙм“°кұ°лӮҳ н•ҳлӮҳлЎң collapseн•ҳл©ҙ
C02/P8 schema кө¬нҳ„мқ„ мӢңмһ‘н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

| table | literal column/type | constraint | м„ұкІ© |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `task_driver_candidate` | `candidate_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY`, `project_id TEXT NOT NULL`, `candidate_digest TEXT NOT NULL`, `payload_json TEXT NOT NULL` | `project_id REFERENCES core_project(id)`, `UNIQUE(candidate_digest)` | immutable candidate |
