| `task_identity` | `task_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY`, `project_id TEXT NOT NULL`, `created_at TEXT NOT NULL`, `identity_digest TEXT NOT NULL`, `payload_json TEXT NOT NULL` | project FK, `UNIQUE(task_id,project_id)`, `UNIQUE(identity_digest)` | current rowмҷҖ л¶„лҰ¬лҗң immutable task ID owner |
| `task_driver_intent` | `intent_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY`, `project_id TEXT NOT NULL`, `intent_kind TEXT NOT NULL`, `valid_at TEXT NOT NULL`, `known_at TEXT NOT NULL`, `intent_digest TEXT NOT NULL`, `payload_json TEXT NOT NULL` | project FK, `UNIQUE(intent_digest)` | immutable intent; л‘җ мӢңк°„мқҖ query cutoffмқҙкі  native clock refлҠ” payloadм—җ ліҙмЎҙ |
| `task_driver_record` | `driver_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY`, `project_id TEXT NOT NULL`, `target_intent_id TEXT NOT NULL`, `idempotency_key TEXT NOT NULL`, `driver_digest TEXT NOT NULL`, `payload_json TEXT NOT NULL` | project/intent FK, `UNIQUE(idempotency_key)`, `UNIQUE(driver_digest)` | immutable Driver |
| `task_driver_policy` | `policy_ref_key TEXT PRIMARY KEY`, `project_id TEXT NOT NULL`, `policy_digest TEXT NOT NULL`, `valid_from TEXT NOT NULL`, `valid_to TEXT`, `payload_json TEXT NOT NULL` | project FK, `UNIQUE(policy_digest)` | immutable policy revision |
| `task_driver_policy_revocation` | `revocation_ref_key TEXT PRIMARY KEY`, `policy_ref_key TEXT NOT NULL`, `revoked_at TEXT NOT NULL`, `known_at TEXT NOT NULL`, `revocation_digest TEXT NOT NULL`, `payload_json TEXT NOT NULL` | policy FK, `UNIQUE(revocation_digest)` | immutable revocation |
| `task_driver_event` | `event_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY`, `project_id TEXT NOT NULL`, `driver_id TEXT NOT NULL`, `event_sequence INTEGER NOT NULL`, `idempotency_key TEXT NOT NULL`, `event_kind TEXT NOT NULL`, `recorded_at TEXT NOT NULL`, `valid_at TEXT NOT NULL`, `event_digest TEXT NOT NULL`, `payload_json TEXT NOT NULL` | project/driver FK, `UNIQUE(idempotency_key)`, `UNIQUE(event_digest)`, `UNIQUE(project_id,event_sequence)` | append-only нҢҗлӢЁ/м Ғмҡ© event; `valid_at`мқҖ provisional cutoffмқҙкі  native fact/knowledge clocksлҘј lossless ліҙмЎҙ |
| `task_driver_authority_attestation` | `event_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY`, `evidence_digest TEXT NOT NULL`, `payload_json TEXT NOT NULL` | event FK, `UNIQUE(evidence_digest)` | immutable authority мҰқлӘ… нҸ¬мқён„° |
| `task_driver_writer_attestation` | `evidence_digest TEXT PRIMARY KEY`, `project_id TEXT NOT NULL`, `driver_id TEXT NOT NULL`, `writer_role TEXT NOT NULL`, `valid_at TEXT NOT NULL`, `payload_json TEXT NOT NULL` | project/driver FK | immutable writer binding мҰқлӘ… |
| `task_id_reservation` | `reservation_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY`, `project_id TEXT NOT NULL`, `driver_id TEXT NOT NULL`, `idempotency_key TEXT NOT NULL`, `task_id TEXT NOT NULL`, `allocated_at TEXT NOT NULL`, `finalized_event_id TEXT NOT NULL`, `payload_json TEXT NOT NULL` | project/driver/final Driver event FK, composite `(task_id,project_id)`вҶ’task_identity, `UNIQUE(driver_id,idempotency_key)`, `UNIQUE(task_id)` | apply transaction м•Ҳм—җм„ң л°ңкёүВ·finalizeлҗҳлҠ” immutable reservation |
| `task_driver_task_baseline` | `task_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY`, `project_id TEXT NOT NULL`, `task_revision_ref_json TEXT`, `work_status TEXT NOT NULL`, `baseline_digest TEXT NOT NULL`, `payload_json TEXT NOT NULL` | composite `(task_id,project_id)`вҶ’task_identity, `UNIQUE(baseline_digest)` | immutable legacy crosswalk baseline |
| `task_event` | `task_event_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY`, `task_id TEXT NOT NULL`, `project_id TEXT NOT NULL`, `event_kind TEXT NOT NULL`, `from_status TEXT`, `to_status TEXT`, `valid_at TEXT NOT NULL`, `known_at TEXT NOT NULL`, `driver_event_id TEXT`, `reverses_task_event_id TEXT`, `event_digest TEXT NOT NULL`, `payload_json TEXT NOT NULL` | composite `(task_id,project_id)`вҶ’task_identity, optional Driver event/self-reversal FK, `UNIQUE(event_digest)` | кіөмӢқ append-only м—…л¬ҙ event; cutoffмҷҖ owner-native clocksмқҳ ratified lossless crosswalk м „ schema кі м • кёҲм§Җ |
| `task_application_receipt` | `driver_event_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY`, `project_id TEXT NOT NULL`, `task_id TEXT NOT NULL`, `task_event_id TEXT NOT NULL`, `before_work_status TEXT`, `after_work_status TEXT`, `receipt_digest TEXT NOT NULL`, `payload_json TEXT NOT NULL` | Driver event/task event FK, composite `(task_id,project_id)`вҶ’task_identity, `UNIQUE(task_event_id)`, `UNIQUE(receipt_digest)` | immutable atomic apply кІ°кіј; creation reversalмқҖ after status null н—Ҳмҡ© |

P8 mail schemaлҠ” task tableкіј к°ҷмқҖ writer к¶Ңн•ңмқ„ кіөмң н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. к°ҷмқҖ л¬јлҰ¬ HPPм—җ мһҲм–ҙлҸ„
`mail_classification_coordinator`мҷҖ `project_history_projector`лҠ” лі„лҸ„ logical identityлӢӨ. к¶ҢмһҘ tableмқҖ
лӢӨмқҢкіј к°ҷмңјл©° D22 schema-v2/cutover кІ°м • м „м—җлҠ” synthetic DBм—җл§Ң м„Өм№ҳн•ңлӢӨ.

| mail table (`TARGET`) | н•өмӢ¬ column/constraint | writer/transaction role |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `mail_occurrence_identity` | `mail_occurrence_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY`, `source_owner_ref_json TEXT NOT NULL`, `native_occurrence_digest TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE`, `first_known_at TEXT NOT NULL`, `metadata_digest TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE` | projectмҷҖ лҸ…лҰҪлҗң immutable identity; source payload м ҖмһҘ кёҲм§Җ; UPDATE/DELETE reject |
| `mail_project_assignment_current` | `mail_occurrence_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY REFERENCES mail_occurrence_identity`, `project_code TEXT`, `assignment_revision INTEGER NOT NULL CHECK(assignment_revision>=1)`, `last_event_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES mail_project_assignment_event(event_id) DEFERRABLE INITIALLY DEFERRED`, `operation_id TEXT NOT NULL`, `generation_id TEXT NOT NULL`, `classification_epoch INTEGER NOT NULL CHECK(classification_epoch>=1)`, `updated_at TEXT NOT NULL` | classification coordinatorл§Ң expected revision+active classification epoch CASлЎң л°”кҫёлҠ” materialized current |
| `mail_project_assignment_event` | `event_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY`, `mail_occurrence_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES mail_occurrence_identity`, `event_kind TEXT NOT NULL CHECK(event_kind IN ('classified','reclassified_out','reclassified_in','unclassified'))`, `from_project_code TEXT`, `to_project_code TEXT`, `operation_id TEXT NOT NULL`, `generation_id TEXT NOT NULL`, `classification_epoch INTEGER NOT NULL CHECK(classification_epoch>=1)`, `valid_at TEXT NOT NULL`, `known_at TEXT NOT NULL`, `recorded_at TEXT NOT NULL`, `metadata_digest TEXT NOT NULL UNIQUE` | append-only assignment/reclassification history; UPDATE/DELETE trigger reject |
| `mail_projection_outbox` | `outbox_id TEXT PRIMARY KEY`, `event_id TEXT NOT NULL REFERENCES mail_project_assignment_event(event_id)`, `project_code TEXT NOT NULL`, `projection_kind TEXT NOT NULL CHECK(projection_kind IN ('csv','ics','xlsx'))`, `generation_id TEXT NOT NULL`, `classification_epoch INTEGER NOT NULL CHECK(classification_epoch>=1)`, `status TEXT NOT NULL CHECK(status IN ('pending','claimed','published','failed'))`, `claimed_by TEXT`, `claimed_projector_epoch INTEGER`, `published_projector_epoch INTEGER`, `attempt_count INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0 CHECK(attempt_count>=0)`, `published_manifest_digest TEXT`, `committed_at TEXT NOT NULL`, `UNIQUE(event_id,project_code,projection_kind,generation_id)` | current+eventмҷҖ к°ҷмқҖ DB transactionм—җм„ң origin classification epochлЎң enqueue; projectorл§Ң active projector epoch CASлЎң claim/publish |

н•ң л¶„лҘҳ operationмқҖ `BEGIN IMMEDIATE` м•Ҳм—җм„ң occurrence identity нҷ•мқё, current revision CAS,
append-only assignment event, н•ҙлӢ№ project projection outboxлҘј н•Ёк»ҳ commitн•ңлӢӨ. AвҶ’B мһ¬л¶„лҘҳлҠ” к°ҷмқҖ
`operation_id`, `generation_id`, `classification_epoch`лЎң Aмқҳ `reclassified_out`кіј Bмқҳ `reclassified_in`мқ„
appendн•ҳкі  A historyлҘј мӮӯм ңн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. Currentмқҳ `last_event_id`лҠ” Bмқҳ `reclassified_in`мқ„ к°ҖлҰ¬нӮӨл©°,
unclassified м „нҷҳмқҙл©ҙ `unclassified` eventлҘј к°ҖлҰ¬нӮЁлӢӨ. `reclassified_out`мқҖ current лҢҖн‘ң eventк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ.
Deferred FKлҘј commit м „м—җ кІҖмӮ¬н•ҙ current/event/outbox мӣҗмһҗм„ұмқ„ schemaм—җм„ңлҸ„ к°•м ңн•ңлӢӨ. File publishлҠ” DB transaction л°–мқҙлҜҖлЎң staged manifestмҷҖ
atomic replaceлҘј м“°лҗҳ outbox generationмқҙ logical exactly-once кІҪкі„лӢӨ.

Literal indexлҠ” лӢӨмқҢ м—¬м„Ҝ к°ңлҘј мөңмҶҢк°’мңјлЎң л‘”лӢӨ.

```sql
CREATE INDEX idx_task_identity_project
  ON task_identity(project_id, task_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_task_driver_intent_project_known
  ON task_driver_intent(project_id, known_at, intent_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_task_driver_record_project_driver
  ON task_driver_record(project_id, driver_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_task_driver_event_project_sequence
  ON task_driver_event(project_id, event_sequence);
CREATE INDEX idx_task_event_task_known
  ON task_event(task_id, known_at, task_event_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_task_event_project_valid
  ON task_event(project_id, valid_at, task_event_id);
```

Mail v2мқҳ мөңмҶҢ indexмҷҖ mutation guardлҠ” лі„лҸ„лӢӨ.

```sql
CREATE INDEX idx_mail_assignment_event_occurrence_known
  ON mail_project_assignment_event(mail_occurrence_id, known_at, event_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_mail_assignment_event_generation
  ON mail_project_assignment_event(generation_id, operation_id, event_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_mail_projection_outbox_claim
  ON mail_projection_outbox(status, committed_at, outbox_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_mail_projection_outbox_generation
  ON mail_projection_outbox(generation_id, project_code, projection_kind, outbox_id);
```

`mail_occurrence_identity`мҷҖ `mail_project_assignment_event`лҠ” UPDATE/DELETEлҘј н•ӯмғҒ кұ°л¶Җн•ңлӢӨ.
`mail_project_assignment_current`лҠ” coordinatorмқҳ к°ҷмқҖ `BEGIN IMMEDIATE` transactionм—җм„ң expected
`assignment_revision`кіј active `classification_epoch`к°Җ лӘЁл‘җ л§һмқ„ л•Ңл§Ң CASн•ңлӢӨ. Outboxмқҳ identity/event/project/
generation/classification-epoch/kind columnмқҖ immutableмқҙкі , projectorлҠ” active `projector_epoch`лҘј
`claimed_projector_epoch`мҷҖ `published_projector_epoch`м—җ кё°лЎқн•ҳл©ҙм„ң `pendingвҶ’claimedвҶ’published|failed`
мғҒнғңмҷҖ attempt/manifest fieldл§Ң CASн•ңлӢӨ. Stale classification/projector epoch, missing event FK,
current `last_event_id` FK, generation mismatchлҠ” transaction
м „мІҙлҘј rollbackн•ңлӢӨ.

Append-only UPDATE/DELETE кұ°л¶Җ trigger лҢҖмғҒмқҖ `task_driver_candidate`, `task_identity`, `task_driver_intent`,
`task_driver_record`, `task_driver_policy`, `task_driver_policy_revocation`, `task_driver_event`, л‘җ
attestation table, `task_id_reservation`, `task_driver_task_baseline`, `task_event`,
`task_application_receipt`лӢӨ. `core_item`л§Ң event replayмқҳ mutable current projectionмқҙлӢӨ.
ReservationмқҖ pending rowлҘј UPDATEн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. Apply transaction м•Ҳм—җм„ң task IDлҘј л°ңкёүн•ҳкі 
final Driver eventк№Ңм§Җ н•ң лІҲм—җ кё°лЎқн•ҳл©°, мӢӨнҢЁ мӢң м „мІҙ rollbackн•ңлӢӨ.

`task_event.event_kind`мқҳ мөңмҶҢ allowlistлҠ” `task_created`, `task_creation_reversed`, `status_changed`, `task_reopened`,
`task_reanchored`, `completion_recorded`, `completion_reversed`, `decision_recorded`,
`verification_recorded`, `outcome_recorded`, `task_archived`лӢӨ. Completion/Decision/Verification/OutcomeмқҖ
лі„лҸ„ mutable current tableмқ„ лҠҳлҰ¬кё°ліҙлӢӨ н•ҙлӢ№ immutable event IDлҘј к°Ғк°Ғмқҳ typed entity IDлЎң мӮ¬мҡ©н•ңлӢӨ.
ArtifactлҠ” payloadк°Җ м•„лӢҲлқј external `ArtifactRevision` typed refл§Ң eventм—җ л‘”лӢӨ. мқҙ л°©мӢқмқҙ
completion/outcomeлі„ л‘җ лІҲм§ё history storeлҘј л§Ңл“ңлҠ” кІғліҙлӢӨ лӢЁмҲңн•ҳлӢӨ.

`task_identity`к°Җ immutable task IDмҷҖ event FKлҘј мҶҢмң н•ҳкі  `core_item`мқҖ current projectionл§Ң
мҶҢмң н•ңлӢӨ. л”°лқјм„ң мғҲ task rollbackмқҖ мӣҗ `task_created`лҘј к°ҖлҰ¬нӮӨлҠ” м •нҷ•нһҲ н•ң
`task_creation_reversed.reverses_task_event_id`лҘј appendн•ң л’Ө к°ҷмқҖ transactionм—җм„ң н•ҙлӢ№
`core_item` projection rowлҘј м ңкұ°н•  мҲҳ мһҲлӢӨ. IdentityмҷҖ л‘җ eventлҠ” лӮЁлҠ”лӢӨ. кё°мЎҙ task rollbackмқҖ
reversal event л’Ө baseline current rowлҘј мһ¬кө¬м¶•н•ңлӢӨ. ReplayлҠ” create-reversal мҢҚмқ„ historyм—җлҠ”
ліҙмЎҙн•ҳлҗҳ currentм—җлҠ” лӮҙліҙлӮҙм§Җ м•Ҡмңјл©°, мқҙ к·ңм№ҷмқҖ C01B pure testмҷҖ C02 FK/transaction testм—җм„ң
кі м •н•ңлӢӨ.

Task DB л°–мқҳ source revisionкіј knowledge binding л¬јлҰ¬ ownerлҠ” мғҲ generic ledgerк°Җ м•„лӢҲлқј мқҙлҜё
`TEMPORAL_KNOWLEDGE_ONTOLOGY_V0.md`мҷҖ redesign storage contractк°Җ кі м •н•ң лӢӨмқҢ target shapeлҘј мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ©н•ңлӢӨ.

```text
_workmeta/<project_code>/
в”ңв”Җ knowledge/source_revision_records/<source_revision_id>.yaml
в”ңв”Җ knowledge/source_revision_events/<YYYY-MM>.jsonl
в””в”Җ ontology/knowledge_bindings/events/<YYYY-MM>.jsonl

_workmeta/system/
в”ңв”Җ knowledge/source_revision_records/<source_revision_id>.yaml
в””в”Җ knowledge/source_revision_events/<YYYY-MM>.jsonl
```

| record | кё°мЎҙ/лӘ©н‘ң owner | н•„мҲҳ metadataмҷҖ кІҪкі„ |
| --- | --- | --- |
| SourceRevision | мң„ `knowledge/source_revision_records` | schema, typed source ref, revision ID, digest, valid_at/known_at, pointer, supersedes; body/file м—ҶмқҢ |
| source revision state event | мң„ мӣ”лі„ `knowledge/source_revision_events` | event ID, exact revision ref, state, clocks, supersedes; append-only JSONL |
| knowledge application/binding event | project мӣ”лі„ `ontology/knowledge_bindings/events` | event лҳҗлҠ” binding ID, exact project/task/source/knowledge refs, predicate, clocks, supersedes; fuzzy text м—ҶмқҢ |
| mail/voice/PC/file/run occurrence | В§3.4мқҳ к°Ғ technical source owner | common envelopeлҠ” adapter outputмқҙл©° л‘җ лІҲм§ё occurrence ledgerлҘј л§Ңл“Өм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ |
| NodeObservation | кё°мЎҙ `reports/file_activity/**` | logical file/revision/observation/packet refs; generic temporal pathлЎң ліөмӮ¬н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ |
| ArtifactRevisionмҷҖ non-knowledge relation | `UNKNOWN/D06` | кё°мЎҙ ownerк°Җ нҷ•мқёлҗҳкё° м „ materialize кёҲм§Җ; dev-ERPмҷҖ projectionмқҖ typed refл§Ң ліҙмң  |
| ProjectionReceipt | H06/P9мқҳ owner-approved report/run evidence path | input cutoff/digest, output digest, gap, writer attestation; лі„лҸ„ truthк°Җ м•„лӢҳ |

SourceRevisionмқҖ revisionлі„ immutable file, source мғҒнғңмҷҖ knowledge applicationмқҖ мӣ”лі„ append-only eventлӢӨ.
Occurrence/file/run historyлҠ” кё°мЎҙ source-local ownerлҘј мң м§Җн•ңлӢӨ. C06A adapterлҠ” мқҙ ownerлі„ partitionмқ„
кІҖмҰқн•ҳкі  exact typed refл§Ң лӮҙліҙлӮҙл©°, лӘЁл“  recordлҘј н•ң `_workmeta/**/ledgers/temporal` treeлЎң ліөмӮ¬н•ҳм§Җ
м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. Knowledge мҷё relationмқҳ physical ownerк°Җ н•„мҡ”н•ҳл©ҙ D06м—җм„ң кё°мЎҙ кі„м•Ҫкіј crosswalk/migrationмқ„
лЁјм Җ мҠ№мқён•ҙм•ј н•ҳл©°, owner кІ°м • м „м—җлҠ” synthetic validatorл§Ң н—Ҳмҡ©н•ңлӢӨ.

#### 6.2A IngressВ·personal WorkSessionВ·accepted query logical records (`TARGET` only)

м•„лһҳлҠ” мҠ№мқёлҗң DDL/table/pathк°Җ м•„лӢҲлқј D27~D29к°Җ exact ownerлҘј м •н•  л•Ң мӮ¬мҡ©н•  мөңмҶҢ logical shapeлӢӨ.
нҳ„мһ¬ `erp_mcp_work_session`мқҖ one-shot compatibility facadeлЎң лӮЁкё°л©° accepted start, ordered closeout,
missing-closeout лҳҗлҠ” completion proposalлЎң мҶҢкёү н•ҙм„қн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

| logical record | мөңмҶҢ field | мң мқј writerмҷҖ кёҲм§Җ |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `TaskAssignmentRef` | task/project/account, `assignment_epoch`, task revision, assignment event ref | ERP assignment owner; personal coordinatorк°Җ л°ңкёүВ·мҲҳм • кёҲм§Җ |
| `ActorDelegationGrant` | user/device/agent/opaque-thread/task/project/artifact/revision/action, parent refs, issued/expiry/revoked refs | auth broker; human grantвҲ©trusted deviceвҲ©agent policyвҲ©object/action, earliest expiryмҷҖ cascading revoke к°•м ң |
| `PersonalWorkSession` | session ID, assignment ref, actor account, producer node, start key/time/digest, nullable supersedes session | personal session coordinator; `{assignment epoch,account}` active primary н•ҳлӮҳ кё°ліё |
| `PersonalThreadBinding` | binding ID, session ID, thread namespace, **opaque thread-ref digest**, bound time, supersedes binding, binding digest | raw Codex thread ID м ҖмһҘВ·мқ‘лӢө кёҲм§Җ; handoff overwrite кёҲм§Җ |
| `WorkSessionEvent` | event/session ID, global sequence, kind, previous/event digest, idempotency key, occurred/received clocks, bounded summary/output/verification/next/stop/artifact refs, nullable closeout kind | н•ң actor+node chain; task current/eventВ·Wiki/RAG write кёҲм§Җ |
| `IngestReceipt` | receipt/session/event, `accepted|duplicate|held_gap|quarantined|rejected`, next expected sequence, received time, digest, conflict/quarantine ref | reconciler; same seq/same digest no-op, same seq/different digest quarantine, gap projection 0 |
| `CompletionProposalLink` | proposal/task/session/closeout refs, expected task revision, digest, `pending`, Driver candidate ref, created time | proposal writer; кіөмӢқ task мҷ„лЈҢмҷҖ knowledge promotion кёҲм§Җ |
| `StorageBindingPromotionReceipt` | promotion/operation ID, occurrence/revision/content/from/to binding/project refs, `reference|copy|move|derive`, authority/actor/writer, scan/retention/ACL refs, clocks, input/output digests, status, rollback/supersession ref | ingress promoter only; payload body/pathлҠ” receiptм—җ м—ҶмқҢ |
| `BinaryTransferTicket` | opaque ticket, full actor/delegation chain, task/project/artifact/revision/action/method/audience, hash/size/media/expiry/revoke refs | HPP ticket verifier; URL-only authorityВ·client destination pathВ·cross-ticket field swap кёҲм§Җ |
| `ArtifactRevision` | artifact/revision ID, immutable content hash/size/media, source/derived lineage, policy label, accepted receipt | exact revision owner; redacted derivativeлҠ” immutable new revisionмқҙкі  raw fallback кёҲм§Җ |
| `AcceptedGenerationManifest` | scope/project, lane or query kind, generation/cutoff/coverage/gaps, source revision set digest, API/CSV/XLSX result digests, accepted pointer revision | accepted-generation coordinator; unaccepted generationмқ„ currentлЎң л…ём¶ң кёҲм§Җ |

Client-local outbox envelopeлҠ” session/node/sequence/previous digest/payload digest/idempotency keyмҷҖ
verified server receipt ID/digest/statusлҘј к°Җм§„лӢӨ. ServerлҠ” local `pending_outbox`лҘј м¶”м •н•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡмңјл©°,
clientлҠ” durable ack кІҖмҰқ м „ compactн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. exact local writer/path, fsync л°©мӢқ, м•”нҳёнҷ”, retentionмқҖ
D28 `VERIFY_HP`мқҙкі  мқҙ л¬ём„ңм—җм„ң мғқм„ұн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

Candidate branchмқҳ `task_driver_apply_receipt` лӘ…м№ӯмқҖ C02 м„Өкі„ лҰ¬л·°м—җм„ң
`task_application_receipt`лЎң м •к·ңнҷ”н• м§Җ ownerк°Җ кІ°м •н•ңлӢӨ. кё°мЎҙ `event_log`лҠ” л°”лЎң мӮӯм ңн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
`task_event`лҘј кіөмӢқ typed мӣҗмһҘмңјлЎң м“°кі , нҳёнҷҳ кё°к°„ лҸҷм•Ҳ к°ҷмқҖ transactionм—җм„ң `event_log`м—җ н•ң лІҲ
mirrorн•ңлӢӨ. лӘЁл“  consumer м „нҷҳкіј replay parity л’Өм—җл§Ң mirror м ңкұ°лҘј кІҖнҶ н•ңлӢӨ.

Append-only tableм—җлҠ” UPDATE/DELETE кұ°л¶Җ triggerлҘј л‘”лӢӨ. лӢЁ, trigger DDLмқҖ synthetic DBм—җм„ң
up/down migrationкіј restoreлҘј нҶөкіјн•ң л’Өм—җл§Ң live нӣ„ліҙк°Җ лҗңлӢӨ. migration лҸ„кө¬мқҳ downмқҖ tableмқ„
мҰүмӢң dropн•ҳлҠ” л°©мӢқмқҙ м•„лӢҲлқј target writer OFFвҶ’readback export digestвҶ’synthetic restoreк№Ңм§ҖлҘј
кІҖмҰқн•ңлӢӨ. Live commit л’Ө rollbackмқҖ В§13.2мқҳ reversal event+current rebuildлҘј мӮ¬мҡ©н•ҳл©°,
pre-migration DB restoreлҠ” TaskEngine eventк°Җ м•„м§Ғ 0мқё л°°нҸ¬ мӢӨнҢЁ лҳҗлҠ” лі„лҸ„ event
export/re-import кІҖмҰқмқ„ л§Ҳм№ң мһ¬лӮң ліөкө¬м—җл§Ң мӮ¬мҡ©н•ңлӢӨ.

### лҸ„мӢқ 5 вҖ” DB current rowмҷҖ append-only event

```mermaid
flowchart LR
  D["TaskDriverEvent<br/>нҢҗлӢЁ/authority мӣҗмһҘ"] --> T["BEGIN IMMEDIATE<br/>лӢЁмқј transaction"]
  R["task_id_reservation"] --> T
  T --> E["task_event<br/>append-only кіөмӢқ м—ӯмӮ¬"]
  T --> C["core_item<br/>нҳ„мһ¬ мғҒнғң projection"]
  T --> P["ApplicationReceipt<br/>apply кІ°кіј"]
  T --> L["event_log<br/>н•ңмӢң compatibility mirror"]
  E --> X["replay"] --> C2["мһ¬кө¬м¶• current"]
  C -. "л№„көҗ" .-> C2
```

Transaction л¶ҲліҖмӢқ:

1. `BEGIN IMMEDIATE` л’Ө project, expected revision, authority, writer attestationмқ„ лӢӨмӢң кІҖмӮ¬н•ңлӢӨ.
2. к°ҷмқҖ Driver/idempotency keyк°Җ мқҙлҜё final receiptлҘј к°Җм§Җл©ҙ к°ҷмқҖ receiptлҘј л°ҳнҷҳн•ҳкі  no-opн•ңлӢӨ.
3. createмқҙл©ҙ ERP allocatorк°Җ IDлҘј м •н•ҳкі  `task_identity`мҷҖ reservationмқ„ л§Ңл“Өкұ°лӮҳ кё°мЎҙ
   identity/reservationмқ„ мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ©н•ңлӢӨ.
4. Driver apply event, task event, `core_item` projection, compatibility event, receiptк°Җ лӘЁл‘җ м„ұкіөн•ҙм•ј commitн•ңлӢӨ.
5. н•ҳлӮҳлқјлҸ„ мӢӨнҢЁн•ҳл©ҙ rollbackн•ҳкі  `409 conflict`, `423 writer_not_primary` лҳҗлҠ” quarantine кІ°кіјл§Ң
   л°ҳнҷҳн•ңлӢӨ. л¶Җл¶„ м Ғмҡ©мқҖ м—ҶлӢӨ.

### 6.3 IDВ·revisionВ·relation graph

кё°мЎҙ owner-issued project/task/source IDлҠ” л°”кҫём§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. мғҲ digestлҠ” лҸҷмқјм„ұ кІҖмҰқкіј event/revision
мӢқлі„м—җ м“°л©°, кё°мЎҙ IDлҘј hash IDлЎң rekeyн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

### лҸ„мӢқ 3 вҖ” IDВ·relationВ·revision graph

```mermaid
flowchart LR
  S["Source<br/>owner ID мң м§Җ"] --> SR["SourceRevision<br/>immutable digest"]
  SR --> O["Occurrence<br/>owner-native fact / knowledge clocks"]
  SR --> RI["RagIndex"] --> RC["RagChunk"]
  SR --> WR["WikiRevision"]
  SR --> TI["TaskIntent"] --> TD["TaskDriver<br/>valid_at / known_at query cutoffs"] --> DE["DriverEvent"]
  DE --> TR["Task ID reservation"] --> ID["TaskIdentity<br/>immutable ID owner"]
  ID --> T["Task/core_item<br/>mutable current projection"]
  ID --> TE["TaskEvent<br/>append-only"] --> CO["Completion"]
  CO --> AR["ArtifactRevision"]
  CO --> VE["Verification"] --> OU["Outcome"]
  O -. "RelationEvent<br/>exact typed ref" .-> T
  TE -. "projection relation" .-> B9["B9/ENGINE-12 node"]
```

Typed ref wire shapeлҠ” лӢӨмқҢмІҳлҹј кі м •н•ңлӢӨ.

```json
{"entity_type":"task","owner_surface":"dev_erp","entity_id":"<owner-issued-id>"}
```

- relation endpointлҠ” bare IDлҘј л°ӣм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
- digest basisлҠ” canonical JSON, NFC text, sorted semantic set, full SHA-256лҘј мӮ¬мҡ©н•ңлӢӨ.
- м§§мқҖ н‘ңмӢң IDк°Җ м¶©лҸҢн•ҳкұ°лӮҳ к°ҷмқҖ aliasк°Җ м—¬лҹ¬ full digestлҘј к°ҖлҰ¬нӮӨл©ҙ writeн•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡкі  quarantineн•ңлӢӨ.
- `valid_at`/`known_at`мқҖ point-in-time query cutoffлӢӨ. Persisted source eventлҠ” owner-native
  `occurred_at`/`effective_from|to`/`project_applied_at`кіј `recorded_at`/`ingested_at`мқ„ ліҙмЎҙн•ҳкі ,
  normalized cutoff fieldк°Җ н•„мҡ”н•ҳл©ҙ P2 owner-approved crosswalkлЎң losslessн•ҳкІҢ нҢҢмғқн•ңлӢӨ.
- correctionмқҖ кіјкұ° rowлҘј мҲҳм •н•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡкі  supersede/reversal eventлҘј м¶”к°Җн•ңлӢӨ.

### 6.4 л‘җ мғҒнғңм¶•

### лҸ„мӢқ 6 вҖ” нҢҗлӢЁ/м Ғмҡ© мғҒнғңмҷҖ work status

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
  state "Driver нҢҗлӢЁ/м Ғмҡ© м¶•" as D {
    [*] --> candidate
    candidate --> review_required
    candidate --> approved: deterministic policy
    review_required --> approved
    review_required --> rejected
    approved --> applied
    candidate --> superseded
    review_required --> superseded
    approved --> superseded: expiry/revocation/correction event
  }
  state "м—…л¬ҙ м§„н–ү м¶•" as W {
    [*] --> not_started
    not_started --> in_progress
    in_progress --> waiting
    waiting --> in_progress
    in_progress --> blocked
    blocked --> in_progress
    in_progress --> done
    done --> not_started: reopen reversal
    not_started --> cancelled
    not_started --> merged
    not_started --> archived
  }
```

`approved`лҠ” мқјмқҙ мҷ„лЈҢлҗҗлӢӨлҠ” лң»мқҙ м•„лӢҲкі , `done`мқҖ мғҲ м ңм•Ҳмқҙ мһҗлҸҷ мҠ№мқёлҗҗлӢӨлҠ” лң»мқҙ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ.
`decision_application_state`лҠ” lifecycle м •ліёмқҳ
`candidate|review_required|approved|applied|rejected|superseded`л§Ң м“ҙлӢӨ. Expiry/revocation/block reasonмқҖ
лі„лҸ„ authority eventмқҙл©° мһ„мқҳ мғҒнғңк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. Work axisлҠ”
`not_started|in_progress|waiting|blocked|done|cancelled|merged|archived`лҘј м“ҙлӢӨ. нҳ„н–ү
`unclassified|open|doing` л“ұмқҖ D03 crosswalk м „к№Ңм§Җ legacy projectionм—җл§Ң мң м§Җн•ңлӢӨ. мғҲ мғҒнғңк°Җ н•„мҡ”н•ҳл©ҙ
C01B м „м—җ protected lifecycle contractмқҳ лі„лҸ„ owner мҠ№мқёкіј same-slice syncк°Җ н•„мҡ”н•ҳлӢӨ.

### 6.5 м ңм•Ҳ APIмҷҖ CLI

лӢӨмқҢмқҖ C03 мқҙнӣ„мқҳ proposed surfaceлӢӨ. routeлҘј л§Ңл“Өкё° м „ C01B/C02/C08F contractк°Җ лЁјм Җ нҶөкіјн•ҙм•ј н•ңлӢӨ.

| method/route лҳҗлҠ” command | golden wire schema ref | request/response | auth/write owner | idempotencyВ·мҳӨлҘҳ |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `POST /api/task-engine/candidates` | `docs/contracts/task_engine_candidate_api.v1.schema.json` | typed source revision + candidate / candidate refВ·digest | logical producer; SQLite writeлҠ” coordinator | duplicate=same result; invalid `400`; boundary `403/422` |
| `POST /api/task-engine/drivers` | `docs/contracts/task_engine_driver_api.v1.schema.json` | intent + Driver / Driver refВ·digest | human/trusted producer attestation; coordinator writes | idempotency UNIQUE; collision `409 quarantine` |
| `POST /api/task-engine/drivers/:id/events` | `docs/contracts/task_engine_driver_event_api.v1.schema.json` | approve/reject/block/revoke / event refВ·digest | human лҳҗлҠ” bounded policy authority; coordinator writes | expiry/revocation; stale `409`, forbidden `403` |
| `POST /api/task-engine/drivers/:id/apply` | `docs/contracts/task_engine_apply_api.v1.schema.json` | expected revision + apply event / ApplicationReceipt | apply authorityлҘј кІҖмҰқн•ң **sole coordinator** | `Idempotency-Key` н•„мҲҳ; same receipt/no-op; wrong authority `423` |
| `GET /api/task-engine/drivers/:id` | `docs/contracts/task_engine_projection_api.v1.schema.json` | typed refsмҷҖ event/receipt projection | project read | DB м „нӣ„ count/digest л¶ҲліҖ |
| `GET /api/task-engine/replay` | `docs/contracts/task_engine_replay_api.v1.schema.json` | project ref + cutoff / projection digestВ·gap report | admin/project read, query-only | mutation `0`; bad cutoff `400` |
| `GET /api/context-life-tree` кё°мЎҙ surface | кё°мЎҙ ENGINE-12 response + replay `$defs` | daily projection | project read | new adapterлҸ„ owner mutation `0` |
| `POST /api/mail-history/occurrences/:id/classification` (`TARGET P8`) | proposed `docs/contracts/mail_history_classification.v2.schema.json` | expected assignment revision + `classification_epoch` + from/to project + operation/generation / assignment events+outbox refs | `mail_classification_coordinator`; ERP task authority м—ҶмқҢ | local lock+valid classification lease н•„мҲҳ; stale `409/423`, retry=same events |
| `node guild_hall/gateway/project_mail_history_projector.mjs --claim-generation <id>` (`TARGET P8`) | proposed generation manifest schema | outbox claim with active `projector_epoch`вҶ’staged CSV/ICS/XLSXвҶ’source-epoch digest parityвҶ’publish receipt | `project_history_projector` only | stale projector lease reject; same generation no-op |
| `node guild_hall/gateway/validate_project_mail_history_generation.mjs --generation <id>` (`TARGET P8`) | same manifest schema | DB event/outboxвҶ”CSV/ICS/XLSX row count+digest parity | read-only validator | mutation `0`; mismatch nonzero/fail closed |
| `npm.cmd run validate:task-engine-core-v1` (`TARGET`; C01Bк°Җ root `package.json`м—җ л“ұлЎқ) | not_applicable | pure contract/synthetic replay | local validator | registration м „ `not_run`; exit `0`к°Җ C01B/P7 acceptance |
| `node tools/task_engine_inventory.mjs --query-only --json` (`FORMAL RECEIPT RETAINED`; current execution authority/live binding HOLD) | `docs/contracts/task_engine_inventory_manifest.v1.schema.json` | five-lane owner/root/writer/caller/consumer/source-availability + schema/count aggregate manifest | retained C00Q receipt л’Ө лі„лҸ„ current C00B owner authorityмқҳ read-only | source commandлҠ” мЎҙмһ¬н•ҳм§Җл§Ң live commandк°Җ м•„лӢҳ; migration import/raw value кёҲм§Җ. descriptor/evidence authorityк°Җ н•ҳлӮҳлқјлҸ„ м—Ҷкұ°лӮҳ л§ҢлЈҢлҗҳл©ҙ BLOCKED; authorityк°Җ нҷ•мқён•ң current л¶Җмһ¬В·gapмқҖ inventory findingмқҙл©° H00 completeness PASSк°Җ м•„лӢҳ |
| `node tools/task_engine_migration_dry_run.mjs --plan <opaque-ref>` | `docs/contracts/task_engine_migration_manifest.v1.schema.json` | no-write crosswalk/conflict manifest | approved operator | conflict exit nonzero, apply м—ҶмқҢ |
| `node tools/task_engine_schema_migration.mjs --dry-run` | migration manifest schema | DDL/collision/up-down plan | local synthetic by default | `--apply`лҠ” approval+maintenance+backup receipt лӘЁл‘җ м—Ҷмңјл©ҙ write 0 |
| `node tools/task_engine_replay.mjs --fixture <synthetic>` | replay API `$defs` | digest 2нҡҢ | test only | byte-identical digest мҡ”кө¬ |
| `node tools/task_engine_runtime_binding.mjs inspect --binding <local-binding> --json` | `docs/contracts/task_engine_runtime_binding.v1.schema.json` | current mode/digest/expiry/role aggregate | local read-only | raw path/secret м¶ңл Ҙ 0; invalid nonzero |
| `node tools/task_engine_runtime_binding.mjs plan --mode off\|pilot\|production ...` | same binding schema | canonical candidate + digest | owner-approved local operator | write 0; invalid scope/expiry nonzero |
| `node tools/task_engine_runtime_binding.mjs apply --candidate <candidate> --expected-current-digest <digest-or-null> --owner-approval-ref <opaque>` | same binding schema | atomic replace receipt | owner-approved local operator | explicit apply+CAS; conflict `409`, partial write 0 |

#### 6.5A Personal MCP lifecycleВ·query target surface (`TARGET`, feature OFF)

нҳ„мһ¬ кө¬нҳ„лҗң personal MCP 8к°ң toolмқҖ В§3.2/`ERP-MCP-V0`мқҳ CURRENTлӢӨ. м•„лһҳ toolмқҖ м•„м§Ғ кө¬нҳ„лҗҳм§Җ
м•Ҡм•ҳкі  AX/Q side-cardмқҳ лі„лҸ„ мҠ№мқё лҢҖмғҒмқҙлӢӨ. `erp_publish_work_session`мқҖ legacy one-shot facadeлЎң
ліҙмЎҙн•ҳл©° lifecycle start/closeoutмңјлЎң мЎ°мҡ©нһҲ л°”кҫём§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

| proposed MCP tool | request/result н•өмӢ¬ | authВ·idempotency | н—Ҳмҡ© mutation / кёҲм§Җ |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `erp_get_my_tasks` | account-scoped task assignmentsмҷҖ revision refs | brokered actor chain; cursor generation pin | business row `0`; current bearer agenda compatibilityлҠ” legacy facadeлЎңл§Ң мң м§Җ |
| `erp_start_or_bind_work_session` | exact assignment revision+opaque thread-ref digest+nodeвҶ’session/start receipt | account+registered node+active assignment; `(assignment,actor,start_key)` same digest=same receipt, conflict/stale/cardinality=`409` | session+binding+receiptл§Ң; task/history/knowledge `0` |
| `erp_publish_work_checkpoint` | session sequence+previous digest+bounded resultвҶ’ingest receipt | bound actor/node/current assignment; same seq/digest duplicate, different digest quarantine, gap held | session event/receiptл§Ң |
| `erp_closeout_work_session` | terminal `completed_candidate|blocked|handoff|abandoned` event | checkpointмҷҖ к°ҷмқҖ chain; terminal retry idempotent | task status/event `0`; handoffлҠ” old row overwrite кёҲм§Җ |
| `erp_submit_completion_proposal` | accepted closeout+expected task revisionвҶ’pending proposal/Driver candidate link | self/approved capability; same proposal digest no-op | proposal/linkл§Ң; кіөмӢқ completionВ·knowledge promotion `0` |
| `erp_list_unclosed_work_sessions` | accepted startмҷҖ terminal closeoutмқҳ server-side gap candidate | self/admin explicit scope | local pending outbox м¶”м • кёҲм§Җ; мЎ°нҡҢ лҢҖмғҒ owner row `0` |
| `erp_get_work_session_receipt` | receipt status/digest/next sequence | self/admin; foreign existence-safe deny | business row `0` |
| `erp_get_project_history` | accepted generation/cutoff/coverage/gaps+typed rows | explicit project ACL+generation-pinned cursor | projection/query owner row `0`; snapshot reverse import кёҲм§Җ |
| versioned `erp_get_task_context` | accepted P5 context receipt, exact source/history/knowledge refs | task access+project ACL | legacy response лі‘н–ү; unaccepted contextлҘј acceptedлЎң н‘ңмӢң кёҲм§Җ |
| `erp_search_knowledge` | explicit `scope=project|common`, exact source/Wiki revision+content+locator+claim ceiling | matching grant; scope лҲ„лқҪ/implicit fallback reject | RAG/Wiki/canon/task mutation `0` |
| `erp_submit_knowledge_candidate` | exact evidence+weakest claim ceilingвҶ’candidate receipt | candidate capability; stronger promotion state `422` | candidate ledger н•ң кііл§Ң append; Wiki/RAG/canon/ontology/task `0` |
| `erp_prepare_binary_upload` | artifact/revision intent+declared hash/size/mediaвҶ’bounded HTTPS upload ticket | enrolled device+delegation intersection; URL alone invalid | HPP quarantine ticketл§Ң; destination pathВ·project binding `0` |
| `erp_prepare_exact_revision_download` | exact artifact+revision+audienceвҶ’bounded range-capable HTTPS download ticket | artifact/revision/action ACL, expiry/revoke recheck | exact accepted revision bytes only; latest/raw fallbackВ·directory access `0` |

кіөнҶө TARGET мҳӨлҘҳлҠ” `401` invalid/revoked/expired, `403` capability/node/scope, foreign objectм—җлҠ”
existence leak м—ҶлҠ” `404`, `409` stale/idempotency/sequence/generation, `422` shape/evidence/claim,
`423` feature/writer inactive, `429` rate limitмқҙлӢӨ. Read toolмқҳ вҖңzero mutationвҖқмқҖ ліҙнҳё лҢҖмғҒ task/history/
knowledge/business row delta `0`мқ„ лң»н•ңлӢӨ. CURRENT мқёмҰқмқҙ `erp_mcp_access_token.last_used_at`мқ„ к°ұмӢ н• 
мҲҳ мһҲмңјлҜҖлЎң audit touchк№Ңм§Җ DB byte-zeroлқјкі  мЈјмһҘн•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡмңјл©°, н–Ҙнӣ„ access eventк°Җ н•„мҡ”н•ҳл©ҙ лі„лҸ„
лӘ…мӢңм Ғ audit owner/contractлЎң л¶„лҰ¬н•ңлӢӨ.

В§6.5мқҳ TaskEngine/mail POST write routeлҠ” C08F/P8мқҳ runtime binding loaderлҘј кіөнҶө preconditionмңјлЎң м“°кі ,
coordinatorк°Җ transaction м•Ҳм—җм„ң к°ҷмқҖ binding digestлҘј лӢӨмӢң кІҖмҰқн•ңлӢӨ. C03 кө¬нҳ„ мӢңм җм—җлҠ” binding
instanceк°Җ м—ҶмңјлҜҖлЎң routeлҠ” н•ӯмғҒ `423 binding_not_active`мҷҖ write `0`мқҙлӢӨ. C09D OFF, C10 pilot,
G01 production revision мҷёмқҳ лі„лҸ„ env flagлӮҳ fallback grantлҠ” м—ҶлӢӨ.
В§6.5A personal MCP routeмқҳ exact binding ownerлҠ” D28/AX-G1м—җм„ң лі„лҸ„лЎң м •н•ҳл©°, к·ё м „м—җлҠ” feature OFFлӢӨ.

Golden JSON schemaмқҳ top-level fieldлҠ” лӢӨмқҢм—җм„ң лҠҳлҰ¬кұ°лӮҳ мқҙлҰ„мқ„ л°”кҫёл Өл©ҙ contract reviewк°Җ н•„мҡ”н•ҳлӢӨ.

| schema | request/query required fields | success response required fields |
| --- | --- | --- |
| candidate API | `schema_version`, `project_ref`, `source_revision_refs`, `candidate_spec`, `requested_at` | `schema_version`, `candidate_ref`, `candidate_digest`, `stored_status`, `duplicate`, `receipt_ref` |
| Driver API | `schema_version`, `intent`, `driver`, `requested_at` | `schema_version`, `intent_ref`, `driver_ref`, `driver_digest`, `decision_state`, `duplicate` |
| Driver event API | `schema_version`, `driver_ref`, `event`, `authority_attestation` | `schema_version`, `event_ref`, `event_digest`, `decision_state`, `duplicate` |
| apply API | `schema_version`, `driver_ref`, `apply_event`, `expected_task_revision_ref` | `schema_version`, `application_receipt`, `task_ref`, `task_event_ref`, `duplicate` |
| projection API | path `driver_id` | `schema_version`, `driver`, `events`, `application_receipt`, `projection_digest`, `gap_codes` |
| replay API | `project_ref`, `valid_at`, `known_at` | `schema_version`, `cutoff`, `task_projection_digest`, `life_tree_projection_digest`, `gap_codes` |
| inventory manifest | CLI flags `--query-only --json` | `schema_version`, `query_only`, `baseline_refs`, laneлі„ `physical_owner_ref/default_root_ref/writer_candidates/direct_caller_candidates/consumer_candidates/source_availability_summary`, `source_authority_refs`, `table_counts`, `index_names`, `trigger_names`, `enum_counts`, `unresolved_live_proofs`, `zero_mutation`, `manifest_digest`; `source_availability_summary`лҠ” P0 inventory fieldмқҙл©° H00мқҳ six-state coverage receiptк°Җ м•„лӢҳ |
| migration manifest | `schema_version`, `mode`, `source_refs`, `target_schema_ref` | `crosswalk_counts`, `conflict_counts`, `orphan_counts`, `delete_count`, `prerequisite_receipts`, `manifest_digest` |
| runtime binding | В§11.2Aмқҳ 18к°ң canonical field м „мІҙ | inspect/plan/apply receiptмқҳ `schema_version`, `mode`, `binding_digest`, `previous_binding_digest`, `changed`, `error_code` |

лӘЁл“  HTTP мҳӨлҘҳ envelopeлҠ” `schema_version`, `error_code`, `retryable`, nullable `conflict_ref`, nullable
`quarantine_ref`л§Ң public/log-safe fieldлЎң к°–лҠ”лӢӨ. Clientк°Җ writer attestationмқ„ кҫёл©° ліҙлӮҙм§Җ лӘ»н•ҳкІҢ
coordinator identityмҷҖ writer attestationмқҖ server-side bindingм—җм„ң мЈјмһ…н•ңлӢӨ.

API requestлҠ” title/body лҢҖмӢ  source ownerм—җм„ң мҠ№мқёлҗң мөңмҶҢ fieldл§Ң л°ӣкі , public logм—җлҠ” typed ref,
digest, error codeл§Ң лӮЁкёҙлӢӨ. LLM outputмқҖ candidateлҘј л§Ңл“Ө мҲҳ мһҲм§Җл§Ң approve/apply authorityк°Җ м—ҶлӢӨ.

### 6.6 Mail history sole-writer, outbox, parity contract

`CURRENT` public code evidence:

- JS `guild_hall/gateway/project_mail_history_writer.mjs::upsertProjectMailHistory()`лҠ” CSVвҶ’XLSXвҶ’ICSлҘј
  мҲңм°Ё `writeFile`н•ҳкі  `_workmeta` CSV/ICSмҷҖ `_workspaces` XLSXлҘј м“ҙлӢӨ.
- Python `mail_fetch/collector/storage/project_mail_history.py::ProjectMailHistoryWriter`лҸ„ к°ҷмқҖ logical
  кІҪлЎңлҘј м“°м§Җл§Ң лі„лҸ„ XLSX renderer/shapeлҘј к°Җм§„лӢӨ.
- `outlook_mail_reconcile.mjs`лҠ” project mail-history CSVлҘј м§Ғм ‘ к°ұмӢ н•ҳл©° XLSX generationмқ„ мҶҢмң н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
- dev-ERP `tools/scan_mail_ledger.mjs`лҠ” кё°мЎҙ CSVлҘј `core_mail`лЎң ingestн•ңлӢӨ.
- мқҙ м„ё writerмҷҖ ERP assignment/event, file projections мӮ¬мқҙм—җлҠ” кіөнҶө process lock, roleлі„ lease/
  classificationВ·projector epoch, atomic outbox, same-generation parity/failback validatorк°Җ м—ҶлӢӨ.

л”°лқјм„ң `TARGET` normal authorityлҠ” HPPмқҳ л‘җ logical identityлЎң м ңн•ңн•ңлӢӨ. мқҙ м Ҳмқҳ mail outboxлҠ”
`project_history_projector`к°Җ лӢҙлӢ№н•ҳлҠ” 5к°ң lane мӨ‘ mail laneмқҳ к°ҖмһҘ к°•н•ң parity кІҪкі„лӢӨ. Voice,
structured PC work, file, run/log laneмқҖ к°Ғ кё°мҲ  source ownerлҘј ліҙмЎҙн•ң мұ„ H06м—җм„ң acceptedлҗң
event/refмҷҖ projection manifestл§Ң к°ҷмқҖ projectorм—җ мһ…л Ҙн•ңлӢӨ.

| logical identity | normal rights | prohibited |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `mail_classification_coordinator` | source occurrenceлҘј project-independent IDлЎң л“ұлЎқн•ҳкі  DB assignment current+event+outboxлҘј н•ң transactionмңјлЎң commit | CSV/XLSX м§Ғм ‘ publish, ERP task write, raw body copy |
| `project_history_projector` | mailмқҖ committed outbox, лӮҳлЁём§Җ 4к°ң laneмқҖ accepted event/ref manifestлҘј valid `projector_epoch`м—җм„ң claimн•ҙ н”„лЎңм қнҠёлі„ CSV/XLSXлҘј к°ҷмқҖ generationмңјлЎң materialize; mail ICSлҸ„ н•Ёк»ҳ мң м§Җ | classification current/event ліҖкІҪ, task write, source truth ліҖкІҪ |
| active voice writer identity | TARGET HPP лҳҗлҠ” accepted failover leaseмқҳ Macмқҙ voice source/runtimeмқ„ лӢЁлҸ… мғқмӮ°; MacмқҖ mail/5-lane coverage monitorмҷҖ alert candidate мң м§Җ | HPPмҷҖ Mac лҸҷмӢң shared voice write л°Ҹ лӘЁл“  project-history CSV/XLSX write allowlistлҠ” empty |
| `project_history_emergency_fallback` | нҸүмҶҢ dormant; explicit failoverм—җм„ңл§Ң five-lane projector leaseлҘј л°ӣкі , mail coordinator к¶Ңн•ңмқҖ coverageмҷҖ лі„лҸ„ мҠ№мқёмқҙ мһҲмқ„ л•Ңл§Ң л°ӣмқҢ | мһҗлҸҷ мҠ№кІ©В·мһҗлҸҷ failbackВ·voice identity к¶Ңн•ң мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ©В·ERP task write |

P8мқҳ cutoverлҠ” feature-OFF synthetic fixtureм—җм„ң direct writer reject к·ңм№ҷмқ„ кІҖмҰқн•  лҝҗ live writerлҘј
м „нҷҳн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. лі„лҸ„ мҠ№мқёлҗң P9м—җм„ңл§Ң н•ң н”„лЎңм қнҠёмқҳ HPP-primary bounded switchмҷҖ rollbackмқ„ н•ҳкі ,
P10м—җм„ңл§Ң production cutoverВ·failover/failbackмқ„ н—Ҳмҡ©н•ңлӢӨ. кё°мЎҙ CSV/XLSX кІҪлЎңмҷҖ consumerлҠ” мң м§Җн•ҳлҗҳ,
м „нҷҳ лҢҖмғҒ лІ”мң„м—җм„ңлҠ” projectorк°Җ мғқм„ұн•ң `projection_generation_id`мҷҖ manifestк°Җ м—ҶлҠ” direct writeлҘј
кұ°л¶Җн•ңлӢӨ. `mail_occurrence_id`лҠ” projectлҘј нҸ¬н•Ён•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡмңјл©° reclassification м „нӣ„ лҸҷмқјн•ҳлӢӨ.

## 7. м „мІҙ file/folder/repository/knowledge м ҖмһҘ кө¬мЎ°

### лҸ„мӢқ 2 вҖ” source-local + public/project/common/system physical tree

```text
source-local owners                         # мӣҗл¬ё/current/revisionмқҳ к¶Ңмң„мһҗ
в”ңв”Җ mail / voice / SE schedule / files
в””в”Җ owner-approved revision pointer в”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”Җв”җ
                                                  в”Ӯ
Soulforge public Git                              в”Ӯ
в”ңв”Җ .registry/                 # species/class canon
в”ңв”Җ .unit/                     # active subject owner
в”ңв”Җ .workflow/                 # orchestration canon
в”ңв”Җ .party/                    # reusable orchestration template
в”ңв”Җ .mission/                  # мҠ№мқёлҗң mission planл§Ң
в”ңв”Җ docs/architecture/         # root contracts
в”ңв”Җ guild_hall/                # public-safe engines/adapters
в””в”Җ ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/ # derived UI consumer + ERP app code; canon owner м•„лӢҳ, raw payload м—ҶмқҢ

owner-approved local/private planes
в”ңв”Җ _workspaces/<project_code>/                  # actual logical project worksite/body; actual project payloadВ·artifact owner
в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ ... source/artifact payload              # project payload
в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ reference_payloads/rag/                  # project RAG target
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ reports/{л©”мқј_мқҙл Ҙ,мқҢм„ұ_мқҙл Ҙ,PC_м—…л¬ҙ_мқҙл Ҙ,нҢҢмқј_мқҙл Ҙ,мӢӨн–ү_мқҙл Ҙ}/*.xlsx
в”Ӯ                                                # established OneDrive junctionмқҙ physical materialization/shared sync; narrow runtime exclusions below
в”ңв”Җ _workspaces/knowledge/rag/                  # truly common payload only
в”ңв”Җ _workspaces/system/rag/                     # metadata-only system output
в”ңв”Җ _workmeta/<project_code>/                   # project metadata/pointer/hash/receipt
в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ reports/voice_source_events/**           # canonical technical voice events
в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ reports/file_activity/**                 # canonical technical file observation/event/checkpoint
в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ runs/<run_id>/**                         # canonical run/log metadata
в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ reports/{л©”мқј_мқҙл Ҙ,мқҢм„ұ_мқҙл Ҙ,PC_м—…л¬ҙ_мқҙл Ҙ,нҢҢмқј_мқҙл Ҙ,мӢӨн–ү_мқҙл Ҙ}/*.csv
в”Ӯ  в”Ӯ                                            # proposed derived metadata views; mail pathлҠ” кё°мЎҙ
в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ knowledge/source_revision_records/**     # contract-defined immutable source revisions
в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ knowledge/source_revision_events/**      # contract-defined monthly source events
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ ontology/knowledge_bindings/events/**    # contract-defined monthly knowledge application events
в”ңв”Җ _workmeta/system/
в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ knowledge/source_revision_records/**     # truly common exact source revisions
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ knowledge/source_revision_events/**      # common monthly source events + system evidence
в”ңв”Җ HPP private central custody TARGET          # no live binding claim; exact physical binding/service healthлҠ” VERIFY_HP
в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ active dev-ERP DB + WAL/SHM
в”Ӯ  в”ңв”Җ RAW/quarantine/inbox
в”Ӯ  в””в”Җ queue/outbox/runtime/checkpoint
в”ңв”Җ guild_hall/state/                           # local runtime/checkpoint; public GitВ·OneDrive м ңмҷё
в””в”Җ private-state/                              # selected cross-project continuity metadata
```

| node | payload/metadata | reader | writer | tracking | migration sourceвҶ’target |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| source-local mail/voice/schedule/file | authoritative payload+revision | approved adapter | source owner | source revision/receipt | ліөмӮ¬н•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡкі  pointer лҳҗлҠ” мҠ№мқё materialization |
| ERP service ingress inboxes | chat/MCP uploadлЎң мӨ‘м•ҷ serviceк°Җ м§Ғм ‘ мҲҳл №н•ң bytes | item/task-scoped service | inbox service writer | opaque descriptor, size/hash, upload receipt | project/artifact ownerлЎң мһҗлҸҷ мҠ№кІ© кёҲм§Җ; explicit promotion м „ service custody |
| HPP central runtime custody (`TARGET`) | active DB/WAL/SHM, accepted central RAW/quarantine, central queue/outbox/checkpoint logical classes | HPP loopback services through strict office-LAN MCP/API | classлі„ sole HPP writer | private binding/backup receipts | no live binding claim; exact physical pathВ·network/cert/service healthлҠ” public л¬ём„ң л°– `VERIFY_HP`; cloud syncмҷҖ remote disk access `0` |
| logical ingress promotion plane | storage bindingВ·promotion receipt; exact physical pathлҠ” D27 м „ м—ҶмқҢ | approved promoter/validator | `ingress_promoter` нӣ„ліҙ 1к°ң | operation/digest/authority/policy refs | pointer кё°ліё, approved copy/move/deriveл§Ң; source/projector/task writerмҷҖ л¶„лҰ¬ |
| public Git roots | public-safe code/contract/example | all developers | designated public dev lane | public Git | candidate branchвҶ’latest main bounded patch |
| `_workspaces/<project>/...` | actual logical project bodyмҷҖ project payload/artifact, human-authored filesВ·XLSX | approved project tools | work/tool PC task owner | public Git м ңмҷё; physical materialization/shared syncлҠ” established OneDrive junction | active DB/WAL/SHM, accepted central ingress RAW/quarantine, central queue/outbox/checkpoint, active runtime truth кёҲм§Җ; source approved copy, no-delete |
| project RAG target | project source/index/chunk/answer/work-card | project-scoped RAG | project RAG writer | metadata receiptлҠ” `_workmeta/<project>` | legacy common pathвҶ’project path copy/readback |
| common RAG | common-only payload | common reader | common knowledge writer | `_workmeta/system` pointer | foreign project asset `0` нҷ•мқё |
| system RAG | metadata-only output | diagnostics | system metadata writer | local/private | body/chunk/answer кёҲм§Җ |
| `_workmeta/<project>` | pointer/hash/run/review metadata | project owner agents | bounded task owner | private Git | raw payload л°ңкІ¬ мӢң worksiteлЎң мқҙлҸҷ кі„нҡҚ нӣ„ owner мҠ№мқё |
| `_workmeta/system` | common review/5-field/aggregate | system reviewer | authorized system metadata writer | private Git | project-specific payload кёҲм§Җ |
| source revision/application metadata | contract-defined `knowledge/source_revision_*`мҷҖ project `ontology/knowledge_bindings/events` | temporal/context adapters | ownerлі„ кё°мЎҙ/мҠ№мқё writer | private Git | generic temporal treeлЎң ліөмӮ¬ кёҲм§Җ; exact ref crosswalkл§Ң |
| technical history owners | `voice_source_events`, `file_activity`, `runs`, source-local mail events | P1 adapters/context | к°Ғ source ownerмқҳ кё°мЎҙ writer | private/local source contract | лӢӨлҘё ліҙкі  нҸҙлҚ”лЎң мқҙлҸҷн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ |
| five user history views | metadata CSV + human XLSX | owner/UI | HPP `project_history_projector` sole normal writer | CSV private Git, XLSX worksite | source truth м•„лӢҳ; exact refsлЎң rebuild; лӢӨлҘё PC normal write `0` |
| accepted query generation | API/CSV/XLSX result digestsмҷҖ accepted pointer | ERP UI/MCP/query adapter | accepted-generation coordinator | generation manifest/current-pointer event | API primary, files audit snapshot; reverse importВ·implicit fallback кёҲм§Җ |
| dev-ERP DB | task/Driver/event/current/receipt + approved mail identity/assignment/outbox | ERP/projections | task tables=`TaskEngineTransactionCoordinator` 1к°ң; mail tables=`mail_classification_coordinator` 1к°ң; мғҒнҳё table write кёҲм§Җ | local backup/metadata receipt | schema migrationмқҖ C09AвҶ’C09вҶ’C09RвҶ’C09D(feature OFF)вҶ’C10 gate |
| `guild_hall/state` | machine runtime/checkpoint | local operator | role-specific process | local only | лӢӨлҘё PCлЎң нҶөм§ё sync кёҲм§Җ |
| `private-state` | selected continuity metadata | owner ops | designated always-on plane | private Git | secret/raw м—…л¬ҙ мӣҗл¬ё кёҲм§Җ |

### 7.1 Reference/copy/move/deriveмҷҖ л‘җ мў…лҘҳмқҳ вҖңнҢҢмқј м ҖмһҘвҖқ

Source payload storageмҷҖ н”„лЎңм қнҠёлі„ мқҙл Ҙ file projectionмқҖ лӢӨлҘё нқҗлҰ„мқҙлӢӨ.

```text
source/work PC в”Җв”Җ MCP control + authenticated HTTPS upload в”Җв”Җ> HPP custody inbox/source owner
                                       в””в”Җ approved promoter в”Җ> project storage binding/revision
accepted event/ref в”Җв”Җ HPP projector в”Җв”Җ> CSV/ICS/XLSX audit snapshot
accepted generation в”Җв”Җ query adapter в”Җ> ERP UI/MCP primary view
```

- нҢҖмӣҗ PCк°Җ мһҗкё° мқҙл Ҙ CSVлҘј л§Ңл“  л’Ө HPPк°Җ GitмңјлЎң н•©м№ҳлҠ” л°©мӢқмқҖ TARGETмқҙ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. нҢҖмӣҗмқҖ immutable
  session/file/run event лҳҗлҠ” upload receiptлҘј ліҙлӮҙкі  HPPлҠ” accepted refsлҘј server-sideлЎң м·Ён•©н•ңлӢӨ.
- GitмқҖ public code/contract лҳҗлҠ” private metadata historyмқҳ л°°нҸ¬В·к°җмӮ¬ мұ„л„җмқҙм§Җ live ingress/event busк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ.
- OneDrive junctionмқҖ `_workspaces/<project>` actual logical project bodyмқҳ physical materialization/shared-sync
  mechanismмқҙм§Җ HPP runtime transportлӮҳ reverse-copy channelмқҙ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. Active DB/WAL/SHM, accepted central
  ingress RAW/quarantine, central queue/outbox/checkpointмҷҖ active runtime truthлҠ” к·ё sync лҢҖмғҒмқҙ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ.
- н”„лЎңм қнҠё л¶„лҘҳ ліҖкІҪмқҖ source occurrence IDлҘј л°”кҫём§Җ м•Ҡкі  classification/promotion binding eventлҘј appendн•ң
  л’Ө мғҲ accepted generationмқ„ л§Ңл“ лӢӨ. old bindingВ·generationмқҖ м§Җмҡ°м§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
- ProjectorлҠ” derived history bytesлҘј м“ё мҲҳ мһҲм§Җл§Ң source payloadлҘј copy/promoteн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. PromoterлҠ”
  storage bindingмқ„ л§Ңл“Ө мҲҳ мһҲм§Җл§Ң CSV/XLSX accepted generationмқ„ publishн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

HWP мӣҗл¬ёмқҖ м§Ғм ‘ RAG мһ…л ҘмңјлЎң мқҪм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. project worksiteм—җм„ң HWPX нҢҢмғқліё, normalization status,
hash pointer, receiptк°Җ лЁјм Җ мғқкёҙ л’Ө HWPX revisionмқ„ SourceRevisionмңјлЎң м—°кІ°н•ңлӢӨ.

## 8. мһ…л ҘвҶ’TaskDriverвҶ’ERP closed loop

### лҸ„мӢқ 4 вҖ” sourceм—җм„ң feedbackк№Ңм§Җ

```mermaid
sequenceDiagram
  participant S as "Source owner"
  participant L as "P1 history/coverage"
  participant C as "P2-P5 context gate"
  participant A as "P6 discovery"
  participant D as "TaskDriver ledger"
  participant H as "Human/Policy authority"
  participant E as "Sole TaskEngine coordinator"
  participant P as "Personal session coordinator"
  participant W as "Worker/Codex/workflow"
  participant V as "Verification"
  participant K as "Feedback/Knowledge candidate"

  S->>L: append-only event/revision + coverage window
  L->>C: common envelope + exact refs + gap codes
  C->>C: ID/clock/revision/RAG/Wiki/context validation
  C-->>A: accepted context receipt
  A->>D: candidate-only TaskIntent + context receipt digest
  D-->>A: same digestл©ҙ same candidate/no-op
  D->>H: к·јкұ°В·ліҖкІҪм•ҲВ·мӨ‘лӢЁмЎ°кұҙ кІҖнҶ 
  H->>D: approve/reject/block event + authority ref
  D->>E: approved apply event + idempotency key
  E->>E: reservation + task_event + current + receipt (1 transaction)
  E-->>D: ApplicationReceipt
  E->>P: кіөмӢқ task assignment projection
  P->>P: exact assignmentм—җ start+bind receipt
  P->>W: accepted task context
  W->>P: ordered checkpoints
  W->>P: terminal closeout (official completion м•„лӢҳ)
  P-->>D: completion proposal candidate only
  W->>V: artifact/decision/verification evidence
  V->>E: verified outcome event лҳҗлҠ” correction
  V->>K: source feedback нӣ„ліҙ + knowledge нӣ„ліҙ + follow-up Driver нӣ„ліҙ
  K-->>S: sourceлі„ л№„м“°кё° handoff
  K-->>D: лӢӨмқҢ мқјмқҖ candidateлЎңл§Ң мһ¬м§„мһ…
```

Closed-loop к·ңм№ҷ:

1. P1 adapterлҠ” `source_ref`, `source_revision_ref`, project-independent `occurrence_ref`, clocks,
   coverageлҘј envelopeлЎң лӮҙліҙлӮј лҝҗ task нӣ„ліҙлҘј л§Ңл“Өм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
2. P5 `context_acceptance_gate`к°Җ exact refs, RAG/Wiki lineageмҷҖ gap semanticsлҘј accepted receiptлЎң
   лӢ«кё° м „ P6 discoveryлҠ” мӢңмһ‘н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
3. P6 discoveryлҠ” accepted contextм—җм„ң candidate-only TaskIntentлҘј л§Ңл“Өл©° ERP writeлҠ” 0мқҙлӢӨ.
4. DriverлҠ” cause, proposed patch, expected task revision, reason code, stop condition, authority
   requirementлҘј canonical digestм—җ нҸ¬н•Ён•ңлӢӨ.
5. human approval лҳҗлҠ” exact deterministic policyк°Җ м—Ҷмңјл©ҙ apply eventлҘј л§Ңл“Ө мҲҳ м—ҶлӢӨ. policyлҠ”
   ref, scope, valid_from/to, expiry, revocationмқ„ к°Җм ём•ј н•ңлӢӨ.
6. Sole coordinatorлҠ” task IDлҘј л°ңкёү/мҳҲм•Ҫн•ҳлҠ” мң мқјн•ң л¬јлҰ¬ DB writerлӢӨ. мһ¬мӢңлҸ„лҠ” к°ҷмқҖ reservation/task/receiptлҘј
   л°ҳнҷҳн•ңлӢӨ.
7. workerлҠ” taskлҘј мҲҳн–үн•ҳлҗҳ source truthлӮҳ Driver authorityк°Җ лҗҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
8. completionмқҖ follow-up taskлҘј м§Ғм ‘ мғқм„ұн•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡкі  мғҲ Driver candidateл§Ң л§Ңл“ лӢӨ.
9. verification мӢӨнҢЁлҠ” кё°мЎҙ мҷ„лЈҢлҘј мӮӯм ңн•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡкі  correction/reversal eventлҘј м¶”к°Җн•ңлӢӨ.
10. feedback writerмҷҖ knowledge candidate writerлҠ” TaskEngine coordinatorмҷҖ л¶„лҰ¬н•ңлӢӨ.
11. Personal sessionмқҖ exact assignmentм—җ start/bindн•ҳкі  м—¬лҹ¬ checkpointлҘј л°ӣмқ„ мҲҳ мһҲлӢӨ. кі„нҡҚ кё°ліёк°’мқҖ
    `{assignment epoch,account}`лӢ№ active primary н•ҳлӮҳмқҙл©° actor/nodeк°Җ л°”лҖҢл©ҙ old bindingмқ„ лҚ®м§Җ м•Ҡкі 
    terminal handoff+мғҲ session supersessionмңјлЎң м—°кІ°н•ңлӢӨ.
12. closeoutкіј completion proposalмқҖ task status/event/currentлҘј л°”кҫём§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. кіөмӢқ мҷ„лЈҢлҠ” лі„лҸ„
    ERP authorityк°Җ expected task revisionкіј verificationмқ„ нҷ•мқён•ҙ append-only task eventлЎң кё°лЎқн•ңлӢӨ.
13. Client-local pending outboxмҷҖ serverк°Җ кі„мӮ°н•ң missing-closeout candidateлҠ” лӢӨлҘё мғҒнғңлӢӨ. Accepted start
    м—Ҷмқҙ missingмңјлЎң л¶ҖлҘҙм§Җ м•Ҡкі , durable server ack кІҖмҰқ м „ local outboxлҘј м§Җмҡ°м§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
14. Source classification, upload receipt, history acceptance, payload promotion, `ArtifactRevision` acceptance,
    knowledge acceptanceлҠ” к°Ғк°Ғ лӢӨлҘё event/authorityлӢӨ. м•һмқҳ н•ҳлӮҳлЎң л’Ө мғҒнғңлҘј мһҗлҸҷ м¶”лЎ н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

## 9. verificationВ·feedbackВ·RAGВ·WikiВ·ontologyВ·мғқлӘ…мҲҳ

### 9.1 completionм—җм„ң м§ҖмӢқк№Ңм§Җ

`done`мқҖ лҒқмқҙ м•„лӢҲлқј кІҖмҰқ лҢҖкё° лҳҗлҠ” кІҖмҰқ мҷ„лЈҢ мӮ¬мӢӨмқ„ eventлЎң м—°кІ°н•ҳлҠ” м§Җм җмқҙлӢӨ. fruitлҠ” мөңмҶҢн•ң
completion refлҘј к°Җм§Җкі , к°ҖлҠҘн•ң кІҪмҡ° artifact revision, decision, verification, outcome refлҘј
к°Ғк°Ғ exact typed relationмңјлЎң к°–лҠ”лӢӨ. ownerк°Җ м •н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҖ canonical ownerлҠ” `UNKNOWN`мңјлЎң лӮЁкё°кі 
free-textлҘј мһ„мқҳ entityлЎң мҠ№кІ©н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

FeedbackмқҖ м„ё к°ҲлһҳлӢӨ.

- source feedback candidate: мӣҗмІң мӢңмҠӨн…ңм—җ лҸҢл ӨмӨ„ м ңм•Ҳ. source writerк°Җ лі„лҸ„ мҠ№мқёВ·м Ғмҡ©н•ңлӢӨ.
- knowledge candidate: exact source/evidenceк°Җ л¶ҷмқҖ нӣ„ліҙ. Wiki/RAG writerмқҳ кІҖнҶ  м „м—җлҠ” truthк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ.
- follow-up Driver candidate: лӢӨмқҢ н•  мқј м ңм•Ҳ. ERPм—җ м§Ғм ‘ м“°м§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

### 9.2 RAGВ·WikiВ·ontology кө¬м¶• мҲңм„ң

1. лӘЁл“  legacy RAG assetкіј reader/writer/CLI/UI consumerлҘј asset kindлі„лЎң inventoryн•ңлӢӨ.
2. project/common/system owner resolverмҷҖ lexical/native containment, symlink/traversal, Windows sibling
   collision guardлҘј synthetic testлЎң кі м •н•ңлӢӨ.
3. SourceвҶ’SourceRevisionвҶ’ExtractionRunвҶ’EvidenceLocatorвҶ’RagIndexвҶ’RagChunkмқҳ 6мў… ID basisлҘј golden fixtureлЎң
   кі м •н•ңлӢӨ.
4. one-project dry-runм—җм„ң copy targetкіј conflict/orphan manifestл§Ң л§Ңл“ лӢӨ.
5. мҠ№мқё нӣ„ copy/rebuildн•ҳкі  old/new reader кІ°кіјлҘј readbackн•ңлӢӨ. source originalкіј legacy indexлҠ”
   мӮӯм ңн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
6. WikiRevision writerлҠ” source/claim exact refмҷҖ project ACLмқ„ нҶөкіјн•ң bodyл§Ң owner-approved pathм—җ
   м“ҙлӢӨ. `_workmeta`мҷҖ system RAGм—җлҠ” bodyлҘј м“°м§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
7. RelationEventк°Җ B9d backlinkмҷҖ knowledge graphлҘј нҲ¬мҳҒн•ңлӢӨ. fuzzy matchлҠ” review-needed linkмқј лҝҗ
   confirmed relationмқҙ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ.

### 9.3 нҢҖ мЎ°нҡҢВ·RAG/Wiki мӮ¬мҡ© кі„м•Ҫ

нҢҖмӣҗмқҖ project file tree м „мІҙлҘј л°°нҸ¬л°ӣм•„м•јл§Ң м§ҖмӢқмқ„ м“°лҠ” кІғмқҙ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. TARGETмқҳ кё°ліё мқҪкё° мҲңм„ңлҠ”
`ERP UI/MCP вҶ’ accepted generation вҶ’ project history/context/RAG/Wiki exact revision`мқҙлӢӨ. CSV/ICS/XLSXмҷҖ
private metadata GitмқҖ к°җмӮ¬В·мҳӨн”„лқјмқё snapshotВ·ліөкө¬ к·јкұ°мқҙл©° live queryлӮҳ мһҗлҸҷ reverse importк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ.

| мҡ”мІӯ | н•„мҲҳ scope/кІ°кіј | кёҲм§Җ |
| --- | --- | --- |
| project history/context | explicit project grant, accepted generation/cutoff/coverage/gaps, exact typed refs | foreign-project мЎҙмһ¬ leak, stale/unaccepted generation fallback |
| project knowledge | `scope=project`, exact source/Wiki revision+content+locator+weakest claim ceiling | common мһҗлҸҷ fallback, bare path/fuzzy hitмқҳ accepted мҠ№кІ© |
| common knowledge | `scope=common`кіј лі„лҸ„ common grant | project body нҳјмһ…, projectвҶ’common м•”л¬ө м „нҷҳ |
| team feedback | exact evidenceлҘј к°Җм§„ candidate receipt | Wiki/RAG index/canon/ontology/task м§Ғм ‘ write |

AuthorizationмқҖ artifact/revision/action лӢЁмң„мқҙл©° лӘ©лЎқВ·detailВ·кІҖмғүВ·downloadк°Җ к°ҷмқҖ existence-leak м •мұ…мқ„
м“ҙлӢӨ. RAGлҠ” ACL-aware pre-filterмҷҖ post-filterлҘј лӘЁл‘җ м Ғмҡ©н•ҳкі  field/chunk visibilityлҘј cache keyм—җ
кІ°л°•н•ңлӢӨ. RevocationВ·policy revision л’Ө stale cache hitмқҖ `0`мқҙм–ҙм•ј н•ңлӢӨ. Sensitive Excel/PPTлҠ” hidden
sheet/slide, formula, comment/note, embedded objectк№Ңм§Җ policy лҢҖмғҒмңјлЎң ліҙкі , кІҖмҰқлҗң immutable redacted
derivative revisionл§Ң л°ҳнҷҳн•ңлӢӨ. DerivativeлҠ” exact raw/source revision lineageлҘј мң м§Җн•ҳлҗҳ raw fallbackмқҖ
н—Ҳмҡ©н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

нҢҖмӣҗмқҙ WorkSessionмқҳ `knowledge` л¬ёмһҗм—ҙм—җ м ҒмқҖ л©”лӘЁлҠ” current one-shot session fieldмқј лҝҗ knowledge
candidate, Wiki revision лҳҗлҠ” canon entryк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. нҢҖ submissionмқҖ candidate ledgerк°Җ н—Ҳмҡ©н•ҳлҠ” м•Ҫн•ң
claim ceilingл§Ң appendн•ҳл©° `validated_private|canon_candidate|canon_entry` к°ҷмқҖ к°•н•ң мғҒнғңлҘј мҡ”мІӯн•ҳл©ҙ
`422`лЎң кұ°л¶Җн•ңлӢӨ. Reviewer/approver/writerк°Җ sourcebound кІҖмҰқкіј ACLмқ„ нҶөкіјмӢңнӮЁ л’Өм—җл§Ң лі„лҸ„ promotionмқҙ
мқјм–ҙлӮңлӢӨ.

### лҸ„мӢқ 7 вҖ” B9 мһҘкё° мғқлӘ…мҲҳмҷҖ ENGINE-12 мқјмқј projection

```mermaid
flowchart TB
  L["Task/Relation/Source append-only ledger"]
  L --> B["B9 мһҘкё° мғқлӘ…мҲҳ<br/>gateвҶ’branchвҶ’historyвҶ’fruit"]
  L --> D["ENGINE-12 мқјмқј мғқлӘ…мҲҳ<br/>н•ҳлЈЁмқҳ mail/ERP/SE/voice/Codex/file"]
  L --> R["RAGВ·WikiВ·ontology graph"]
  B --> U["лҸҷмқј ERP UIмқҳ мһҘкё° view"]
  D --> U2["лҸҷмқј ERP UIмқҳ мҳӨлҠҳ view"]
  R --> U3["к·јкұ°/м§ҖмӢқ view"]
  U -. "мЎ°нҡҢл§Ң; owner write 0" .-> L
  U2 -. "мЎ°нҡҢл§Ң; owner write 0" .-> L
  U3 -. "нӣ„ліҙл§Ң; truth мһҗлҸҷмҠ№кІ© 0" .-> L
```

Primary tree parentлҠ” н•ҳлӮҳл§Ң л‘”лӢӨ. лӮҳлЁём§Җ кҙҖкі„лҠ” cross-linkлӢӨ. к°ҷмқҖ owner eventлҘј B9мҷҖ мқјмқј
л ҢмҰҲм—җ ліөм ң м ҖмһҘн•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡкі  projection IDк°Җ мӣҗ event typed refлҘј к°ҖлҰ¬нӮЁлӢӨ. лҸҷмқј
`valid_at/known_at` cutoffлЎң task/B9/daily replayлҘј л‘җ лІҲ мӢӨн–үн–Ҳмқ„ л•Ң digestк°Җ к°ҷм•„м•ј н•ңлӢӨ.

## 10. AX WorkspaceВ·personal CodexВ·AgentRun нӣ„мҶҚ кө¬м¶•

мқҙ м ҲмқҖ лІ”мң„м—җлҠ” нҸ¬н•Ён•ҳм§Җл§Ң core TaskDriverмқҳ м„ н–үмЎ°кұҙмңјлЎң л‘җм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. Core one-project pilotмқҙ
нҶөкіјн•ң л’Ө лі„лҸ„ owner мҠ№мқёмңјлЎң мӢңмһ‘н•ңлӢӨ.

### 10.1 AX Workspace

AX WorkspaceлҠ” ERP кіөмӢқ н•  мқјмқ„ лҢҖмІҙн•ҳлҠ” л‘җ лІҲм§ё task appк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. к°ңмқёмқҙ н•ң н”„лЎңм қнҠём—җм„ң
CodexмҷҖ н•Ёк»ҳ вҖңм§ҖкёҲ л¬ҙм—Үмқ„ ліҙкі , л¬ҙм—Үмқ„ мӢңлҸ„н•ҳкі , м–ҙл–Ө к·јкұ°лҘј л§Ңл“Өм—ҲлҠ”м§ҖвҖқлҘј кҙҖлҰ¬н•ҳлҠ” мһ‘м—…л©ҙмқҙлӢӨ.

`CURRENT`м—җлҠ” мқҙлҜё `src/erp_mcp_service.mjs`мқҳ `erp_mcp_work_session` table,
`publishWorkSession()` idempotency/replay, server publish routeмҷҖ testsк°Җ мһҲлӢӨ. л”°лқјм„ң WorkSessionмқ„
`concept only`лЎң мһ¬кө¬м¶•н•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡкі  one-shot structured result facadeлЎң REUSE/MODIFYн•ңлӢӨ. н•ҳм§Җл§Ң нҳ„мһ¬
recordлҠ” unordered independent recordмқҙл©° start, immutable assignment epoch, ordered sequence, thread
binding, closeout, durable client outbox/ack, handoff/supersessionмқҙ м—ҶлӢӨ. мқҙлҘј closeout лҳҗлҠ” complete
sessionмңјлЎң мҶҢкёү н•ҙм„қн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. dev-ERP л°– structured capture ownerмҷҖ project-exact source lineageлҸ„
gapмқҙлӢӨ. Codex м „мІҙ лҢҖнҷ”, нҷ”л©ҙ, нӮӨ мһ…л Ҙ, OS нҷңлҸҷмқҳ мғҒмӢң мҲҳм§‘мқҖ D19 мҠ№мқё м „ кё°ліё `OFF/DEFER`лӢӨ.

TARGET UXлҠ” deviceл§ҲлӢӨ one-time human-approved enrollmentлҘј н•ҳкі  routine workм—җм„ңлҠ” OS-protected
brokerк°Җ silent token refresh/delegationмқ„ мҲҳн–үн•ңлӢӨ. л§Ө tool callВ·chunkл§ҲлӢӨ мӮ¬лһҢм—җкІҢ л¬»м§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
Step-upмқҖ new/recovered device, scope expansion, restricted reveal/download, promotion/move/delete,
official completion, knowledge promotionм—җл§Ң мҡ”кө¬н•ңлӢӨ. Audit actor chainмқҖ
`user_id+device_id+agent_id+opaque thread_ref+task_id+project_id+artifact_id+revision_id+action+expiry`лҘј
л¶„лҰ¬ ліҙмЎҙн•ңлӢӨ. EnrollmentВ·refreshлҠ” local outbox/ackмҷҖ unfinished-session recoveryлҘј м—Ҷм• м§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

к¶ҢмһҘ мөңмҶҢ entity:

| entity | мөңмҶҢ field | м“°кё° owner | ERPмҷҖмқҳ кҙҖкі„ |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `CodexSeat` | seat ref, account/owner ref, allowed project scopes, capability policy ref | owner | task write к¶Ңн•ң мһҗмІҙк°Җ м•„лӢҳ |
| `TaskAssignmentEpoch` | task/project/account, assignment epoch/revision/event ref | ERP assignment owner | personal session writerк°Җ л°ңкёүВ·мҲҳм • кёҲм§Җ |
| `PersonalWorkSession` | session ref, assignment ref, actor, node, started, start digest, supersedes ref | personal session coordinator | `{assignment epoch,account}` active primary н•ҳлӮҳ кё°ліё; node/actor ліҖкІҪмқҖ handoff |
| `PersonalThreadBinding` | session, thread namespace, opaque thread-ref digest, binding/supersedes digest | personal session coordinator | raw thread IDмҷҖ м „м—ӯ taskвҶ”thread 1:1 м ҖмһҘ кёҲм§Җ |
| `WorkSessionEvent` | append-only checkpoint/closeout, global sequence/digest chain, bounded result fields | personal session coordinator | м§Ғм ‘ task/history/knowledge mutation кёҲм§Җ |
| `IngestReceipt` | accepted/duplicate/held-gap/quarantined/rejected, next sequence, digest | session reconciler | serverк°Җ local pending outboxлҘј м¶”м •н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ |
| `WorkArtifactRef` | artifact revision typed ref, digest, access label | source/artifact owner | payload ліөмӮ¬ м—Ҷмқҙ pointer |
| `CompletionProposalLink` | session closeoutвҶ”Driver candidate/task expected revision | proposal writer | closeoutВ·proposalмқҖ official completionмқҙ м•„лӢҳ |

м„ё мғҒнғңм¶•мқ„ н•©м№ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

| м¶• | мҳҲмӢң | authority |
| --- | --- | --- |
| ERP task | open/doing/blocked/done/reopened | sole TaskEngine/ERP coordinator |
| personal session | started/active/terminal closeout/handoff/superseded | personal session coordinator |
| local transport | pending/sent/acked/held/quarantined | н•ҙлӢ№ nodeмқҳ durable outbox + server receipt |

UI/MCPлҠ” project м„ нғқ, accepted generation, нҳ„мһ¬ session, кҙҖл Ё ERP task/Driver, evidence, blocker, stop
condition, receiptлҘј ліҙм—¬мӨҖлӢӨ. Project/common knowledge scopeлҠ” мӮ¬мҡ©мһҗк°Җ лӘ…мӢңн•ҳл©° fallbackн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
вҖңERPм—җ м Ғмҡ©вҖқмқҖ Driver apply APIлҘј нҳём¶ңн•ҳлҗҳ нҳ„мһ¬ seatк°Җ authorityмқём§Җ м„ңлІ„к°Җ лӢӨмӢң кІҖмӮ¬н•ңлӢӨ. MCP/к°ңмқё
CodexлҠ” candidate producerмқҙмһҗ primary query clientмқј мҲҳ мһҲм§Җл§Ң TaskEngine coordinatorлӮҳ л‘җ лІҲм§ё
truthк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ.

### 10.2 AgentRun

`.mission`мқҖ мҠ№мқёлҗң лӘ©н‘ң/кі„нҡҚ, `.workflow`лҠ” мӢӨн–ү м Ҳм°Ё, `.party`лҠ” мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ© orchestration templateлӢӨ.
`AgentRun`мқҖ мқҙл“Өмқ„ мӢӨм ңлЎң н•ң лІҲ мӢӨн–үн•ң runtime instanceмқҙлҜҖлЎң лі„лҸ„ IDмҷҖ receiptлҘј к°Җм ём•ј н•ңлӢӨ.

```text
MissionRef в”Җв”җ
WorkflowRef в”ңв”Җ> AgentRun в”Җ> CapabilityUseEvent в”Җ> AgentRunReceipt
PartyRef в”Җв”Җв”Җв”ҳ       в”Ӯ
                    в””в”Җ> TaskDriverCandidateRef / EvidenceRef
```

AgentRunмқҖ capability scope, input pointer, model/tool label, start/end, stop reason, deterministic
validator receiptлҘј кё°лЎқн•ҳлҗҳ raw prompt/м—…л¬ҙ payloadлҘј public лҳҗлҠ” `_workmeta`м—җ ліөмӮ¬н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
AgentRun м„ұкіөмқҖ task `done`мқҙлӮҳ verification passмҷҖ к°ҷм§Җ м•ҠлӢӨ.
AgentRunмқҖ P1 run/log history prerequisiteк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. P1мқҖ кё°мЎҙ run metadataмҷҖ structured receiptsлЎң
coverageлҘј лӢ«кі , AgentRun control planeмқҖ P9 мқҙнӣ„ лі„лҸ„ owner gateм—җм„ңл§Ң кІҖнҶ н•ңлӢӨ.

### 10.3 optional team gatewayВ·engineering workbenchмҷҖ anti-second-truth

ліөмһЎн•ң engineering taskлҠ” Soulforgeк°Җ official assignment/contextлҘј м ңкіөн•ң л’Ө н•ң WorkSession м•Ҳм—җм„ң
м—¬лҹ¬ specialist candidateлЎң лӮҳлҲҢ мҲҳ мһҲлӢӨ. мқҙл•Ң мҷёл¶Җ лҸ„кө¬мқҳ native task/session/memory/dispatch/`done`мқҖ
лӘЁл‘җ client-local coordination evidenceлӢӨ. Orcaнҳ• workbenchмқҳ terminal idleВ·worker completionВ·decision
gateмҷҖ Hermesнҳ• shellмқҳ Kanban `done`В·goal judgeВ·memoryлҠ” ERP status, WorkSession closeout, AgentRun
success, verification pass, owner approval лҳҗлҠ” accepted knowledgeлЎң м§Ғм ‘ ліҖнҷҳн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

```text
ERP/TaskEngine official assignment
  -> Soulforge MCP accepted context/query
  -> one PersonalWorkSession + one writable surface coordinator
     -> direct Codex OR Orca-type engineering workbench OR Hermes-type team gateway/shell candidate path
  -> candidate diff/artifact + validator receipt
  -> WorkSession checkpoint/closeout + completion proposal
  -> separate TaskEngine authorityк°Җ official completion нҢҗлӢЁ
```

DefaultлҠ” `direct_codex`мқҙл©° мҷёл¶Җ adapterлҠ” лӘЁл‘җ `OFF/DEFER`лӢӨ. Generic adapter contractмҷҖ negative
fixturesлҘј лЁјм Җ лӢ«кі , Orcaнҳ•кіј Hermesнҳ• trialмқҖ м„ңлЎң лҸ…лҰҪлҗң P10 gateлЎң мӢӨн–үн•ңлӢӨ. л‘ҳмқҖ к°ҷмқҖ taskм—җм„ң
мӨ‘мІ©н•ҳкұ°лӮҳ write-capable tokenмқ„ кіөмң н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. Hermesнҳ• gatewayлҠ” worker/workbenchлҘј spawnн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
мҙҲкё° Orcaнҳ• workerлҠ” agent мһҗмІҙ subagent/team spawnлҸ„ лҒ„кі , Orca coordinatorк°Җ м§Ғм ‘ кҙҖлҰ¬н•ҳлҠ” 2~3к°ң
workerл§Ң н—Ҳмҡ©н•ҙ orchestration layerлҘј н•ҳлӮҳлЎң м ңн•ңн•ңлӢӨ. AR-G1/G2 м „ external runмқҖ AgentRunмқҙ м•„лӢҲл©°
bounded WorkSession evidence refмқј лҝҗмқҙлӢӨ.

### 10.4 нӣ„мҶҚ phase gate

| gate | м„ н–үмЎ°кұҙ | мӮ°м¶ңл¬ј | кёҲм§Җ |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| AX-G1 | core C10 pilot pass, D01~D09+D12+D28+D29 кІ°м • | lifecycle/query schemaВ·UI design packet | ERP writer ліөм ң |
| AX-G2 | start/bind/sequence/outbox/ack/closeout/query synthetic tests | feature-OFF implementation | live MCP direct task/knowledge write |
| AX-G3 | AX-G2 pass, one-seatВ·one-project owner pilot мҠ№мқё | direct client candidate-only lifecycle+accepted query baseline | external tool мһҗлҸҷ нҸ¬н•ЁВ·team rolloutВ·official completion мһҗлҸҷнҷ” |
| AR-G1 | AX-G2 лҳҗлҠ” лҸ…лҰҪ н•„мҡ”м„ұ мҰқлӘ… | AgentRun contract | mission/workflow/party мқҳлҜё ліҖкІҪ |
| AR-G2 | capability/adversarial tests | bounded run receipt | unattended privilege escalation |
| EXT-G0 | core C10 pilot pass, D30 generic boundary кІ°м • | direct Codex vs optional gateway/workbench authorityВ·fit comparison, frozen engineering-task rubric | AX-G1~G3 м°ЁлӢЁ, м„Өм№ҳВ·кө¬лҸ…В·live м—°кІ°В·м ңн’Ҳмқ„ canon ownerлЎң кі м • |
| EXT-G1 | EXT-G0+AX-G2 pass, public-safe engineering task мҠ№мқё | generic adapter/non-nesting/receipt negative tests | AgentRun н•„мҲҳнҷ”, vendor installВ·real payloadВ·live endpoint |
| ORCA-T1 | AX-G3 direct baseline+EXT-G1 pass, D32мҷҖ лі„лҸ„ owner/Level 3 мҠ№мқё | matched direct-Codex baselineмқҙ мһҲлҠ” public-safe engineering task 1кұҙ candidate-only trial | Hermes nesting, permission bypass, binary multi-writer, direct main/push/PR |
| ORCA-T2 | ORCA-T1 pass, лі„лҸ„ owner/Level 3 мҠ№мқё | 2мЈј лҳҗлҠ” 10кұҙ нҷ•мһҘ к°Җм№ҳ мӢңн—ҳ | T1 кІ°кіј м—ҶлҠ” нҷ•лҢҖ, production/team rollout |
| HERMES-T1 | AX-G3 direct baseline+EXT-G1 pass, D31мҷҖ лі„лҸ„ owner/Level 3 мҠ№мқё | one-seat gateway/query/candidate-only trial | Orca nesting, worker/workbench spawn, Kanban/goalвҶ’ERP мҷ„лЈҢ, team rollout |

## 11. PC м—ӯн• В·л°°нҸ¬В·alertВ·мһҘм•  ліөкө¬

### 11.1 `HISTORICAL_REPORTED` runtime кё°мӨҖм„  вҖ” мқҙлІҲ ліҙм •м—җм„ң fresh мһ¬кҙҖм°°н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ

| кҙҖм°° | кІ°кіј | кө¬м¶• мқҳлҜё |
| --- | --- | --- |
| кі„нҡҚ/к°ңл°ң checkout | лӢ№мӢң clean main, originкіј лҸҷмқј | мқҙм „ snapshotмқј лҝҗ нҳ„мһ¬ к¶Ңмң„к°Җ м•„лӢҳ; мқҙлІҲ кі„нҡҚ кё°мӨҖм„ мқҖ В§2.1мқҳ `main@9df7e577...` |
| мҡҙмҳҒ shell/attestation | `56b5b951` кі„м—ҙлЎң м„ңлЎң мқјм№ҳ, origin/mainліҙлӢӨ 7 commit л’Ө | мҡҙмҳҒмқ„ мөңмӢ  mainкіј лҸҷмқјн•ҳлӢӨкі  л§җн•  мҲҳ м—ҶмқҢ |
| data backend binding | мҡҙмҳҒ shellкіј лі„лҸ„мқё source/data checkoutмқ„ к°ҖлҰ¬нӮҙ | нҳ„мһ¬ contract мқҳлҸ„м—җлҠ” л§һм§Җл§Ң release auditмқҳ вҖңл‘җ checkout same SHAвҖқ к°Җм •кіј м¶©лҸҢ |
| health | loopback HTTP `200` | process мғқмЎҙ мҰқкұ°мқј лҝҗ release readinessк°Җ м•„лӢҳ |
| core-only release audit | exit `1` | activation л¶Ҳк°Җ |
| audit blockers | Git status timeout 2кұҙ, snapshot кө¬мЎ° invalid, DB backup stale, restore test invalid/unbound, payload backup generation stale | мӣҗмқё л¶„лҰ¬мҷҖ recovery evidence н•„мҡ” |
| restore evidence | кҙҖм°°лҗң report 19к°ң мӨ‘ valid `0` | live schema/writer м „нҷҳ кёҲм§Җ |
| file activity runtime | scheduler/artifact/local stateк°Җ кҙҖм°° мӢң `0`; sole reconciler/operational primary лҜём§Җм • | live collector/reconciler activation кёҲм§Җ |

Git timeout blockerлҠ” auditмқҳ кі м • 5мҙҲ н•ңлҸ„ліҙлӢӨ мӢӨм ң statusк°Җ мҳӨлһҳ кұёлҰ° м •нҷ©мқҙ мһҲм–ҙ false blockerмқј мҲҳ
мһҲлӢӨ. к·ёлҹ¬лӮҳ timeoutмқ„ кі м№ң л’Өм—җлҸ„ source/data checkoutкіј runtime shellм—җ к°ҷмқҖ expected commitмқ„
к°•м ңн•ҳлҠ” нҳ„мһ¬ audit кі„м•Ҫ м¶©лҸҢмқҙ лӮЁмқ„ мҲҳ мһҲлӢӨ. мқҙ л¬ём ңлҠ” D16м—җм„ң лӢӨмқҢ л‘ҳ мӨ‘ н•ҳлӮҳлҘј ownerк°Җ
кІ°м •н•ҙм•ј н•ңлӢӨ.

- Aм•Ҳ: мҡҙмҳҒмҡ© pinned backend-code checkoutкіј project-data bindingмқ„ л¶„лҰ¬н•ңлӢӨ.
- Bм•Ҳ: release auditм—җм„ң executable code sourceмҷҖ data rootлҘј м„ңлЎң лӢӨлҘё к°ңл…җ/attestationмңјлЎң кІҖмҰқн•ңлӢӨ.

к°ңл°ң checkoutмқ„ мҡҙмҳҒ shellлЎң лӢЁмҲң ліөмӮ¬н•ҳкұ°лӮҳ project data truthлҘј runtime checkoutм—җ н•©м№ҳлҠ” н•ҙлІ•мқҖ
кёҲм§Җн•ңлӢӨ.

### лҸ„мӢқ 8 вҖ” PC roleВ·packetВ·reconcilerВ·ERP writer topology

```mermaid
flowchart LR
  W["work_pc<br/>м—…л¬ҙ мӣҗл¬ё/н”„лЎңм қнҠё мһ‘м—…"]
  P["portable_dev_pc<br/>мҲҳм§‘В·public к°ңл°ң"]
  T["tool_pc<br/>heavy build/test"]
  D["dev_worker_pc<br/>мҠ№мқё packetмқҳ branch producer"]
  N["always_on_node<br/>checkpoint/queue/кІҪлҹү мҡҙмҳҒ"]
  M["Mac temporary voice failover<br/>source HOLD/outbox<br/>concurrent shared write=[]"]
  H["HPP TARGET voice primary<br/>central ingress/custody<br/>Task Engine/AX"]
  R["Sole file reconciler<br/>нҢҢмқј ledgerл§Ң"]
  E["Sole TaskEngine coordinator<br/>logical authorityлі„ command"]
  MC["HPP mail_classification_coordinator<br/>assignment event+outbox"]
  MP["HPP project_history_projector<br/>five-lane sole normal CSV/ICS/XLSX writer"]
  MF["dormant project_history_emergency_fallback<br/>explicit failover only"]
  Q["immutable packet<br/>producer+sequence+digest"]

  W --> Q
  P --> Q
  T --> Q
  D --> Q
  Q --> N --> R
  Q --> E
  M -->|"failover voice events only"| Q
  Q --> H
  Q --> MC --> MP
  MF -. "lease/epoch м—Ҷмңјл©ҙ write 0" .-> MC
  R -. "typed file/source relation" .-> E
  R -. "task write к¶Ңн•ң м—ҶмқҢ" .-> E
```

| logical role | primary мұ…мһ„ | н—Ҳмҡ© write | кё°ліё м°ЁлӢЁ |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `work_pc` | мӢӨм ң м—…л¬ҙВ·project worksite | н•ҙлӢ№ taskмқҳ `_workspaces/<project>`, `_workmeta/<project>` | gateway/night watch/task auto-apply |
| `portable_dev_pc` | мқҙлҸҷ мҲҳм§‘В·public к°ңл°ң | public bounded branch, approved metadata | operational primary |
| `tool_pc` | heavy build/test/tool-bound work | approved project runкіј public dev lane | always-on job мһҗлҸҷ мҠ№кІ© |
| `dev_worker_pc` | immutable task packet мҲҳн–ү | м§Җм • branch/allowed paths | main merge, private мӣҗл¬ё, мҡҙмҳҒ writer |
| `always_on_node` | checkpoint, queue, healer, кІҪлҹү мҡҙмҳҒ | `guild_hall/state`, selected `private-state` | public auto commit/push, TaskEngine coordinator мһҗлҸҷ кІёмһ„ |
| sole file reconciler | file packet м •л ¬В·мӨ‘ліө/м¶©лҸҢ нҢҗм • | file activity ledger/projection | ERP task mutation |
| sole TaskEngine coordinator | candidate/decision/apply commandмқҳ мң мқјн•ң SQLite writeмҷҖ apply transaction | Driver ledger + task reservation/event/current/receipt | source payload/RAG truth/file ledger мҲҳм • |
| Mac temporary voice failover | HPP unavailable/cutover м „ voice payload/session/source-event мғқмӮ°; мқҙнӣ„ source HOLD/outboxВ·monitor | active failover leaseмқҳ voice owner surface, alert candidate | HPPмҷҖ лҸҷмӢң shared write, central custody, normal mail/project-history write |
| HPP TARGET `voice_operational_primary` | cutover л’Ө shared voice session/queue/library, ASR/context processingмқҳ лӢЁмқј normal writer | voice owner surfaceмҷҖ accepted HPP custody API | exact binding/receipt м „ activation, Macкіј лҸҷмӢң write, owner мҠ№мқё м—ҶлҠ” NAS mutation |
| HPP `mail_classification_coordinator` | mail occurrence/assignment current+event+outbox atomic commit | dev-ERP mail coordination tables only | file projection, Driver/task/current/receipt tables, raw source write |
| HPP `project_history_projector` | mail outboxмҷҖ лӮҳлЁём§Җ lane accepted manifestлҘј н”„лЎңм қнҠёлі„ CSV/XLSXлЎң sole normal publish; mail ICS мң м§Җ | five project-history views | classification/event/task/source mutation |
| HPP `transfer_service` | authenticated HTTPS upload/download, quarantine/inbox acceptance, hash/readback/finalize | HPP quarantine/inbox binary only | project binding, client-supplied path, direct SMB, task/history mutation |
| HPP `promoter` | accepted artifact revisionмқҳ approved project storage bindingкіј rollback receipt | HPP project binding only | quarantine intake, projector/task/source mutation, delete without retention approval |
| dormant `project_history_emergency_fallback` | explicit failover leaseм—җм„ңл§Ң five-lane projector; mail coordinatorлҠ” coverage+лі„лҸ„ мҠ№мқё лІ”мң„ | active epoch allowlist only | automatic promotion/failback, voice identity reuse, ERP task write |

мң„ м—ӯн• мқҖ `TARGET` logical identitiesлӢӨ. Public кі„м•Ҫл§ҢмңјлЎң нҳ„мһ¬ live bindingмқ„ м¶”лЎ н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
accepted C00Q tool л’Ө P0/C00Bм—җм„ң local identity/lease ownerлҘј opaque metadataлЎң нҷ•мқён•ҳкі  D21~D23 owner кІ°м •мқҙ м—Ҷмңјл©ҙ лӘЁл‘җ
feature OFFлӢӨ.

HPP outage мӨ‘ clientлҠ” durable local outboxлҘј `HOLD`лЎң мң м§Җн•ҳкұ°лӮҳ last-accepted generationмқ„ read-onlyлЎң
ліёлӢӨ. HPP drive/UNC/SMB mount, copied SQLite/WAL/SHM, alternate central queue лҳҗлҠ” split writerлЎң ліөкө¬н•ҳм§Җ
м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. Reconnect л’Ө ticket/grant/revisionмқ„ лӢӨмӢң кІҖмҰқн•ҳкі  idempotent replayн•ҳл©° ack м „ local stateлҘј
compactн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

### 11.2 immutable packet

Packet мөңмҶҢ field:

```yaml
packet_schema: soulforge.node_packet.v1
producer_node_ref: <opaque-logical-ref>
producer_account_ref: <opaque-account-ref-or-null>
producer_role: <allowed-role>
packet_kind: file_observation|work_session_event|run_receipt|other-approved-metadata
sequence: <monotonic-integer>
created_at: <strict-utc>
project_ref: <typed-ref>
task_assignment_ref: <typed-ref-or-null>
work_session_ref: <typed-ref-or-null>
source_revision_refs: []
intent_or_file_event_refs: []
payload_digest: sha256:<64hex>
previous_packet_digest: <digest-or-null>
signature_or_attestation_ref: <opaque-ref>
```

ReconcilerлҠ” `(producer,sequence,digest)` duplicateлҘј no-op, к°ҷмқҖ sequenceмқҳ лӢӨлҘё digestлҘј quarantine,
gapмқ„ alert candidateлЎң л§Ңл“ лӢӨ. Packet лҸ„м°©мқҖ source мҠ№мқё, task мҠ№мқё, writer мҠ№кІ©мқ„ лң»н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
PacketмқҖ metadata refл§Ң мҡҙл°ҳн•ңлӢӨ. Payload upload transport, storage custody/promotion acknowledgement,
history projection receiptлҠ” м„ңлЎң лӢӨлҘё contractмқҙл©° packet receiptлЎң bytes мҠ№кІ©мқ„ м¶”лЎ н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

Personal outboxмқҳ server receipt statusлҠ” `accepted|duplicate|held_gap|quarantined|rejected`лӢӨ. ClientлҠ”
eventлҘј durable local outboxм—җ кё°лЎқн•ң л’Ө ліҙлӮј мҲҳ мһҲкі , server receipt ID/digest/statusлҘј кІҖмҰқВ·durable
м ҖмһҘн•ң л’Өм—җл§Ң н•ҙлӢ№ entryлҘј compactн•ңлӢӨ. Server commit л’Ө client ack м „ crash/rebootлҠ” к°ҷмқҖ
session/sequence/digestлҘј мһ¬м „мҶЎн•ҙ `duplicate` receiptлҘј л°ӣм•„м•ј н•ңлӢӨ. Same sequenceмқҳ лӢӨлҘё digestмҷҖ
gapмқҖ projectionмқ„ м „м§„мӢңнӮӨм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. Exact outbox path, encryption, fsync/retentionкіј stale/missing SLAлҠ”
D28 м „ `VERIFY_HP`мқҙкі , GitВ·CSV/XLSXлҘј outboxлӮҳ live transportлЎң мӮ¬мҡ©н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

### 11.2A TaskEngine runtime binding control plane

Public contractлҠ”
`ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/docs/contracts/task_engine_runtime_binding.v1.schema.json`, local instanceлҠ”
`guild_hall/state/local/task_engine_runtime_binding.yaml`мқҙлӢӨ. Local нҢҢмқјмқҖ Gitм—җ л„Јм§Җ м•Ҡкі  secret,
raw root, hostnameмқ„ лӢҙм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. лӢӨмқҢ fieldлҘј лӘЁл‘җ schemaк°Җ кІҖмҰқн•ңлӢӨ.

```yaml
schema_version: soulforge.task_engine_runtime_binding.v1
binding_revision_id: <typed-revision-ref>
mode: off|pilot|production
node_identity_ref: <opaque-typed-ref>
runtime_commit: <40hex>
runtime_tree_digest: sha256:<64hex>
coordinator_identity_ref: <opaque-typed-ref-or-null-for-off>
logical_authority_refs: []
reconciler_identity_ref: <opaque-typed-ref-or-null-for-off>
project_allowlist: []
route_allowlist: []
not_before: <strict-utc>
expires_at: <strict-utc>
issued_at: <strict-utc>
owner_approval_ref: <opaque-ref>
previous_binding_digest: <sha256-or-null>
revokes_binding_digest: <sha256-or-null>
binding_digest: sha256:<64hex>
```

`mode=off`лҠ” allowlistк°Җ лӘЁл‘җ л№„м–ҙм•ј н•ңлӢӨ. `pilot`мқҖ project н•ң к°ң, лӘ…мӢң route, ownerк°Җ м •н•ң м§§мқҖ
expiryк°Җ н•„мҲҳлӢӨ. `production`лҸ„ л¬ҙкё°н•ң bindingмқҙ м•„лӢҲл©° G01 owner approvalкіј lease expiryлҘј к°Җм§„лӢӨ.
DigestлҠ” мһҗкё° мһҗмӢ мқ„ м ңмҷён•ң canonical objectлЎң кі„мӮ°н•ңлӢӨ. Missing, malformed, digest mismatch,
not-yet-valid, expired, revoked, runtime commit/tree mismatch, node/coordinator mismatchлҠ” лӘЁл‘җ
default-denyлӢӨ.

C08F/P8мқҖ operational identityлӮҳ leaseлҘј л°ңкёүн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҖ мұ„ к°ҷмқҖ parserлҘј мӮ¬мҡ©н•ҳлҠ” м„ё consumerлҘј
public schemaВ·synthetic fixtureВ·feature-OFF лІ”мң„м—җм„ң лЁјм Җ л§Ңл“ лӢӨ.

1. `tools/task_engine_runtime_binding.mjs`лҠ” кё°ліё dry-runмқҙл©° candidateлҘј schema кІҖмҰқн•ң л’Ө
   `--apply --expected-current-digest <digest-or-null> --owner-approval-ref <opaque>`м—җм„ңл§Ң exact local
   pathм—җ м“ҙлӢӨ. Sibling temp write+flush+platform-tested atomic replaceлҘј мӮ¬мҡ©н•ҳкі  CASк°Җ лӢӨлҘҙл©ҙ old
   fileмқ„ к·ёлҢҖлЎң л‘”лӢӨ.
2. `server.mjs`лҠ” write requestл§ҲлӢӨ bindingмқ„ мғҲлЎң мқҪм–ҙ route/project/identity/expiryлҘј кІҖмӮ¬н•ҳкі ,
   `TaskEngineTransactionCoordinator`лҠ” `BEGIN IMMEDIATE` м§Ғнӣ„мҷҖ commit м§Ғм „м—җ к°ҷмқҖ binding revision
   digestлҘј лӢӨмӢң кІҖмӮ¬н•ңлӢӨ. OFF replacement/revocationмқҖ мғҲ transactionмқ„ л§үкі , commit м „ mismatchлҠ”
   rollbackн•ңлӢӨ. Bindingмқ„ process-lifetime cacheн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмңјлҜҖлЎң updateм—җ restartк°Җ н•„мҡ”н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлӢӨ.
3. `runtime_release_audit.mjs`лҠ” `--task-engine-binding <path> --expected-task-engine-mode
   off|pilot|production`мқ„ л°ӣм•„ к°ҷмқҖ loader кІ°кіј, runtime commit/tree, role identityлҘј кІҖмҰқн•ңлӢӨ.

кұ°л¶Җ envelopeмқҖ missing/off/expired/revoked `423 binding_not_active`, malformed/digest mismatch
`503 binding_invalid`, project/route mismatch `403 binding_scope_violation`, CAS м¶©лҸҢ
`409 binding_revision_conflict`лЎң кі м •н•ңлӢӨ. Loader/auditк°Җ нҢҢмқјмқ„ м—ҙ мҲҳ м—Ҷмқ„ л•Ң fallback modeлӮҳ нҷҳкІҪ
ліҖмҲҳ grantлҘј л§Ңл“Өм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. C09DлҠ” OFF revisionл§Ң, C10мқҖ fresh owner-approved pilot revisionкіј мў…лЈҢ
OFF revisionл§Ң, G00/G01мқҖ мқҙнӣ„ лі„лҸ„ promotion revisionл§Ң мқҙ writerлЎң л§Ңл“ лӢӨ.

### 11.2B Project-history process lock, mail owner lease, fencing, failover/failback

**Claim ceiling вҖ” `TARGET`, plan-owned proposed contract.** мқҙ м Ҳмқҳ `HPP`, л‘җ logical identity, lock
мқҙлҰ„, durable lease/CAS owner, `classification_epoch`В·`projector_epoch`, emergency fallback,
`EвҶ’E+1вҶ’E+2` failover/failback м Ҳм°ЁлҠ” нҳ„мһ¬ кө¬нҳ„мқҙлӮҳ кё°мЎҙ public canonмқ„ кё°мҲ н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. Public
sourceлҠ” generic PC-role л¶„лҰ¬, HPP target/Mac temporary-failover voice лІ”мң„, current multi-writer gapл§Ң л’·л°ӣм№Ён•ңлӢӨ.
`HPP`лҠ” owner-designated high-performance-PC logical host candidateмқҙл©° live bindingмқҖ
`UNKNOWN/VERIFY_HP`лӢӨ. D21~D23 owner кІ°м •, кҙҖл Ё public contract sync, C08B/P10 Level 3 evidence
м „м—җлҠ” м–ҙлҠҗ PCм—җлҸ„ mail/project-history authorityВ·leaseВ·role switchВ·failover/failbackмқ„ л¶Җм—¬н•ҳкұ°лӮҳ
мҷ„лЈҢлЎң мЈјмһҘн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

Mail coordinatorмҷҖ five-lane `project_history_projector`лҠ” **roleлі„ host-local lock**кіј
owner-controlled cross-node leaseлҘј лӘЁл‘җ мҡ”кө¬н•ңлӢӨ. `mail_classification_coordinator.lock`мқҖ DB command
process н•ҳлӮҳ, `project_history_projector.lock`мқҖ лӢӨм„Ҝ lane м „мІҙмқҳ file projector process н•ҳлӮҳл§Ң мһЎлҠ”лӢӨ.
Laneлі„ lockмқҖ л§Ңл“Өм§Җ м•ҠмңјлҜҖлЎң н•ң PC м•Ҳм—җм„ңлҸ„ л‘җ projectorк°Җ м„ңлЎң лӢӨлҘё laneмқ„ н•‘кі„лЎң к°ҷмқҖ
project-history treeлҘј лҸҷмӢңм—җ м“ё мҲҳ м—ҶлӢӨ. Cross-node leaseлҠ” logical roleл§ҲлӢӨ н•ҳлӮҳлӢӨ. Classification
leaseмқҳ monotonic counterлҠ” `classification_epoch=C_n`, projector leaseмқҳ counterлҠ”
`projector_epoch=P_n`мқҙл©° м„ңлЎң лҸ…лҰҪмқҙлӢӨ. н•ң мҡҙмҳҒ generationмқҳ fence мғҒнғңлҘј
`E_n=(C_n,P_n)` vectorлЎң н‘ңкё°н•  лҝҗ `C_n=P_n`мқ„ мҡ”кө¬н•ҳкұ°лӮҳ л‘җ к°’мқ„ н•ң н•„л“ңлЎң н•©м№ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
Projector leaseмқҳ project/lane allowlistк°Җ мҠ№мқё лІ”мң„лҘј мўҒнһҢлӢӨ.

к°Ғ leaseлҠ” logical role, node identity, project scope, `not_before`, `expires_at`, role epoch,
previous/revoked digest, approver refлҘј к°Җм§„лӢӨ. нҷҳкІҪліҖмҲҳлӮҳ hostnameмңјлЎң roleмқ„ м¶”м •н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
Assignment event/outboxмқҳ origin `classification_epoch`лҠ” projectorк°Җ л°”лҖҢм–ҙлҸ„ мҲҳм •н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
ProjectorлҠ” claim/publish л•Ң мһҗкё° `projector_epoch`лҘј лі„лҸ„ columnкіј manifestм—җ кё°лЎқн•ңлӢӨ. Mail manifestлҠ”
`accepted_event_cutoff`, `source_epoch_digest`, `max_classification_epoch`, `projector_epoch`, row count,
ordered digestлҘј к°Җм§„лӢӨ. C09/D21мқҖ C10 м „м—җ durable lease ownerмҷҖ л‘җ roleмқҳ exact CAS record/pathлҘј
