кІ°м •н•ҙм•ј н•ҳл©°, placeholder мғҒнғңм—җм„ңлҠ” pilotлҸ„ мӢңмһ‘н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

лӢӨмқҢ кІҪкі„лҠ” **лӘЁл‘җ** мһҗкё° roleмқҳ current leaseмҷҖ epochлҘј мһ¬кІҖмҰқн•ҳкі  stale epochлҘј кұ°л¶Җн•ңлӢӨ.

1. classification DB transaction мӢңмһ‘ м§Ғнӣ„мҷҖ commit м§Ғм „: active `classification_epoch`
2. outbox claim/reclaim/update: active `projector_epoch`мҷҖ immutable origin `classification_epoch`
3. CSV/ICS/XLSX staged-generation manifest мғқм„ұ: active `projector_epoch`мҷҖ canonical `source_epoch_digest`
4. parity validator м§Ғм „кіј final atomic publish м§Ғм „: к°ҷмқҖ projector epoch, cutoff, source-epoch digest
5. publish receiptмҷҖ mail outbox completion лҳҗлҠ” non-mail accepted-manifest completion кё°лЎқ: active projector epoch

Recovery reclaimмқҖ кё°мЎҙ `claimed_projector_epoch` leaseк°Җ revokedмқҙкі , rowк°Җ freeze checkpoint мқҙм „м—җ
commitлҗҗмңјл©°, accepted publish receipt/manifestк°Җ м—Ҷмқ„ л•Ңл§Ң `claimed(P_old)вҶ’claimed(P_new)` CASлҘј н—Ҳмҡ©н•ңлӢӨ.
мқҙлҜё `published`мқҙкі  manifest digestк°Җ accepted receiptмҷҖ мқјм№ҳн•ҳл©ҙ мғҲ publish м—Ҷмқҙ same-generation no-opмқҙлӢӨ.
Digestк°Җ лӢӨлҘҙкұ°лӮҳ partial stageл§Ң лӮЁм•ҳмңјл©ҙ quarantine нӣ„ publish OFFлЎң л©Ҳм¶ҳлӢӨ.

м •мғҒ HPP vectorлҘј `E=(C_E,P_E)`лқјкі  н•  л•Ң manual failoverлҠ” лӢӨмқҢ мҲңм„ңл§Ң н—Ҳмҡ©н•ңлӢӨ.

```text
freeze HPP mail classification + five-lane projector
  -> checkpoint mail DB/outbox and all five view generations; prove parity at (C_E,P_E)
  -> revoke C_E and P_E leases
  -> fallback shadow catch-up/replay for approved lanes (publish OFF)
  -> issue durable E+1=(C_E+1,P_E+1) role records
  -> promote mail classification at C_E+1 only if D23 coverage+approval exists;
     otherwise keep C_E+1 disabled/revoked and record partial/not_collected gap
  -> parity/readback
  -> promote five-lane projector at P_E+1 with an exact lane allowlist
  -> recover an old C_E outbox only when it was committed at/before the freeze checkpoint and
     the lease carries recovery_from_classification_epoch=C_E; claim/publish records P_E+1
  -> prove stale C_E DB writes and stale P_E outbox/stage/final-publish rejection
```

Manual failbackлҸ„ мһҗлҸҷ мҠ№кІ©мқҙ м•„лӢҲлқј мғҲ vector `E+2=(C_E+2,P_E+2)`лҘј м“ҙлӢӨ. C_E+1мқҙ disabledмҳҖм–ҙлҸ„
к·ё durable fence recordлҘј кұҙл„Ҳлӣ°кұ°лӮҳ мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ©н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

```text
freeze fallback at (C_E+1,P_E+1)
  -> checkpoint/parity and revoke both role records
  -> HPP shadow catch-up/replay for all approved lanes (publish OFF)
  -> issue C_E+2 and P_E+2; promote HPP mail classification first at C_E+2
  -> parity/readback
  -> promote HPP five-lane projector second at P_E+2
  -> prove stale C_E/C_E+1 DB writes and P_E/P_E+1 outbox/all-lane publish rejection
```

мһҗлҸҷ failoverВ·мһҗлҸҷ failbackмқҖ м—ҶлӢӨ. Macмқҳ м ңн•ңлҗң mail accessлҠ” `coverage.state=partial|not_collected`
gapмқ„ лӮј мҲҳ мһҲмқ„ лҝҗ м „мІҙ л¶Җмһ¬лҘј нҷ•м •н•ҳкұ°лӮҳ normal projector leaseлҘј м–»м§Җ лӘ»н•ңлӢӨ. Emergency identityк°Җ
five-lane projector leaseлҘј л°ӣлҚ”лқјлҸ„ voice identityк°Җ мҠ№кІ©лҗҳлҠ” кІғмқҙ м•„лӢҲкі  ERP task writeлҠ” кі„мҶҚ 0мқҙлӢӨ. RTO/RPO, lease
issuer/revoker, failover approverмҷҖ fallback coverageлҠ” D21~D23мқҙ кІ°м •н•ңлӢӨ.

### 11.3 л°°нҸ¬В·alertВ·ліөкө¬

л°°нҸ¬ мҲңм„ң:

1. clean mainм—җм„ң code/tests/docsлҘј bounded sliceлЎң publishн•ңлӢӨ.
2. feature OFF мғҒнғңлЎң synthetic schema/replayлҘј нҶөкіјн•ңлӢӨ.
3. C09R backup мғқм„ұкіј isolated restore drillмқҙ validм—¬м•ј runtime ліҖкІҪмқ„ н—Ҳмҡ©н•ңлӢӨ.
4. C09Dм—җм„ң approved runtime artifactлҘј pinned revisionмңјлЎң л°°нҸ¬н•ҳкі  source/data bindingмқ„ лі„лҸ„
   attestн•ҳлҗҳ лӘЁл“  TaskEngine writer/route/jobмқҖ feature OFFлЎң л‘”лӢӨ.
5. C09L contract-owned source/knowledge metadata receiptмҷҖ C09D feature-OFF deployment receipt л’Ө C10 one-project pilotм—җм„ң
   coordinatorлҘј м§§кІҢ мјңкі  мҰүмӢң OFFлЎң
   лҗҳлҸҢлҰҙ мҲҳ мһҲм–ҙм•ј н•ңлӢӨ.
6. G00м—җм„ң public contractмҷҖ local bindingмқ„ feature-OFFлЎң кІҖмҰқн•ңлӢӨ.
7. full validationкіј лі„лҸ„ G01 owner мҠ№мқё л’Өм—җл§Ң operational-primary bindingмқ„ нҷңм„ұнҷ”н•ңлӢӨ.

AlertлҠ” мғҒнғң ліҖнҷ”к°Җ мһҲмқ„ л•Ңл§Ң нӣ„ліҙлҘј л§Ңл“Өкі  cooldown, weekend, recovery clockмқ„ к°Җм§„лӢӨ.
н•„мҲҳ alert codeлҠ” `writer_not_primary`, `packet_conflict`, `packet_gap`, `replay_mismatch`,
`backup_stale`, `restore_invalid`, `projection_mutation`, `cross_project_violation`мқҙлӢӨ. Alert channelкіј
мӢӨм ң м „мҶЎмқҖ V14 м „м—җлҠ” OFFлӢӨ.

Recovery мҲңм„ң:

1. target writer/scanner/scheduler/alert OFF
2. queue intake freezeмҷҖ last good checkpoint кі м •
3. DB/RAG/packet digestмҷҖ runtime/source/data attestation read-only л№„көҗ
4. valid backupмқ„ лі„лҸ„ мң„м№ҳм—җ restoreн•ҳкі  schema/replayлҘј м§„лӢЁн•ңлӢӨ. Commitлҗң eventк°Җ мһҲлҠ” live DBлҘј
   мқҙ ліөкө¬ліёмңјлЎң мҰүмӢң лҚ®м–ҙм“°м§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
5. мқҪмқ„ мҲҳ мһҲлҠ” live historyк°Җ мһҲмңјл©ҙ reversal/current rebuildлЎң old readerлҘј ліөмӣҗн•ңлӢӨ. DB мһ¬лӮңмқҙл©ҙ
   current DB/WAL/SHM кІ©лҰ¬мҷҖ event exportвҶ’restoreвҶ’re-import кІҖмҰқмқ„ лЁјм Җ мҷ„лЈҢн•ңлӢӨ.
6. event history ліҙмЎҙкіј current parity нҷ•мқё
7. ownerк°Җ operational-primary/failoverлҘј лӘ…мӢңм ҒмңјлЎң мһ¬м§Җм •

Ingress/access rollbackмқҖ binding/writer OFFвҶ’queue freezeмҷҖ affected item quarantineвҶ’prior accepted pointer
мң м§Җ мҲңм„ңлӢӨ. OneDrive workspaceм—җм„ң HPP custodyлЎң reverse-copyн•ҙ ліөкө¬н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. лҜёлһҳ binding switchлҸ„
copy+hash+readbackмқ„ лЁјм Җ мҷ„лЈҢн•ҳкі  exact receiptк°Җ acceptedлҗң л’Өм—җл§Ң pointerлҘј м „нҷҳн•ңлӢӨ. Retention/legal
hold owner approval м—ҶлҠ” deleteлҠ” rollback лӢЁкі„м—җм„ңлҸ„ кёҲм§Җн•ңлӢӨ.

FailoverлҠ” мһҗлҸҷ мҠ№кІ©н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. failover nodeк°Җ к°ҷмқҖ physical machineмқҙм–ҙлҸ„ лі„лҸ„ identity, clean
operational clone, valid checkpoint, writer lease/attestationмқ„ к°Җм ём•ј н•ңлӢӨ.

## 12. кө¬нҳ„ slice/WBSВ·dependency DAGВ·critical path

Full YAML packetл§Ң лі„лҸ„ мҠ№мқё к°ҖлҠҘн•ң мөңмҶҢ мӢӨн–ү лӢЁмң„лӢӨ. Phase cardлҠ” мҲңм„ңмҷҖ лҜёлһҳ scopeлҘј кі м •н•ҳлҠ”
л№„мӢӨн–ү routeлӢӨ. effortлҠ” `S/M/L`, riskлҠ” `low/medium/high`мқҳ мғҒлҢҖк°’мқҙл©° лӮ м§ң м•ҪмҶҚмқҙ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ.
`C`лҠ” core, `G`лҠ” activation gate, `AX/AR/IQ/ML`мқҖ нӣ„мҶҚ phaseлӢӨ.

### 12.0 Authoritative P0~P10 phase override

мқҙ н‘ңк°Җ м•„лһҳм—җ ліҙмЎҙлҗң кё°мЎҙ C-cardмқҳ phase/depends-onліҙлӢӨ мҡ°м„ н•ңлӢӨ. кё°мЎҙ mixed cardлҠ” **к·ёлҢҖлЎң
мӢӨн–ү к°ҖлҠҘн•ң task packetмқҙ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ**. к°Ғ н–үм—җ м§Җм •лҗң sub-actionл§Ң н•ҙлӢ№ phaseм—җм„ң н—Ҳмҡ©н•ҳл©°, к°ҷмқҖ
card м•Ҳмқҳ later-phase DB/API/writer/runtime actionмқҖ к·ё phase acceptance receiptк°Җ мғқкёё л•Ңк№Ңм§Җ write
allowlistм—җм„ң м ңмҷён•ңлӢӨ.

| phase | required acceptance | phase route / future slice action | explicitly blocked until later |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| P0 | baseline/source-owner inventory receipt | `C00A` public blocker preflight вҶ’ `C00Q` public/synthetic query-tool foundation вҶ’ `C00B` separately authorized query-only inventory | exact C00Q child packet л°–мқҳ code, schema/DB/path materialization, task discovery м „л¶Җ |
| P1 | five-lane envelope+coverage+replay/export receipt | `H00вҶ’H01/H02/H03/H04/H05вҶ’H06` | typed business relation, RAG, task candidate/Driver/ERP write |
| P2 | ID/ref/clock crosswalk/packet identity receipt | `C01A` typed identity only + `C08A` immutable packet identity only | SourceRevision materialization, Wiki, TaskDriver, runtime binding foundation/lease activation |
| P3 | immutable revision/relation lineage receipt | `C06A` source/file/artifact/relation only | RAG/Wiki indexing, context acceptance, discovery |
| P4 | exact revision-bound RAG/Wiki receipt | `C05` resolver + `C06B` Wiki/source lineage only | task discovery, Driver, ERP writer |
| P5 | deterministic `context_acceptance_gate` receipt | `C07A` context assembly/coverage validation only | P6 discovery until receipt accepted |
| P6 | candidate-only discovery acceptance | `C04A` source adaptersвҶ’TaskIntent candidate, ERP write `0` | P7 TaskDriver until P6 receipt accepted |
| P7 | TaskDriver authority/idempotency acceptance | `C01B` pure TaskDriver contract | P8 schema/outbox/ERP writer until P7 receipt accepted |
| P8 | sole-writer/atomicity/mail-outbox/binding-foundation acceptance | parallel `C02` + `C08F`, then `C03вҶ’C04B`: feature-OFF binding loader, mail assignment/outbox, five-lane projector and ERP persistence | local pilot binding, live role/lease/failover, life-tree pilot |
| P9 | one-project pilot + rollback + read-only tree receipt | `C09A/C09/C09L/C09R/C09D/C10` + `C07B` feedback/life-tree | multi-project/live roles/failover/AX/AgentRun/ML |
| P10 | separate owner approval per capability | `C08B`, `G00/G01`, `C09S`, `AX01/AR01/IQ01/ML01` | any unapproved capability or automatic failback |

#### 12.0A IngressВ·queryВ·personal lifecycle side-card DAG

м•„лһҳ side-cardмқҳ **P0~P9** `Pn` н–үмқҖ core `Pn` acceptance л’Ө, `P(n+1)` м „ мӢӨн–үн•  мҲҳ мһҲлӢӨлҠ” лң»мқҙлӢӨ.
к°ҷмқҖ core phaseмқҳ acceptanceм—җ нҸ¬н•Ёлҗҳкұ°лӮҳ кё°мЎҙ P edgeлҘј л°”кҫёкұ°лӮҳ `P(n+1)`мқ„ unlockн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
P10мқҖ aggregate core acceptanceлӮҳ P11мқҙ м—ҶмңјлҜҖлЎң мҳҲмҷёлӢӨ. I10/Q10/W10мқҖ accepted P9 л’Ө к°Ғк°Ғ лҸ…лҰҪлҗң
capability-specific owner approvalВ·Level 3 gateлЎң мӢӨн–үн•ҳл©° м„ңлЎңлҘј unlockн•ҳкұ°лӮҳ н•ҳлӮҳмқҳ P10 receiptлЎң
н•©м№ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. `I`лҠ” ingress/promotion, `Q`лҠ” accepted query, `W`лҠ” personal WorkSessionмқҙлӢӨ.

| phase | ingress `I` side-card | query/knowledge `Q` side-card | WorkSession `W` side-card |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| P0 | I0 source-kind custody/staging/quarantine/promoter inventory | Q0 tool/route/ACL/generation/consumer inventory | W0 current one-shot writer/callerмҷҖ thread/node capability inventory |
| P1 | I1 H01 attachmentмҷҖ H04 ERP/chat/MCP upload receiptк°Җ payload promotionмқҙ м•„лӢҳмқ„ кі м • | Q1 accepted-generation+audit snapshot schema | W1 H03лҠ” current bounded one-shot occurrenceл§Ң мҲҳмҡ©; lifecycle completenessлЎң H03/H06мқ„ л§үм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ |
| P2 | I2 storage-binding/operation/packet typed identity | Q2 actor/project/scope/generation/cursor typed identity | W2 node+account+assignment/session packet identity fixture; local outbox physical path м—ҶмқҢ |
| P3 | I3 sourceвҶ’bindingвҶ’promotion/derived-revision lineage | Q3 exact revision/locator/claim response schema | W3 session evidence/artifact typed refs only |
| P4 | I4 promoted revisionмқҳ RAG/Wiki eligibility gate | Q4 project/common resolver+explicit ACL+no-fallback contract | W4 session queryлҠ” accepted exact knowledge refл§Ң мӮ¬мҡ© |
| P5 | I5 contextлҠ” accepted revision/promotion refл§Ң мҶҢл№„ | Q5 accepted task-context query receipt | W5 exact assignment/context binding design input |
| P6 | I6 classification/uploadлҠ” candidate-only, task row delta 0 | Q6 candidate-only team knowledge submission contract | W6 closeout/proposalлҸ„ candidate-onlyлқјлҠ” pure fixture |
| P7 | I7 Driver provenanceм—җ promotion receipt exact ref | Q7 Driver provenance read projection | W7 closeoutвҶ’Driver candidate link contract, official completion л¶„лҰ¬ |
| P8 | I8 feature-OFF promoter/receipt/authority-separation contract | Q8 feature-OFF ERP UI/MCP adapters+atomic accepted pointer/API-file parity | W8 schema/API fixture м„Өкі„л§Ң; core P8 acceptanceлӮҳ writer к¶Ңн•ңм—җ нҸ¬н•Ён•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ |
| P9 | I9 н•ң project promotion/copy/readback/rollback pilot | Q9 one-project ACL/parity/no-fallback pilot | W9 core C10 PASS л’Ө AX-G1 design review; м•„м§Ғ live personal write м—ҶмқҢ |
| P10 | I10 scan/ACL/retention/backupВ·production promoter лі„лҸ„ activation | Q10 UI query/MCP query/candidate submitмқ„ capabilityлі„ лі„лҸ„ activation | W10 н•өмӢ¬ AX-G1вҶ’AX-G2вҶ’AX-G3 direct baselineкіј м„ нғқ EXT-G0вҶ’EXT-G1вҶ’ORCA-T1/ORCA-T2В·HERMES-T1 лҸ…лҰҪ trialвҶ’team rolloutмқ„ к°Ғк°Ғ лі„лҸ„ мҠ№мқё |

I8/Q8мқҖ feature-OFF synthetic contractмқј лҝҗ exact physical path, service binding, live data, node leaseлҘј
л§Ңл“Өм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. W lifecycleмқҖ P1 historyлӮҳ core P8мқҳ м„ н–үмЎ°кұҙмқҙ м•„лӢҲл©° кё°мЎҙ AX gateлҘј м•һлӢ№кё°м§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

P10 external surfaceлҠ” н•өмӢ¬ AX-G1~G3 кІҪлЎңлҘј м°ЁлӢЁн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ” м„ нғқнҳ• sibling branchлӢӨ. `EXT-G0` л№„көҗмҷҖ
`EXT-G1` generic negative contract л’Ө `ORCA-T1`кіј `HERMES-T1`мқ„ л”°лЎң мӢ¬мӮ¬н•ҳкі , Orca нҷ•лҢҖлҠ” лӢӨмӢң
`ORCA-T2`лЎң л¶„лҰ¬н•ңлӢӨ. н•ң trialмқҖ лӢӨлҘё trial, AR01, IQ/ML, production activation лҳҗлҠ” team rolloutмқ„
unlockн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. Tool-native completionмқҖ candidate evidenceмқҙкі  TaskEngine official completionмқҖ лі„лҸ„лӢӨ.

`A8-SYNTH`лҠ” public/pathless/feature-OFF secure-access contractВ·fixture side-cardлӢӨ. D27~D29мҷҖ exact public
security child packet prerequisiteк°Җ acceptedлҗҳл©ҙ core P8кіј л¬ҙкҙҖн•ҳкІҢ лҸ…лҰҪ мӢӨн–үн•  мҲҳ мһҲлӢӨ. One-time device
enrollment/mTLS verifier вҶ’ OS-protected broker refresh вҶ’ human/device/agent/task-object-action delegation
intersection вҶ’ upload/download ticket verifierл§Ң н•©м„ұ кІҖмҰқн•ҳл©° P1, TaskEngine, P8, P9 лҳҗлҠ” I/Q/W live
bindingмқ„ unlockн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

нҳ„мһ¬ source foundationмқҖ `tools/a8_synth_secure_access.mjs`, strict packet/output schemaмҷҖ focused testлЎң
мЎҙмһ¬н•ңлӢӨ. 7мў… source custody, transfer/finalize/range, WorkSession crash/ack/handoff, ACL/RAG/cache/redactionмқ„
кі„мӮ°н•ҳлҠ” 60-ID public fixture receiptлҘј л§Ңл“Ө мҲҳ мһҲм§Җл§Ң, fixtureмқҳ external bindingмқҖ
`synthetic_fixture_only`, `owner_acceptance=false`лӢӨ. л”°лқјм„ң focused PASSлҠ” implementation evidenceмқј лҝҗ
D27~D29 owner acceptanceлӮҳ formal A8-SYNTH acceptanceк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ.

`A8-CANARY`лҠ” мІ« live implementationмқҙлӢӨ. `A8-SYNTH PASS` + accepted private `VERIFY_HP` exact binding
receipt + strict private office-LAN binding + explicit owner approvalмҷҖ Level 3 live gateк°Җ лӘЁл‘җ мһҲм–ҙм•ј н•ңлӢӨ.
к·ё л’Өм—җлҸ„ one seatВ·one projectВ·one small fileм—җм„ң
`enrollвҶ’prepare uploadвҶ’HTTPS transferвҶ’hash/readbackвҶ’idempotent finalize receipt/revisionвҶ’queryвҶ’exact revision
downloadвҶ’optional validated redacted derivative/XLSX`л§Ң мҲҳн–үн•ңлӢӨ. VPN/Tailscale/remote lane, mail/voice bulk,
team/production activationкіј core phase unlockмқҖ `0`мқҙлӢӨ.

#### 12.0.1 Packet executability claim ceiling

`READY_FOR_OWNER_REVIEW`лҠ” м•„лһҳ phase orderмҷҖ мІ« мҠ№мқё м„ нғқмқ„ кІҖнҶ н•  мӨҖл№„к°Җ лҗҗлӢӨлҠ” лң»мқҙм§Җ, лӘЁл“  н–үмқҙ
кө¬нҳ„ мҠ№мқё к°ҖлҠҘн•ң packetмқҙлқјлҠ” лң»мқҙ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ.

| surface | нҳ„мһ¬ packet мғҒнғң | write лҳҗлҠ” ratification м „ н•„мҲҳ мЎ°кұҙ |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `C00` parent | `routing_only_non_executable` | `C00AвҶ’C00QвҶ’C00B` мҷё action мғҒмҶҚ кёҲм§Җ; P0 acceptanceлҠ” C00B PASS н•ҳлӮҳлҝҗ |
| `C00A` | `historical_blocker_receipt_retained` | accepted `BLOCKED` receiptлҠ” C00Q prerequisite evidenceлЎң ліҙмЎҙлҗңлӢӨ. лӢ№мӢң/current мӢӨн–ү к¶Ңн•ңкіј P1 unlockмқҖ `false` |
| `C00Q` | `formal_receipt_retained_execution_authority_expired` | inventory CLI/schema/testмқҳ public/synthetic formal receiptлҠ” ліҙмЎҙлҗңлӢӨ. мқҙ receiptлҠ” live/private queryВ·report write к¶Ңн•ңмқҙлӮҳ P0 effectлҘј л¶Җм—¬н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ |
| `C00B` | `judge_foundation_exists_live_hold` | pure judge/receipt schema/test foundationмқҖ мЎҙмһ¬н•ңлӢӨ. retained C00Q receiptмҷҖ лі„лҸ„лЎң В§18.2 `C00B-HOLD-01..08`мқҳ current authority/source/profile/output/expiryк°Җ мһҲм–ҙм•ј query-only live metadataлҘј мқҪмқҢ. P0 source-availability inventoryл§Ң мҶҢмң н•ҳкі  H00 six-state completenessлҠ” мӮ¬мҡ©н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ. кё°мЎҙ doctor/workspace inventoryлҠ” C00-LIVE-01..04 лҢҖмІҙ л¶Ҳк°Җ |
| `H00` | exact pinned `canon_candidate`мқҳ ratification-only gate | C00B PASS л’Ө нҳ„мһ¬ contract/helper/testлҘј к·ёлҢҖлЎң ratify/hold. нҢҢмқј нҺём§‘мқҖ мғҲ exact packet н•„мҡ” |
| `H01..H06` | `non_executable_phase_card` | literal existing/BUILD paths, symbols, exact validator commands, dependency/decision refsлҘј к°Җм§„ full YAML child packet |
| `A8-SYNTH` | `source_foundation_exists_formal_acceptance_hold` | strict schemaмҷҖ 60-ID computed public/pathless/feature-OFF fixture sourceлҠ” мЎҙмһ¬н•ңлӢӨ. D27~D29мҷҖ exact public security child packet prerequisite acceptance + fresh full B/V м „м—җлҠ” formal acceptanceк°Җ м•„лӢҲл©° P1/P8/P9/TaskEngine/live/A8-CANARY/team/production unlock `0` |
| `A8-CANARY` | `non_executable_live_hold` | `A8-SYNTH PASS` + accepted private `VERIFY_HP` exact binding receipt + strict office-LAN binding + explicit owner approval + Level 3 live gate. One seat/project/small file exact revision only; bulk/team/production/core unlock `0` |
| `C01/C04/C06/C07/C08` split rows | `non_executable_phase_card` | composite inheritance кёҲм§Җ. splitлі„ full YAML child packetкіј exact allowed-path allowlist |
| standalone full YAML cards (`C02`, `C03`, `C05`, `C08F` л“ұ) | approval candidate after dependencies | м•„м§Ғ м—ҶлҠ” file/scriptлҠ” н•ҙлӢ№ cardмқҳ `BUILD` outputмқҙлӢӨ. owning cardк°Җ л§Ңл“  л’Өм—җл§Ң downstream validatorк°Җ мҶҢл№„ |

Full child packetмқҖ prompt В§10мқҳ лӘЁл“  fieldлҘј мұ„мҡ°кі , generic `tests`, `README`, `package scripts`,
`<module>/**` лҳҗлҠ” вҖңadapter/modulesвҖқ к°ҷмқҖ categoryлҘј `allowed_write_paths`лЎң мӮ¬мҡ©н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. к°Ғ
entryлҠ” literal file pathмҷҖ `existing MODIFY | proposed BUILD`лҘј кө¬л¶„н•ҳкі , exact symbolВ·command,
approval-time baseline, dependency receipt, rollback, stop, owner gateлҘј н•Ёк»ҳ кі м •н•ңлӢӨ.

Split definitions:

- `C01A`: ID contract/shared temporal identity only; depends `H06`. `C01B`: TaskIntent/TaskDriver/
  authority/idempotency pure contract only; depends accepted `C04A/P6` receipt.
- `C04A`: candidate-only discovery adapter; depends accepted `C07A/P5` receipt. `C04B`: mail assignment/
  outbox and ERP apply adapters; depends accepted `C01B/P7`, `C02`, `C08F`, `C03` receipts in that order.
- `C06A`: immutable Source/File/Artifact revision and RelationEvent; depends P2. `C06B`: exact
  revision-bound Wiki/knowledge projection; depends `C06A` and C05.
- `C07A`: deterministic context assembly and acceptance receipt only. `C07B`: feedback and B9/ENGINE-12
  read-only pilot projection only after P8.
- `C08A`: public immutable packet/typed identity contract only. `C08F`: P8 public runtime-binding schema,
  fail-closed loader, CAS tool and audit integration with synthetic/feature-OFF fixtures only; local binding instance,
  role lease or process activation м—ҶмқҢ. `C08B`: operational lease/fencing/failover/failback/alerts only at P10.

| split phase card (`non_executable`) | inputs вҶ’ outputs | target surfaces (write allowlist м•„лӢҳ) | future child-packet validators | rollback / stop / owner gate |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `C01A/P2` | H06 receipt вҶ’ typed ID/ref/clock contract | `docs/architecture/foundation/ID_CONTRACT_V1.md`, foundation/shared READMEs, `guild_hall/shared/temporal_identity.mjs`, `.test.mjs`, CHANGELOG | exact child packetмқҖ `node --test guild_hall/shared/temporal_identity.test.mjs`; golden ID/collision, query-cutoffвҶ”owner-native-clock lossless crosswalk, null/packet identity | revert / stop on rekey, ambiguous or lossy clock mapping / protected ID contract+clock crosswalk approval |
| `C08A/P2` | H06+C01A вҶ’ immutable packet identity/chain schema | `guild_hall/file_activity/packet_transport*`, public schemas/tests/README/CHANGELOG | duplicate/conflict/gap/chain, no live binding | revert / stop on node inference or transport activation / packet contract approval |
| `C06A/P3` | P2 receipt вҶ’ Source/File/Artifact revision + RelationEvent | shared temporal relation/writer modules/tests/README/CHANGELOG | revision/content exactness, append/supersede, no fuzzy join | reader OFF+revert / stop on physical owner ambiguity / D06 |
| `C05+C06B/P4` | P3 receipt вҶ’ owner-aware RAG + exact WikiRevision | existing RAG resolver/writer/Wiki modules/tests/README/CHANGELOG | path isolation, source-revision locator, no-delete, ACL | target OFF+legacy reader / stop on owner/ACL gap / D07+D08 |
| `C07A/P5` | P4+H06 receipts вҶ’ deterministic context + acceptance receipt | context assembly/validator modules/tests, proposed context schema, README/CHANGELOG | gaps, clocks, exact refs, replay 2нҡҢ, owner mutation 0 | context gate closed / stop on missing lane or fuzzy relation / P5 acceptance owner |
| `C04A/P6` | accepted P5 receipt вҶ’ TaskIntent candidates | source-specific discovery adapters/tests/README/CHANGELOG; ERP store/schema excluded | candidate replay/idempotency, ERP row delta 0, direct writer 0 | discovery OFF+revert / stop on apply path / P6 acceptance owner |
| `C01B/P7` | accepted P6 receipt вҶ’ pure TaskDriver/authority/idempotency contract | `ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/src/task_driver.mjs`, its tests/API schemas/README, root `package.json`, CHANGELOG; persistence/store excluded | exact child packetмқҖ direct TaskDriver test л’Ө root `npm.cmd run validate:task-engine-core-v1`; why/why-now, expiry/revocation, same-key replay, no DB open | revert / stop on ERP schema/write / P7 acceptance owner |
| `C08F/P8` | accepted P7+C08A вҶ’ public binding schema/loader/CAS/audit foundation | runtime-binding source/tool/schema/tests, runtime-audit tests, README/CHANGELOG; local binding/state/lease path м ңмҷё | missing/malformed/off/expiry/revocation/scope/CAS/atomic-replace fixtures, no fallback, local instance 0 | revert / stop on role issue, local binding creation or process activation / foundation contract approval |
| `C02вҶ’C03вҶ’C04B/P8` | accepted P7+H06/MAIL + parallel C02/C08F receipts вҶ’ C03 facade/binding integration вҶ’ C04B mail assignment/event/outbox + five-lane projector feature-OFF | dev-ERP persistence/store/server/tests, gateway mail coordinator/history projector/validators, schemas/READMEs/CHANGELOG | V01~16 applicable + MAIL-01~12 synthetic + HP-HISTORY-10 cutover fixture, crash matrix, parity, stale epoch, cutover allowlistм—җм„ң non-HPP caller `0`; P8 live switch `0`, P9мқҖ лі„лҸ„ мҠ№мқёлҗң one-project bounded switchл§Ң, production role switchлҠ” P10к№Ңм§Җ кёҲм§Җ | all writers OFF+old reader / stop on missing preceding receipt, direct writer or parity gap / D01~D05+D21~D24 |
| `C07B/P9` | accepted P8 + one-project allowlist вҶ’ feedback/B9/ENGINE-12 read-only projection | context graph/life-tree/feedback modules/tests/README/CHANGELOG | owner mutation 0, cutoff/replay/tree parity | adapters OFF / stop on unrelated project or mutation / P9 pilot approval |
| `C08B/P10` | accepted P9+C08F + explicit capability approval вҶ’ operational lease/fencing/manual failover or production-role policy | lease/fence/ops contracts and approved local binding/evidence paths only; C08F loader/CAS мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ© | Level 3, role epoch vector `(C_E,P_E)вҶ’(C_E+1,P_E+1)вҶ’(C_E+2,P_E+2)`, stale writer reject, RTO/RPO | binding OFF+old primary / stop on auto failback or missing approver / D21~D23 + capability approval |

лӘЁл“  split rowлҠ” routing cardмқј лҝҗ write authorityк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. Exact child packetмқҖ н•ҙлӢ№ rowмқҳ scopeл§Ң
ліөмӮ¬н•ҳкі  full fieldмҷҖ literal pathлҘј мғҲлЎң кі м •н•ңлӢӨ. Legacy card actionмқ„ мһҗлҸҷ мғҒмҶҚн•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡмңјл©°,
unambiguously assignн•  мҲҳ м—ҶлҠ” actionмқҖ `DEFER`лӢӨ.

`validate:task-engine-core-v1`мқҖ CURRENT scriptк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. C01AлҠ” мң„ direct identity testл§Ң мӢӨн–үн•ҳкі ,
C01B child packetмқҙ cross-root validatorмқҳ ownerмқё root `package.json`м—җ мқҙ scriptлҘј мІҳмқҢ л“ұлЎқн•ңлӢӨ.
н•„мҡ”н•ҳл©ҙ dev-ERP packageмқҳ app-local subscriptлҘј rootк°Җ нҳём¶ңн•  мҲҳ мһҲм§Җл§Ң root commandк°Җ canonical
entrypointлӢӨ. C01B registrationкіј direct testк°Җ PASSн•ҳкё° м „ C02/C03/C04BлҠ” мқҙ commandлҘј мӢӨн–үн•ҳкұ°лӮҳ
мЎҙмһ¬н•ңлӢӨкі  мЈјмһҘн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

### лҸ„мӢқ 9 вҖ” WBS dependency DAGмҷҖ critical path

```mermaid
flowchart LR
  P0["P0 C00AвҶ’C00QвҶ’C00B<br/>public blockerвҶ’synthetic toolвҶ’approved query"] --> P1["P1 H00-H06 histories+coverage<br/>H01C sent/received observations"]
  P1 --> P2["P2 C01A/C08A IDsВ·refsВ·clocks"]
  P2 --> P3["P3 C06A immutable revisions"]
  P3 --> P4["P4 C05/C06B exact RAGВ·Wiki"]
  P1 --> H7A["H07A Slack source/binding contract"]
  P3 --> H7B["H07B Slack revision/context Shadow"]
  H7A --> H7B
  P4 --> P5["P5 C07A context_acceptance_gate"]
  H7B --> P5
  P5 -->|"accepted receipt"| P6["P6 C04A candidate-only discovery"]
  P6 -->|"accepted receipt"| P7["P7 C01B TaskDriver"]
  P7 -->|"accepted receipt"| P8["P8 C02+C08FвҶ’C03вҶ’C04B<br/>binding foundation+sole writers+outbox"]
  P8 --> P9["P9 C09*/C10/C07B one-project pilot"]
  P9 -->|"separate approval"| P10["P10 C08B/G*/AX/AR/IQ/ML activation"]
  A8S["A8-SYNTH independent<br/>public pathless fixtures"] -->|"private receipt + office LAN + owner + Level 3"| A8C["A8-CANARY<br/>one small file exact revision"]
```

Core critical pathлҠ” `C00AвҶ’C00QвҶ’C00BвҶ’H00вҶ’applicable D19/D20/D26/D33 lane decisionsвҶ’(H01A..H05 pure shadows+H01C)вҶ’D25вҶ’H01..H05 acceptanceвҶ’D22 display-field subset/D24/H06вҶ’P2вҶ’P3вҶ’P4вҶ’P5вҶ’P6вҶ’P7вҶ’P8вҶ’P9`мқҙл©°,
Slack extensionмқҖ `H00+D34вҶ’H07A`, `P3+H07AвҶ’H07BвҶ’P5`лЎң лі‘л ¬ н•©лҘҳн•ңлӢӨ. H07мқҖ H06/P2лҘј
л¶Ҳн•„мҡ”н•ҳкІҢ л§үм§Җ м•Ҡм§Җл§Ң м Ғмҡ©лҗң Slack sourceмқҳ лҜёмҷ„лЈҢлҘј P5м—җм„ң мҲЁкёё мҲҳ м—ҶлӢӨ.
P8 лӮҙл¶ҖлҠ” `C02`мҷҖ `C08F`лҘј лі‘л ¬ кІҖмҰқн•ң л’Ө `C03вҶ’C04B` мҲңм„ңлӢӨ.
P10мқҖ н•ҳлӮҳмқҳ л¬¶мқҢ мҠ№мқёмқҙ м•„лӢҲлқј capabilityлі„ лі„лҸ„ мҠ№мқёмқҙлӢӨ. AX/AgentRunкіј Engineering IQ/MLмқҖ
P1~P9мқҳ м„ н–үмЎ°кұҙмқҙ м•„лӢҲл©°, C09SлҸ„ н•ң н”„лЎңм қнҠё pilotмқ„ common/system ownerлЎң мһҗлҸҷ нҷ•мһҘн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
D21мқҳ synthetic fenceлҠ” P8, durable owner/pilotмқҖ P9, live roleмқҖ P10мқҙл©° D23 emergency fallbackмқҖ
P10мқҙлӢӨ. D22мқҳ DB/outboxлҠ” P8, bounded cutoverлҠ” P9, operational policyлҠ” P10 мҶҢмң лӢӨ. лӘЁл‘җ H01 pure
shadowмқҳ м„ н–үмЎ°кұҙмқҙ м•„лӢҲл©° D22 redacted view targetл§Ң H01 л’Ө H06/P8м—җм„ң лі„лҸ„лЎң м Ғмҡ©н•ңлӢӨ.

### C00 вҖ” P0 baseline/source-owner inventory closureмҷҖ tooling prerequisite л¶„лҰ¬

`TEAX-C00`мқҖ мӢӨн–ү packetмқҙ м•„лӢҲлқј м•„лһҳ м„ё childмқҳ мҲңм„ңлҘј кі м •н•ҳлҠ” parent routeлӢӨ. кё°мЎҙ
`guild-hall:doctor --device-capabilities`лҠ” advisory capabilityл§Ң ліҙкі н•ҳкі  live/readiness кІҖмӮ¬лҘј н•ҳм§Җ
м•Ҡмңјл©°, workspace-system inventoryлҠ” `_workspaces/system` л©”нғҖлҚ°мқҙн„°мҷҖ м„ нғқм Ғ private reportлҘј мң„н•ң
лі„лҸ„ surfaceлӢӨ. м–ҙлҠҗ кІғлҸ„ лӢӨм„Ҝ laneмқҳ `C00-LIVE-01..04` authoritative evidence producerк°Җ м•„лӢҲлҜҖлЎң
лҢҖмІҙмһ¬лЎң мӮ¬мҡ©н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

```yaml
slice_id: TEAX-C00
packet_kind: routing_only_non_executable
subpacket_order: [TEAX-C00A, TEAX-C00Q, TEAX-C00B]
p0_acceptance_rule: only accepted TEAX-C00B PASS unlocks TEAX-H00
inheritance_rule: no child inherits another child's read/write/authority allowlist
current_result: HOLD
```

| child | нҳ„мһ¬ мғҒнғң | н—Ҳмҡ© лӘ©н‘ңмҷҖ кІҪкі„ | лӢӨмқҢ unlock |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `TEAX-C00A` | `historical_blocker_receipt_retained` | В§18.1мқҳ public-only мӢӨн–үм—җм„ң compact stdout blocker receiptлҘј л§Ңл“Өм—Ҳкі  code/DB/private/live/report write `0`мқ„ ліҙмЎҙн–ҲлӢӨ | accepted `BLOCKED` receiptк°Җ C00Q prerequisite historyлҘј мҰқлӘ…н•  лҝҗ P1мқҖ мһ кёҲ мң м§Җ |
| `TEAX-C00Q` | `formal_receipt_retained_execution_authority_expired` | `tools/task_engine_inventory.mjs`, лҢҖмқ‘ test, manifest schemaмқҳ public/synthetic formal receipt `task_engine_c00q_formal_acceptance_pass_v1`мқ„ ліҙмЎҙн•ңлӢӨ. live/private inputВ·report writeВ·DB mutation `0` | receiptлҠ” prerequisite evidenceмқј лҝҗ нҳ„мһ¬ мӢӨн–ү к¶Ңн•ңмқҙлӮҳ P0 effectк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. C00BлҠ” лі„лҸ„ current authorityмҷҖ strict PASSк°Җ н•„мҡ”н•ҳлӢӨ. |
| `TEAX-C00B` | `non_executable_hold` | C00Q мӮ°м¶ңл¬јмқ„ ліҖкІҪн•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡкі , лі„лҸ„ мҠ№мқёлҗң profileВ·laneлі„ authority/sourceВ·metadata outputВ·expiryм—җм„ң query-only aggregateл§Ң мғқм„ұ. raw к°’В·м—…л¬ҙ мӣҗл¬ёВ·source/tracked/runtime mutation `0`; stdout-only default, exact approved metadata output one-writeл§Ң мҳҲмҷё | `C00-LIVE-01..04`к°Җ authority-backed inventory evidenceлЎң лӘЁл‘җ лӢ«нһҲкі  zero-mutation receiptк°Җ мһҲмқ„ л•Ңл§Ң P0 PASS; лӢӨмқҢ gateлҠ” H00 ratificationлҝҗ |

C00QлҠ” evidence producerмқҳ нҳ•мӢқкіј fail-closed guardл§Ң л§Ңл“ лӢӨ. C00Bк°Җ м“ё exact physical sourceмҷҖ authorityлҘј
л°ңлӘ…н•ҳкұ°лӮҳ live readinessлҘј мҰқлӘ…н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. н•„мҡ”н•ң lane descriptor/evidence authorityк°Җ н•ҳлӮҳлқјлҸ„ м—Ҷкұ°лӮҳ
л§ҢлЈҢлҗҳл©ҙ C00BлҠ” `BLOCKED`лӢӨ. л°ҳл©ҙ authorityк°Җ current owner/writer/consumer/sourceмқҳ л¶Җмһ¬лӮҳ gapмқ„
нҷ•мқён•ң кІғмқҖ мң нҡЁн•ң inventory findingмқј мҲҳ мһҲм§Җл§Ң history completenessлҘј лң»н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. C00BлҠ”
`PROJECT_HISTORY_ENVELOPE_V0`мқҳ six-state coverage receiptВ·gap vocabularyлҘј H00 ratification м „м—җ м“°м§Җ
м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. C00Q acceptance мһҗмІҙлҠ” P1мқ„ м—ҙм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. C00QлҠ” P0 acceptance actionмқҙ м•„лӢҲлқј лі„лҸ„ мҠ№мқёлҗң
public/synthetic tooling prerequisiteлӢӨ. P0мқҳ мӢӨм ң evidence collectionкіј acceptanceлҠ” C00Bк№Ңм§Җ read-onlyмқҙл©°,
C00Qмқҳ public code deltaлҘј DBВ·м—…л¬ҙ лҚ°мқҙн„°В·runtime ліҖкІҪ к¶Ңн•ңмңјлЎң нҷ•мһҘн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

### H00~H06 вҖ” P1 append-only history and coverage phase cards

кіөнҶө forbidden pathлҠ” raw mail/audio/transcript/file/run payload, live scheduler/network/alert,
TaskDriver/ERP task schema, source owner mutation, unrelated project, `_workmeta` body copyлӢӨ.
м•„лһҳ н–үмқҖ dependencyмҷҖ future target surfaceлҘј кі м •н•ҳлҠ” `non_executable_phase_card`лӢӨ. H00мқҳ
нҳ„мһ¬ exact candidate ratificationмқ„ м ңмҷён•ҳкі , н–үмқҳ category/glob н‘ңнҳ„мқҖ write allowlistк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ.

| phase card | goal / depends_on | inputs вҶ’ outputs | target surfaces (write allowlist м•„лӢҳ) | future child-packet validators | rollback / stop / owner gate |

| `H00` | common envelope+coverage contract ratification / accepted+unexpired `C00B PASS` | five owner mapsлҠ” sequencing/advisory evidenceлЎңл§Ң мӮ¬мҡ© вҶ’ existing candidateмқҳ ratify лҳҗлҠ” HOLD receipt; live lane membership/existence нҢҗм •мқҖ H01~H05 мҶҢмң  | `docs/architecture/workspace/PROJECT_HISTORY_ENVELOPE_V0.md`, `guild_hall/shared/project_history_envelope.mjs`, `guild_hall/shared/project_history_envelope.test.mjs`мқҳ read-only pinned candidate; write `0` | approval-time three-blob match + exact `node --test guild_hall/shared/project_history_envelope.test.mjs` 20/20 + Level 2 receipt; envelope schema, clock/null semantics, digest, raw sentinel | file delta м—ҶмқҢ / stop on precondition expiry, blob/test/review drift, owner or clock ambiguity / owner `RATIFY | HOLD` |

| `H03` | structured PC work + external SE schedule history / `H00`; internal `H03AвҶ’H03B` | H03A current one-shot ERP MCP WorkSession/approved instruction fixtures + daily-ledger projection-only fixture + H03B owner-approved schedule current/revision/event fixture вҶ’ combined structured history+gap receipt | `erp_mcp_service.mjs`, server/tests, daily-ledger modules/tests, proposed schedule contract, README, CHANGELOG | one-shot record idempotency, task-chat/full-conversation payload reject, daily-ledger non-occurrence/projection-only, schedule stale revision/current-event replay; start/closeout completenessлҠ” лІ”мң„ л°– | adapter OFF+revert / H03A alone cannot close H03; personal lifecycleмқ„ P1 prerequisiteлЎң л§Ңл“Өм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ; stop on surveillance or D20 exact owner/path/writer gap / D19+D20; D26 exact structured-work/schedule mapping м „ adapter кёҲм§Җ, D25 H03 coverage policy м „ lane acceptance кёҲм§Җ |

к°Ғ H phaseмқҳ exact child packetмқҖ full YAML field, literal file allowlist, new BUILD filename, symbol,
exact command, dependency receiptмҷҖ owner decision refлҘј к°Җм ём•ј н•ңлӢӨ. H03мқҖ H03AмҷҖ H03B л‘җ packetмңјлЎң
л¶„лҰ¬н•ҳкі  H03BлҠ” D20 owner/current/revision/event/writer кІ°м • м „ `HOLD`лӢӨ. H01мқҖ H01CлҘј нҸ¬н•Ён•ҳкі ,
H07A/H07BлҠ” к°Ғк°Ғ лі„лҸ„ child packetмқҙлӢӨ. H01~H06 child packetмқҙ
к°Ғк°Ғ мҠ№мқёлҗҳкё° м „ adapter/exporter кө¬нҳ„мқ„ мӢңмһ‘н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. Accepted outputл§Ң лӢӨмқҢ phase input receiptк°Җ
лҗҳл©° H06 acceptance м „ C01A/P2лҠ” мӢңмһ‘н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. H07мқҖ H06/P2лҘј л§үм§Җ м•Ҡкі  лі‘л ¬ м„Өкі„н•  мҲҳ мһҲм§Җл§Ң,
нҳ„мһ¬мІҳлҹј Slack project channelмқ„ м Ғмҡ© sourceлЎң мұ„нғқн•ң кІҪмҡ° H07B acceptance м „ P5 context acceptanceлҠ”
Slack gapмқ„ мҲЁкё°кұ°лӮҳ `not_applicable`лЎң л°”кҝҖ мҲҳ м—ҶлӢӨ.

#### H01 exact child-packet readiness verdict вҖ” `HOLD / REVISE` (2026-07-15)

H01мқҳ нҳ„мһ¬ legacy evidenceлҠ” м¶©л¶„нһҲ мӢқлі„лҗҗм§Җл§Ң executable packetмқҖ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. м•„лһҳ holdлҘј лӘЁл‘җ лӢ«мқҖ
лі„лҸ„ packetмқҙ мҠ№мқёлҗ  л•Ңк№Ңм§Җ мғҲ adapter/schema/testлҘј л§Ңл“Өм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

| hold | лӢ«м•„м•ј н•  exact н•ӯлӘ© | authority effect |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `H01-HOLD-01` | accepted+unexpired C00B PASS л’Ө exact H00 RATIFY receipt | H01 reviewл§Ң к°ҖлҠҘ; build к¶Ңн•ңмқҖ лі„лҸ„ |
| `H01-HOLD-02` | D26-mail exact `{entity_type, owner_surface, entity_id}` binding, project-independent opaque ID scope/canonicalization, event/revision relation, existence/conflict validator | H01A adapter input allowlistл§Ң нҷ•м • |
| `H01-HOLD-03` | one pure adapter, one direct test, one mail shadow contract/schemaмқҳ literal BUILD pathВ·exported symbolВ·schema owner | generic `gateway modules/tests`лҘј write allowlistлЎң мӮ¬мҡ© кёҲм§Җ |
| `H01-HOLD-04` | full child YAML, approval-time baseline, literal allowed/forbidden paths, exact direct test+`npm.cmd run validate:gateway`, output/receipt, rollback/stop gate | exit `0`л§ҢмңјлЎң H01 acceptance кёҲм§Җ |
| `H01-HOLD-05` | D25 mail expected-source set, `known_at` window, freshness, gap vocabulary, applicability rule/ref | H01B coverage acceptanceл§Ң unlock |
| `H01-HOLD-06` | H01/P8/P9/P10 phase attribution receipt | H01 file/DB/caller mutation `0`; P8 synthetic writer, P9 one-project parity, P10 live failover/failback к¶Ңн•ңкіј л¶„лҰ¬ |
| `H01-HOLD-07` | D33 owner+team received/sent expected-source matrix, exact message occurrence vs mailbox observation identity, sender/to/cc/bcc semantics, thread relation, confidence ceilingкіј unmatched-copy policy | H01C synthetic reconciliationл§Ң unlock; team sent coverage, live collector, DB/backfill к¶Ңн•ңмқҖ мғқкё°м§Җ м•ҠмқҢ |

surfaceк°Җ м•„лӢҲлҜҖлЎң H01м—җм„ң мӢӨн–үВ·мҲҳм •н•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡкі  static consumer inventoryлЎңл§Ң мӮ¬мҡ©н•ңлӢӨ. Existing regressionмқҖ

### C01 вҖ” legacy composite reference (м§Ғм ‘ мӢӨн–ү кёҲм§Җ; C01A/P2мҷҖ C01B/P7лЎң л¶„лҰ¬)

```yaml
rollback: new reader OFF; correction/inactive eventл§Ң appendн•ҳкі  source revision/event originalмқҖ мӮӯм ңн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ
```

```yaml
inputs: [C08F binding loader/CAS writer, C08B/G00 operational binding receipt, zero-blocker release audit, valid restore, pilot pass, explicit owner activation]
outputs: [operational-primary/writer binding receipt, monitored rollout state]
code_delta: [none; C08F loader/writerмҷҖ C08B/G00 contractк°Җ кІҖмҰқн•ң production revisionл§Ң мӮ¬мҡ©]
db_delta: [none beyond approved live writer operations]
api_delta: [approved routes enabled]
folder_delta: [none]
docs_contract_changelog_delta: [G00м—җм„ң мҷ„лЈҢ; G01 мӨ‘ contract gap л°ңкІ¬ мӢң activation мӨ‘лӢЁ]
owner_and_writers: [owner-designated always-on identity, sole file reconciler, sole SQLite coordinator with separate logical authorities]
acceptance_checks: [V14 alert clock, require-live audit zero blocker, failover manual drill, rollback readiness, fresh B/V Level 3]
regression_checks: [full validators and post-activation read-only audit]
migration_or_backfill: completed in C10; broad expansionмқҖ лі„лҸ„ project gate
rollback: all target jobs OFF + old reader/controller restore + projection replay
stop_conditions: [any blocker, stale backup, ambiguous primary, uncontrolled notification/network]
owner_gate: explicit production activation approval; C10 мҠ№мқёмқҙ мқҙлҘј лҢҖмӢ н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ
risk_and_effort: very-high / M
next_slice: per-project bounded expansion only
```

### 12.1 sliceлі„ н•„мҲҳ review level

мқҙ н‘ңлҠ” к°Ғ YAML packetмқҳ м¶”к°Җ мқҳл¬ҙ fieldлӢӨ. лҚ” лӮ®мқҖ reviewлЎң лҢҖмІҙн•  мҲҳ м—Ҷкі , Level 3мқҖ fresh
executorмҷҖ лі„лҸ„ verifierк°Җ лӘЁл‘җ мһҲм–ҙм•ј н•ңлӢӨ. Review passлҸ„ owner мҠ№мқёмқҙлӮҳ activationмқ„ л§Ңл“Өм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

| slice | minimum review | мқҙмң  |
| --- | --- | --- |
| C00A | `inspector_and_judge` | public candidate mapкіј expected blocker receipt нҢҗм • |
| C00Q | `full_b_v_gate` | future live evidence producerмқҳ query-only/raw/zero-mutation guardлҘј syntheticлЎң кө¬м¶• |
| C00B | `inspector_and_judge` | separately authorized source-availability inventoryмҷҖ P0 closure/H00-entry нҢҗм •; completenessВ·H01 start к¶Ңн•ң м—ҶмқҢ |
| H00,H02~H05 | `inspector_and_judge` | history envelope/adapterмҷҖ owner-boundary ліҖкІҪ |
| H01,H06 | `full_b_v_gate` | лӢӨмӨ‘ mail writer м¶•мҶҢ, coverage/parity acceptance authority |
| C01A | `full_b_v_gate` | protected foundation ID contract/canon candidate |
| C06A,C05,C06B,C07A,C04A,C01B | `inspector_and_judge` мқҙмғҒ | P2~P7 к°Ғ acceptance gate; лӢӨмқҢ phase authorityлҘј м—ҙкё° м „ лҸ…лҰҪ нҢҗм • |
| C02,C03,C04B | `full_b_v_gate` | P8 DB schema, sole ERP writer, mail event/outbox/parity/fencing |
| C07B | `inspector_and_judge` | P9 read-only feedback/life-tree projection |
| C08A | `inspector_and_judge` | immutable packet identity contract, live authority м—ҶмқҢ |
| C08F | `full_b_v_gate` | future write routesмқҳ fail-closed binding loader/CAS/audit foundation; feature OFFВ·local instance 0 |
| C08B | `full_b_v_gate` | watchdog/operational lease/fencing/failover/failback authority |

## 13. branch/schema/RAG/data migrationВ·backfillВ·rollback

лӘЁл“  migrationмқҖ к°ҷмқҖ мҲңм„ңлҘј л”°лҘёлӢӨ. вҖңdry-run м„ұкіөвҖқмқҖ apply мҠ№мқёмқҙ м•„лӢҲл©°, вҖңapply м„ұкіөвҖқмқҖ
activation мҠ№мқёмқҙ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ.

### лҸ„мӢқ 10 вҖ” migrationкіј rollback state machine

```mermaid
stateDiagram-v2
  [*] --> inventory
  inventory --> blocked: unknown/conflict/к¶Ңн•ң м—ҶмқҢ
  inventory --> dry_run: evidence complete
  dry_run --> blocked: orphan/collision/writer gap
  dry_run --> backup_restore_design: pass
  backup_restore_design --> isolated_restore_drill: лі„лҸ„ owner мҠ№мқё
  isolated_restore_drill --> blocked: restore invalid
  isolated_restore_drill --> copy_rebuild_backfill: pass
  copy_rebuild_backfill --> readback
  readback --> rollback_drill
  readback --> rollback: mismatch
  rollback_drill --> owner_gate: pass
  rollback_drill --> rollback: fail
  owner_gate --> activation: лі„лҸ„ activation мҠ№мқё
  owner_gate --> rollback: ліҙлҘҳ/кұ°м Ҳ
  rollback --> old_reader_restored
  old_reader_restored --> [*]
  blocked --> [*]
```

### 13.1 migrationлі„ exact plan

| лҢҖмғҒ | inventory | dry-run | copy/rebuild/backfill | readback | rollback drill | activation |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| candidate branch | exact refs, merge-base, file/symbol/oracle drift | latest-main patch previewмҷҖ allowed paths | C00Q, P1~P8 л°Ҹ C09Aм—җм„ң file-by-file мһ¬кө¬нҳ„; wholesale merge кёҲм§Җ | focused+full tests, blob oracle | slice commit revert | code publishмҷҖ runtime deploy л¶„лҰ¬ |
| TaskDriver schema | C09 live table/index/trigger query-only inventory | C02/C09A synthetic DDL collision/up/down | C09R valid restoreмҷҖ C09D feature-OFF deploy л’Ө C10 fresh lockм—җм„ң approved DBм—җ new table; legacy rowлҠ” мІҳмқҢм—” м•Ҳ мҳ®к№Җ | schema version/FK/index/trigger/receipt | coordinator OFF + reversal/current rebuild + old reader; committed event м—ҶлҠ” л°°нҸ¬ мӢӨнҢЁл§Ң verified DB restore | C10 л’Ө G00/G01 |
| task event/current | лӘЁл“  mutation callerмҷҖ status count | legacy event/status crosswalk + creation-reversal FK fixture | one coordinator transaction; old historyлҠ” typed alias/backfill eventлЎң м—°кІ° | current=replay aggregate/digest; reversed createлҠ” identity/event мң м§ҖВ·current м—ҶмқҢ | old reader/facade restore; new event history ліҙмЎҙ | caller `0`/parity л’Ө compatibility м¶•мҶҢ |
| completion/reopen | delete callerмҷҖ completion aggregate | reopen/re-done synthetic | кіјкұ° row мҲҳм • м—Ҷмқҙ reversal event м¶”к°Җ; н•„мҡ”н•ң legacy baselineл§Ң | task ID/old completion/ref ліҙмЎҙ | compatibility view мһ¬кө¬м¶• | TREE04 pass |
| task ID | allocator/caller/duplicate inventory | reservation collision/retry fixture | кё°мЎҙ ID мң м§Җ, мғҲ IDл§Ң coordinatorк°Җ immutable reservation | same keyвҶ’same task/receipt | лҜёcommit transaction rollback; commit л’Өм—җлҠ” reversal event/current rebuild | ID01~04 pass |
| mail history v2 | JS/Python/Outlook direct writers, scanner, CSV/ICS/XLSX shapeмҷҖ coverage inventory | v1вҶ’v2 occurrence/assignment/outbox crosswalk, AвҶ’B event pair, generation manifest, roleлі„ lease/epoch/failover dry-run | HPP coordinator/projectorлҘј shadowлЎң replay; existing pathsм—җ same-generation staged publish, source/event мӮӯм ң 0 | DB current+event+outboxвҶ”CSV/ICS/XLSX ordered digest, partial Mac gap | P8/P9мқҖ synthetic/normal-primary rollbackл§Ң; мӢӨм ң epoch-vector failover/failback drillмқҖ C08B/P10 лі„лҸ„ мҠ№мқё | P8 acceptance л’Ө P9 one-project, productionмқҖ P10 лі„лҸ„ |
| voice/PC-work/file/run-log views | к°Ғ technical owner/event/refмҷҖ proposed CSV/XLSX shapeВ·consumer inventory | accepted cutoff/gap/generation manifestмҷҖ HPP sole-writer dry-run | HPP projectorк°Җ shadow fixtureлЎңл§Ң 4к°ң derived viewлҘј мғқм„ұ; technical owner/event ліҖкІҪ 0 | source event/ref+cutoffвҶ”CSV/XLSX ordered digest, HPP мҷё normal caller 0 | projector OFF, technical owner/reader мң м§Җ; generated viewлҠ” rebuild | H06/P8 acceptance л’Ө P9 one-project, productionмқҖ P10 лі„лҸ„ |
| source/relation ID | sourceлі„ owner ID/revision coverage | canonical basis/golden/collision/alias + existing owner-path crosswalk | C09Lм—җ verified SourceRevisionкіј knowledge-binding eventл§Ң append; primary ID rekeyВ·occurrence ліөмӮ¬ кёҲм§Җ | orphan/ambiguous/fuzzy join/duplicate-owner count | new reader OFF; original ID/event files мң м§Җ | ID/TREE pass |
| contract-owned temporal metadata | C09 owner/ACL/pointer/writer inventory | C09A/C06A owner-adapter/no-second-truth manifest | C09L н•ң projectмқҳ existing contract paths л’Ө лі„лҸ„ C09Sм—җм„ң owner-approved common source revisionл§Ң materialize | projection receipt, replay digest, duplicate logical record 0 | reader OFF + correction/inactive event; record мӮӯм ң м—ҶмқҢ | C10 exact refs; C09S лі„лҸ„ gate |
| project/common RAG | лӘЁл“  source/index/chunk/trace/answer/review/work-card consumer | owner target, conflict/orphan/no-delete manifest | н•ң projectл§Ң copy/rebuild; original/legacy index мң м§Җ | old/new query digestВ·coverageВ·ACL | target writer OFF, old reader restore | C10 лі„лҸ„ gate |
| Wiki/ontology | reader/writer/body owner/ACL inventory | revision/source/claim fixture | approved body ownerм—җ new revision; metadata planeмқҖ pointerл§Ң | exact source/claim relation | new writer OFF, old reader мң м§Җ | truth promotion лі„лҸ„ gate |
| B9/ENGINE-12 | owner eventвҶ”projection ID coverage | synthetic rebuild/cutoff | adapter projection rebuildл§Ң | task/B9/daily digest parity | old adapters restore | viewлі„ zero-mutation pass |
| PC packet/reconciler | roles/bindings/checkpoint/tail/lease | duplicate/conflict/gap/failover fixture | signed packet queueмҷҖ stateлҘј shadowлЎң кө¬м¶• | full vs checkpoint+tail replay | all jobs OFF, last-good checkpoint | D10+V13/V14 лі„лҸ„ gate |
| runtime release | shell/source/data refs, audit blockers, backup/restore | pinned artifact/attestation preview | C09D maintenance windowм—җ dedicated runtime checkoutл§Ң approved SHAлЎң feature-OFF deploy | require-live audit zero blocker + runtime binding receipt | C09D normal rollbackмқҖ binding OFF+old code, current DB мң м§Җ; C10 л’Өм—җлҠ” л№„нҢҢкҙҙ reversal | G00 binding л’Ө G01 лі„лҸ„ мҠ№мқё |
| AX Workspace | session/MCP/task-writer caller inventory | synthetic one-seat store | feature OFF, session data only | candidate/receipt linkмҷҖ project ACL | feature OFF/session store restore | AX-G3 |
| HPP MCP custody/access | pathless logical-class/actor/grant/ticket inventory | `A8-SYNTH` public/pathless enrollmentвҶ’mTLSвҶ’brokerвҶ’delegationвҶ’ticket verifier adversarial fixtures; core dependency м—ҶмқҢ | `A8-SYNTH PASS`+accepted private `VERIFY_HP` exact binding receipt+strict office LAN+explicit owner+Level 3 л’Ө `A8-CANARY` one seat/project/small file only | receipt/revision/ticket/audience/hash/size and optional redacted derivative lineage | binding/writer OFF, queue freeze/quarantine, prior accepted pointer; no OneDrive reverse-copy/delete | VPN/remote/bulk/team/productionмқҖ лі„лҸ„ future gate |

### 13.2 schema versionкіј down/rollback

- `meta.task_driver_persistence_schema_version`мқҖ exact expected valueмҷҖ лӢӨлҘҙл©ҙ startup/applyлҘј л§үлҠ”лӢӨ.
- migration scriptлҠ” `--dry-run`мқҙ кё°ліёмқҙкі , `--apply`лҠ” owner approval receipt, maintenance lock,
  valid backup/restore receipt м„ё к°Җм§ҖлҘј лӘЁл‘җ мҡ”кө¬н•ңлӢӨ.
- live down/rollbackм—җм„ң append-only eventлҘј мӮӯм ңн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. Commitлҗң pilot eventк°Җ мһҲмңјл©ҙ primary
  rollbackмқҖ к°ҷмқҖ coordinator transactionмқҳ reversal event+current rebuild, writer OFF, old reader ліөмӣҗмқҙлӢӨ.
  Verified pre-migration DB м „мІҙ ліөкө¬лҠ” C09D traffic freeze лҸҷм•Ҳ лӘЁл“  legacy/TaskEngine writerк°Җ 0мқҙкі 
  before/after DB/WAL/SHM лҸҷмқјм„ұмқҙ мҰқлӘ…лҗң мһ¬лӮңм—җл§Ң мҳҲмҷём ҒмңјлЎң н—Ҳмҡ©н•ңлӢӨ. м •мғҒ C09D rollbackмқҖ
  binding OFF+old code м „нҷҳмқҙл©° нҳ„мһ¬ DBлҘј мң м§Җн•ңлӢӨ.
  Commit л’Ө DB мһ¬лӮң ліөкө¬к°Җ л¶Ҳк°Җн”јн•ҳл©ҙ current DB/WAL/SHMмқ„ лЁјм Җ кІ©лҰ¬ ліҙмЎҙн•ҳкі , лі„лҸ„ мҠ№мқёлҗң
  event exportвҶ’restoreвҶ’re-importвҶ’replay/readback м Ҳм°Ёк°Җ кІҖмҰқлҗҳкё° м „м—җлҠ” м„ұкіө rollbackмңјлЎң нҢҗм •н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
- backfillмқҖ мӣҗл¬ё мһ¬н•ҙм„қмқҙ м•„лӢҲлқј legacy owner ID/status/eventлҘј typed alias/baselineмңјлЎң м—°кІ°н•ңлӢӨ.
- conflict, orphan, unknown enumмқҖ мһ„мқҳ ліҙм •н•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡкі  quarantine manifestм—җ лӮЁкёҙлӢӨ.
- Storage/promotion rollbackмқҖ prior accepted pointerлҘј мң м§Җн•ң мұ„ target binding/writerлҘј OFFн•ҳкі  queueлҘј
  freeze/quarantineн•ңлӢӨ. лҜёлһҳ switchлҠ” copy+hash+readback л’Өм—җл§Ң к°ҖлҠҘн•ҳл©° OneDrive reverse-copyмҷҖ
  retention approval м—ҶлҠ” deleteлҠ” кёҲм§Җн•ңлӢӨ.

### 13.3 branch integration мЈјмқҳ

Candidateмқҳ мң мҡ©н•ң pure codeлҠ” мһ…л Ҙмқҙм§Җл§Ң, лӢӨмқҢмқҖ к·ёлҢҖлЎң нҶөн•©н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

- мҳӨлһҳлҗң merge-baseм—җм„ң л°”лҖҗ README/package/CHANGELOGлҘј нҳ„мһ¬ нҢҢмқј мң„м—җ лҚ®м–ҙм“°кё°
- lifecycle/ENGINE-13/redesign oracleмқҳ branch ліҖкІҪ
- result task IDк°Җ мқҙлҜё л°ңкёүлҗҗлӢӨкі  к°Җм •н•ҳлҠ” persistence кІҪлЎң
- live DBм—җ install н•ЁмҲҳлҘј мһҗлҸҷ нҳём¶ңн•ҳлҠ” startup м—°кІ°
- project RAG pilotмқ„ мӢӨм ң `_workspaces`м—җ л°”лЎң м Ғмҡ©н•ҳлҠ” кІҪлЎң

## 14. V-01~V-16В·regressionВ·securityВ·replay кІҖмҰқ кі„нҡҚ

### 14.5 MAIL-01~12 sole-writer/parity/fencing tests

| ID | кІҖмҰқ | н•©кІ© мҰқкұ° |
| --- | --- | --- |
| MAIL-01 | JS/Python/Outlook/ERP scanner/projector caller graphкіј sole normal caller | cutover allowlistм—җлҠ” HPP coordinator/projectorл§Ң; direct project-history writer `0` |
| MAIL-02 | same-node process lock | л‘җ лІҲм§ё coordinator/projectorк°Җ lock нҡҚл“қ мӢӨнҢЁ, DB/file delta `0` |
| MAIL-03 | AвҶ’B reclassification identity | к°ҷмқҖ `mail_occurrence_id`, operation/generation/`classification_epoch`мқҳ `reclassified_out/in`, current.last_eventлҠ” in-event FK, delete `0` |
| MAIL-04 | DB transaction crash points | identity/current/event/outboxмқҳ before/after each failpointм—җм„ң partial commit `0` |
| MAIL-05 | commit л’Ө stage/final-publish crash | committed outbox мң м§Җ, incomplete stage л¬ҙмӢң, previous accepted generation ліҙмЎҙ |
| MAIL-06 | outbox replay logical exactly-once | NнҡҢ retryк°Җ лҸҷмқј generation/manifestлҘј л°ҳнҷҳн•ҳкі  duplicate row/publish `0` |
| MAIL-07 | DB/CSV/ICS/XLSX generation parity | cutoff, generation, source_epoch_digest/max_classification_epoch, projector_epoch, row count, ordered digestк°Җ лӘЁл‘җ лҸҷмқј |
| MAIL-08 | stale role epoch reject | DB transactionмқҖ stale `classification_epoch`, outbox claim/stage/final publishлҠ” stale `projector_epoch` write `0`; origin epochлҠ” л¶ҲліҖ |
| MAIL-09 | failover state machine | P8мқҖ synthetic `(C_E,P_E)` freeze/revokeвҶ’`(C_E+1,P_E+1)` classification-firstвҶ’projector-second, pre-checkpoint old-outbox recovery allowlistмҷҖ stale-role reject; мӢӨм ң failover role switchлҠ” C08B/P10 лі„лҸ„ мҠ№мқё |
| MAIL-10 | failback state machine | P8мқҖ synthetic `(C_E+1,P_E+1)` freeze/revokeвҶ’`(C_E+2,P_E+2)` HPP catch-up/promoteмҷҖ мһҗлҸҷ failback `0`; мӢӨм ң failback drillмқҖ C08B/P10 лі„лҸ„ мҠ№мқё |
| MAIL-11 | partial Mac coverage | `partial`мқҖ exact count `>=0`+non-empty gap, `not_collected`лҠ” null count+non-empty gapмқҙл©° м „мІҙ mail л¶Җмһ¬лЎң н•ҙм„қлҗҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ |
| MAIL-12 | raw/private exclusion | body/html/recipient payload/attachment/path/secretк°Җ DB event, outbox, manifest, CSV/XLSXм—җ `0` |

мқҙ н‘ңмқҳ мөңмў… acceptance ownerлҠ” н•ң phaseк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. H01AлҠ” `MAIL-03`мқҳ project-independent identityмҷҖ
append-only supersession л¶Җл¶„, shadow surfaceмқҳ `MAIL-12`, `D26-FX-02/12/13/15/16`л§Ң мҶҢмң н•ңлӢӨ.
H01BлҠ” ratified D25 mail policy л’Ө `MAIL-11` contract/synthetic fixtureл§Ң мҶҢмң н•ҳкі  мӢӨм ң Mac/source
coverage receiptлҠ” лі„лҸ„ authority м „ `UNKNOWN/VERIFY_HP`лӢӨ. Current caller graphлҠ” H01 read-only evidenceм§Җл§Ң
`MAIL-01` acceptanceк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. P8мқҖ `MAIL-01/02`, full DB/FK/epoch `MAIL-03`, `MAIL-04..08`, synthetic-only
`MAIL-09/10`кіј `MAIL-11/12` regressionмқ„ мҶҢмң н•ңлӢӨ. P9мқҖ н•ң н”„лЎңм қнҠё DBвҶ”CSV/ICS/XLSX parityмҷҖ bounded
switch/rollbackмқ„, P10мқҖ мӢӨм ң role/leaseмҷҖ manual `MAIL-09/10` failover/failback л°Ҹ D23 emergency
fallbackмқ„ мҶҢмң н•ңлӢӨ. м•һ phaseмқҳ н•©м„ұ PASSлҘј л’Ө phaseмқҳ live authorityлЎң мҠ№кІ©н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

#### 14.6B HP-INGRESSВ·HP-SESSIONВ·HP-QUERY acceptance

| ID | кІҖмҰқ | н•©кІ© мҰқкұ° |
| --- | --- | --- |
| HP-INGRESS-01 | source subtypeлі„ custody/staging/quarantine/promotion owner | exact owner/binding matrix unresolved `0`; D27 лҜёкІ°м • н•ӯлӘ©мқҖ PASS лҢҖмӢ  HOLD |

| HP-INGRESS-03 | upload receiptмқҳ claim ceiling | project promotion/ArtifactRevision/Wiki/RAG/task mutation мһҗлҸҷ л°ңмғқ `0` |
| HP-INGRESS-04 | reference/copy/move/derive decision matrix | durabilityВ·hashВ·sizeВ·ACLВ·retention proof; unauthorized copy/move/delete `0` |
| HP-INGRESS-05 | promotion idempotency/conflict | same operation+digest no-op, same operation+different digest quarantine |
| HP-INGRESS-06 | security gate | blocked type лҳҗлҠ” required scan missing/failedмқҙл©ҙ promotion `0`; extension/hashлҘј malware scanмңјлЎң мҳӨмқё `0` |

#### 14.6.1 D26 pre-approval synthetic fixture matrix

м•„лһҳ fixtureлҠ” кө¬нҳ„ мҠ№мқёмқҙлӮҳ D26 ratificationмқҙ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. к°Ғ H sliceк°Җ мӢңмһ‘лҗ  л•Ң owner-approved exact typed
ref allowlistмҷҖ кІ°н•©н•  м„Өкі„ лӘ©лЎқмқҙл©°, `TBD`лҘј fixtureк°Җ мһ„мқҳ к°’мңјлЎң мұ„мҡ°кұ°лӮҳ н•©кІ©мңјлЎң л°”кҫём§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

| ID | synthetic input | н•©кІ© лҳҗлҠ” ліҙмЎҙн•ҙм•ј н•  кІ°кіј | л°ҳл“ңмӢң reject/HOLDн•  кІ°кіј | owner gate |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |

лӘЁл“  н•ӯлӘ©мқҖ pre-approval fixtureмқҙл©° нҳ„мһ¬ acceptance мҰқкұ°к°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. нҠ№нһҲ `TBD`, owner scope,
normalization лҳҗлҠ” gap vocabularyк°Җ н•„мҡ”н•ң `D26-FX-01`, `03`, `05`~`07`, `09`, `13`, `16`~`20`мқҖ
н•ҙлӢ№ кІ°м • м „ expected `HOLD`лӢӨ. H06мқҖ мқҙ HOLDлҘј л№Ҳ мқҙл ҘмқҙлӮҳ `complete_no_events`лЎң л°”кҫём§Җ м•Ҡкі 
HP-HISTORY-08/11 blockerлЎң м „лӢ¬н•ңлӢӨ.

### 14.7 мӢӨн–ү мҲңм„ңмҷҖ adversarial set

1. C00A public blocker preflight вҶ’ separately approved C00Q public/synthetic query-tool foundation вҶ’ separately approved C00B P0 baseline/source-owner inventory
2. H00~H06 + H01C sent/received reconciliation + MAIL/HP-HISTORY/HP-COMMкіј HP-INGRESSмқҳ contract/shadow schema, custody, coverage, replay/export tests; live caller-zero/payload promotion/cutover/failover claim м—ҶмқҢ
3. P2~P3 foundation acceptance, лі‘л ¬ H07A contract л’Ө H07B Slack immutable revision/project-context Shadow, P4~P5мҷҖ `context_acceptance_gate`; м Ғмҡ© Slack gapмқ„ `not_applicable`лЎң мҲЁкё°м§Җ м•ҠмқҢ
4. P6 candidate-only discoveryмҷҖ P7 Driver acceptance
5. P8 core acceptance л’Ө лі„лҸ„ I8/Q8 approvalм—җм„ң feature-OFF ingress receiptмҷҖ accepted-query pointer fixtureлҘј кІҖмҰқн•ңлӢӨ. P8 core мһҗмІҙлҠ” same мһ…л Ҙ replay 2нҡҢ byte-identical digest, sole-writer/mail-outbox/cutoverмҷҖ synthetic classification/projector epoch-vector testsлҘј мҶҢмң н•ңлӢӨ. Personal lifecycleмқҖ core P8 gate м•„лӢҳ
6. duplicate, conflicting digest, expired/revoked authority, stale expected revision, short-ID collision,
   path traversal, symlink escape, cross-project ACL, clock regression, packet gap adversarial tests
7. accepted C00Q toolмқ„ мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ©н•ң HP query-only inventoryмҷҖ C09A migration dry-run
8. P9 core one-project HPP-primary/task pilotкіј rollback drillмқ„ лЁјм Җ лӢ«лҠ”лӢӨ. к·ё PASS л’Ө лі„лҸ„ I9/Q9 approvalм—җм„ңл§Ң one-project promotion/query pilotмқ„ н•ҳкі , AX-G1 reviewлҘј мӢңмһ‘н•ңлӢӨ. мӢӨм ң failover/failbackкіј personal team rolloutмқҖ P10 лі„лҸ„ мҠ№мқё
9. HP-SESSION/HP-QUERY crashВ·ACLВ·generationВ·candidate-only synthetic setкіј root/dev-ERP/docs regression
10. В§12.1 sliceлі„ minimum independent review. кіөк°ң кё°мӨҖм„  `main@310640b7a5692298227026b547a68bcb25d2b330`мқҳ
    plan-scope validation/reviewлҠ” `PASS`мқҙл©°, к·ё л’Ө л¬ём„ң deltaлҠ” publish м „ к°ҷмқҖ лІ”мң„мқҳ validatorмҷҖ
    independent reviewлҘј лӢӨмӢң нҶөкіјн•ҙм•ј н•ңлӢӨ. authority/migration/live mutation/workflow sliceлҠ”
    fresh executor + separate verifier Level 3

мҰқкұ° packetмқҖ commit/allowed paths, opaque refs, к°Ғ кІҖмҰқмқҳ pass/fail/blockedмҷҖ exit, before/after
aggregate/digest, public/private boundary verdict, rollback кІ°кіј лҳҗлҠ” `not_run` мқҙмң , reviewer verdictлҘј
к°Җм§„лӢӨ.

нҳ„мһ¬ plan publish validatorлҠ” лӢӨмқҢмқ„ мӮ¬мҡ©н•ңлӢӨ.

```text
git diff --check
npm run ui:docs:check
npm run validate:path-policy
npm run ui:done:check
immutable oracle working-tree diff + before/after blob
AC-01~AC-25 completeness
fresh root validation/review (кіөк°ң кё°мӨҖм„  `main@310640b7a5692298227026b547a68bcb25d2b330`к№Ңм§Җ PASS;
нӣ„мҶҚ deltaлҠ” publish м „ мһ¬кІҖмҰқ)
```

Implementation лӢЁкі„мқҳ мөңмҶҢ regressionмқҖ `validate:task-engine-core-v1`,
`validate:task-engine-rag-v1`, `validate:file-activity`, `validate:rag`, full dev-ERP tests, root testsлҘј
нҸ¬н•Ён•ңлӢӨ. мӢӨн–үн•ҳм§Җ лӘ»н•ң н•ӯлӘ©мқҖ м„ұкіөмңјлЎң к°„мЈјн•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡкі  `not_run`кіј blockerлҘј кё°лЎқн•ңлӢӨ.

## 15. one-project pilotмҷҖ лӢЁкі„лі„ activation

Pilot projectлҠ” ownerк°Җ м§Җм •н•ңлӢӨ. agentлҠ” project codeлҘј л§Ңл“Өкұ°лӮҳ мӢӨм ң мқҙлҰ„мқ„ public л¬ём„ңм—җ м“°м§Җ
м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. TaskлҠ” 1~3к°ңлЎң м ңн•ңн•ҳкі , unrelated row/pathлҠ” allowlist л°–мқҙлӢӨ.

| лӢЁкі„ | кё°ліё мғҒнғң | н•ҳлҠ” мқј | нҶөкіј мЎ°кұҙ | мӢӨнҢЁ мӢң |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| P0 baseline/inventory | OFF/read-only | C00A public blocker вҶ’ C00Q synthetic tool вҶ’ C00B approved source owner/writer/consumer/source-availability inventory | exact refs, raw leak 0, authority-attested current gap+next proof, C00B P0 receipt вҶ’ H00 only | `BLOCKED`; H00 ratification м „ six-state completenessмҷҖ exact C00Q child packet л°–мқҳ codeВ·лӘЁл“  DB/live write мӢңмһ‘ кёҲм§Җ |
| P1 histories/coverage | OFF/shadow | H00~H06 mailВ·voiceВ·structured PC workВ·fileВ·run/log append-only envelopeмҷҖ coverage; H01м—җлҠ” sent/received mailbox observation reconciliation нҸ¬н•Ё. H07A Slack contractлҠ” лі‘л ¬ мӨҖл№„ | MAIL/HP-HISTORY/HP-COMM, replay/export parity, gap honesty | adapters/exporters OFF, source owners ліҙмЎҙ |
| P2 IDs/refs/clocks | synthetic | C01A/C08A stable IDs, typed refs, owner-native clocksмҷҖ valid/known query-cutoff crosswalk | collision/orphan/bare join 0, lossless clock/packet receipt | scoped revert; P3 кёҲм§Җ |
| P3 immutable revisions | synthetic/shadow | C06A source/file/artifact revisionкіј relation lineage; accepted H07Aк°Җ мһҲмңјл©ҙ H07B Slack message/edit/delete revision ShadowлҘј лі‘л ¬ кІҖмҰқ | append/supersede, exact content/revision, no rekey, HP-COMM-07~12 | reader/Slack collector OFF, original events ліҙмЎҙ |
| P4 exact RAG/Wiki | writer OFF | C05/C06B project/common resolverмҷҖ revision-bound RAG/Wiki | exact locator/source revision, isolation, no-delete | target reader/writer OFF, legacy мң м§Җ |
| P5 validated context | read-only | C07A history+time+relation+RAG/Wiki+gap assembly; м Ғмҡ©лҗң Slack project channelмқҖ accepted H07B sourceлҘј н•Ёк»ҳ мқҪмқҢ | deterministic `context_acceptance_gate` receipt, mapped channel project scope exact, duplicate task candidate 0 | P6 кёҲм§Җ; Slack gapВ·unmapped channelмқ„ мҲЁкё°м§Җ м•ҠмқҢ |
| P6 discovery | candidate-only | C04A accepted contextм—җм„ң TaskIntent candidate мғқм„ұ | ERP/task row delta 0, candidate replay/idempotency | discovery OFF; P7 кёҲм§Җ |
| P7 TaskDriver | synthetic | C01B why/why-now, authority, expiry/revocation, idempotency | Driver acceptance receipt | P8 schema/writer кёҲм§Җ |
| P8 sole writers/outbox | feature OFF/synthetic | parallel C02+C08F вҶ’ C03 вҶ’ C04B ERP atomic writer, mail current+event+outbox, five-lane HPP projector/parity/fencing | V01~16 applicable + MAIL-01~12 synthetic + HP-HISTORY-10 cutover fixture, direct/non-HPP writer 0; live role switch 0 | coordinator/projector OFF, old reader мң м§Җ |
| P9 one-project pilot | bounded ON then OFF | C09*/C10 1~3 task + one-project five-lane derived generation + C07B feedback/read-only life trees | exact refs, unrelated delta 0, sourceвҶ”CSV/XLSX parity, replay/rollback, event ліҙмЎҙ | all target writers OFF + non-destructive rollback |
| P10 separate activation | default OFF | C08B/G00/G01/C09S/AX/AR/IQ/MLмқ„ к°Ғк°Ғ лі„лҸ„ мҠ№мқё; manual failover/failback | capabilityлі„ Level 3, lease/epoch, RTO/RPO, rollback | ліҙлҘҳк°Җ кё°ліё; automatic failback `0` |

P9 pilot approvalмқҖ P10, scheduler, network transport, team write, alert delivery, broader corpus,
failover/failback, AX/AgentRun/ML activation мҠ№мқёмқҙ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. к°Ғ кё°лҠҘмқҖ лі„лҸ„ gateлҘј к°–лҠ”лӢӨ.

## 16. Engineering IQВ·ML мһҘкё° нҷ•мһҘм„ 

Engineering IQлҠ” лӘЁлҚё м җмҲҳліҙлӢӨ лЁјм Җ **кІҖмҰқ к°ҖлҠҘн•ң trace**лҘј л§Ңл“ лӢӨ.

```text
RequirementRevision
  вҶ’ FunctionRef
  вҶ’ InterfaceRef
  вҶ’ RiskRef
  вҶ’ DecisionRef
  вҶ’ VerificationRef
  вҶ’ OutcomeRef
  вҶ’ CorrectionRef
```

к°Ғ edgeлҠ” typed endpoint, valid_at/known_at, source/evidence ref, relation event, supersedesлҘј к°Җм§„лӢӨ.
Trace UIлҠ” coverage, missing verification, stale decision, correction chainмқ„ мқҪкё° м „мҡ©мңјлЎң ліҙм—¬мӨҖлӢӨ.
н”„лЎңм қнҠё мӣҗл¬ёмқ„ central training storeлЎң ліөмӮ¬н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

ML/rankingмқҖ лӢӨмқҢ мЎ°кұҙмқ„ лӘЁл‘җ л§ҢмЎұн•  л•Ңл§Ң shadow candidateк°Җ лҗңлӢӨ.

- ownerк°Җ label м •мқҳ, minimum volume/quality, class balance, privacy boundaryлҘј кІ°м •
- labelл§ҲлӢӨ source/decision/verification/outcome provenanceк°Җ мЎҙмһ¬
- deterministic rule/baselineкіј frozen holdoutмқҙ мЎҙмһ¬
- shadow scoreк°Җ task/sourceлҘј м§Ғм ‘ м“°м§Җ м•ҠмқҢ
- calibration, false positive, subgroup bias, drift, rollback кё°мӨҖмқ„ нҶөкіј

нҳ„мһ¬лҠ” canonical traceмҷҖ verified label poolмқҙ `UNKNOWN`мқҙлҜҖлЎң IQ01кіј ML01мқҖ `DEFER`лӢӨ. мқҙ лІ”мң„лҘј
core TaskDriver мқјм •м—җ лҒјмӣҢ л„Јм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

## 17. owner кІ°м •н‘ңВ·UNKNOWNВ·VERIFY_HP

### 17.1 ownerк°Җ кІ°м •н•  кІғ

| ID | кІ°м • | к¶ҢмһҘ м•Ҳм „ кё°ліёк°’ | мҳҒн–Ҙ slice | кІ°м • м „ н—Ҳмҡ© / кёҲм§Җ |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| D01 | TaskDriver physical storeмҷҖ task-table physical writer | dev-ERP SQLite same-transaction table + `TaskEngineTransactionCoordinator` 1к°ң; logical authorityл§Ң л¶„лҰ¬. Mail table writerлҠ” D21мқҳ лі„лҸ„ identity | C02/C10 | pure/synthetic н—Ҳмҡ© / live install кёҲм§Җ |
| D02 | кіөмӢқ typed `task_event` мӢ м„Ө vs `event_log` нҷ•мһҘ | мғҲ `task_event` + н•ңмӢң mirror | C02/C03 | fixture н—Ҳмҡ© / legacy м ңкұ° кёҲм§Җ |
| D03 | legacy `unclassified/open/doing`кіј canonical work status/reopen мқҳлҜё, `valid_at/known_at` query cutoffмҷҖ source-native clock crosswalk | lifecycle м •ліёмқҳ л‘җ м¶•В·к°’мқҖ к·ёлҢҖлЎң мӮ¬мҡ©; legacy statusлҠ” explicit crosswalk, reopenмқҖ same task reversal. `valid_at/known_at`мқҖ query cutoffлЎң л‘җкі  persisted source eventмқҳ fact/knowledge clocksлҘј ліҙмЎҙн•ҳлҠ” lossless mappingмқ„ ownerк°Җ ratifyн•ңлӢӨ. ambiguous status лҳҗлҠ” lossy clock mappingмқҖ DEFER | C01A/C01B/C03/C06A/C07A | synthetic status/clock crosswalk dry-run / мғҲ decision stateВ·мқҳлҜё мһҗлҸҷ ліҖнҷҳкіј native clock collapse кёҲм§Җ |
| D04 | human-onlyмҷҖ bounded auto-apply лІ”мң„ | кё°ліё human-only; policyлҠ” opt-in+expiry+revocation | C04A/C04B/G01 | candidate н—Ҳмҡ© / auto-open/apply кёҲм§Җ |
| D05 | task ID allocator/reservation/retry authority | sole coordinatorл§Ң л°ңкёүВ·мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ© | C02/C10 | synthetic reservation / мҷёл¶Җ caller ID л°ңкёү кёҲм§Җ |
| D06 | SourceRevisionмҷҖ relation/application exact physical owner/writer | SourceRevisionмқҖ кё°мЎҙ `_workmeta/<project|system>/knowledge/source_revision_records`+мӣ”лі„ events, knowledge applicationмқҖ project `ontology/knowledge_bindings/events` мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ©; occurrenceлҠ” source-local мң м§Җ. Non-knowledge relation ownerлҠ” contract sync м „ UNKNOWNмқҙл©° generic ledger кёҲм§Җ | C06A/C09L/C09S/C10 | owner adapter/validator / live materializationВ·parallel truthВ·fallback кёҲм§Җ |
| D07 | legacy RAG project/common л¶„лҘҳмҷҖ pilot project | unresolvedлҠ” project/common м–ҙлҠҗ мӘҪм—җлҸ„ мһҗлҸҷ мқҙлҸҷн•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡкі  quarantine | C05/C10 | inventory/dry-run / copyВ·delete кёҲм§Җ |
| D08 | WikiRevisionВ·knowledge truth promotion authority | source-bound candidateмҷҖ owner promotion л¶„лҰ¬ | C06B | reader/candidate / truth мһҗлҸҷмҠ№кІ© кёҲм§Җ |
| D09 | Verification/Outcome canonical ownerмҷҖ fruit мөңмҶҢ relation | completion ref н•„мҲҳ, лӮҳлЁём§Җ лҜём •мқҖ UNKNOWN; мһҗлҸҷ close кёҲм§Җ | C07B/C10 | gap projection / мһ„мқҳ entity мғқм„ұ кёҲм§Җ |

Macмқҙ expected sourceлқјл©ҙ source coverage factsлҠ” D25 policy inputмңјлЎңл§Ң м“°кі  normal project-history write allowlistлҠ” emptyлӢӨ. лі„лҸ„ dormant `project_history_emergency_fallback`мқҖ explicit P10 approvalм—җм„ңл§Ң five-lane projectorлҘј л§Ўкі , mail coordinatorлҠ” coverage+лі„лҸ„ мҠ№мқёмқҙ мһҲмқ„ л•Ңл§Ң лҸҷмһ‘ | D25/C08B/P10 | monitor/alert candidate / normalВ·automatic writeмҷҖ ERP task write кёҲм§Җ |

| D25 | live five-lane completeness кё°мӨҖ | C00Bмқҳ authority-backed source-availability inventoryлҘј мһ…л ҘмңјлЎң л°ӣкі  H00мқҳ м—¬м„Ҝ stateмҷҖ count/null matrixлҠ” мһ¬м •мқҳн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. нҳ„мһ¬ `UNKNOWN/VERIFY_HP`; D25лҠ” laneлі„ coverage expected source set, `known_at` window, freshness threshold, gap vocabulary, applicability rule/refлҘј м •н•Ё | H01~H06 | public/synthetic / C00Bм—җм„ң completeness PASSВ·мғҲ stateВ·мһ„мқҳ gap code мЈјмһҘ кёҲм§Җ |
| D26 | source-to-lane exact typed identityмҷҖ H05 run schema allowlist | В§3.4.4мқҳ candidateлҘј exact `{entity_type,owner_surface,entity_id}` allowlistлЎң owner ratifyн•ңлӢӨ. voice event/revisionкіј mail owner, D19 instruction owner, D20 schedule owner, H04 file event subtypeмқҖ м•„м§Ғ `TBD`; `logical_file_id`лҠ” lineage refлӢӨ. daily ledger/contextлҠ” projection refмқј лҝҗ occurrence/event/countк°Җ м•„лӢҲл©° task-chat completion-hook/full-message summaryлҠ” coverageк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. H05лҠ” report-authoring exact schemaл¶Җн„° мӢңмһ‘н•ҳкі  current five-field `id`лҠ” full-record digest/conflict/boundary кі„м•Ҫ м „ ineligible, `runs/**` recursion кёҲм§Җ | H01~H06 | public/synthetic / `TBD`В·unknown schemaВ·projection мӨ‘ліөВ·cross-lane duplicateВ·private run scan кёҲм§Җ |
| D27 | ingress custodyВ·promoterВ·reference/copy/move/deriveмҷҖ per-source security policy | plan defaultлҠ” pointer/hash/referenceмқҙл©° мӨ‘м•ҷ serviceк°Җ м§Ғм ‘ uploadлҘј л°ӣмңјл©ҙ к·ё inboxк°Җ custodyлҘј к°Җм§„лӢӨ. exact mail raw/attachment owner tension, promoter identity/path, destination binding, retention/legal hold, ACL, required malware scan, backup/restore, deletion authorityлҘј source kindлі„ кІ°м •н•ңлӢӨ. projector/task writerмҷҖ л¶„лҰ¬н•ҳкі  move/delete кё°ліё кёҲм§Җ | I0~I10/H01/H04/P2/P3/P8/P9/P10 | public/synthetic matrix / physical folder мғқм„ұВ·payload read/copy/move/deleteВ·scan enforcementВ·live promotion кёҲм§Җ |
| D28 | personal WorkSession cardinalityВ·thread/node bindingВ·outbox/ackВ·missing SLAВ·completion approver | ownerк°Җ plan defaultлЎң `{assignment epoch,account}` active primary н•ҳлӮҳмҷҖ multiple checkpoint, closeoutвү official completionмқ„ мұ„нғқн–ҲлӢӨ. exact opaque thread-ref capability, registered node, handoff/supersession, local outbox writer/path/fsync/encryption/retention, stale/missing SLA, official completion authorityлҠ” лі„лҸ„ нҷ•м • | W0~W10/AX01 | schema/synthetic fixture / current record мҶҢкёү н•ҙм„қВ·raw thread м ҖмһҘВ·live team writeВ·auto completion кёҲм§Җ |
| D29 | ERP UI/MCP primary queryВ·accepted generationВ·ACL/no-fallbackВ·team knowledge candidate authority | ownerк°Җ ERP UI/MCP primary read, files=audit snapshot, explicit `project|common` scope/no implicit fallback, team candidate-onlyлҘј plan defaultлЎң мұ„нғқн–ҲлӢӨ. exact grant/admin existence-leak policy, manifest/current-pointer owner, cursor/retention, candidate reviewer/approver/writerмҷҖ project ID crosswalkлҠ” нҷ•м • н•„мҡ” | Q0~Q10/P4/P5/P8/P9/P10 | schema/read-only/synthetic / accepted pointer advanceВ·live endpointВ·implicit fallbackВ·direct Wiki/RAG/canon/task write кёҲм§Җ |
| D30 | generic external agent surface schemaВ·truth ceilingВ·non-nesting | direct Codexк°Җ кё°ліёмқҙкі  `TeamAgentGatewayAdapter`мҷҖ `EngineeringWorkbenchAdapter`лҠ” sibling optional MCP clientлӢӨ. native task/session/memory/doneмқҖ client-local, WorkSession writer н•ҳлӮҳ, surface ліҖкІҪмқҖ revoke+handoff+supersession, official completionмқҖ лі„лҸ„ TaskEngine authority | EXT-G0/EXT-G1 | official-doc/read-only comparisonкіј public synthetic negative fixture / AX-G1~G3 м°ЁлӢЁВ·installВ·live endpointВ·cross-adapter nestingВ·native done promotion кёҲм§Җ |

| D32 | Orcaнҳ• workbench versionВ·worktreeВ·permissionВ·credentialВ·diff/artifactВ·Git policy | stable pinned version, Manual launch, one coordinator+disjoint workers, no native subteams, public-safe code task, direct main/push/PR 0, Codex current-main bounded reimplementation | ORCA-T1/ORCA-T2/P10 | frozen rubric/public synthetic fixture / permission bypassВ·host-secret accessВ·Hermes nestingВ·binary multi-writer кёҲм§Җ |
