| D34 | Slack app/workspace/channel identityВ·project bindingВ·history/revision/retentionВ·user mappingВ·attachment boundary | stable `workspace_id+channel_id` effective-dated project binding, allowlisted joined project channels, outer event delivery dedupeмҷҖ logical message/thread/edit/delete revision л¶„лҰ¬, HPP sole normal collector. project channelмқҖ authoritative default project scopeм§Җл§Ң taskлҠ” candidate-only. DM/common/unmapped/Slack ConnectлҠ” explicit rule м „ HOLD | H07A/H07B/P3/P5/P9/P10 | HP-COMM-07~12 / auto join/post, name/fuzzy project mapping, raw/secret/attachment copy, message/reaction completion promotion, live appВ·tokenВ·scheduler нҷңм„ұнҷ” кёҲм§Җ |

#### 17.1.1 мІ« мҠ№мқёкіј нӣ„мҶҚ ratification мһ…л Ҙ

м•„лһҳ н‘ңлҠ” owner кІ°м •мқ„ лҢҖмӢ н•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡкі , `мҠ№мқё` н•ң лӢЁм–ҙк°Җ л¬ҙм—Үмқ„ нҸ¬н•Ён•ҙм•ј н•ҳлҠ”м§Җ кі м •н•ңлӢӨ. кІ°м •мқҖ
лҜёлҰ¬ кё°лЎқн•  мҲҳ мһҲм§Җл§Ң м„ н–ү acceptance мҲңм„ңлҘј кұҙл„Ҳлӣ°лҠ” к¶Ңн•ңмқҖ л§Ңл“Өм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

| gate / earliest apply | ownerк°Җ exactн•ҳкІҢ лӢөн•  кІғ | лӢөмқҙ м—Ҷмқ„ л•Ң м•Ҳм „ кё°ліёк°’ | мҠ№мқё м „ н—Ҳмҡ© | кёҲм§Җ | acceptance evidence / unlock |
| --- | --- | --- | --- | --- | --- |
| `C00A` / retained | historical accepted `BLOCKED` receipt | prerequisite evidence only, current execution authority `false`, P1 `BLOCKED` | retained public receipt ref | private/live query, report write, code mutation | C00Q prerequisite historyл§Ң ліҙмЎҙ, P1мқҖ кі„мҶҚ мһ кёҲ |
| `C00Q` / retained | frozen inventory CLI/test/schema exact refsмҷҖ `task_engine_c00q_formal_acceptance_pass_v1` | formal receipt retained, execution approval expired | public/synthetic foundationкіј retained receipt кІҖмҰқ | live/private input, report write, DB/API/runtime mutation, P1 unlock | мғҲ мӢӨн–үмқҖ мғҲ authorityк°Җ н•„мҡ”н•ҳл©° retained receiptлҠ” P0 effectк°Җ м•„лӢҳ |
| `C00B` / retained C00Q receipt л’Ө | `owner_authorized_query_only`; approval-time SHA, laneлі„ exact authority/source/profile, metadata output, approval refВ·expiry | `non_executable_hold`, live facts `UNKNOWN/VERIFY_HP`, P1 `BLOCKED` | retained frozen C00Q tool receiptмҷҖ лі„лҸ„ мҠ№мқёлҗң metadata-only source | doctor/workspace inventoryлЎң лҢҖмІҙ, raw/private payload, tool ліҖкІҪ, source/tracked/runtime mutation, exact one-path л°– output write, H00 six-state completeness м„ мӮ¬мҡ© | C00-LIVE-01..04 authority-backed inventory closureВ·zero-mutation receipt вҶ’ C00B PASSлҠ” H00 ratification reviewл§Ң н—Ҳмҡ© |
| `H00` / accepted+unexpired C00B PASS л’Ө | `main@16190bff6c1dd9e101c11a078b97e84f1c1c43ea`мқҳ м„ё exact blobкіј independent event envelope+coverage receipt pair, literal `unknown`, `known_at` half-open window, six-state count/null/gap semanticsлҘј к°Ғк°Ғ `RATIFY | HOLD`; content-addressed-until-revoked policyмҷҖ issued-at мҠ№мқё | `canon_candidate` HOLD | м„ё pinned public fileмқҳ approval-time blob match, exact test 20/20 receipt, fresh Level 2 review | file edit, adapter, migration, live use, completeness claim, D19~D34 мһҗлҸҷмҠ№мқё | owner decision ref + bound blob/test/review receipts; overall RATIFYлҠ” H01~H05 exact child-packet reviewл§Ң м—ҙкі  adapter/H06/writer к¶Ңн•ңмқҖ кі„мҶҚ false |
| `D19` / H03A м „ | negative boundaryлҘј лЁјм Җ ratify; мӢ к·ң instruction/receipt sourceл§ҲлӢӨ exact owner surface, schema/version, ID allocator, consentВ·retentionмқ„ лі„лҸ„ лӘ…мӢң | existing bounded WorkSessionл§Ң нӣ„ліҙ; лӮҳлЁём§Җ HOLD, broad capture OFF | WorkSessionкіј negative fixture | whole task chatВ·hook full-message summaryВ·screenВ·keystrokeВ·OS capture, owner лҜём • source | allowlist/negative test/direct-caller evidence вҶ’ H03A input binding |
| `D20` / H03B м „ | schedule current owner/path, immutable revision/event owner/path, stable row-ID owner/schedule scope, canonicalization/timezone, sole writer | `HOLD` | synthetic stale-revision/canonicalization fixture | row ID л°ңлӘ…, live event, task discovery | current/revision/event replayмҷҖ stale expected-revision reject вҶ’ H03B |
| `D24` / H06 target нҷ•м • м „ | лӢӨм„Ҝ exact view nameкіј CSV/XLSX(л©”мқјмқҖ ICS нҸ¬н•Ё) target, redacted projection-field allowlist, HPP sole-normal-projector, Mac/лӢӨлҘё PC normal allowlist emptyлҘј logical TARGETмңјлЎң ratify | мқҙлҰ„мқҖ candidate, materialization/export acceptance `OFF` | schema/path/field fixture | unapproved display field export, private folder мғқм„ұ, non-HPP normal write | target path/field allowlistВ·shadow schema fixture вҶ’ H06 target contract; мӢӨм ң мғқм„ұмқҖ P9 лі„лҸ„ |
| `D25` / lane coverage acceptance м „ | policy revisionкіј laneлі„ expected source set, `known_at` window, freshness, gap code, applicability rule/ref | `UNKNOWN/VERIFY_HP`, `HOLD` | H00 six-state synthetic matrix | state/count мһ¬м •мқҳ, gap л°ңлӘ…, live PASS | per-lane policy fixture л’Ө мӢӨм ң receiptлҠ” лі„лҸ„ authority вҶ’ H01~H06 coverage acceptance |
| `D26` / lane adapter м „ | лӘЁл“  В§3.4.4 subtypeмқҳ versioned exact typed triple, owner binding, ID grammar/schema, event/revision relation, existence/conflict validator; five-field ineligible мң м§Җ/н•ҙм ң мЎ°кұҙ | лӘЁл“  `TBD`мҷҖ unknown subtype `HOLD` | `D26-FX-01..20` | wildcard/alias/bare ID, cross-lane duplicate, projection мһ¬мһ…л Ҙ | 20 fixture + lane-owner binding/existence evidence вҶ’ н•ҙлӢ№ H01~H05 adapterмҷҖ мөңмў… H06 |
| `D27` / I8В·A8-SYNTH contract м „ | source-kind custody/staging/quarantine/promoter/destination, HPP logical RAW/ERP/runtime storage classes, transfer-service/promoter sole-writer split, control-vs-binary plane, upload/download ticket binding, operation allowlist, retention/legal hold/ACL/scan/archive-bomb/media/hash/size/backup/delete authority | HPP custody is `TARGET`; pointer/reference кё°ліё, strict office-LAN authenticated HTTPS data plane, client destination pathВ·remote D/UNC/SMBВ·VPN/TailscaleВ·move/deleteВ·live promotion `OFF`; exact path/network/certs/service health `VERIFY_HP` | public custody/actor-ticket matrix, swap/replay/revoke-race/path-traversal/archive-bomb/hash/size/media mismatch, idempotent finalizeмҷҖ exact-revision range fixture | path мғқм„ұ/м—ҙкұ°, payload read/copy/move/delete, cloud-synced DB/central RAW/queue, malware-scan overclaim | D27~D29+exact public security packet acceptance вҶ’ independent A8-SYNTH; canaryлҠ” private receipt+owner+Level 3 лі„лҸ„ |
| `D28` / A8-SYNTHВ·AX-G1 м „ | exact assignment epoch owner, `user/device/agent/opaque-thread/task/project/artifact/revision/action/expiry` actor chain, one-time enrollment/recovery, mTLS trust, OS broker refresh, delegation parent/child/revoke cascade, step-up action set, opaque thread-ref/node binding, local outbox writer/path/fsync/encryption/retention, missing SLA, official completion approver | human grantвҲ©trusted deviceвҲ©agent policyвҲ©task/object/action, earliest expiry, routine silent refresh, one active primary, multiple checkpoints, closeoutвү completion; exact bindingмқҖ `VERIFY_HP` | enrollment/broker/delegation ceiling+revoke cascade, routine no-repeat-prompt, pure lifecycle/outbox/crash/ack replay/adversarial fixture | current record мҶҢкёү migration, raw thread ID, ticket/child grant surviving revoke, per-chunk prompt, team activation | HP-SESSION synthetic вҶ’ independent A8-SYNTH/AX-G2 feature-OFF; canary/one-seat/teamмқҖ к°Ғк°Ғ лі„лҸ„ |
| `D29` / Q8В·A8-SYNTH adapter м „ | artifact/revision/action grant authorityмҷҖ uniform existence policy, project/common grant, accepted-generation manifest/current-pointer/cursor owner, ACL-aware RAG field/chunk pre/post filter+cache key/revoke, exact revision range download, immutable redacted derivative lineage including hidden sheet/slideВ·formulaВ·comment/noteВ·embedded object, candidate reviewer/approver/writer | ERP UI/MCP primary query, files audit snapshot, explicit scope/no fallback, exact revision/action only, redacted derivative no raw fallback, team candidate-only | schema/ACL/existence/generation/API-file parity, field/chunk/cache revoke, derivative lineage, range resume/ticket audience fixture | live endpoint/pointer advance, implicit/latest/raw fallback, direct truth write, unauthorized existence/cache hit | HP-QUERY synthetic вҶ’ independent A8-SYNTH/Q8 feature-OFF; canary exact revisionмқҖ private receipt+owner+Level 3 лі„лҸ„ |
| `D30` / EXT-G0В·EXT-G1 м „ | generic client identity, native state claim ceiling, one WorkSession writer, child write кёҲм§Җ, cross-adapter non-nesting, revoke/handoff/supersession, external receipt crosswalk | direct Codex default, external adapter OFF | official-doc comparisonкіј EXT-G0 design; EXT-G1м—җм„ң HP-EXT public synthetic | AX-G1~G3 м°ЁлӢЁ, install, live MCP, task/knowledge/canon write, native done promotion | D30 кІ°м •вҶ’EXT-G0; EXT-G1 HP-EXT PASSлҠ” product-specific trial reviewл§Ң н—Ҳмҡ© |
| `D31` / HERMES-T1 м „ | exact version/channel/account mapping, MCP include-list/sampling, transcript/memory encryptionВ·retentionВ·deleteВ·consent, attachment custody, delivery idempotency | Hermes adapter OFF, one-seat only | HP-HERMES synthetic | secret read, team rollout, scheduler, Kanban/goal completion promotion, Orca launch | HP-HERMES PASS + owner + Level 3 вҶ’ HERMES-T1л§Ң н—Ҳмҡ© |
| `D32` / ORCA-T1 м „ | exact stable version/hash, Manual command, OS/credential/network roots, base ref/worktree ownership, candidate artifact/validator/Git policy, frozen value rubric | Orca adapter OFF, direct Codex мң м§Җ | HP-ORCA public-safe fixture | bypass/yolo, real payload, direct main/push/PR, Hermes launch, binary multi-writer | HP-ORCA PASS + owner + Level 3 вҶ’ ORCA-T1л§Ң н—Ҳмҡ© |
| `D33` / H01C м „ | accountлі„ received/sent expected sourceмҷҖ applicability/window/freshness, exact native/RFC occurrence ID, mailbox observation ID, sender/to/cc/bcc relation, unmatched/fuzzy candidate policy, team sent acquisition choice | POP3=received-only, owner Outlook/Soulforge SMTP=к°Ғ кҙҖмёЎ лІ”мң„л§Ң, team sent=`UNKNOWN/HOLD` | synthetic one-message/multi-observationВ·threadВ·role fixture | team credential/raw body access, fuzzy confirmed merge, cc/bcc м¶”м •, live source/backfill/DB write | HP-COMM-01~06 PASSлҠ” H01C contract/shadow reviewл§Ң н—Ҳмҡ©; team sent liveлҠ” private binding+owner+Level 3 лі„лҸ„ |
| `D34` / H07A м „ | exact Slack app/workspace authority, channel-ID project binding+effective dates, minimal scopes, joined allowlist, Socket Mode/HTTPS choice, backfill/cursor/retry, retention/delete/legal hold, userвҶ’ERP mapping, Slack Connect/DM/common rule, attachment custody | Slack collector/projector OFF, channel name non-authoritative, unmapped scopes HOLD | public-safe synthetic Events/Web-API fixturesмҷҖ source-supported official-doc review | token/secret/raw payload, auto join/post, live app/event subscription, task/knowledge write | H07A HP-COMM-07~12 contract PASS л’Ө H07BлҠ” P3 receipt н•„мҡ”; one-channel canaryмҷҖ productionмқҖ к°Ғк°Ғ owner+Level 3 лі„лҸ„ |

м•„лһҳлҠ” completed C00A/C00Qмқҳ historical retained мғҒнғңлҘј мҡ”м•Ҫн•ңлӢӨ. нҳ„мһ¬ мғҲлЎң мҡ”мІӯн•  мҲҳ мһҲлҠ” мӢӨн–ү
shapeлҠ” В§18.2мқҳ current-authority C00B packetмқҙл©°, м–ҙл–Ө retained receiptлҸ„ C00B PASSлҘј лҢҖмІҙн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

```yaml
TEAX-C00A:
  historical_result: BLOCKED
  receipt_state: retained
  current_execution_authority: false
TEAX-C00Q:
  historical_result: FORMAL_RECEIPT_RETAINED
  receipt_ref: task_engine_c00q_formal_acceptance_pass_v1
  current_execution_authority: false
current_next_gate: TEAX-C00B
current_required_inputs: [baseline, authority, source, profile, output, expiry, judge_authority]
```

мқҙ historical packetмқҖ private/live query к¶Ңн•ңмқ„ л§Ңл“Өм§Җ м•Ҡм•ҳкі  DB/API queryлҸ„ `0`мқҙм—ҲлӢӨ. CV-02к°Җ лӮЁмқҖ
public-only runмқҖ accepted blocker receiptлЎң лӢ«нҳ”м§Җл§Ң P1мқ„ м—¬лҠ” PASSк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. мқҙнӣ„ C00Q formal
receiptлҸ„ мғқм„ұлҗҗмңјлӮҳ execution approvalмқҖ л§ҢлЈҢлҗҗлӢӨ. нҳ„мһ¬ C00BлҠ” laneлі„
authority/source/profile/output/expiryлҘј мғҲлЎң мҠ№мқёл°ӣм•„м•ј н•ҳл©° retained receiptл§ҢмңјлЎң мӢӨн–ү к°ҖлҠҘн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлӢӨ.

C00Bк°Җ мӢӨм ң `PASS`н•ң л’Өм—җл§Ң лӢӨмқҢ лӢөліҖмқ„ мӮ¬мҡ©н•  мҲҳ мһҲлӢӨ. Ratification мӢңм җм—җлҠ” C00B receiptк°Җ
accepted+unexpiredмқҙкі , approval-time HEADмқҳ м„ё pathк°Җ м•„лһҳ blobкіј лӘЁл‘җ к°ҷмңјл©°, к·ё blob setмқ„ лҢҖмғҒмңјлЎң
н•ң exact 20/20 validator receiptмҷҖ fresh Level 2 review receiptк°Җ мһҲм–ҙм•ј н•ңлӢӨ. нҳ„мһ¬ plan validationмқҙлӮҳ
кіјкұ° test кё°лЎқмңјлЎң лҢҖмІҙн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. н•ҳлӮҳлқјлҸ„ м–ҙкёӢлӮҳл©ҙ H00лҠ” `HOLD`лӢӨ. мқҙ лӢөліҖмқҖ м„ё pinned fileмқ„
кі м№ҳкұ°лӮҳ adapterлҘј кө¬нҳ„н•ҳлҠ” к¶Ңн•ңмқҙ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ.

```yaml
TEAX-H00: RATIFY | HOLD
precondition_receipt: <accepted-TEAX-C00B-receipt-ref>
precondition_guard: accepted-and-unexpired-at-ratification
candidate_ref: main@16190bff6c1dd9e101c11a078b97e84f1c1c43ea
candidate_paths:
  - docs/architecture/workspace/PROJECT_HISTORY_ENVELOPE_V0.md
  - guild_hall/shared/project_history_envelope.mjs
  - guild_hall/shared/project_history_envelope.test.mjs
candidate_blobs:
  PROJECT_HISTORY_ENVELOPE_V0.md: 18f106b6b7f88f12ea0b345f2246c95bf1a2967f
  project_history_envelope.mjs: ea7c23659724b25c487ae0293f7c3c0999108be5
  project_history_envelope.test.mjs: f5edd6c15acdcf060988b005db7e13fec3832a2b
approval_time_head_ref: <exact-40hex>
candidate_blob_guard_receipt_ref: <head-origin-clean-no-lock-three-path-blob-match-receipt-ref>
validator: node --test guild_hall/shared/project_history_envelope.test.mjs
validator_receipt_ref: <exit-0-tests-20-pass-20-fail-0-receipt-ref>
validator_tested_candidate_blobs: candidate_blobs
validator_executed_at: <strict-utc>
review_level: inspector_and_judge
review_receipt_ref: <fresh-level-2-accept-receipt-ref>
review_inputs: [candidate_blobs, validator_receipt_ref]
ratify_items:
  independent_event_envelope_and_coverage_receipt_pair: RATIFY | HOLD
  literal_unknown_semantics: RATIFY | HOLD
  known_at_half_open_window: RATIFY | HOLD
  six_state_count_null_gap_matrix: RATIFY | HOLD
overall_rule: any HOLD means TEAX-H00 HOLD
output: owner-decision-ref-only
file_edit_adapter_migration_live_claim: 0
ratification_validity_policy: content-addressed-until-revoked
ratification_issued_at: <strict-utc>
ratification_expires_at: null
revocation_ref: null
approval_ref: <owner-decision-ref>
authority_effect:
  h00_ratified: true-only-if-all-ratify-and-all-guards-pass
  h01_h05_child_packet_review_unlocked: true-only-if-h00-ratified
  h01_h05_adapter_execution_unlocked: false
  h06_unlocked: false
  d19_to_d26_authority_created: false
  d27_to_d29_authority_created: false
  d25_live_completeness_authority_created: false
  file_edit_authority_created: false
  writer_migration_live_activation_authority_created: false
hold_effect: all-authority-effect-fields-false
```

### 17.2 лӮЁмқҖ `UNKNOWN`кіј next proof

| UNKNOWN | мҷң м•„м§Ғ лӘЁлҘҙлҠ”к°Җ | classification | exact next proof |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| live м „мІҙ task writer мҲҳ | runtime revisionкіј mainмқҙ лӢӨлҘҙкі  лӘЁл“  callerлҘј live traceн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ | `DEFER` | maintenance м „ query-only process/API/DB writer inventory |
| event м—ҶлҠ” mutation aggregate | generic eventмҷҖ current mutationмқҙ л¶„лҰ¬ | `DEFER` | task IDлҘј м¶ңл Ҙн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ” status/event parity aggregate |
| DB/WAL full hash л¬ҙліҖкІҪ | live file lockмңјлЎң hash мӢӨнҢЁ | `DEFER` | maintenance snapshot лҳҗлҠ” SQLite backup APIмқҳ read-only digest receipt |
| valid restore | `HISTORICAL_REPORTED`: мӣҗліё correction кҙҖм°° report 19к°ң мӨ‘ valid 0 | `DEFER` | C09R maintenance-locked coherent DB/payload isolated restore drill |
| sourceлі„ exact revision coverage | mail/voice/schedule/file м „мІҙлҘј live м§‘кі„н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ | `DEFER` | source-kindлі„ missing/duplicate countмҷҖ opaque pointer coverage |
| five-lane live completeness | мқҙлІҲ correctionмқҖ runtime/source windowлҘј fresh мһ¬кҙҖм°°н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ | `DEFER` | accepted C00Q toolмқҳ C00B authority-backed source-availability inventory л’Ө, H00 ratification+D25 policyлҘј м Ғмҡ©н•ң H06 laneлі„ complete_with_events/complete_no_events/partial/failed/not_collected/not_applicable receipt |
| external SE schedule owner/path/writer | current mutationмқҖ мһҲмңјлӮҳ append-only master schedule contractк°Җ м—ҶмқҢ | `DEFER` | D20 + H03 current/event/revision/replay fixture |
| Codex capture boundary outside dev-ERP | WorkSessionмқҖ мһҲмңјлӮҳ dev-ERP л°– structured ownerмҷҖ consent/coverage лҜём • | `DEFER` | D19 + H03 direct-writer/coverage audit; whole conversation remains OFF |
| personal WorkSession lifecycle binding | current one-shot recordм—җлҠ” assignment epoch/start/thread/node/sequence/closeout/outbox ackк°Җ м—ҶмқҢ | `DEFER` | D28 + AX-G1 schema, opaque thread-ref capability probe, HP-SESSION synthetic; P9 core л’Ө feature-OFF |
| local outbox path/encryption/missing SLA | server toolл§ҢмңјлЎң client durable outboxлҘј мҰқлӘ…н•  мҲҳ м—ҶмқҢ | `DEFER` | owner-approved node writer/path/fsync/encryption/retentionмҷҖ crash/reboot pilot; к°’ м¶”м • кёҲм§Җ |
| run/log common source schema and lane assignment | `runs/**`лҠ” мң„м№ҳ ownerмқј лҝҗ кіөнҶө manifestк°Җ м•„лӢҲкі  daily-ledger/context projectionмқ„ source truthлЎң мҳӨмқён•ҳл©ҙ H03/H05 мӨ‘ліөмқҙ мғқкёҙлӢӨ. current five-field `id`лҸ„ full-record identityк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ | `DEFER` | D26 + H05 report-authoring exact-schema/`job_id` immutability fixture + five-field same-ID conflict/boundary redesign; projection event countмҷҖ directory recursion `0` |
| mail normal/fallback writer and epoch | м„ё current file writerк°Җ мһҲкі  live lease/fencing bindingмқҖ public evidenceлЎң нҷ•мқё л¶Ҳк°Җ | `DEFER` | D21~D23 + P8 MAIL-01~12 synthetic + C08B/P10 manual classification/projector epoch-vector drill |
| mail raw/attachment physical custodyмҷҖ project promotion | gateway state raw contractмҷҖ root approved-worksite payload мӣҗм№ҷ мӮ¬мқҙмқҳ exact operational binding лҜёнҷ•м • | `DEFER` | D27 source-kind custody decision, read-only binding inventory, HP-INGRESS fixtures; мһҗлҸҷ мқҙлҸҷ кёҲм§Җ |
| ingress promoter/security policy | кіөнҶө promoterмҷҖ source-kind retention/ACL/malware-scan/backup/delete authority м—ҶмқҢ | `DEFER` | D27 exact role/policy refs л’Ө I8 feature-OFF receipt; extension/hashлҘј scanмңјлЎң лҢҖмІҙ кёҲм§Җ |
| mail DB/CSV/ICS/XLSX parity | current writersк°Җ generation/outboxлҘј кіөмң н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ | `DEFER` | H01/P8 synthetic manifest then P9 one-project parity |
| project/common RAG м „мІҙ consumer | кіөмҡ© defaultк°Җ м—¬лҹ¬ moduleм—җ лӮЁкі  private materialization лҜёмЎ°мӮ¬ | `DEFER` | C05 scanner + C09 owner-approved asset/consumer aggregate |
| Wiki writerмҷҖ project ACL | limited readerл§Ң кҙҖм°° | `DEFER` | synthetic ACL testмҷҖ owner-approved query-only route inventory |
| ERP UI/MCP accepted query generation | current personal MCPм—җ project-history/RAG/Wiki accepted-generation queryк°Җ м—ҶмқҢ | `DEFER` | D29 + Q0/Q4/Q8 feature-OFF, Q9 one-project UI/MCP parity/no-fallback pilot |
| ENGINE-12 endpoint 2кұҙ мӢӨнҢЁ мӣҗмқё | child serverк°Җ `server not ready`лЎң мў…лЈҢ, stderr м—ҶмқҢ | `DEFER` | port/fixture/startup lifecycleмқ„ deterministic captureн•ҙ мһ¬мӢӨн–ү |
| task ledger/autosync second-truth мң„н—ҳ | schema/header/callerк°Җ л¶„мӮ° | `DEFER` | read/write caller graphмҷҖ conflict fixture |
| always-on/reconciler/TaskEngine coordinator binding | runtime clone identityмҷҖ operational primary лҜём§Җм • | `DEFER` | owner D10 + C08F foundation + C08B/G00 identity/binding receipt |
| restore/audit Git blockerмқҳ м •нҷ• мӣҗмқё | auditк°Җ 5мҙҲ timeout detailмқ„ лІ„лҰј | `DEFER` | C08F slow-Git fixtureмҷҖ structured error preservation |
| runtime code/data audit кі„м•Ҫ | нҳ„мһ¬ л‘җ checkout same-SHA к°Җм •кіј к°ңл°ң м „м§„мқҙ м¶©лҸҢ | `DEFER` | D16 м„ нғқ л’Ө C08F revised synthetic/live-dry auditкіј C09D pinned deploy proof |
| workspace extra alias 5к°ң (`HISTORICAL_REPORTED`: мӣҗліё correction audit) | report-only auditл§Ң мҲҳн–ү | `DEFER` | лі„лҸ„ owner-approved junction dry-run map; мқҙ кі„нҡҚм—җм„ң repair кёҲм§Җ |
| conversation hardening мһҗлҸҷ close | installed skillкіј л‘җ Stop hook л¶Җмһ¬ | `DEFER` | лі„лҸ„ мҠ№мқёлҗң skill/hook installВ·doctor мһ¬мӢӨн–ү |
| AX/AgentRun/IQ/ML canon | coreліҙлӢӨ л’Өмқҳ owner м„ нғқкіј evidenceк°Җ м—ҶмқҢ | `DEFER` | C10 л’Ө D12~D15 design packets |

### 17.3 HP-01~HP-22 public/current-code нҢҗм •кіј historical runtime н•ңкі„

Runtime/DB/profile н–үмқҖ мқҙлІҲ correctionм—җм„ң fresh мһ¬кҙҖм°°н•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡм•ҳмңјл©° `HISTORICAL_REPORTED` лҳҗлҠ”
`UNKNOWN/VERIFY_HP`лӢӨ.

## 18. мҠ№мқё л’Ө мІ« мӢӨн–ү sliceмҷҖ exact task packet мҙҲм•Ҳ

мІ« post-plan sliceмҳҖлҚҳ `TEAX-C00A/P0` public-only blocker preflightмҷҖ C00Q formal acceptanceлҠ”
к°Ғк°Ғ retained receiptлЎң ліҙмЎҙлҗҗкі  лӢ№мӢң execution authorityлҠ” л§ҢлЈҢлҗҗлӢӨ. нҳ„мһ¬ лӢӨмқҢ мӢӨн–ү нӣ„ліҙлҠ” лі„лҸ„
current authorityк°Җ мһҲлҠ” C00B query-only strict judgeмқҙл©°, к·ё PASS м—Ҷмқҙ H00/P1мқҙлӮҳ C01A/P2лҘј
мӢңмһ‘н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. В§18.1мқҖ C00A historical candidate/receipt кІҪкі„лҘј м„ӨлӘ…н•ңлӢӨ.

| historical packet field | accepted-run value / boundary |
| --- | --- |
| `slice_id/title/goal` | `TEAX-C00A` / public baselineВ·source candidate inventory / exact blocker receipt |
| `classification_mix` | `[REUSE, DEFER]` |
| `depends_on` | `[]` |
| `plan_evidence_refs / execution_baseline_ref` | observationмқҖ `main@9df7e577...`, candidate `927b3fb0...`, merge-base `15e988b4...`, CV-01~09; accepted runмқҖ approval-time exact baselineм—җ pinлҗҗкі  retained receipt л°–мңјлЎң мғҒмҶҚн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ |
| `execution_mode / allowed_write_paths` | `public_only_stdout` / ephemeralВ·stdout only |
| `forbidden_paths` | public code/docs, DB/schema mutation, raw DB rows, `_workspaces/**`, raw/private payload, runtime state mutation, scheduler/network/alert |
| `inputs` | approved C00A packet, exact public refs, public contracts, public-only profile |
| `outputs` | five-lane public candidate writer/consumer map, live-completeness UNKNOWN, exact `BLOCKED` receipt; P1 unlock `false` |
| `code_delta` | `none` |
| `db_delta/api_delta/folder_delta` | лӘЁл‘җ `none/stdout-only` |
| `docs_contract_changelog_delta` | `not_applicable` |
| `owner_and_writers` | inventory agent only; source/DB/project-history/task writer м—ҶмқҢ |
| `acceptance_checks` | exact refs, raw sentinel 0, public writer/consumer candidate map, coverage UNKNOWN+fixed next proof, tracked zero-mutation |
| `minimum_review` | `inspector_and_judge` |
| `regression_checks` | scoped status/hash and public tree unchanged |
| `migration_or_backfill` | `none` |
| `rollback` | deltaк°Җ м—Ҷм–ҙ `not_applicable` |
| `stop_conditions` | base drift, profile/ACL м—ҶмқҢ, raw value н•„мҡ”, writer ambiguity, any mutation |
| `owner_gate` | accepted historical C00A approval; expiry л’Ө мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ© кёҲм§Җ |
| `risk_and_effort` | `low / S` |
| `next_slice / next_gate` | retained C00A blockerмҷҖ C00Q formal receipt л’Ө нҳ„мһ¬ next gateлҠ” лі„лҸ„ current-authority C00B; C00B PASS м „ H00 кёҲм§Җ |

### 18.1 C00A `public_only_stdout` exact preflight (historical accepted `BLOCKED` receipt)

мқҙ historical packetмқҖ public tracked sourceмқҳ **known candidate**л§Ң stdoutмңјлЎң м—ҙкұ°н–ҲлӢӨ. live callerВ·default rootВ·
consumerВ·coverageлҘј мҷ„кІ°н–ҲлӢӨкі  мЈјмһҘн•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡмңјл©°, CV-02к°Җ лӮЁмқҖ мӢӨн–үмқҖ accepted blocker receiptлЎң лҒқлӮ¬лӢӨ.
`git status` к°ҷмқҖ root-wide pathname enumeration, candidate ref/content, `_workmeta`, `_workspaces`,
`private-state`, `guild_hall/state`, DB/API/runtime/networkлҠ” allowlistк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ.

| lane | literal public tracked read allowlist | exact symbol candidate pattern |
| --- | --- | --- |
| mail | `guild_hall/gateway/project_mail_history_writer.mjs`; `guild_hall/gateway/mail_fetch/collector/storage/project_mail_history.py`; `guild_hall/gateway/outlook_mail_reconcile.mjs`; `ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/tools/scan_mail_ledger.mjs` | `upsertProjectMailHistory|ProjectMailHistoryWriter|runOutlookMailReconcile|applySentDeltas|scanLedger` |
| voice | `guild_hall/voice_capture/voice_capture.mjs`; `guild_hall/voice_capture/delivery_receipt.mjs`; `ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/tools/voice_to_task_candidates.mjs` | `runCaptureSession|writeRecordingLibraryEntry|prepareDeliveryReceipt|acknowledgeDelivery|planVoiceTask|runVoiceToTaskCandidates` |
| structured PC work | `ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/src/erp_mcp_service.mjs`; `guild_hall/daily_ledger/daily_ledger.mjs` | `erp_mcp_work_session|publishWorkSession|validateDailyLedgerObject|renderDailyWorklogDraft` |
| file | `guild_hall/file_activity/file_activity.mjs` | `scanWorkspace|reconcileObservationPackets|validateDurableReceiptArtifact|restoreRevisionStateCheckpoint` |
| run/log | `guild_hall/workflow_runner/report_authoring_handler.mjs`; `.workflow/report_authoring_v0/contracts/workflow_receipt.v1.schema.json`; `ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/src/five_field.mjs` | `runReportAuthoringHandler|workflow_receipt|job_id|composeInputRefs|clampFiveFieldDigest` |

мҠ№мқёлҗң executorк°Җ мӮ¬мҡ©н•  лӘ…л №мқҖ м•„лһҳ лё”лЎқлҝҗмқҙлӢӨ. `<owner-approved-40hex>`лҠ” owner лӢөліҖмқҳ
`execution_baseline_ref`мҷҖ byte-identicalн•ҙм•ј н•ңлӢӨ. `git grep` exit `1`мқҖ н•ҙлӢ№ lane public candidate
лҲ„лқҪмңјлЎң `BLOCKED`, `>1`мқҖ command errorлЎң exit `24`лӢӨ. м¶ңл Ҙ code lineмқҖ ephemeralмқҙл©° receiptм—җлҠ”
repo-relative `path:line#symbol`л§Ң лӮЁкёҙлӢӨ.

```powershell
$ApprovedSha = '<owner-approved-40hex>'
$ApprovalRef = '<owner-decision-ref>'
$ApprovalExpiresAt = '<strict-utc>'
function Stop-C00([int]$Code, [string]$Reason) {
  [ordered]@{
    schema_version = 'soulforge.task_engine_c00_public_stdout_receipt.v1'
    packet_id = 'TEAX-C00A'
    result = 'BLOCKED'
    reason_codes = @($Reason)
    p1_unlocked = $false
    exit_code = $Code
  } | ConvertTo-Json -Depth 6 -Compress | Write-Output
  exit $Code
}

function Get-C00Symbols([string[]]$Lines, [string]$Pattern) {
  $symbolRegex = [regex]$Pattern
  @($Lines | ForEach-Object {
    $match = $symbolRegex.Match($_)
    if ($match.Success) { $match.Value }
  } | Sort-Object -Unique)
}

function Get-C00EvidenceRefs([string[]]$Lines, [string]$Pattern) {
  $locationRegex = [regex]'^(?<path>[^:]+):(?<line>[0-9]+):'
  $symbolRegex = [regex]$Pattern
  @($Lines | ForEach-Object {
    $location = $locationRegex.Match($_)
    $symbol = $symbolRegex.Match($_)
    if ($location.Success -and $symbol.Success) {
      '{0}:{1}#{2}' -f $location.Groups['path'].Value, $location.Groups['line'].Value, $symbol.Value
    }
  } | Sort-Object -Unique)
}

if ($ApprovedSha -notmatch '^[0-9a-f]{40}$') { Stop-C00 20 'BASELINE_REF_INVALID' }
if ([string]::IsNullOrWhiteSpace($ApprovalRef) -or $ApprovalRef.StartsWith('<')) { Stop-C00 20 'APPROVAL_REF_INVALID' }
if ($ApprovalExpiresAt -notmatch '^[0-9]{4}-[0-9]{2}-[0-9]{2}T[0-9]{2}:[0-9]{2}:[0-9]{2}Z$') { Stop-C00 20 'APPROVAL_EXPIRY_INVALID' }
$ExpiryInstant = [DateTimeOffset]::Parse($ApprovalExpiresAt, [Globalization.CultureInfo]::InvariantCulture, [Globalization.DateTimeStyles]::AssumeUniversal)
if ($ExpiryInstant -le [DateTimeOffset]::UtcNow) { Stop-C00 20 'APPROVAL_EXPIRED' }
if (Test-Path -LiteralPath '.git/index.lock') { Stop-C00 22 'INDEX_LOCK_PRESENT' }

$HeadBefore = (git rev-parse HEAD).Trim()
$OriginBefore = (git rev-parse origin/main).Trim()
$TreeBefore = (git rev-parse 'HEAD^{tree}').Trim()
if ($LASTEXITCODE -ne 0 -or $HeadBefore -ne $ApprovedSha -or $OriginBefore -ne $ApprovedSha) { Stop-C00 20 'BASELINE_DRIFT' }
git diff --quiet --no-ext-diff
if ($LASTEXITCODE -ne 0) { Stop-C00 21 'TRACKED_WORKTREE_DIRTY' }
git diff --cached --quiet --no-ext-diff
if ($LASTEXITCODE -ne 0) { Stop-C00 21 'TRACKED_INDEX_DIRTY' }

$MailMatches = @(git grep -n -I -E 'upsertProjectMailHistory|ProjectMailHistoryWriter|runOutlookMailReconcile|applySentDeltas|scanLedger' -- guild_hall/gateway/project_mail_history_writer.mjs guild_hall/gateway/mail_fetch/collector/storage/project_mail_history.py guild_hall/gateway/outlook_mail_reconcile.mjs ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/tools/scan_mail_ledger.mjs)
$MailExit = $LASTEXITCODE
$VoiceMatches = @(git grep -n -I -E 'runCaptureSession|writeRecordingLibraryEntry|prepareDeliveryReceipt|acknowledgeDelivery|planVoiceTask|runVoiceToTaskCandidates' -- guild_hall/voice_capture/voice_capture.mjs guild_hall/voice_capture/delivery_receipt.mjs ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/tools/voice_to_task_candidates.mjs)
$VoiceExit = $LASTEXITCODE
$PcWorkMatches = @(git grep -n -I -E 'erp_mcp_work_session|publishWorkSession|validateDailyLedgerObject|renderDailyWorklogDraft' -- ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/src/erp_mcp_service.mjs guild_hall/daily_ledger/daily_ledger.mjs)
$PcWorkExit = $LASTEXITCODE
$FileMatches = @(git grep -n -I -E 'scanWorkspace|reconcileObservationPackets|validateDurableReceiptArtifact|restoreRevisionStateCheckpoint' -- guild_hall/file_activity/file_activity.mjs)
$FileExit = $LASTEXITCODE
$RunLogMatches = @(git grep -n -I -E 'runReportAuthoringHandler|workflow_receipt|job_id|composeInputRefs|clampFiveFieldDigest' -- guild_hall/workflow_runner/report_authoring_handler.mjs .workflow/report_authoring_v0/contracts/workflow_receipt.v1.schema.json ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/src/five_field.mjs)
$RunLogExit = $LASTEXITCODE
if ($MailExit -gt 1 -or $VoiceExit -gt 1 -or $PcWorkExit -gt 1 -or $FileExit -gt 1 -or $RunLogExit -gt 1) { Stop-C00 24 'PUBLIC_COMMAND_ERROR' }

$HeadAfter = (git rev-parse HEAD).Trim()
$OriginAfter = (git rev-parse origin/main).Trim()
$TreeAfter = (git rev-parse 'HEAD^{tree}').Trim()
git diff --quiet --no-ext-diff
$WorktreeDiffExit = $LASTEXITCODE
git diff --cached --quiet --no-ext-diff
$IndexDiffExit = $LASTEXITCODE
if ($HeadAfter -ne $HeadBefore -or $OriginAfter -ne $OriginBefore -or $TreeAfter -ne $TreeBefore -or $WorktreeDiffExit -ne 0 -or $IndexDiffExit -ne 0) { Stop-C00 21 'TRACKED_STATE_CHANGED' }

$LiveProofs = @('C00-LIVE-01', 'C00-LIVE-02', 'C00-LIVE-03', 'C00-LIVE-04')
$ReasonCodes = @('CV_02_LIVE_PROOF_UNAVAILABLE')
if ($MailExit -eq 1) { $ReasonCodes += 'PUBLIC_MAIL_CANDIDATE_MISSING' }
if ($VoiceExit -eq 1) { $ReasonCodes += 'PUBLIC_VOICE_CANDIDATE_MISSING' }
if ($PcWorkExit -eq 1) { $ReasonCodes += 'PUBLIC_PC_WORK_CANDIDATE_MISSING' }
if ($FileExit -eq 1) { $ReasonCodes += 'PUBLIC_FILE_CANDIDATE_MISSING' }
if ($RunLogExit -eq 1) { $ReasonCodes += 'PUBLIC_RUN_LOG_CANDIDATE_MISSING' }

$LaneManifest = [ordered]@{
  mail = [ordered]@{
    owner_refs = @('public_candidate:guild_hall/gateway/project_mail_history_writer.mjs', 'public_candidate:guild_hall/gateway/mail_fetch/collector/storage/project_mail_history.py', 'public_candidate:guild_hall/gateway/outlook_mail_reconcile.mjs')
    writer_symbols = @(Get-C00Symbols $MailMatches 'upsertProjectMailHistory|ProjectMailHistoryWriter|runOutlookMailReconcile|applySentDeltas')
    consumer_symbols = @(Get-C00Symbols $MailMatches 'scanLedger')
    public_evidence_refs = @(Get-C00EvidenceRefs $MailMatches 'upsertProjectMailHistory|ProjectMailHistoryWriter|runOutlookMailReconcile|applySentDeltas|scanLedger')
    coverage_state = 'UNKNOWN'
    next_proof = $LiveProofs
  }
  voice = [ordered]@{
    owner_refs = @('public_candidate:guild_hall/voice_capture/voice_capture.mjs', 'public_candidate:guild_hall/voice_capture/delivery_receipt.mjs')
    writer_symbols = @(Get-C00Symbols $VoiceMatches 'runCaptureSession|writeRecordingLibraryEntry|prepareDeliveryReceipt|acknowledgeDelivery')
    consumer_symbols = @(Get-C00Symbols $VoiceMatches 'planVoiceTask|runVoiceToTaskCandidates')
    public_evidence_refs = @(Get-C00EvidenceRefs $VoiceMatches 'runCaptureSession|writeRecordingLibraryEntry|prepareDeliveryReceipt|acknowledgeDelivery|planVoiceTask|runVoiceToTaskCandidates')
    coverage_state = 'UNKNOWN'
    next_proof = $LiveProofs
  }
  structured_pc_work = [ordered]@{
    owner_refs = @('public_candidate:ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/src/erp_mcp_service.mjs')
    writer_symbols = @(Get-C00Symbols $PcWorkMatches 'erp_mcp_work_session|publishWorkSession')
    consumer_symbols = @(Get-C00Symbols $PcWorkMatches 'validateDailyLedgerObject|renderDailyWorklogDraft')
    public_evidence_refs = @(Get-C00EvidenceRefs $PcWorkMatches 'erp_mcp_work_session|publishWorkSession|validateDailyLedgerObject|renderDailyWorklogDraft')
    coverage_state = 'UNKNOWN'
    next_proof = $LiveProofs
  }
  file = [ordered]@{
    owner_refs = @('public_candidate:guild_hall/file_activity/file_activity.mjs')
    writer_symbols = @(Get-C00Symbols $FileMatches 'scanWorkspace|reconcileObservationPackets')
    consumer_symbols = @(Get-C00Symbols $FileMatches 'validateDurableReceiptArtifact|restoreRevisionStateCheckpoint')
    public_evidence_refs = @(Get-C00EvidenceRefs $FileMatches 'scanWorkspace|reconcileObservationPackets|validateDurableReceiptArtifact|restoreRevisionStateCheckpoint')
    coverage_state = 'UNKNOWN'
    next_proof = $LiveProofs
  }
  run_log = [ordered]@{
    owner_refs = @('public_candidate:guild_hall/workflow_runner/report_authoring_handler.mjs', 'public_candidate:.workflow/report_authoring_v0/contracts/workflow_receipt.v1.schema.json')
    writer_symbols = @(Get-C00Symbols $RunLogMatches 'runReportAuthoringHandler')
    consumer_symbols = @(Get-C00Symbols $RunLogMatches 'workflow_receipt|job_id|composeInputRefs|clampFiveFieldDigest')
    public_evidence_refs = @(Get-C00EvidenceRefs $RunLogMatches 'runReportAuthoringHandler|workflow_receipt|job_id|composeInputRefs|clampFiveFieldDigest')
    coverage_state = 'UNKNOWN'
    next_proof = $LiveProofs
  }
}

$Receipt = [ordered]@{
  schema_version = 'soulforge.task_engine_c00_public_stdout_receipt.v1'
  packet_id = 'TEAX-C00A'
  execution_mode = 'public_only_stdout'
  approval_ref = $ApprovalRef
  approval_expires_at = $ApprovalExpiresAt
  inventory_scope = 'literal-public-static-files-in-section-18.1'
  inventory_profile = 'public-only'
  approved_baseline_sha = $ApprovedSha
  observed = [ordered]@{
    head_before = $HeadBefore
    origin_main_before = $OriginBefore
    tree_before = $TreeBefore
    head_after = $HeadAfter
    origin_main_after = $OriginAfter
    tree_after = $TreeAfter
    worktree_diff_before = 'clean'
    index_diff_before = 'clean'
    worktree_diff_after = 'clean'
    index_diff_after = 'clean'
  }
  command_results = [ordered]@{ mail = $MailExit; voice = $VoiceExit; structured_pc_work = $PcWorkExit; file = $FileExit; run_log = $RunLogExit }
  lane_manifest = $LaneManifest
  required_live_proofs = $LiveProofs
  unresolved_live_proofs = $LiveProofs
  raw_sentinel_violations = @()
  raw_payload_copied = $false
  tracked_zero_mutation = $true
  result = 'BLOCKED'
  reason_codes = @($ReasonCodes | Sort-Object -Unique)
  p1_unlocked = $false
  exit_code = 3
}

$AllowedTopKeys = @('schema_version', 'packet_id', 'execution_mode', 'approval_ref', 'approval_expires_at', 'inventory_scope', 'inventory_profile', 'approved_baseline_sha', 'observed', 'command_results', 'lane_manifest', 'required_live_proofs', 'unresolved_live_proofs', 'raw_sentinel_violations', 'raw_payload_copied', 'tracked_zero_mutation', 'result', 'reason_codes', 'p1_unlocked', 'exit_code')
$AllowedLaneKeys = @('owner_refs', 'writer_symbols', 'consumer_symbols', 'public_evidence_refs', 'coverage_state', 'next_proof')
$UnknownKeys = @($Receipt.Keys | Where-Object { $_ -notin $AllowedTopKeys })
foreach ($Lane in $LaneManifest.Values) { $UnknownKeys += @($Lane.Keys | Where-Object { $_ -notin $AllowedLaneKeys }) }
if ($UnknownKeys.Count -gt 0) { Stop-C00 23 'UNKNOWN_RECEIPT_FIELD' }

$ForbiddenKeys = @('mail_body', 'mail_html', 'recipient_payload', 'attachment_payload', 'transcript_text', 'file_bytes', 'absolute_path', 'unc_path', 'raw_log', 'secret', 'token', 'password', 'cookie')
$ReceiptJson = $Receipt | ConvertTo-Json -Depth 12 -Compress
$RawViolations = @($ForbiddenKeys | Where-Object { $ReceiptJson -match ('\"' + [regex]::Escape($_) + '\"\s*:') })
if ($RawViolations.Count -gt 0) { Stop-C00 23 'RAW_SENTINEL_VIOLATION' }

$ReceiptJson | Write-Output
exit 3
```

лӘ…л №мқҖ м•„лһҳ fixed live-proof IDлҘј мӮӯм ңн•ҳкұ°лӮҳ `resolved`лЎң м¶”м •н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

| proof ID | мөңмў… C00Bк°Җ лӢ«м•„м•ј н•  live мӮ¬мӢӨ | C00A public-only мғҒнғң / next proof |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `C00-LIVE-01` | laneлі„ current physical ownerмҷҖ default root | `UNRESOLVED`; accepted C00Q tool л’Ө separately approved C00B owner/path inventory |
| `C00-LIVE-02` | laneлі„ current writerВ·direct caller м „мІҙ м§‘н•© | `UNRESOLVED`; accepted C00Q tool л’Ө C00B read-only caller graph with authority |
| `C00-LIVE-03` | laneлі„ current consumer м „мІҙ м§‘н•© | `UNRESOLVED`; accepted C00Q tool л’Ө C00B read-only consumer graph with authority |
| `C00-LIVE-04` | laneлі„ current source-native coverage capability/availabilityмҷҖ exact current gap reason; H00 six-state completeness receiptк°Җ м•„лӢҳ | `UNRESOLVED`; accepted C00Q tool л’Ө C00B metadata-only source-availability aggregate with authority |

м •мғҒ кІҪлЎңмқҳ exact blockмқҖ grep мӣҗл¬ёмқ„ л°–мңјлЎң нқҳлҰ¬м§Җ м•Ҡкі  м•„лһҳ YAMLкіј лҸҷнҳ•мқё compact JSON н•ң мӨ„л§Ң
stdoutм—җ лӮё л’Ө exit `3`н•ңлӢӨ. Hard-stopлҸ„ мөңмҶҢ JSON blocker receipt н•ң мӨ„л§Ң лӮёлӢӨ.
к°Ғ laneмқҖ `owner_refs`, `writer_symbols`, `consumer_symbols`,
`public_evidence_refs`, `coverage_state`, `next_proof`лҘј лӘЁл‘җ к°Җм§„лӢӨ. `mail_body`, `mail_html`,
`recipient_payload`, `attachment_payload`, `transcript_text`, `file_bytes`, `absolute_path`, `unc_path`,
`raw_log`, `secret`, `token`, `password`, `cookie` key лҳҗлҠ” unknown keyлҠ” exit `23`мқҙлӢӨ.

```yaml
schema_version: soulforge.task_engine_c00_public_stdout_receipt.v1
packet_id: TEAX-C00A
execution_mode: public_only_stdout
approval_ref: <owner-decision-ref>
approval_expires_at: <strict-utc>
inventory_scope: literal-public-static-files-in-section-18.1
inventory_profile: public-only
approved_baseline_sha: <40hex>
observed:
  head_before: <40hex>
  origin_main_before: <40hex>
  tree_before: <40hex>
  head_after: <40hex>
  origin_main_after: <40hex>
  tree_after: <40hex>
  worktree_diff_before: clean
  index_diff_before: clean
  worktree_diff_after: clean
  index_diff_after: clean
command_results: { mail: 0, voice: 0, structured_pc_work: 0, file: 0, run_log: 0 }
lane_manifest:
  mail: { owner_refs: [], writer_symbols: [], consumer_symbols: [], public_evidence_refs: [], coverage_state: UNKNOWN, next_proof: C00-LIVE-01..04 }
  voice: { owner_refs: [], writer_symbols: [], consumer_symbols: [], public_evidence_refs: [], coverage_state: UNKNOWN, next_proof: C00-LIVE-01..04 }
  structured_pc_work: { owner_refs: [], writer_symbols: [], consumer_symbols: [], public_evidence_refs: [], coverage_state: UNKNOWN, next_proof: C00-LIVE-01..04 }
  file: { owner_refs: [], writer_symbols: [], consumer_symbols: [], public_evidence_refs: [], coverage_state: UNKNOWN, next_proof: C00-LIVE-01..04 }
  run_log: { owner_refs: [], writer_symbols: [], consumer_symbols: [], public_evidence_refs: [], coverage_state: UNKNOWN, next_proof: C00-LIVE-01..04 }
required_live_proofs: [C00-LIVE-01, C00-LIVE-02, C00-LIVE-03, C00-LIVE-04]
unresolved_live_proofs: [C00-LIVE-01, C00-LIVE-02, C00-LIVE-03, C00-LIVE-04]
raw_sentinel_violations: []
raw_payload_copied: false
tracked_zero_mutation: true
result: BLOCKED
reason_codes: [CV_02_LIVE_PROOF_UNAVAILABLE]
p1_unlocked: false
exit_code: 3
```

мқҙ C00A commandмқҳ м •мғҒ мҷ„лЈҢлҠ” live proofлҘј м¶”м •н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмңјлҜҖлЎң exit `3`мқҳ м•Ҳм „н•ң `BLOCKED`лӢӨ.
P0 exit `0`мқҖ accepted C00Q toolмқ„ мӮ¬мҡ©н•ң лі„лҸ„ C00B judgeк°Җ baselineВ·лӘЁл“  required live proofВ·
authorityВ·raw sentinelВ·zero-mutationмқ„ м „л¶Җ PASSн–Ҳмқ„ л•Ңл§Ң м“ҙлӢӨ. м—¬кё°м„ң proof
PASSлҠ” source inventoryмқҳ мҰқкұ°к°Җ лӢ«нҳ”лӢӨлҠ” лң»мқҙлӢӨ. Authority-attested current л¶Җмһ¬В·gapмқҖ later-lane
blockerлҘј ліҙмЎҙн•ң мұ„ inventory proofлҘј лӢ«мқ„ мҲҳ мһҲм§Җл§Ң, missing/expired authorityлҠ” C00BлҘј `BLOCKED`лЎң
л‘”лӢӨ. C00B judge receiptлҠ” лӘЁнҳён•ң `p1_unlocked: true` лҢҖмӢ  `p0_accepted: true`,
`next_gate: TEAX-H00_RATIFICATION`, `h00_review_unlocked: true`,
`p1_adapter_execution_unlocked: false`, `h00_ratified: false`,
`d21_to_d26_authority_created: false`, `writer_or_activation_authority_created: false`лҘј exact fieldлЎң
кі м •н•ҙм•ј н•ңлӢӨ. C00A blocker receiptмқҳ `p1_unlocked`лҠ” legacy fixed-false fieldлЎңл§Ң лӮЁкі  `true`к°Җ лҗ  мҲҳ
м—Ҷмңјл©° C00B manifest/receiptм—җлҠ” лӮҳнғҖлӮҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. `20`мқҖ
`BASELINE_DRIFT`, `21`мқҖ tracked dirty/mutation, `22`лҠ” index lock, `23`мқҖ raw/unknown receipt field,
`24`лҠ” command/path allowlist мң„л°ҳ лҳҗлҠ” command errorлӢӨ. нҳ„мһ¬ public-only fixtureмқҳ expected receiptлҠ”
`result: BLOCKED`, `reason_codes: [CV_02_LIVE_PROOF_UNAVAILABLE]`, `p1_unlocked: false`, `exit_code: 3`мқҙлӢӨ.
мқҙ expected fixtureлҠ” мқҙлІҲ л¬ём„ң ліҙм •м—җм„ң мӢӨн–үн•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡм•ҳлӢӨ.

### 18.2 C00Q/C00B dependency breakмҷҖ мҠ№мқё кІҪкі„

м•„лһҳ C00Q м„ё нҢҢмқјкіј C00B pure judge foundationмқҖ sourceлЎң мЎҙмһ¬н•ңлӢӨ. C09A/P9к°Җ мІҳмқҢ л§Ңл“ӨлҸ„лЎқ л‘җлҠ”
кіјкұ° мҲңнҷҳмқҖ source м°Ёмӣҗм—җм„ң м ңкұ°лҗҗлӢӨ. мқҙнӣ„ exact refsмҷҖ fresh full B/VлЎң
`task_engine_c00q_formal_acceptance_pass_v1` formal receiptк°Җ мғқм„ұлҗҗкі  к·ё prerequisite evidenceлҠ”
ліҙмЎҙн•ңлӢӨ. лӢӨл§Ң н•ҙлӢ№ execution approvalмқҖ `2026-07-19T06:00:00Z`м—җ л§ҢлЈҢлҗҗмңјл©° live bindingкіј C00B
strict PASSлҠ” кі„мҶҚ `HOLD`лӢӨ.

| current C00Q exact source | мғҒнғңмҷҖ кІҪкі„ |
| --- | --- |
| `ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/tools/task_engine_inventory.mjs` | `EXISTS`; default fail-closed query-only evidence producer, retained public/synthetic formal receipt мһҲмқҢ, live source binding м—ҶмқҢ |
| `ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/test/task_engine_inventory.test.mjs` | `EXISTS`; synthetic DB/path/authority/source-availability fixturesл§Ң мӮ¬мҡ© |
| `ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/docs/contracts/task_engine_inventory_manifest.v1.schema.json` | `EXISTS`; five-lane C00-LIVE-01..04мҷҖ zero-mutation field кі„м•Ҫ |
| `ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/README.md` | `EXISTS`; commandВ·guardВ·schema ownerмҷҖ C00Q/C00B authority ceiling кё°лЎқ |
| `CHANGELOG.md` | `EXISTS`; public tool/contract ліҖкІҪкіј live мӢӨн–ү `0` кё°лЎқ |

нҳ„мһ¬ app `docs/contracts/`лҠ” C00Q/C00B/A8-SYNTH strict schemaлҘј мҶҢмң н•ҳкі  app-local `docs/README.md`мҷҖ
CHANGELOGлҠ” м—ҶлӢӨ. schema directoryмқҳ мұ…мһ„мқҖ к°ҖмһҘ к°Җк№Ңмҡҙ owner surfaceмқё app `README.md`мҷҖ root
`CHANGELOG.md`м—җм„ң лӢ«лҠ”лӢӨ. Formal acceptance packetмқҖ exact source pathл§Ң allowlistлЎң мӮјкі 
`package.json`/lockfileмқҖ л°”кҫём§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. лі„лҸ„
script л“ұлЎқмқҙлӮҳ Ajv dependencyлҘј нғқн•ҳл Өл©ҙ exact package/lock pathмҷҖ dependency ownerлҘј мғҲ packetм—җ
м¶”к°Җ мҠ№мқён•ҙм•ј н•ҳл©°, parent/root м„Өм№ҳм—җ м•”л¬өм ҒмңјлЎң кё°лҢҖм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

#### 18.2.1 C00Q readiness verdict вҖ” `FORMAL RECEIPT RETAINED / EXECUTION AUTHORITY EXPIRED / LIVE BINDING HOLD`

| HOLD ID | нҳ„мһ¬ closure мғҒнғң | м•Ҳм „ кё°ліёк°’ / лӢ«лҠ” мҰқкұ° |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `C00Q-HOLD-01` | accepted C00A blocker receiptмҷҖ C00Q approval-time SHA/ref/expiryлҠ” accepted runм—җм„ң лӢ«нҳ”кі  formal receiptлҠ” ліҙмЎҙлҗЁ; нҳ„мһ¬ execution approvalмқҖ л§ҢлЈҢ | retained receiptлҘј current мҠ№мқёмңјлЎң мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ©н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ; мғҲ мӢӨн–үмқҖ мғҲ exact authorityк°Җ н•„мҡ” |
| `C00Q-HOLD-02` | descriptor schemaмҷҖ literal CLI grammarмқҳ frozen receiptлҠ” ліҙмЎҙлҗЁ | `--db`, `--source`, `--authority` л“ұмқ„ м¶”к°Җ л°ңлӘ…н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ; input-only locatorмҷҖ output-safe opaque ref/digest кІҪкі„лҘј мң м§Җ |
| `C00Q-HOLD-03` | generic adapter/expected-source guardмҷҖ live instance л¶„лҰ¬к°Җ кө¬нҳ„В·мӢңн—ҳлҗҗмңјлӮҳ actual source/authority/profile bindingмқҖ м—ҶмқҢ | actual expected source setВ·locatorВ·authority grantВ·profileмқ„ л°ңлӘ…н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ. unknown adapter/authority/sourceлҠ” exit `3 BLOCKED`; H00 six-state completeness нҢҗм •мқҙлӮҳ м„ м–ёк°’л§ҢмңјлЎң C00-LIVE-01..04 resolved мІҳлҰ¬ кёҲм§Җ |
| `C00Q-HOLD-04` | canonicalizationВ·digest domainВ·exit codeмқҳ accepted-run full B/V receiptлҠ” ліҙмЎҙлҗЁ | retained exact blob/digest behaviorлҘј мң м§Җн•ҳкі  `0=review_ready`, `3=BLOCKED`, invalid/guard/raw codeлҘј м¶©лҸҢ м—Ҷмқҙ кІҖмҰқ |
| `C00Q-HOLD-05` | acceptance нҷҳкІҪмқҳ pinned dependency materializationкіј direct command receiptлҠ” ліҙмЎҙлҗЁ | root dependencyлҠ” accepted runм—җм„ңл§Ң мһ„мӢң мӮ¬мҡ©н–Ҳкі  package/lock ліҖкІҪ `0`; мғҲ мӢӨн–үмқҖ мғҲ authority н•„мҡ” |
| `C00Q-HOLD-06` | C00Q formal receiptлҠ” ліҙмЎҙлҗҗмңјлӮҳ authority ceilingкіј лі„лҸ„ C00B judge кІҪкі„лҠ” к·ёлҢҖлЎң | C00Q exit `0`кіј retained receiptлҠ” P0 PASSк°Җ м•„лӢҲл©° outputм—җ `p1_unlocked`/approval grantлҘј л‘җм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ; C00B separate judgeл§Ң P0 receiptлҘј нҢҗм • |

кіөк°ң мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ© к·јкұ°лҠ” `tools/team_preflight.mjs`мқҳ `DatabaseSync(...,{readOnly:true})` л’Ө мҰүмӢң
`PRAGMA query_only=ON`мқ„ кұ°лҠ” мқҙмӨ‘ guardмҷҖ `test/team_preflight_read_only.test.mjs`мқҳ synthetic write
rejectВ·before/after SHA-256/size/mtime equalityлӢӨ. л°ҳлҢҖлЎң `src/store.mjs#openStore`лҠ” WALВ·DDLВ·migrationВ·
backfillмқ„ мҲҳн–үн•ҳлҜҖлЎң C00Qк°Җ нҳём¶ңн•ҳкұ°лӮҳ importн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. C00Q synthetic validatorлҠ” мқҙ нҢЁн„ҙм—җ лҚ”н•ҙ
`PRAGMA query_only` readback `1`, `total_changes()=0`, finally-close, deterministic digest,
missing authority/source `BLOCKED`, raw/title/body/path/secret sentinel `0`мқ„ кІҖмҰқн•ҙм•ј н•ңлӢӨ. C00BлҠ”
accepted frozen tool/schema refмҷҖ laneлі„ exact authority/source/profile/output/expiryлҘј лі„лҸ„ owner
approvalлЎң л°ӣм•„м•ј н•ҳл©°, toolмқ„ мҲҳм •н•ҳкұ°лӮҳ doctor/device/workspace-system кІ°кіјлЎң live proofлҘј лҢҖмІҙн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

retained C00Q receiptлҘј мғҲ baselineм—җм„ң мһ¬кІҖмҰқн•ҙм•ј н•  л•Ңмқҳ canonical root-cwd validatorлҠ”
`node --check ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/tools/task_engine_inventory.mjs`мҷҖ
`node --test ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/test/task_engine_inventory.test.mjs`лӢӨ. C00Bмқҳ canonical root-cwd
command нӣ„ліҙлҠ” `node ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/tools/task_engine_inventory.mjs --query-only --json`мқҙм§Җл§Ң,
accepted C00Q receiptмҷҖ C00B exact authority packet м „м—җлҠ” мӢӨн–үн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

#### 18.2.2 C00B readiness verdict вҖ” `PURE JUDGE FOUNDATION EXISTS / LIVE BINDING HOLD`

C00B pure judge/receipt schema/focused testлҠ” source foundationмңјлЎң мЎҙмһ¬н•ңлӢӨ. к·ёлҹ¬лӮҳ C00BлҠ” C00Q лҸ„кө¬лҘј
live sourceм—җ л°”мқёл”©н•ҳлҠ” мӢӨн–үкіј к·ё manifestлҘј нҢҗм •н•ҳлҠ” separate judgeлҘј н•Ёк»ҳ к°ҖлҰ¬нӮӨл©°, нҳ„мһ¬ exact
authority packetмқҖ м—ҶлӢӨ. м•„лһҳ н•ӯлӘ©мқ„ м „л¶Җ ownerк°Җ кі м •н•ҳкё° м „м—җлҠ” live command
нӣ„ліҙлҘј мӢӨн–үн•ҳкұ°лӮҳ C00-LIVE-01..04лҘј лӢ«м•ҳлӢӨкі  мЈјмһҘн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

2026-07-16 м¶”к°Җ binding-producer foundationмқҖ owner-approved private binding inputм—җм„ң private C00Q
descriptor, safe aggregate evidence, digest-bound C00B packetмқ„ мғқм„ұн•ҳлҸ„лЎқ н•ң кіөк°ң лҸ„кө¬В·strict schemaВ·
focused test кі„м•ҪмқҙлӢӨ. мӢқлі„мһҗлҠ” `task_engine_inventory_c00b_binding_producer.mjs`,
`soulforge.task_engine_inventory_c00b_binding_input.v1`,
`soulforge.task_engine_inventory_safe_aggregate_evidence.v1`, `validate:task-engine-c00b-binding-v1`мқҙл©°
frozen C00Q/C00B нҢҢмқјмқҖ ліҖкІҪн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. нҳ„мһ¬ live-ready descriptorлҠ” м—Ҷкі  private л©ҙм—җлҠ” 5-lane
`attested_gap` proposal descriptorл§Ң мһҲмңјл©° public мҪ”л“ң defaultлҠ” live bindingмқҙ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. LocatorлҠ”
private input-onlyлӢӨ. File mtimeмқҖ business freshnessк°Җ м•„лӢҲкі  л¶Ҳмҷ„м „н•ң
grantлҠ” fail closedн•ңлӢӨ. C00B PASSлҸ„ H00 reviewл§Ң м—ҙл©° P1В·writerВ·activationмқ„ м—ҙм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
ProducerлҠ” лЁјм Җ locatorлҘј м¶ңл Ҙн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ” digest proposalл§Ң л§Ңл“Өкі , к·ё digestВ·source contractВ·descriptorВ·
safe aggregate evidenceм—җ лі„лҸ„лЎң кІ°н•©лҗң private authority inputмқҙ мһҲм–ҙм•ј final packetмқ„ л§Ңл“ лӢӨ. Producerк°Җ
к¶Ңн•ң digestлҘј мҠӨмҠӨлЎң мұ„мҡ°лҠ” кІғмқҖ кёҲм§Җн•ңлӢӨ. Private control artifact writeлҠ” grantм—җ digestлЎң кІ°н•©лҗң real
output rootмҷҖ м„ё exact filenameмңјлЎңл§Ң н—Ҳмҡ©н•ҳл©°, мқҙлҠ” C00B judgeмқҳ `stdout_only/durable_writes: 0` м—…л¬ҙ
мһҗлЈҢ м¶ңл Ҙ кі„м•Ҫкіј кө¬л¶„н•ңлӢӨ. Temp filenameмқҖ л§Ңл“Өм§Җ м•Ҡкі  failure cleanupлҸ„ output pathnameмқ„ мӮӯм ңн•ҳм§Җ
м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. м „мІҙ packetмқҙ proposal мғҒнғңм—¬лҸ„ descriptorлҠ” лі„лҸ„ `descriptor_binding_state: approved`мҷҖ л‘җ
artifact digestм—җ кІ°н•©лҗң `descriptor_materialization_approved`к°Җ мһҲм–ҙм•јл§Ң м“ё мҲҳ мһҲлӢӨ. м—…л¬ҙ freshnessлҠ”
source-owned/authority-attested timestamp, мөңлҢҖ stale мҙҲ,
source authority evidence ref мқјм№ҳлЎң кІҖмҰқн•ҳкі  file mtimeмңјлЎң лҢҖмІҙн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
Proposal лӢЁкі„мқҳ source evidence authorityлҠ” aggregate carrierлҘј мғқлһөн•  мҲҳ мһҲм§Җл§Ң, final packetмқҖ sourceл§ҲлӢӨ
safe aggregate evidence digestмҷҖ м •нҷ•нһҲ мқјм№ҳн•ҳлҠ” `aggregate:<64hex>` ref н•ҳлӮҳлҘј
`source_evidence_authority.evidence_refs`м—җ нҸ¬н•Ён•ҙм•ј н•ңлӢӨ. Observation evidence refsм—җлҠ” carrierлҘј л‘җм§Җ м•Ҡмңјл©°
missingВ·wrongВ·duplicateВ·misplaced carrierлҠ” лӘЁл‘җ fail closedн•ңлӢӨ. Final packetмқҖ write м „м—җ unchanged frozen
C00B judge preflightлҘј нҶөкіјн•ҙм•ј н•ҳлҜҖлЎң digest-consistent nested manifest extraлҸ„ producer кІҪкі„м—җм„ң м°ЁлӢЁн•ңлӢӨ.

| HOLD ID | C00B current closure мғҒнғң | м•Ҳм „ кё°ліёк°’ / лӢ«лҠ” мҰқкұ° |
| --- | --- | --- |
| `C00B-HOLD-01` | C00A blockerмҷҖ frozen C00Q full-B/V receiptлҠ” retained; current C00B approval-time `HEAD==origin/main`, exact root cwdВ·command/flags, commit/blob/digest refs, approval refВ·expiryВ·revocationмқҖ лі„лҸ„ н•„мҡ” | current ref/expiryк°Җ м—Ҷкұ°лӮҳ driftн•ҳл©ҙ query `0`; C00BлҠ” frozen C00Q нҢҢмқјмқ„ кі м№ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ |
| `C00B-HOLD-02` | executor node identityмҷҖ exact bootstrap profileВ·inventory authority, issued-atмҷҖ effective expiry | profileмқ„ нҸҙлҚ” мЎҙмһ¬лӮҳ doctor advisoryлЎң мҠ№кІ©н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ. private/local binding sourceк°Җ н•„мҡ”н•ҳл©ҙ valid owner-approved `owner-with-state`мҷҖ inventory authorityк°Җ лӘЁл‘җ мһҲм–ҙм•ј н•ҳл©°, packet/source-authority expiry мӨ‘ к°ҖмһҘ мқҙлҘё к°’мқ„ м Ғмҡ©. мқҙкІғмқҖ operational-primary/writer grantк°Җ м•„лӢҳ |
| `C00B-HOLD-03` | laneлі„ P0 inventory expected source set, required/optional/not-applicable owner rule, input-only descriptor/locator, adapter ID/version, source-evidence authority scopeмҷҖ freshness | execution authorityВ·source evidence authorityВ·P0 judge authorityлҘј л¶„лҰ¬. authority-attested current л¶Җмһ¬/gapмқҖ inventory findingмңјлЎң ліҙмЎҙн•  мҲҳ мһҲм§Җл§Ң missing/expired authority лҳҗлҠ” required source лҲ„лқҪмқҖ `BLOCKED`; D25 history-completeness expected setкіј кө¬л¶„ |
| `C00B-HOLD-04` | sourceлі„ literal read allowlist, query/PRAGMA allowlist digest, row/time boundмҷҖ concurrency/quiescence мЎ°кұҙ | root-wide enumerationВ·globВ·raw rowВ·migration/import кёҲм§Җ; descriptor locatorлҠ” мһ…л Ҙм—җл§Ң мһҲкі  outputмқҖ opaque ref/digestл§Ң мӮ¬мҡ© |
| `C00B-HOLD-05` | metadata-only output field allowlist, output owner/destination, retentionкіј durable receipt ref | нҳ„мһ¬ м•Ҳм „ кё°ліёк°’мқҖ stdout-onlyВ·м§ҖмҶҚ write `0`; private metadata receiptк°Җ н•„мҡ”н•ҳл©ҙ exact one-path write allowlistмҷҖ лі„лҸ„ мҠ№мқёмқ„ л°ӣм•„ `source/tracked zero-mutation + approved output one-write`лЎң н‘ңнҳ„. public outputм—җлҠ” host path/account/file name/raw valueлҘј л‘җм§Җ м•ҠмқҢ |
| `C00B-HOLD-06` | sourceлі„ zero-mutation мҰқлӘ…лІ• | SQLiteлҠ” `readOnly:true`+`PRAGMA query_only=ON` readback `1`+`total_changes()=0`; main/WAL/SHM лҳҗлҠ” source-specific before/after SHA-256В·sizeВ·mtimeВ·existence equivalenceлҘј кі м •. lock/concurrent driftм—җлҠ” мӮ¬м „ мҠ№мқёлҗң equivalent digest/quiescent л°©лІ•л§Ң м“°кі  м—Ҷмңјл©ҙ `BLOCKED`; size/mtimeл§ҢмңјлЎң лҢҖмІҙ кёҲм§Җ |
| `C00B-HOLD-07` | C00-LIVE-01..04 inventory closureмҷҖ H00/D25 coverage acceptanceмқҳ л¶„лҰ¬ | C00Bмқҳ `source_availability_summary`лҠ” P0 availability/observabilityлҝҗ. H00 ratification м „ six-stateВ·`known_at` windowВ·gap codeВ·coverage receipt мғқм„ұ кёҲм§Җ; C00B PASSлҠ” history completenessк°Җ м•„лӢҳ |
| `C00B-HOLD-08` | evidence producerмҷҖ inspector/judgeмқҳ лі„лҸ„ receipt л°Ҹ authority effect | tool exit `0`мқҖ `review_ready_manifest`лҝҗ. `inspector_and_judge`к°Җ exact approvalsмҷҖ л„Ө proofлҘј кІҖмҰқн•ң л’Өм—җл§Ң TEAX-C00B P0 receiptлҘј л§Ңл“Өл©°, exact effectлҠ” `p0_accepted=true`, `next_gate=TEAX-H00_RATIFICATION`, H00 reviewл§Ң unlock, adapter/H00 ratification/D21~D26/writer/activation authorityлҠ” лӘЁл‘җ `false` |

Public к·јкұ°мғҒ device capability probeлҠ” advisoryмқҙл©° readiness/live checksлҘј мҲҳн–үн•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡкі ,
workspace-system inventoryлҠ” `_workspaces/system` metadataмҷҖ м„ нғқм Ғ private reportлҘј мң„н•ң лӢӨлҘё ownerлӢӨ.
л‘ҳ лӢӨ C00B source authorityлӮҳ C00-LIVE-01..04мқҳ лҢҖмІҙ мҰқкұ°к°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ. лҳҗн•ң H00 нӣ„ліҙ
`PROJECT_HISTORY_ENVELOPE_V0`лҠ” ratification м „ completeness нҢҗм •мқ„ кёҲм§Җн•ҳлҜҖлЎң, C00Bм—җм„ң к·ё six-state
matrixлҘј м„ мӮ¬мҡ©н•ҳл©ҙ `C00BвҶ’H00` мҲңм„ңк°Җ мҲңнҷҳн•ңлӢӨ. мң„ source-availability кІҪкі„к°Җ к·ё мҲңнҷҳмқ„ лҒҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

TEAX-C00AмҷҖ C00Qмқҳ кіјкұ° accepted receiptлҠ” ліҙмЎҙлҗҗм§Җл§Ң нҳ„мһ¬ мӢӨн–ү к¶Ңн•ңмқҖ л§ҢлЈҢлҗҗлӢӨ. лӢӨмқҢ м§„н–үмқҖ
current-baseline C00B exact authorityмҷҖ strict judge PASSк°Җ н•„мҡ”н•ҳл©°, retained C00Q receiptл§ҢмңјлЎң мқҙлҘј
лҢҖмІҙн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. мқҙ л¬ём„ң publish мһҗмІҙлҠ” C00B лҳҗлҠ” H00 мҠ№мқёмңјлЎң к°„мЈјн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. мҠ№мқё л’Өм—җлҸ„ `.mission`мқҙлӮҳ queueлҘј мһҗлҸҷмңјлЎң
л§Ңл“Өкұ°лӮҳ approved мғҒнғңлЎң мҳ¬лҰ¬м§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.

## 19. мҠ№мқё м „ мӨ‘лӢЁмЎ°кұҙВ·publishВ·handoff

### лҸ„мӢқ 11 вҖ” owner кІ°м •кіј activation gate

```mermaid
flowchart LR
  P["нҳ„мһ¬: C00A blocker + C00Q formal receipt retained<br/>execution authority expired"] --> OB{"Owner: C00B exact current query authority?"}
  OB -- "ліҙлҘҳ" --> STOP
  OB -- "лі„лҸ„ мҠ№мқё" --> B["C00B frozen tool + approved metadata sources"]
  B --> C0{"C00B receipt PASS?"}
  C0 -- "BLOCKED" --> STOP
  C0 -- "PASS" --> O1{"Owner: H00 exact candidate ratification?"}
  O1 -- "HOLD" --> STOP
  O1 -- "ratified" --> DI{"Applicable D19/D20/D26/D33 lane identity<br/>and owner decisions resolved?"}
  DI -- "HOLD/BLOCKED" --> STOP
  DI -- "yes" --> LP{"H01~H05 exact child packets<br/>lane owner gates approved?"}
  LP -- "no" --> STOP
  LP -- "yes" --> H["H01A~H05 pure contract shadows<br/>H01C observation reconciliation"]
  H --> DP{"D25 lane coverage policy resolved?"}
  DP -- "HOLD/BLOCKED" --> STOP
  DP -- "yes" --> HB["H01B + lane coverage receipt fixtures<br/>contract/synthetic only"]
  HB --> HG{"H01~H05 accepted?"}
  HG -- "HOLD/BLOCKED" --> STOP
  HG -- "yes" --> DV{"D22/D24 target view/field policy resolved?"}
  DV -- "HOLD/BLOCKED" --> STOP
  DV -- "yes" --> H6["H06 five-lane acceptance<br/>ratified D25 coverage policy applied"]
  H6 --> H6G{"H06 PASS?"}
  H6G -- "BLOCKED" --> STOP
  H6G -- "PASS" --> P2["P2 IDs/refs/clocks"] --> P3["P3 immutable revisions"] --> P4["P4 exact RAG/Wiki"]
  P3 --> H7{"Applied Slack source:<br/>D34 + H07A/H07B accepted?"}
  H7 -- "HOLD/BLOCKED" --> STOP
  H7 -- "PASS" --> P5["P5 context_acceptance_gate"]
  P4 --> P5
  P5 -->|"receipt accepted"| P6["P6 candidate-only discovery"]
  P6 -->|"receipt accepted"| P7["P7 TaskDriver"]
  P7 -->|"receipt accepted"| P8["P8 sole ERP writer + mail outbox"]
  P8 --> O9{"Owner: P9 one-project pilot?"}
  A8S["A8-SYNTH independent<br/>public pathless fixtures"] --> A8G{"private VERIFY_HP receipt +<br/>strict office LAN + owner + Level 3?"}
  A8G -- "yes" --> A8C["A8-CANARY<br/>one seat/project/small file"]
  A8G -- "no" --> STOP
  O9 -- "м•„лӢҲмҳӨ" --> STOP
  O9 -- "мҳҲ" --> P9["1~3 task + mail generation<br/>read-only trees + rollback"]
  P9 --> OIQ{"Owner: after-P9 I9/Q9 side-card?"}
  OIQ -- "ліҙлҘҳ" --> O10{"Owner: which P10 capability?"}
  OIQ -- "лі„лҸ„ мҠ№мқё" --> IQ["one-project payload promotion/query<br/>parity + rollback pilot"] --> O10
  O10 -- "mail failover/failback" --> MF["(C_E,P_E) role-epoch vector manual drill"]
  O10 -- "core production" --> G["G00/G01 bounded activation"]
  O10 -- "common/AX/AgentRun/IQ/ML" --> X["AX lifecycle/query/one-seat/team л“ұ<br/>each separately approved"]
  O10 -- "ліҙлҘҳ" --> STOP
```

лӢӨмқҢ мӨ‘ н•ҳлӮҳл©ҙ нҳ„мһ¬ лҳҗлҠ” лҜёлһҳ sliceлҘј мҰүмӢң мӨ‘лӢЁн•ңлӢӨ.

- approval-timeм—җ pinн•ң мӢӨн–ү Git baseк°Җ мӣҖм§ҒмҳҖкұ°лӮҳ dirty/divergent/detached/conflict/overlap/index lock мғҒнғң
- immutable oracle blob/diffк°Җ ліҖн•Ё
- allowed paths л°– ліҖкІҪ, private/raw/secret л…ём¶ң, source owner м№ЁлІ”
- query-only guard мӢӨнҢЁ лҳҗлҠ” title/body/path к°ҷмқҖ raw valueк°Җ н•„мҡ”н•Ё
- sole coordinator/logical authority/project scope/ID meaningмқҙ лӘЁнҳён•Ё
- P5 receipt м—Ҷмқҙ P6, P6 acceptance м—Ҷмқҙ P7, P7 acceptance м—Ҷмқҙ P8мқ„ мӢңмһ‘н•ҳл Ө н•Ё
- five-lane coverageм—җм„ң `not_collected`лҘј 0кұҙ/completeлЎң н•ҙм„қн•ҳкұ°лӮҳ, approved applicability ref м—Ҷмқҙ
  `not_applicable`лЎң мҲЁкё°кұ°лӮҳ, fuzzy joinмқ„ confirmedлЎң мҠ№кІ©н•Ё
- mail classification/projector leaseВ·epoch мӨ‘ н•ҳлӮҳк°Җ staleн•ҳкұ°лӮҳ DB/outbox/CSV/ICS/XLSX generation parityк°Җ л¶Ҳмқјм№ҳн•Ё
- POP3 received-only sourceлҘј team sent coverageлЎң кі„мӮ°н•ҳкұ°лӮҳ, exact provider/RFC occurrence ref м—Ҷмқҙ
  owner SentВ·team InboxВ·SMTP outbound copyлҘј confirmed mergeн•ҳкұ°лӮҳ, `cc`лҘј assigneeВ·`bcc`лҘј inferred recipientлЎң мҠ№кІ©н•Ё
- к°ҷмқҖ logical mailмқҳ accountлі„ observationм—җм„ң мӨ‘ліө task candidateлҘј л§Ңл“Өкұ°лӮҳ reply/reactionмқ„ official мҷ„лЈҢлЎң к°„мЈјн•Ё
- Slack channel name/fuzzy textлЎң projectлҘј кІ°н•©н•ҳкұ°лӮҳ effective-dated `workspace_id+channel_id` binding м—Ҷмқҙ
  project scopeлҘј нҷ•м •н•ҳкұ°лӮҳ, retry eventлҘј мӨ‘ліө messageлЎң м ҖмһҘн•ҳкұ°лӮҳ edit/deleteк°Җ кіјкұ° revisionмқ„ лҚ®м–ҙм”Җ
- allowlist л°– Slack channelВ·DMВ·commonВ·Slack ConnectВ·attachmentлҘј мһҗлҸҷ ingest/promotionн•ҳкұ°лӮҳ HPP мҷё normal
  Slack collectorк°Җ м“°кұ°лӮҳ, message/reaction/pinмқ„ ERP taskВ·accepted Wiki/RAGм—җ м§Ғм ‘ л°ҳмҳҒн•Ё
- 5к°ң project-history CSV/XLSXлҘј HPP projector л°–мқҳ PCк°Җ м •мғҒ мҡҙмҳҒм—җм„ң м“°кұ°лӮҳ, source event/refмҷҖ
  accepted cutoff/generation parityк°Җ л¶Ҳмқјм№ҳн•Ё
- source custody, upload receipt, classification, promotion, ArtifactRevision/knowledge acceptanceлҘј к°ҷмқҖ
  мғҒнғңлЎң к°„мЈјн•ҳкұ°лӮҳ мҠ№мқё м—Ҷмқҙ payload copy/move/deleteВ·physical ingress folder мғқм„ұмқҙ н•„мҡ”н•Ё
- personal WorkSession closeout/proposalмқ„ ERP кіөмӢқ мҷ„лЈҢлЎң к°„мЈјн•ҳкұ°лӮҳ, accepted server ack м „ local
  outboxлҘј м§Җмҡ°кұ°лӮҳ, local pendingкіј server missing-closeoutмқ„ к°ҷмқҖ мғҒнғңлЎң н•ҙм„қн•Ё
- external clientмқҳ terminal idleВ·worker doneВ·decision gateВ·Kanban doneВ·goal judgeлҘј WorkSession closeout,
  AgentRun success, verification pass, owner approval лҳҗлҠ” ERP official completionмңјлЎң мҠ№кІ©н•Ё
- Hermesнҳ• gatewayмҷҖ Orcaнҳ• workbenchк°Җ м„ңлЎңлҘј launch/callн•ҳкұ°лӮҳ к°ҷмқҖ write-capable WorkSession tokenмқ„
  кіөмң н•ҳкі , child agentк°Җ checkpoint/completion proposalмқ„ м§Ғм ‘ м”Җ
- external agentк°Җ permission-bypass/yoloлЎң мӢӨн–үлҗҳкұ°лӮҳ worktreeлҘј host sandboxлЎң мҳӨмқён•ҳкі  secret/home/D:/
  OneDrive/private repo/networkлҘј allowlist л°–м—җм„ң м ‘к·јн•Ё
- Orcaнҳ• clientк°Җ main commit/push/PRмқ„ м§Ғм ‘ мҲҳн–үн•ҳкұ°лӮҳ unapproved drag/drop/attachmentмҷҖ binary artifactлҘј
  multi-writerлЎң мҲҳм •н•Ё
- query scope/ACL/generation/claim ceilingмқҙ м—Ҷкұ°лӮҳ project/common implicit fallback, snapshot reverse import,
  teamмқҳ Wiki/RAG/canon/ontology/task м§Ғм ‘ м“°кё°к°Җ н•„мҡ”н•Ё
- valid backup/restoreк°Җ м—Ҷкұ°лӮҳ replay/readback/rollbackмқҙ л¶Ҳмқјм№ҳ
- owner-confirmed `_workspaces/<project>` topologyлҘј rename/rematerialize/bootstrap/repairн•ҙм•ј н•ҳкұ°лӮҳ
  topology delta, OneDrive лӮҙ DB/WAL/RAW/queue/outbox/quarantine, non-HPPмқҳ D/UNC/SMB/SQLite м ‘к·јмқҙ мғқк№Җ
- actor chainВ·delegation ceilingВ·earliest expiryВ·revoke cascadeк°Җ л№ м§Җкұ°лӮҳ ticket field swap/replay/race,
  path traversal/archive bomb/hash/size/media mismatch, exact-revision download guardк°Җ fail openн•Ё
- artifact/revision/action existence policyлӮҳ RAG field/chunk/cache filterк°Җ л¶Ҳмқјм№ҳн•ҳкұ°лӮҳ redacted derivativeк°Җ
  hidden sheet/slideВ·formulaВ·comment/noteВ·embedded object lineage м—Ҷмқҙ rawлЎң fallbackн•Ё
- `A8-CANARY`к°Җ `A8-SYNTH PASS`, accepted private `VERIFY_HP` exact binding receipt, strict office-LAN
  binding, explicit owner approval, Level 3 live gate мӨ‘ н•ҳлӮҳ м—Ҷмқҙ мӢӨн–үлҗҳкұ°лӮҳ VPN/Tailscale/remote laneмқҙ н•„мҡ”н•Ё
- scanner/scheduler/network/alert/operational-primaryлҘј лі„лҸ„ мҠ№мқё м—Ҷмқҙ мјңм•ј н•Ё
- `UNKNOWN`мқ„ м¶”м •н•ҙм•ј лӢӨмқҢ лӢЁкі„лЎң к°Ҳ мҲҳ мһҲмқҢ

мқҙлІҲ HPP addendumмқҳ exact public draft scopeлҠ” лӢӨмқҢ 9к°ң changed pathлҝҗмқҙлӢӨ:
`CHANGELOG.md`, `docs/architecture/workspace/MULTI_PC_DEVELOPMENT_V0.md`,
`docs/architecture/workspace/VOICE_CAPTURE_MVP_V0.md`,
`docs/architecture/workspace/WORKSPACE_INTAKE_INBOX_V0.md`,
`ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/docs/AX_WORKSPACE_TASK_ENGINE_INTEGRATED_VALIDATION_PLAN_V0.md`,
`ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/docs/CODEX_TEAM_WORKSPACE.md`, мқҙ master plan,
`ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/docs/WINDOWS_LAN_DEPLOY.md`,
`ui-workspace/apps/dev-erp/docs/slices/ERP-MCP-V0.md`. Fresh Level 2 plan reviewлҠ” acceptedлҗҗм§Җл§Ң
owner approvalВ·publishВ·implementationВ·live authorityлҠ” мғқкё°м§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
мқҙлІҲ correctionм—җм„ңлҠ” companion `_workmeta`
repoк°Җ мһ‘м—… мӢңмһ‘ м „л¶Җн„° unrelated dirty/ahead мғҒнғңлқј review/5-field packetмқ„ м“°м§Җ м•Ҡм•ҳкі  н•ҙлӢ№ repoлҘј
ліҖкІҪн•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡм•ҳлӢӨ. Public кі„нҡҚ нҢҢмқјкіј `CHANGELOG.md`л§Ң publishн•ңлӢӨ.

### кі„нҡҚ лІ”мң„ мөңмў… кІҖмҰқ receipt

м•„лһҳ н‘ңлҠ” мөңмҙҲ correctionкіј 2026-07-15 нӣ„мҶҚ correctionмқҳ historical receiptлӢӨ.
лӘ…л №лӘ…мқҙ к°ҷм•„лҸ„ мқҙлІҲм—җ лӢӨмӢң мӢӨн–үн•ҳм§Җ м•ҠмқҖ мӣҗліё кІ°кіјлҠ” `HISTORICAL_REPORTED`лЎңл§Ң мқҪлҠ”лӢӨ. мқҙлІҲ
follow-upмқҖ fresh inspector `REVISEвҶ’ліҙм •вҶ’ACCEPT`мҷҖ independent judge `REVISEвҶ’ліҙм •вҶ’ACCEPT`лЎң лӢ«м•ҳлӢӨ.
мөңмў… delta commitмқҖ self-referenceлҘј н”јн•ҳкё° мң„н•ҙ л¬ём„ң л°– publish ліҙкі м—җ лӮЁкёҙлӢӨ.

2026-07-16 HPP MCP/storage/access addendumмқҖ мқҙ кё°мЎҙ receiptліҙлӢӨ л’Өмқҳ `source_supported` plan correctionмқҙлӢӨ.
м•„лһҳ кіјкұ° fresh-inspector/validator л¬ёкө¬лҘј мғҲ addendumмқҳ production/runtime кІҖмҰқмңјлЎң мһ¬мӮ¬мҡ©н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ.
нҳ„мһ¬ exact nine-file deltaлҠ” fresh Level 2 inspectorмҷҖ independent judgeк°Җ `ACCEPT_FOR_PLAN_SCOPE`лЎң
нҢҗм •н–ҲлӢӨ. мқҙ нҢҗм •мқҖ plan scopeм—җл§Ң мң нҡЁн•ҳл©° implementation, private binding, P0~P10 acceptance,
owner approval, canary/runtime readiness evidenceк°Җ м•„лӢҲлӢӨ.

мң„ receiptлҠ” кө¬нҳ„, runtime readiness, private inventory, C00B/P0 acceptanceлҘј мҰқлӘ…н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. Final

### AC-01~AC-25 completeness вҖ” verified for plan scope

мөңмҙҲ correctionкіј 2026-07-15 follow-upмқҳ reviewer/validator кІ°кіјлҠ” мң„ historical receipt лІ”мң„м—җм„ңл§Ң
мң нҡЁн•ҳлӢӨ. нҳ„мһ¬ exact nine-file HPP addendumлҸ„ fresh final inspectorмҷҖ independent judgeк°Җ plan scopeм—җм„ң
acceptedн–ҲмңјлҜҖлЎң HPP-specific AC н–үмқ„ `VERIFIED_FOR_PLAN_SCOPE`лЎң лӢ«лҠ”лӢӨ. лӘЁл“ 
`VERIFIED_FOR_PLAN_SCOPE`лҠ” кө¬нҳ„В·C00B мҠ№мқёВ·P0~P10 acceptanceВ·private bindingВ·owner
approvalВ·canary/runtime readinessВ·live activationмқ„ лң»н•ҳм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. C00A/C00Q retained receiptмҷҖлҸ„
лі„к°ңмқҙл©° current execution authorityлҘј л¶Җм—¬н•ҳм§Җ м•Ҡкі , CV-02лҠ” P0 acceptanceлҘј кі„мҶҚ л§үлҠ”лӢӨ.

| AC | мғҒнғң | мқҙ л¬ём„ңмқҳ мҰқкұ° |
| --- | --- | --- |
| AC-01 | `VERIFIED_FOR_PLAN_SCOPE` | В§0~1мқҳ мӢӨм ң кө¬м¶• лӘ©м Ғ; comparisonмқҖ oracleлЎңл§Ң мӮ¬мҡ© |
| AC-02 | `VERIFIED_FOR_PLAN_SCOPE` | В§2 current Git кё°мӨҖм„ ; immutable oracle scoped diff `0` |

Clean scoped commit+push, мқҙ л¬ём„ңмқҳ кІ°м •н‘ң, validator/review evidenceлЎң forward stateк°Җ лӘЁл‘җ
ліҙмЎҙлҗҳл©ҙ `NIGHT_WORK_HANDOFF`лҘј л§Ңл“Өм§Җ м•ҠлҠ”лӢӨ. лҜён•ҙкІ° мӢңлҸ„лӮҳ controller/PC м „нҷҳмңјлЎңл§Ң лӮЁлҠ”
forward stateк°Җ мғқкёё л•Ңл§Ң лі„лҸ„ handoffлҘј л§Ңл“ лӢӨ.

### мқҙлІҲ лӢЁкі„ мөңмў… л¶ҲліҖмӢқ
